
-----title
韶关 (出生地)

href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1012&endYear=1012')">1012年</a>　受黄正悉心教诲，父余庆亦时加指点。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='2ffd9bdc9bed4809adf4f67be0f23c06_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("2ffd9bdc9bed4809adf4f67be0f23c06");'><span id='2ffd9bdc9bed4809adf4f67be0f23c06_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1017&endYear=1017')">1017年</a>　冬，余靖归家，韶州知州许申赞余靖好学。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1018&endYear=1018')">1018年</a>　林从周赴京述职，送次女到韶州与余靖完婚。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1018&endYear=1018')">1018年</a>　余靖拜见王式父子。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='f419185fccd847d9b0ff16ff35a5429d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f419185fccd847d9b0ff16ff35a5429d");'><span id='f419185fccd847d9b0ff16ff35a5429d_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1020&endYear=1020')">1020年</a>，21岁</div><div id='f419185fccd847d9b0ff16ff35a5429d' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1020&endYear=1020')">1020年11月</a>　冬末，余靖归曲江。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='0dddb3cb9f8f457ab7795de53a1f12c8_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("0dddb3cb9f8f457ab7795de53a1f12c8");'><span id='0dddb3cb9f8f457ab7795de53a1f12c8_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1023&endYear=1023')">1023年3月</a>　暮春，余靖告别老师返回韶州。是年，林从周出为两浙提点刑狱。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1023&endYear=1023')">1023年</a>　余靖次男仲荀出生。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='b10f0b05746c484e9ebf88c902c7a58e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b10f0b05746c484e9ebf88c902c7a58e");'><span id='b10f0b05746c484e9ebf88c902c7a58e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1032&endYear=1032')">1032年</a>，33岁</div><div id='b10f0b05746c484e9ebf88c902c7a58e' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>归家省亲，应邀撰文。作品：韶州白云山延寿禅院传法记。韶州新修州衙记。<div id='poem_1158990' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158990' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158990?labeling=true' target='_blank'>韶州白云山延寿禅院传法记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1032年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158990")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158990_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158990'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158990'>昔者金人见梦，经像始东，而图绘缔构、奉遗教者遍于天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158990_comment'></div>既而汉之宗祀，废于当涂，魏之血食，绝于典午，西方塔庙，岿然无改，大雄之德，何其盛哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158990_comment'></div>迄今千祀，寅恭益众，由是王而侯国，商关农井，茍有生聚，必为浮图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158990_comment'></div>大抵南方富于山水，号为千岩竞秀、万壑争流，所以浮图之居，必获奇胜之域也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158990_comment'></div>实性大师，始来居之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158990_comment'></div>绝涧高峰，恍出物外，阴谷夏雪，阳崖冬葩，故非区区林麓之所比也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158990_comment'></div>古者谓穹山浚泽，必能兴云致雨，以济民望，故以白云名之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158990_comment'></div>观夫高士，远迹当世，非独玩云霞之容，同禽鱼之乐而已，盖将脱去声利，深入杳霭，目绝尘累，耳忘俗嚣，而后真性湛然，如太虚月，旁无壅障，乃克通照耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158990_comment'></div>所居高深，所乐旷远者，以此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158990_comment'></div>禅那之学，其来尚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158990_comment'></div>自南北分宗，思让异派，虽达空照理，共归悬解，而临机接应，各禀师模，言有体用，义有纵夺，互相祖习，曰为门风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158990_comment'></div>然而无善可求，无恶可去，直指宗门，令其悟入，云门之教，最号真淳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158990_comment'></div>实性即云门之嫡也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158990_comment'></div>实性者，刘主所赐师号也，名志庠，封州人，姓陈氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158990_comment'></div>广主延入府中，亲问法要，有名《传灯录》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158990_comment'></div>庠既即世，志文开堂嗣之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158990_comment'></div>次曰契本禅师达正，次曰达真禅师云端，次曰妙光大师云福，皆承师嗣法，世赐师名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158990_comment'></div>厥后有惠龙者，凤翔人，姓赵氏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158990_comment'></div>今长老常简，永嘉人，姓徐氏，皆什方名德之选也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158990_comment'></div>自实性至今七世矣，栋宇加饬焉，田畴加辟焉，仓廪加入焉，器用加给焉，徒众加进焉，远近加信焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1158990_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1158990_comment'></div>今夫公侯将相之家，不过一传再传，或当世而绝者，岂非道家所忌、陈平所识阴谋而害人者耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1158990_comment'></div>至于浮图氏，托大义以承嗣，而能世广基构，至于不朽，贤于阴谋者远矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1158990_comment'></div>其可书也，遂志其世云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1158990_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1158969' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158969' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158969?labeling=true' target='_blank'>韶州新修州衙记</a><span class='authorDate'>（明道元年十一月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158969")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158969_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158969'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158969'>古者诸侯宫室、车服，各视其命之数，故台门露寝，将将耽耽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158969_comment'></div>自秦人罢侯，汉沿魏袭，郡有守，州有牧，颁条诏，专生杀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158969_comment'></div>虑其久而固人心，必三岁而易之，修职贡于天子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158969_comment'></div>在千里外，则递促其期，再期而易者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158969_comment'></div>故州民视刺史如路人，刺史视公堂如传舍，民病尚不肯疗，矧肯完葺廨宇耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158969_comment'></div>韶在番禺之北，去天子都城三千里而遥，故为远官，去留之心不固，又可知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158969_comment'></div>皇上即位之八年，以今尚书外郎、太原王君守其土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158969_comment'></div>下车之始，纲目咸振，束黠吏以绳墨，制强宗以斧斤，威声一驰，境内知禁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158969_comment'></div>然后险者倾，疮者平，痼者愈，魇者醒，仆者起，昧者明，霜清物寒，日和春融，畏爱所交，衣被黔首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158969_comment'></div>于是中诏得比内诸侯，满三岁后所请也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158969_comment'></div>政成事简，地居冲要，筑室卑陋，人何所瞻？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158969_comment'></div>不欲视廨舍如前人之视民病也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158969_comment'></div>繇是因基搆，程用度，壮栋梁，丽榱桷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158969_comment'></div>山有羡材，不赋于民；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158969_comment'></div>官有缮工，不兴其役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158969_comment'></div>焕诸侯之采章，谨列郡之仪式。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158969_comment'></div>挈壶所以授朔，树戟所以示威，乃伉高门，以备其制，分争辨讼，夙兴夜寐，外皇中堂，各有攸处，首徇公也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158969_comment'></div>兔穴防奸，简书山积，虎符领兵，器甲犀利，对峙二库，加以层楼，谨曝凉也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158969_comment'></div>接贤序宾，容豆举觯，则有东西小厅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158969_comment'></div>地暖春早，百卉先媚，亭曰探芳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1158969_comment'></div>疏池酾流，一水回合，亭曰环翠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1158969_comment'></div>射侯之亭曰百中，可以观德也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1158969_comment'></div>燕居之亭曰清虚，可以颐神也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1158969_comment'></div>翚飞翼舒，不僭不偪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1158969_comment'></div>城隅一楼，景最奇绝，东溪北山，秀在眉宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1158969_comment'></div>落成之日，露袭竹柏，味䬰颗珠，圆美可爱，亭曰甘露，纪嘉瑞也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1158969_comment'></div>至于胥史分联，廪储供上，风雨之庇，使葺之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1158969_comment'></div>工既毕，民吏趋走扶伏，固请砻石刻文，以纪成绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1158969_comment'></div>星飞一介，见辱嘉命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1158969_comment'></div>谨按图经，控扼五岭，韶为交衢，虞舜南巡，奏乐于此，郡有遗迹，因山得名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1158969_comment'></div>汉置曲江县，为南海之望邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1158969_comment'></div>晋立东衡州，居湖南之属城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1158969_comment'></div>齐梁为始兴郡，置内史以莅之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1158969_comment'></div>伪刘割据，析其地建英、雄二州，故始兴之名移于他部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1158969_comment'></div>皇朝开国，军事民政，咸俾儒臣领之，邕容经略，名存实亡，拟于舜韶，彼则负矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1158969_comment'></div>唇齿江湘，咽喉交广，地之重也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1158969_comment'></div>霜露北均，疫疠南尽，气之和也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1158969_comment'></div>霞駮万拱，云蒸千础，署之广也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1158969_comment'></div>合是数美，为郡国最，不亦善乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1158969_comment'></div>君以天圣庚午，自殿中丞领银菟符，期年之间，再增秩至屯田员外郎，则为郡之才之政，为万乘知，可见矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1158969_comment'></div>明道元年十一月日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1158969_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='5f51a934b35b4e008a652d7169d0c883_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("5f51a934b35b4e008a652d7169d0c883");'><span id='5f51a934b35b4e008a652d7169d0c883_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1038')">1038年</a>，39岁</div><div id='5f51a934b35b4e008a652d7169d0c883' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1038')">1038年</a>　赴泰州前，告假回曲江省视高堂。单身宿于深山寺观有感，赋诗。作品：宿山观。<div id='poem_99519' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99519' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99519?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宿山观</a><span class='authorDate'>（1038年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99519")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_99519_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99519'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99519'>孤枕秋宵永，山寒梦不成。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99519_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99519'>残灯背窗影，急雨带溪声。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99519_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99519'>未分山中老，空思日下名。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99519_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99519'>区区如逆旅，此际若为情。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99519_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_99519'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_99519_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1038')">1038年4月</a>　应州官之请，作文。作品：浈水馆记。<div id='poem_1158968' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158968' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158968?labeling=true' target='_blank'>韶州真水馆记</a><span class='authorDate'>（景祐五年四月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158968")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158968_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158968'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158968'>真水馆者，郡守田曹副郎清河张公所建也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158968_comment'></div>按地志，真水出大庾岭<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>，南与武水合，二水回曲而流，故名曲江。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158968_comment'></div>虞舜南巡，奏《箫韶》于群石之右，故名其山曰韶，由是州以山名，县以水名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158968_comment'></div>凡广东西之通道有三：出零陵下离水者由桂州，出豫章下真水者由韶州，出桂阳下武水者亦由韶州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158968_comment'></div>无虑之官峤南，自京都沿汴绝淮，由堰道入漕渠，溯大江，度梅岭，下真水至南海之东、西江者，唯岭道九十里为马上之役，馀皆篙工楫人之劳，全家坐而致万里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158968_comment'></div>故之峤南虽三道，下真水者十七八焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158968_comment'></div>刘氏之自王也，割韶之壤，置英、雄二州，壤虽减而道如故，韶于岭外为剧郡宜矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158968_comment'></div>今上嗣位，三改元而得景祐，其三年，公自浔江郡易地而领是邦，政均而易从，令约而易乂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158968_comment'></div>雨润霜严，施之有宜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158968_comment'></div>补坠起废，理无遗具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158968_comment'></div>先是，郡有二馆：一临武水曰清辉，一据城之东隅曰皇华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158968_comment'></div>惟真水之要津，则皆亭以居舣舟之次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158968_comment'></div>公乃与宾佐谋曰：「若天子之使、诸侯之宾，将王命，宣民风，乘舳舻由真水而至者，不授以馆，则饩牵积馈虽厚，不得盘桓上舍，优游山水间，地主之礼，犹为缺哉」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158968_comment'></div>然由是择境于胜，相地于隙，取材于羡馀，取工于卒徒，民不知役而功用毕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158968_comment'></div>东瞰真水，故即水名之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158968_comment'></div>凡一堂、一皇、二室、两庑以翼于门，宿息井树具焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158968_comment'></div>前构飞阁，命曰「仁智」，乐山水之趣也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158968_comment'></div>烟齐远水，风生白蘋，栏槛千家，松萝四望，真仁智之所乐也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158968_comment'></div>后之至者，有以见清河公求瘼之外，又能乐山水之嘉，不独饬厨传以异上宾，盖将使仁智者同此乐云耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158968_comment'></div>时景祐五年岁在豕韦四月日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1158968_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1158968'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_1158968_0'>⑴ 字本从水从贞，今朝以音犯庙讳，故改为真。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1158968_comment'></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='50dcfd7ea1864dd7becf8ae92be859a8_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("50dcfd7ea1864dd7becf8ae92be859a8");'><span id='50dcfd7ea1864dd7becf8ae92be859a8_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1038')">1038年</a>，39岁</div><div id='50dcfd7ea1864dd7becf8ae92be859a8' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1038')">1038年11月</a>　应大理寺丞冯恢、殿中丞冯元兄弟之请，为其母作墓志铭。作品：宋故冯翊县太君王夫人墓志铭。<div id='poem_1159025' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159025' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159025?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宋故冯翊县太君王夫人墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1038年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1159025")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159025_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159025'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159025'>夫人姓王氏，金陵人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159025_comment'></div>父讳某，仕李主，为如京使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159025_comment'></div>王师渡江，既黜唐命，革用其俊，授右班殿直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159025_comment'></div>夫人徽柔懿淑，克谨女训，自丱总即干母蛊，枨闑之内，壹以付之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159025_comment'></div>其慈明孝爱，出于资性，闺门整饬，动协仪矩，族姻罔不尚其节焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159025_comment'></div>尝因季春墓祭，出见亲之贫者，即解衣衣之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159025_comment'></div>母曰：「衣岂妄得，何遽与人」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159025_comment'></div>对曰：「纷华非性所适，且怜其窭甚，杼轴可完，宗亲不可携也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159025_comment'></div>母繇此益奇之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159025_comment'></div>凡四时蒸尝，夫人必手钥壹室，牢馔盏醴，菹腥脯醢，洁器异齐，以备其物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159025_comment'></div>常曰：「祀享，人之大事，故须严洁，以表至诚」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159025_comment'></div>幼怀异节，率皆此类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159025_comment'></div>年十九，归于户部郎中许氏，事其姑如其母而加谨焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159025_comment'></div>怡声下色，调膳扇枕，虽隆冬瘅暑，必躬亲之，未尝一委媵妾之手，室中举案，侃侃如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159025_comment'></div>姑亡，不食三日，冒绖被缞，动必以礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159025_comment'></div>其族妇有贤而孝者，族人齿之，必曰何如王氏，其爱慕也如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159025_comment'></div>其与兄伯同居，事其姒如姑之存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159025_comment'></div>岁入地征，月入官奉，悉归兄伯之室，簪毫不以自名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159025_comment'></div>婴孩之费，一请于其姒，曰：「世母在，吾何敢专」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159025_comment'></div>其谦让之性然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159025_comment'></div>户部府君远宦十年，夫人足不逾阃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159025_comment'></div>夫、伯俱亡，抚养诸孤，均若己出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159025_comment'></div>聚居且百口，恩意怡怡，一亡间言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159025_comment'></div>训诲子侄，目见成立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159025_comment'></div>夫人再封邑，临沂以夫封，冯翊以子封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159025_comment'></div>享寿八十，以宝元元年岁次戊寅十一月某日，终于海陵私第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159025_comment'></div>子五人，偕举进士：长曰恂，通州司户参军；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1159025_comment'></div>次曰恢，大理寺丞、知常州晋陵县；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1159025_comment'></div>次曰怡，秦州司理参军；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1159025_comment'></div>次曰元，殿中丞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1159025_comment'></div>次曰平，累举未第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1159025_comment'></div>女二人：长适虞部郎中、知抚州田庆远，次适职方员外郎、知永州张楚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1159025_comment'></div>孙几人，亦各材俊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1159025_comment'></div>卜葬，得某年月日与户部府君合祔，礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1159025_comment'></div>某，元之执，故为铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_34_1159025'>猗欤哲妇，生此南国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1159025_comment'></div>始励柔淑，以植女德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1159025_comment'></div>衷勤孝懿，以光壸则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1159025_comment'></div>终笃慈爱，以宣贤式。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1159025_comment'></div>族人以和，母训以饬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1159025_comment'></div>诸子咸仕，出于风力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1159025_comment'></div>佳城郁郁，义声亡极。</div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1159025_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1038')">1038年12月</a>　应三司副使张存复、殿直曹元素之请，作记。作品：楚州盐城南埸公团壁记。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='bf64eda0d147484bb1f8d1bb9ff0a3bf_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("bf64eda0d147484bb1f8d1bb9ff0a3bf");'><span id='bf64eda0d147484bb1f8d1bb9ff0a3bf_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1039&endYear=1040')">1039-1040年</a>，40-41岁</div><div id='bf64eda0d147484bb1f8d1bb9ff0a3bf' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1039&endYear=1039')">1039年</a>　靖守丧，数天哀号悲痛不已。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1039&endYear=1039')">1039年</a>　秋，泰州友人来函问候，因庭院花落有触哀思，作诗寄友人。作品：落花。<div id='poem_99528' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99528' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99528?labeling=true' target='_blank'>落花</a><span class='authorDate'>（1039年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99528")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_99528_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99528'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99528'>小园斜日照残芳，千里伤春意未忘。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99528_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99528'>金谷已空新步障，马嵬徒见旧香囊。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99528_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99528'>莺来似结啼鸾怨，蝶散应知梦雨狂。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99528_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99528'>清赏又成经岁别，却歌团扇寄回肠。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99528_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_99528'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_99528_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1039&endYear=1039')">1039年</a>　长子伯庄中举，长女适郭师愈。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年</a>　长子伯庄之次之孙舜臣生，伯庄为海阳县主簿，举家迁潮。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年</a>　应曲江县主簿陈有方泣请，为其父陈坦然撰墓碣。作品：宋故殿中丞知梅州陈公墓碣。<div id='poem_1159030' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159030' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159030?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宋故殿中丞知梅州陈公墓碣</a><span class='authorDate'>（康定元年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1159030")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159030_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159030'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159030'>公讳坦然，字某，其先颍川人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159030_comment'></div>高祖父效官容管，属唐季之乱，岭道梗塞，不克北还，遂为普宁郡人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159030_comment'></div>曾祖讳某、祖讳某、考讳某，并仕刘氏，为私署官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159030_comment'></div>考终于知绣州营田事，皇朝赠大理评事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159030_comment'></div>妣陶氏，赠永昌县太君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159030_comment'></div>公即绣州第三子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159030_comment'></div>博学善属词，有胆勇，多权谋，尚然诺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159030_comment'></div>举进士未第，归乡里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159030_comment'></div>景德中，宜州兵杀守帅，胁判官卢成均以叛，伪称南平王，拥众数千人，北攻象州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159030_comment'></div>成均者，公同郡人也，公乃单骑行贼围，为书约矢射成均帐下，为陈祸福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159030_comment'></div>其略曰：「国有患难，乃见忠良。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159030_comment'></div>贪人之利，而背其君，非忠也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159030_comment'></div>怯人之威，而失其志，非勇也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159030_comment'></div>君甲科进士，当以才识济理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159030_comment'></div>今佐一郡，不能抚其众，以至于乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159030_comment'></div>又不能死，乃更甘心伪号，提乌合之徒，剽却郡县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159030_comment'></div>朝廷封疆万里、带甲百万，遣偏师取狂寇，如举太山压卵耳，柰何赤族从叛人入汤镬中耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159030_comment'></div>初，象城疏弱无守备，将陷者数矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159030_comment'></div>成均得书，欲自拔归顺，计未决而王师至，城乃全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159030_comment'></div>贼又别遣一屯分掠南路，径趣容境，所至摧陷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159030_comment'></div>公入语容守陈延赏曰：「贼势剽悍，难以力兢，且胁从之人，本无战心，愿假衙兵数辈见从抵贼营，论以逆顺，当使解甲而归我矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159030_comment'></div>公去贼垒数十步下马，直前为言：「本朝正朔被四海，汝徒无故噪聚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159030_comment'></div>今有诏，止诛首恶，茍能束身改图，自当荣以爵赏，何苦草间觅活」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159030_comment'></div>是时贼中伪补屯卫之职陈、贾二率私相语曰：「此飞檄生也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159030_comment'></div>于是率首领以甲卒数百诣郡降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159030_comment'></div>贼失腹心，皆不战而自溃矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159030_comment'></div>贼平论功，大将以状闻，中旨令本郡敦遣赴阙，与官，仍赐锦袍银带。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1159030_comment'></div>公悉让而不受，愿回前恩，以就殿廷一试，朝命嘉之，诏贡部别名闻奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1159030_comment'></div>中途被病，且遭家艰以归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1159030_comment'></div>服阙，急于禄养，摄主化州吴川簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1159030_comment'></div>秩满，调授杭州馀杭簿，擢漳浦令，再以吏能佐桂州幕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1159030_comment'></div>初为节度判官，以母丧解官，后以观察支使知春州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1159030_comment'></div>入朝，迁著作佐郎、知潭州攸县，移知梅州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1159030_comment'></div>累转太子赞善大夫、殿中丞，卒官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1159030_comment'></div>其佐馀杭也，市有丐者杜氏夫妇，皆八十馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1159030_comment'></div>杜氏名暹，尝为忠懿王幕府官，老无子孙，遂乞于市。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1159030_comment'></div>公闻之恻然，为辍俸钱，构草室数楹以居之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1159030_comment'></div>语同僚暨右族，合币二十万与其足日廪，市什器，营寿藏，识者义之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1159030_comment'></div>其令漳浦也，有海口石门，居风冲道，岁坏舟楫甚众，公乃相地徙港，以避涛怒，商旅至今赖焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1159030_comment'></div>邑西有陈将军祠者，郡图云：仪凤中勋府中郎将陈元光也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1159030_comment'></div>年少强魂，邦人立庙，享祠甚谨，日奉牲币无算。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1159030_comment'></div>岁大旱，遍走群望，弗雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1159030_comment'></div>公乃斋洁诣祠下祷云：「政不修者，令之负；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1159030_comment'></div>祷无验者，神之羞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1159030_comment'></div>国家崇祀典，所以祈民福也，祀茍不应，何用神为」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1159030_comment'></div>即钥扉与神约曰：「七日不雨，此门不复开，丛祠为烬矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1159030_comment'></div>行未百步，霾风拔巨树仆于道，俗素信鬼，及是，吏民股战，神之怒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1159030_comment'></div>公徐曰：「民方嗷，何怒之为」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1159030_comment'></div>乃缓辔截树而去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1159030_comment'></div>果大雨，田收皆倍，邑人刻词以纪其异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1159030_comment'></div>其在桂林也，役徒不足，借禁卒五百伐材以修守具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1159030_comment'></div>郡帅会宾客，饮于堂外，有告变者曰：「役卒二百，挟刃群噪入屯营为逆」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1159030_comment'></div>在座相顾失色，郡帅曰：「当闭城，以虎翼五百擒之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1159030_comment'></div>公即屏人语帅曰：「今以乱擒之，彼知就擒则死，必力斗，适所以坚其叛意耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1159030_comment'></div>及其衅尚浅，君诱而致之，可无患」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1159030_comment'></div>乃从白直数人，直趋其屯，责其主校苛刻，乃复人人恩慰，问其劳苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1159030_comment'></div>叛卒环泣曰：「苦则思乱，人之常情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1159030_comment'></div>若从公命，得免于役，以全视息，为再造矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1159030_comment'></div>皆释仗随公而归，帅亦原之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1159030_comment'></div>其罢阳春也，有张氏女者，父为供奉官，夫吏辇下，犯贿流岭南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1159030_comment'></div>夫死，家属当还都，邵阳邮卒以刃胁为妇，留且半岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1159030_comment'></div>公经途闻之，执卒送官抵罪，公解骖暨万钱贻之，官遣部送，还其父子，皆章章在人视听者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1159030_comment'></div>公历七官，干局外职，司符牒劾事，凡九十馀狱，民无一辞为怨，其周才也如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1159030_comment'></div>公之宰攸县也，政无不革，乃经度署表而鼎新之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1159030_comment'></div>落成之日，而诏书至，徙梅州，心常恋恋焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1159030_comment'></div>捐馆之夕，攸之宿吏数十，见公朱衣垂鱼，据鞍导从，炜晔入门，升厅如平生，厅帘坠地如割，众惊异之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1159030_comment'></div>后半月而凶问至，邑人塑其像，立祠于邑西云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1159030_comment'></div>公以明道元年四月甲辰，终于梅州官舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1159030_comment'></div>某年某月某日，归葬于某，夫人杨氏祔焉，杨氏先公早世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1159030_comment'></div>子六人，曰直方、有方、知方、居方、义方、应方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1159030_comment'></div>居方举进士；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1159030_comment'></div>有方补郊社斋郎，为曲江簿，亦能官；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1159030_comment'></div>义方、应方尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1159030_comment'></div>女二人，长适某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1159030_comment'></div>康定元年，曲江君因方趺圆首之令，泣以遗状来请铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1159030_comment'></div>嗟其名不书于史氏，遂铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_75_1159030'>古之为吏，不专禄仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1159030_comment'></div>器能轶群，名不坠矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1159030_comment'></div>后之为吏，去才取位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1159030_comment'></div>官品不登，善斯委矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1159030_comment'></div>吁嗟陈公，识优命否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1159030_comment'></div>勒铭幽石，以颂遗美。</div><div id='poem_sentence_80_1159030_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='3dc9b9ef29c1466fb502bf5600a588d1_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("3dc9b9ef29c1466fb502bf5600a588d1");'><span id='3dc9b9ef29c1466fb502bf5600a588d1_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1041')">1040-1041年</a>，41-42岁</div><div id='3dc9b9ef29c1466fb502bf5600a588d1' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年</a>　在水南寺茶肆，品赏仁化白毛茶，誉之为“茶圃一旗春”此茶遂更负盛名。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年</a>　同榜进士王子元从江西上饶来探靖，靖偕之出游兼还愿，有诗并序。作品：游大峒山。<div id='poem_99572' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99572' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99572?labeling=true' target='_blank'>游山五题<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span>游大峒山</a><span class='authorDate'>（1040年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99572")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_99572_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99572'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99572'>十里松桧风，万仞斗峭壁。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99572_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99572'>阳崖雷自奔，阴壑雪犹积。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99572_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99572'>势争衡霍雄，地控楚越扼。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99572_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99572'>胡为千载间，名未光图籍。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99572_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_99572'>物乃因人彰，闻人于在昔。<div id='poem_sentence_4_99572_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_99572'>不逢巢许高，箕山亦<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_99572", 99572, "Clauses/11/Comments/0")'>顽碧</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_5_99572_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_99572'>我今共游览，逍遥非俗格。<div id='poem_sentence_6_99572_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_99572'>剧论穷古今，玄谈叩虚寂。<div id='poem_sentence_7_99572_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_99572'>攀萝蹑孤峰，和云坐幽石。<div id='poem_sentence_8_99572_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_99572'>濯缨清泠泉，留为不朽迹。<div id='poem_sentence_9_99572_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_99572'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_99572_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年</a>　同榜进士王子元从江西上饶来探靖，靖偕之出游兼还愿，有诗。作品：题白莲庵。宿月华上方。会宿宝林道场。<div id='poem_99573' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99573' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99573?labeling=true' target='_blank'>游山五题<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>题白莲庵<span class='inlineComment2'>（长老琳公旧隐之地）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1040年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99573")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_99573_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99573'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99573'>掩室昔宴居，冥心遗万化。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99573_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99573'>菡萏本无染，纷华共高谢。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99573_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99573'>夜禅杉月落，晨斋庭鸟下。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99573_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99573'>栋间云气浮，地面秋香诧。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99573_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_99573'>演法辞故栖，幽踪贲寒野。<div id='poem_sentence_4_99573_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_99573'>蜡屐此同游，愿结宗雷社。<div id='poem_sentence_5_99573_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_99573'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_99573_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_99468' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99468' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99468?labeling=true' target='_blank'>同李秘校谭员外宿月华上方</a><span class='authorDate'>（1040年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99468")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_99468_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99468'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99468'>上方逢夏夕，月色遍千山。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99468_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99468'>但觉星河近，偶同江海闲。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99468_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99468'>事抛兴废外，谈极有无间。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99468_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99468'>却笑明朝俗，红尘随马还。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99468_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_99468'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_99468_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_99467' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99467' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99467?labeling=true' target='_blank'>同李秘校谭员外月华长老谒慈济禅师会宿宝林道场</a><span class='authorDate'>（1040年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99467")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_99467_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99467'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99467'>祖堂留胜迹，再宿此登临。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99467_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99467'>云月自明暗，山川无古今。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99467_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99467'>谷声猿啸远，泉脉虎跑深。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99467_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99467'>共到忘言处，休论佛与心。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99467_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_99467'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_99467_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年</a>　三司副使段少连出知广州，与靖同朝为官，彼此景慕，约靖赴穗一游，靖因上饶从事来访，函告段明年成行。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年</a>　是年，应约作记。作品：月华山花界寺传法住持记。<div id='poem_1158999' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158999' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158999?labeling=true' target='_blank'>韶州月华山花界寺传法住持记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1040年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158999")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158999_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158999'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158999'>人之大伦，在乎三本：父者生之，君者治之，师者教之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158999_comment'></div>父子天性至亲而不易，君臣同体至一而不可择，惟师则不然，去就之分，视德之轻重，故无位而尊、无赏而归者，道之所在云耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158999_comment'></div>子夏之居西河，康成之处北海，传经著录，不异洙泗，岂有督之者哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158999_comment'></div>金仙之教，被于中国，自汉至梁，逾五百祀，但以崇塔庙、勤香火为事耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158999_comment'></div>及心法西来，百年之间，传至大鉴而法斯溥矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158999_comment'></div>月华山者，招提惠朗禅师演法之地也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158999_comment'></div>招提视大鉴犹曾祖父也，大鉴门人高第者，庐陵思、衡岳让。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158999_comment'></div>让传大寂，居江西，世呼马祖是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158999_comment'></div>思传希迁，居南岳之石头，建中、贞元间，方袍之学心者，江衡千里，道路如织，亦西河、北海之风也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158999_comment'></div>石头之入室者，有大小朗，招提为大朗，以其不出招提三十年，故号招提朗焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158999_comment'></div>其门人刘轲为之碑甚详云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158999_comment'></div>朗，曲江人，俗姓欧阳氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158999_comment'></div>年十三于州邓林寺出家，二十于岳寺受戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158999_comment'></div>既而曰：「戒岂律我哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158999_comment'></div>乃往龚公谒大寂，得佛无知见之说，遂归于岳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158999_comment'></div>昼探井臼之役，夜与其徒发坼幽键。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158999_comment'></div>石头即世，终丧乃去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158999_comment'></div>贞元十一年，将游罗浮，途次曲江之都渚，乃曰：「兹地清气盘郁，亦足以栖神矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158999_comment'></div>遂驻锡居之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158999_comment'></div>四方学者，寻声而至，无虚日矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1158999_comment'></div>招提既没，众散而寺亦榛废，其后百馀岁，当刘氏称汉于南海也，有实智禅僧清裔者，自范金铜罗汉像十八躯进献刘主中宗，因得延见，引问之际，器识高远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1158999_comment'></div>刘主乃于碧玉殿备浮图氏威仪，俾裔升正座说法，其主自处西向听之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1158999_comment'></div>仍俾奉罗汉像，自铨胜地，以图熏修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1158999_comment'></div>乃即招提故基置寺，以国命赐名，龛其像，至今存焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1158999_comment'></div>实以癸亥年来，至壬申为乱兵所害，其徒光政继主其院三十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1158999_comment'></div>真宗皇帝即位改元之岁，赐寺额曰花界。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1158999_comment'></div>四年，光政因众命以院让道寻，再为什方居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1158999_comment'></div>传八世，至今长老琳公，景祐元年以州命而尸之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1158999_comment'></div>自贞元十一年至是岁，凡二百四十三年，自招提至琳公，凡十二代，以其属自相传、不敢处师座者五，馀则以国命、州命、众命，凡有所宗者七世焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1158999_comment'></div>然而学徒或来或不来，所谓去就之分，视德之轻重也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1158999_comment'></div>琳生曲江都渚，邓姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1158999_comment'></div>祥符初，寺为外火所延，一瓦无完。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1158999_comment'></div>琳公时在徒弟中，与知事辈戮力营竖，既而叹曰：「识心达本，是谓沙门，何泥于有为耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1158999_comment'></div>乃优游江淮，遍参师席。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1158999_comment'></div>初，博通内外典，攻诗属文，所至推为文章僧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1158999_comment'></div>寻复悔曰：「多闻亦病耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1158999_comment'></div>遂讳作词章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1158999_comment'></div>洞山自宝禅师见之，曰：「此大乘器也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1158999_comment'></div>既印其心，又欲以院让之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1158999_comment'></div>再让皆不受，还曲江，于方山结庵而居，今所谓白莲庵也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1158999_comment'></div>漕使郑公载疏名以请之，再辞，不免，升座而学人四至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1158999_comment'></div>完旧创新，无物不具，植茶树果，给众皆馀，此又馀力于有为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1158999_comment'></div>因书其始末云，年月日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_42_1158999_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年</a>　是年，应约作铭。作品：南华寺慈济大师寿塔记。<div id='poem_1159045' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159045' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159045?labeling=true' target='_blank'>韶州南华寺慈济大师寿塔铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1040年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1159045")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159045_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159045'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159045'>天下伽蓝，以夏腊继承，自相统率者，盖万数焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159045_comment'></div>由郡县之令，选于州乡，以领其徒者，且千数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159045_comment'></div>其名山福地，奉朝廷之命，择于丛林，以阐其教者，无数十焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159045_comment'></div>菩提达磨心法东传，以衣为證，止于大鉴，故曹溪之比，又加少焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159045_comment'></div>今皇帝嗣统之初地，奉母仪内助之慈，尊释氏西来之教，诏于衡庐择人绍隆祖席，佥曰：「当今雄辩通识，无逾云盖禅师者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159045_comment'></div>湖南按察使即以名闻，诏赐命服师号以宠之，俾择名僧自佐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159045_comment'></div>禅师名宝缘，兴元人，游方至随州，参智门禅师祚，投针契理，得意忘言，以心印心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159045_comment'></div>不烦机接，遂为之嗣，即云门之嫡也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159045_comment'></div>寻领众居唐兴、南台、云盖，皆南岳之名蓝也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159045_comment'></div>黜空破有，不涉名相，临锋迅发，直示宗乘，诸方称伏，谓之禅窟，故诏旨求人，无敢先者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159045_comment'></div>驻锡兹山，殆将逾纪，一音演说，四方流布，众中得法而去者，多为人师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159045_comment'></div>其机缘语句，门人各著序录，此不复记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159045_comment'></div>教门崇建，规制鼎新，可谓祖堂中兴矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159045_comment'></div>既而叹曰：「嘻，止矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159045_comment'></div>佛言世间出世间法备矣，山河大地，有时而尽，况于人乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159045_comment'></div>虽性空无著，体质当有所归，愚夫以死为讳，小乘以涅槃为乐，皆非中道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159045_comment'></div>吾其自营寿藏，以安时处顺，可乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159045_comment'></div>旁凿竁道，上为窣堵，在寺之西南二里而遥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159045_comment'></div>因僧惠实砻石，乞铭以志之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159045_comment'></div>其铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_1159045'>拘士烦思，以身为累。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159045_comment'></div>达人静观，如幻之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159045_comment'></div>花叶盛衰，根性不隳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159045_comment'></div>见闻觉知，岂藏于斯？</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1159045_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年</a>　是年，应约作记。作品：韶州善化院记。<div id='poem_1158997' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158997' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158997?labeling=true' target='_blank'>韶州善化院记</a><span class='authorDate'>（康定元年九月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158997")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158997_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158997'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158997'>仲尼居鲁，而儒学之风隆于洙泗；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158997_comment'></div>秦皇好兵，而将帅之材出于山西；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158997_comment'></div>六祖开化曹溪，而塔庙之兴布于曲江。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158997_comment'></div>盖圣贤特出，熏而炙之，故跂高慕远者与习俱盛也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158997_comment'></div>韶州生齿登黄籍也三万一千户，削发隶祠曹者三千七百名，建刹为精舍者四百馀区，岂非祖风宏扇，人心偃顺而钦崇者夥乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158997_comment'></div>乡曰丰乐，里曰长容，北出州治三十里而遥，有院曰善化，唐朝旧额也，五代兵火之后，其名仅存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158997_comment'></div>雍熙二年，始有草茅之室，檀越列名请袁州僧皓隆主其熏修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158997_comment'></div>迄至道中，隆师示寂，上足绍缘尸承厥位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158997_comment'></div>缘师袁姓，亦分宜人，弱岁随隆来，及其卒而嗣焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158997_comment'></div>初，院在山椒，垣壝隘陋，自景德初年，缘师乃经始宽平，而徙其基，揭旧名而署之，募资购材，斧斤不绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158997_comment'></div>至天禧之末而考室，凡十八年间，乃得环合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158997_comment'></div>立鸱而名殿，以安其像；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158997_comment'></div>度筵而筑堂，以崇其法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158997_comment'></div>重楼而击钟，以庶乎息苦；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158997_comment'></div>连床而会食，以示其容众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158997_comment'></div>至于庋阁之司，舂炊之所，折衷丰约，罔不具焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158997_comment'></div>清溪如带，缭绕前左，长梁下亘，虚亭上覆，徙倚轩槛，可以优游，真尘外之嘉致也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158997_comment'></div>又尝于雍熙、至道间，悉委瓶盂羡馀，市东皋之田，以具饘粥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158997_comment'></div>于戏！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158997_comment'></div>能创其基者，父之事也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1158997_comment'></div>能继其志者，子之力也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1158997_comment'></div>文王无忧于其国，以王季为之父也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1158997_comment'></div>臧孙有后于其家，以哀伯为之子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1158997_comment'></div>浮屠氏托大义于父子，而本非骨肉之爱，乃能恢崇堂构，以昭前人之光；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1158997_comment'></div>又能捐其蓄积，市易田产，以贻后世之利，此其可书以垂劝也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1158997_comment'></div>彼滔滔然趋走权贵之门，窥伺常住，以图割削，用实私橐者，视师之绩，得无愧乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1158997_comment'></div>以某尝帖职于修书之殿，伻词其实，以示亡穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1158997_comment'></div>既嘉之，因不复让。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1158997_comment'></div>康定元年九月日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1158997_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年</a>　次子仲荀中举。弟希端之子仲菲出世，次女适孙郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年3月</a>　转官。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='80e5a56172f34a8ba847d19415d0dd62_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("80e5a56172f34a8ba847d19415d0dd62");'><span id='80e5a56172f34a8ba847d19415d0dd62_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1042')">1041-1042年</a>，42-43岁</div><div id='80e5a56172f34a8ba847d19415d0dd62' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年10月</a>　应学正谭伯顾之请，为作记。作品：惠州海丰县新修文宣王庙记。<div id='poem_1158976' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158976' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158976?labeling=true' target='_blank'>惠州海丰县新修文宣王庙记</a><span class='authorDate'>（康定二年六月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158976")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158976_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158976'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158976'>夫教化之本，自学校始；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158976_comment'></div>学校之兴，自乡遂始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158976_comment'></div>周人有乡先生、遂大夫分掌其令，以谨其习，而荐其贤能焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158976_comment'></div>乡校所建，则有皮弁之荐、《小雅》之歌，以享先圣先师，古之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158976_comment'></div>自秦人蚕食六国，废周之令，《诗》、《书》之教，轻于虮虱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158976_comment'></div>汉兴杂霸，学者惟集于长安，郡县之学寖微矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158976_comment'></div>唐室虽欲尊儒，而不得其本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158976_comment'></div>春秋祭菜，专为孔子祠宫，已事而逡，郁生荆棘，因循其弊，以至于今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158976_comment'></div>矧今之县令，惟以断笞杖、督赋租为称职耳，其能劝学以警俗者几何哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158976_comment'></div>吾友谭君，初命为海丰，民守农亩，吏守曹事，阖境恬然，夜亡犬声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158976_comment'></div>下车期年，政既成矣，乃曰：「习俎豆，所以敦风俗；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158976_comment'></div>兴学校，所以励善良；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158976_comment'></div>严祀事，所以教肃祗；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158976_comment'></div>考前计，所以辨制度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158976_comment'></div>古之建学，必居公宫南之左，明堂亦学也，在国之阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158976_comment'></div>县虽小，亦国也，子男之制，其可忽哉」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158976_comment'></div>旧有庙学处之西偏，编竹覆葵以为其宫，隙雨霾风以昏其像。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158976_comment'></div>岁二月上丁，率诸生祗其常事，跼蹐庭下，退与诸生谋建新庙而崇学馆，诸生闻之，愿倾私楮以赞其成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158976_comment'></div>遂状其事，得请于州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158976_comment'></div>徙祠舍于邑之东南隅，伐山歛材，易葵以瓦，冕服玉璪，仪容大备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1158976_comment'></div>颜子西向以为先师，十哲坐塑以为从祀，丹朱其器以荐乎牢醴，垩白其堂以业乎讲诵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1158976_comment'></div>工既毕，遣书请词以识之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1158976_comment'></div>夫素王之道，犹天地之大、日月之明、江海之浸、阴阳之变，日用于百姓而不知其仁，泽及于万世而不为其私，口颂目訾，不加损益，所以尊而奉之者，教之所存焉耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1158976_comment'></div>今海壖远国，王化广被，夫子之道，同其污隆，兴葺黉舍，希风邹鲁，此亦政之所存焉耳，乃书之以示于后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1158976_comment'></div>康定二年六月日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1158976_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年11月</a>　有诗。作品：送海琳游南海。<div id='poem_99503' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99503' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99503?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送海琳游南海</a><span class='authorDate'>（1041年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99503")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_99503_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99503'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99503'>触目尽尘累，如师真不群。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99503_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99503'>圆明水中月，去住岭头云。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99503_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99503'>意为乘风快，名应过海闻。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99503_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99503'>翛然此高迹，世网慢纷纷。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99503_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_99503'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_99503_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年12月</a>　应邀作记。作品：韶州曹溪宝林山南华禅寺重修法堂记。<div id='poem_1158994' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158994' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158994?labeling=true' target='_blank'>韶州曹溪宝林山南华禅寺重修法堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（康定二年十二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158994")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158994_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158994'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158994'>孟子曰：「圣人者，百世之师也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158994_comment'></div>盖至圣之道，高深广博，百世而下，遗烈犹存，贤者袭其规模，学者窥其户牖，此其所以日钻岁仰，归之无穷者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158994_comment'></div>然而道之大者，必久而后隆；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158994_comment'></div>事之美者，不一而能具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158994_comment'></div>昔者六祖大鉴禅师初传信器，归隐海峤，混迹弋猎，艰难备尝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158994_comment'></div>及其建梵宫，登师座，敷陈真觉，开导人天，其亦勤矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158994_comment'></div>灭度以来，四百馀载，虽千灯继照，光遍河沙，而布金遗址，筌蹄寂寞，向非睿哲当天，英材接迹，讲求世务，馀力佛乘，曷能恢复宗风以续先轨者哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158994_comment'></div>天禧四年，前转运使、起居舍人陈绛上言：「曹溪演法之地，四方瞻仰，岁入至丰，僧徒至众，主者不能均济，率多侵牟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158994_comment'></div>乞于名山佥选宿德，俾其举扬宗旨，招来学徒」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158994_comment'></div>制诏曰可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158994_comment'></div>于是南阳赐紫僧普遂首膺是命，庄献皇太后、今皇帝亲遣中贵人诣山，迎致信衣，禁闱瞻礼，遂师得于便座召对移刻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158994_comment'></div>陛辞之日，赐号智度禅师，锡以藏经、供器、金帛等，当时恩顾，莫与为比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158994_comment'></div>归作衣楼藏殿，以示光宠，馀亦未遑开缉也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158994_comment'></div>遂师即示，中旨付荆湖南路博访高僧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158994_comment'></div>今长老缘师自南岳云台山再当是选，绍光正念，宣扬了义，居者蒙润，来者如归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158994_comment'></div>乃击钟而谋曰：「嗣其业者为之子也，诲于人者为之师也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158994_comment'></div>子之克劭，然后起家；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158994_comment'></div>师之不严，何以尊道？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158994_comment'></div>此世教之所以壮堂构也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158994_comment'></div>日明月暗，墙壅户通，因分别以见尘缘，视顽虚而识空性，此梵刹之所以崇堂宇也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1158994_comment'></div>由是蓄羡馀，广购募，穷山跨谷，以求栋干，殚能极艺，以召匠硕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1158994_comment'></div>协定星之期，观大壮之象，材得以呈其美，工得以肆其巧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1158994_comment'></div>计广以席，度深以筵，外像祗陀之居，中施师子之座。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1158994_comment'></div>寻声至者，圜立于前；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1158994_comment'></div>如渴饮河，满腹而去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1158994_comment'></div>嗟乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1158994_comment'></div>圣不世出，故微言易绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1158994_comment'></div>昔仲尼生于邹鲁，去世未久，而杨、墨、申、韩，各就其术，为异同之论，以戕贼教化，所赖荀、孟大儒，开陈仁义，然后君臣上下，大伦以笃，夫子之道，不绝如线，况其远者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1158994_comment'></div>如来生于西域万里之外，寂灭千岁，教乃东被。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1158994_comment'></div>而语皆重译，书不同文，故翻经著论，得以纷纶其说，昏遇迷妄，贪著福报，沦家耗国，弃实趋权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1158994_comment'></div>亦赖诸祖以实际理地密相付嘱，然后知佛不外求，见于自性，造恶修善，俱同妄作，所以遣空破有，不陷邪观者，宗乘维持之力也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1158994_comment'></div>不然者，天下嗷嗷奔走，有为之果，何能已乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1158994_comment'></div>初，大鉴以诸佛大法眼藏传清源思，思传石头迁，如是展转相传，至今长老缘师，为十世矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1158994_comment'></div>佛教之来中国也，达摩最后，诸祖出世，各分宗派，而曹溪之胄最众，乃知道在乎要，不在乎先后矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1158994_comment'></div>缘师，兴元南郑人，本府出家受具，得大乘之要于汉东祚师，遂振锡至于南岳，郡将邦伯，悉饮其名，乃于唐兴、南台、云盖三启禅师，称为岳中之冠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1158994_comment'></div>及被朝旨，乃克归绍本统而肯其基构，六祖之道由是中兴矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1158994_comment'></div>前所谓必久而隆、不壹而具者，有待而然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1158994_comment'></div>缘师状其事，请辞錾石，以图不朽，且予里闬所托，故于辞为备云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1158994_comment'></div>康定二年十二月日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_38_1158994_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年</a>　其父余庆因妻丧获准归休。仲荀以任泷水县尉路远不能照料家庭，请改近官，为韶州长史。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年</a>　孙禹臣、嗣昌出世。伯庄调任惠阳县主簿。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='a6c92b6295144bb3899745aa0dad4ec4_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a6c92b6295144bb3899745aa0dad4ec4");'><span id='a6c92b6295144bb3899745aa0dad4ec4_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年</a>，43岁</div><div id='a6c92b6295144bb3899745aa0dad4ec4' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年3月</a>　靖居丧期满，调京复任集贤校理，孙复为国子监直讲，富弼为知制诰，晏殊为同平章事。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='34a489be74ee4831aa11ff97407ad85f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("34a489be74ee4831aa11ff97407ad85f");'><span id='34a489be74ee4831aa11ff97407ad85f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1049')">1046-1049年</a>，47-50岁</div><div id='34a489be74ee4831aa11ff97407ad85f' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年8月</a>　到曲江后，接敕诰，授光禄少卿依旧分司南京，韶州居信，有谢表。作品：谢转光禄少卿。<div id='poem_1158757' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158757' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158757?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢转光禄少卿表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1046年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158757")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158757_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158757'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158757'>臣某言：今月八日，进奏院递到敕诰，蒙恩授臣光禄少卿，依旧分司南京、韶州居住者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158757_comment'></div>居深坎窞，恩出天慈，俯念戴盆之函，莫遂循墙之让<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158757_comment'></div>伏念臣禀受愚暗，生长遐荒，爰自弱龄，幸亲儒术，未脱饭牛之贱，敢思糜爵之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158757_comment'></div>盖遇国家海宇澄清，仕途宽裕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158757_comment'></div>高则贤科射策，采卿相之材；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158757_comment'></div>次则卿品荐能，分甲乙之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158757_comment'></div>小吏计年而进考，商人校粟以论资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158757_comment'></div>戎旃奋起于卒徒，勋门泽及于僮隶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158757_comment'></div>广为甄录，庸赞治平，所谓得人而昌，何云数路而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158757_comment'></div>由是例趋贡籍，偶中文程，逮于壮年，再膺诏目，遂陪邦彦，久服朝绅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158757_comment'></div>亦尝预刊前史之阙文，参修当世之大典，载笔而书言动，抱蕝而正礼仪，补衮职蹈无讳之讥，冒兵锋而使不测之虏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158757_comment'></div>叙其微效，擢在近班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158757_comment'></div>言思报国之忠，身罹负俗之谤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158757_comment'></div>箦中之辱，昔贤亦有非辜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158757_comment'></div>日边之遥，丹诚无以上诉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158757_comment'></div>退分冗秩，还侍亲庭，雁鹜久费于稻粱，禽鱼幸返于林薮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158757_comment'></div>采兰洁膳，聊同孺子之欢；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158757_comment'></div>种树灌园，诚为拙者之效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158757_comment'></div>永言毁废，当绝照临，岂意恩波，下沾穷辙？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158757_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下，纯仁广覆，至洽旁罗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1158757_comment'></div>一物未泰而比之纳隍，群贤虽积而勤于顿网。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1158757_comment'></div>顺民心而敷治，因天瑞以建元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1158757_comment'></div>溥念臣工，众罹罪罟，重为缘坐，轻或诋诬，凡曰瑕疵，率加湔洗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1158757_comment'></div>乐羊居外，靡开盈箧之书；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1158757_comment'></div>陈平有谋，不问受金之过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1158757_comment'></div>如臣远迹，素乏异才，进本孤根，退因积毁，所嗟圣世，遂作锢人，徒成画饼之名，莫展铅刀之用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1158757_comment'></div>忽蒙零露之均泽，忍使当春而独枯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1158757_comment'></div>茍非造化之恩，宁及沉冥之地？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1158757_comment'></div>唯知死报，无路捐驱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1158757_comment'></div>但臣无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1158757_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年10月16日</a>　又接中书劄子，云奉圣旨令三司接续支与靖光禄少卿俸，有谢表。作品：谢续支请受表。<div id='poem_1158783' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158783' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158783?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢续支请受表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1046年10月16日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158783")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158783_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158783'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158783'>臣某言：今月十六日，准中书劄子，奉圣旨依前守光禄少卿、分司南京，许于韶州居住，令三司接续支与请受者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158783_comment'></div>有命自天，再沾于幽隐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158783_comment'></div>无功受禄，但益于战兢<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158783_comment'></div>伏念臣素乏器能，生在遐陬，幸逢圣代，登历仕阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158783_comment'></div>夫何闇浅之材，常居文雅之选，屡蒙驱策，罔避险夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158783_comment'></div>顷因专对之勤，擢在迩臣之列，深虞福过，寻已谤生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158783_comment'></div>仇人之诉得行，逐客之书难上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158783_comment'></div>退归田里，坐易岁时，甘海峤以陆沉，沐天慈之再造，起于谪籍，付以伍符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158783_comment'></div>上荷君恩，固无宜于坚让；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158783_comment'></div>适当父病，难舍之而远行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158783_comment'></div>重沥血诚，果从私便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158783_comment'></div>吏议俾停于月廪，家居尤畏于简书，本冀承颜之欢，几成糊口之患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158783_comment'></div>遽蒙宸眷，荐锡纶言，虽容彭泽之归，仍续郑均之禄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158783_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下尧心广爱，乾体无私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158783_comment'></div>明比日升，极大荒而普照；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158783_comment'></div>恩同春燠，虑一物之偏枯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158783_comment'></div>虽居江海之遥，时沾雨露之泽，当图死报，难以言宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158783_comment'></div>臣无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1158783_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年</a>　有感于王子元患难之交，有诗。作品：和王子元过大庾岭。和王子元同归曲江有感。和王子元重阳日千善寺会饮。<div id='poem_99557' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99557' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99557?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和王子元过大庾岭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1046年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99557")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_99557_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99557'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99557'>秦皇戍五岭，兹为楚越隘。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99557_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99557'>尉佗去黄屋，舟车通海外。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99557_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99557'>峭巘倚云汉，推轮日倾害。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99557_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99557'>贤哉张令君，镌凿济行迈。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99557_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_99557'>地失千仞险，途开九野泰。<div id='poem_sentence_4_99557_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_99557'>安得时人心，尽夷阴险阂。<div id='poem_sentence_5_99557_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_99557'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_99557_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_99477' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99477' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99477?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和王子元同归曲江有感</a><span class='authorDate'>（1046年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99477")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_99477_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99477'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99477'>年少登科今白头，不才多病分归休。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99477_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99477'>深恩未报云天施，弱质易惊蒲柳秋。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99477_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99477'>进退无机常蹭蹬，穷通知命自夷犹。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99477_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99477'>相逢莫问市朝事，绿水青山是胜游。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99477_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_99477'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_99477_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_99478' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99478' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99478?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和王子元重阳日千善寺会饮</a><span class='authorDate'>（1046年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99478")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_99478_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99478'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99478'>人生聚散苦难期，且喜清游酒满卮。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99478_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99478'>秋径却逢黄菊日，春风休惜落花时。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99478_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99478'>仙翁有谶应须避，楚客多悲亦强为。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99478_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99478'>好景莫教容易过，醉吟何必绕疏篱。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99478_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_99478'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_99478_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年</a>　冬，应知康州李定函请，作记。作品：康州重修文宣王庙记。<div id='poem_1158974' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158974' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158974?labeling=true' target='_blank'>康州重修文宣王庙记<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历五年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1046年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158974")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158974_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158974'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158974'>古者立学必行释奠之礼，天子、诸侯皆亲临之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158974_comment'></div>周人祀周公，鲁人祀孔子为先圣，自汉已来，遂采用鲁礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158974_comment'></div>盖三王之道备于周，尧、舜、文、武之道备于孔子，故后世无以易之而加崇焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158974_comment'></div>孔子之教，与天子正朔相左右，以被四海，虽庠序废兴靡常，而庙食不绝者，教之存焉耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158974_comment'></div>康州在峤南千里，北人踰峤而至者，率以南方暑湿，忧畏疾疟陨穫于内，尅日月以计归，宜乎政之或未暇缉也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158974_comment'></div>殿省丞李君仲求被命到郡，自以壮年蒙国委用，得守土宇，不复计远迩若向之为者，凡可以济当时利后人者，罔不营度焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158974_comment'></div>先是，郡无黉舍，才建庙室以应令奉祠耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158974_comment'></div>庙在子城西偏，广不占亩，栋干庳陋，不称明德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158974_comment'></div>且郡枕郁江下流，其源数千里，其派十数，以合而东，每春夏积雨流潦，潴汇浸淫，毁民庐舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158974_comment'></div>率走高以避江怒，携细拥弱坌入庙下，渎慢神宇，非严师尊教之意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158974_comment'></div>乃相爽垲，去郡东五里而近，得紫极宫之故基而鼎新之，殿堂门序凡五十楹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158974_comment'></div>先圣、先师及世所谓十哲者，皆扶土为像于殿以致恭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158974_comment'></div>七十子而下，又设色肖形于庑以存制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158974_comment'></div>仍齿博士弟子之位于堂以肄经，凡庙学之式参备焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158974_comment'></div>既卒工，抨图来京师以谒记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158974_comment'></div>属予有出疆之役，而不克书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158974_comment'></div>其明年，得罪为郡，又明年，乃阅旧讯而志之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158974_comment'></div>庙之成，以庆历癸未岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158974_comment'></div>董其役者，端溪尉王该，进士乐其成而来居者百馀人云。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_1158974'></div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1158974_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年</a>　孙嗣恭、仲荀第四子出世。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1047&endYear=1047')">1047年</a>　二弟、三弟经商，见兄长两袖清风归来，家庭人口多，于是在南门城外滨武江处建西园别墅，让靖一家居住。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1047&endYear=1047')">1047年3月</a>　应知乐昌黄自元之请，与唐翼、谭允等游仙人石室，作记刻于室壁。作品：同游泐溪石记。<div id='poem_1158964' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158964' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158964?labeling=true' target='_blank'>同游泐溪石室记</a><span class='authorDate'>（皇祐二年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158964")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158964_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158964'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158964'>人之跂高慕远，乐在林壑者，厥游不得其胜，则无所记焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158964_comment'></div>地之蕴灵蓄秀于方域者，所赏不遇其人，则无所发焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158964_comment'></div>游赏之会，其难乎哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158964_comment'></div>予以分司归韶之明年，江夏黄君子京始宰乐昌，其明年以书见遗曰：「弊邑虽小，地多胜概，泐溪石室，宜为称首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158964_comment'></div>元和中，番禺从事李文孺尝志其游，惜其景出涵晖之右，而文不逮于到难，故使兹山不甚显闻于世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158964_comment'></div>若迂高车以辱临之，愿去道茀蜡履以从」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158964_comment'></div>又明年，乃往游焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158964_comment'></div>其始去县郛，西北平行五里而近，西为大山，其厚无极，东亘高阜，积石所成，澄溪下流，人迹中断。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158964_comment'></div>揭溪即阜，属当大窾，外若敞扉，中如华屋，平有度筵之广，高逾结栋之隆，穹中四注，屏舒玉削。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158964_comment'></div>幽崖婉入，如曲房小槛之容；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158964_comment'></div>斜窦旁通，有连甍接庑之势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158964_comment'></div>云蒸雾积，闭阴辟阳，冬漏暖脉，夏含凄气，天地炎凉，所不能制，固仙游之所宅，岩栖之嘉致也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158964_comment'></div>既而遍览幽趣，庶逢前轨，洗尘而视，则有陆羽题名墨迹在焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158964_comment'></div>张炬而入，则有六祖偃息石床存焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158964_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158964_comment'></div>茍非子京奏刀恢恢之暇，以奇胜见招，何由崎岖百里，一届其域？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158964_comment'></div>及窥陈迹，则古之贤哲，寝处为常，乃知世称今人不如古，宜哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158964_comment'></div>子京时又招摄尉唐某、进士谭某同游，既书名于壁，复镵石以志之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158964_comment'></div>今天子亲享明堂之岁三月二十五日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1158964_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1047&endYear=1047')">1047年</a>　应海琳禅师之请，撰铭。作品：韶州月华禅师寿塔铭。<div id='poem_1159043' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159043' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159043?labeling=true' target='_blank'>韶州月华禅师寿塔铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1047年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1159043")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159043_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159043'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159043'>月华山西堂琳禅师，曲江都渚人，姓邓氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159043_comment'></div>少学儒，能谈王霸大略，已而学佛，以诵经披剃，乃游方，犹以诗名往来江淮间，博览广记，推为文章僧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159043_comment'></div>参洞山自宝禅师，宝于江南为禅宗，丛林无出其右者，见师，以大心器之，遂以心印付焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159043_comment'></div>息机南还，结庵于旧山之北，曰白莲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159043_comment'></div>学者闻其名，自远至者无算。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159043_comment'></div>州以众状请出世，师遁于大洞累月，众叩不已，黾勉从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159043_comment'></div>师既乡邦之望，远迩信向，廪有馀粮，人有馀力，栋宇时构，树艺日广，江山清旷，甲于州域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159043_comment'></div>由是搢绅缁素，途经江浒，无不舣舟造室，耳高论，目嘉致，人人自得而还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159043_comment'></div>四方衲子奔走于路，达心要去为人师者数十人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159043_comment'></div>晚年避喧，退居西堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159043_comment'></div>众思其道，郡以疏请复恢禅旨者三焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159043_comment'></div>宝林山者，六祖古道场也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159043_comment'></div>诏择名德，锡殊名命服以居之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159043_comment'></div>漕台以师为举，坚辞不行，乃即庵自甓寿藏曰：「吾当归骨于此」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159043_comment'></div>既而曰：「生平交游之厚者，安道、子元而已」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159043_comment'></div>遂以书来云，愿以铭志诿吾执。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159043_comment'></div>仆以从官鞅掌，学殖荒落，尝评古人之言曰：「志意修则骄富贵，道义重则轻王公」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159043_comment'></div>谓道义内充，志意不屈于王公之尊，富贵之势不能动其心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159043_comment'></div>此理诚高，犹是介者之谈耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159043_comment'></div>学于大雄氏者，道以性通，志非外徇，止观无著，空有俱忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159043_comment'></div>生死不能汩其真，况富贵乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159043_comment'></div>鬼神不能窥其迹，况王公乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159043_comment'></div>师之行高乎哉，不可跂已！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159043_comment'></div>乃为铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_1159043'>湛然性相本无为，涉于形器有时隳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159043_comment'></div>他年幻质此于归，尝言无佛，良遣有知。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1159043_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1047&endYear=1047')">1047年</a>　殿中丞、知韶州潘凤自去冬到任，因景慕余靖人品文采，时时来往，春秋间约其郊游，作记。作品：湧泉亭记。<div id='poem_1158966' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158966' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158966?labeling=true' target='_blank'>涌泉亭记<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历七年五月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1047年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158966")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158966_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158966'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158966'>峤南溪山之胜，曲江称最，然其绝境，多在远郊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158966_comment'></div>徙州治以跨二江，百馀载矣，亭榭池馆，面高临深，前创后续，不逾雉堞，耳目所诣，不为难能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158966_comment'></div>尚书外郎杜君挺之之为守也，狱无冤私，赋役以时，事举条领，民用休息，近郛胜概，亡不周览。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158966_comment'></div>梁济真水，越一长亭，得涌泉焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158966_comment'></div>始其出喧嚣，入杳霭，层峦曲涧，岚碧相照，涧极崖平，泉源在焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158966_comment'></div>横岗屈盘，隐若伏兽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158966_comment'></div>疏洼为沼，泉出石罅，大若涛涌，细如鼎沸，久旱不竭，经冬常满。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158966_comment'></div>南方瘅暑，酷如惔焚，暂息泉上，寒悚毛骨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158966_comment'></div>挺之乘间一来，吟酌永日，自非嘉宾，无预兹赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158966_comment'></div>傍有精庐，因泉得名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158966_comment'></div>于是知事僧谋于众曰：「古之君子必观于水，盖有道焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158966_comment'></div>习氏之名，千载若存，盖有遇焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158966_comment'></div>今太守适意水石，而露坐泉傍，虽旷淡自适，岂吾人之所安也」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158966_comment'></div>乃募金伐材，搆亭泉心，贯之飞梁，虹横波际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158966_comment'></div>翼以堂室，备宾游之憩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158966_comment'></div>外营碓硙，为民事之观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158966_comment'></div>挺之暇则造焉，以涤烦虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158966_comment'></div>既罢郡归阙，且半岁，某与后太守潘伯恭、南康倅李仲求共陟泉亭，一饭一啜，不同于俗<span class='inlineComment2'>（皆当时之事。）</span>，乃书名屋壁以志其游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158966_comment'></div>后一月，又书亭之始以寓，仲求请模石而书之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158966_comment'></div>因叹曰：韶处岭阨，杂产五金，四方之民，聚而游手，牒诉纷拿，称倍他郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1158966_comment'></div>挺之以诚应物，庭无留事，日自适于山水间，乃知为政自有体也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1158966_comment'></div>斯游斯景，书之其无愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1158966_comment'></div>挺之名且，伯恭名夙，仲求名定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1158966_comment'></div>庆历七年五月日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1158966_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1047&endYear=1047')">1047年</a>　与潘凤郊游，作记。作品：韶亭记。<div id='poem_1158965' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158965' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158965?labeling=true' target='_blank'>韶亭记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1047年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158965")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158965_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158965'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158965'>贤人君子乐夫佳山秀水者，盖将寓闲旷之目，托高远之思，涤荡烦绁，开纳和粹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158965_comment'></div>故远则攀萝拂云以跻乎杳冥，近则筑土饬材以寄乎观望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158965_comment'></div>惟韶山去州治八十里，自元精胚胎，阳结阴流，不知炉锤者谁，独秀兹境？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158965_comment'></div>在昔虞舜南狩苍梧，《九韶》之乐奏于石上，山之得名，起于是矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158965_comment'></div>国家丕冒海隅，择材绥远，殿省丞潘君伯恭特膺诏选，来守岭阨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158965_comment'></div>锄强构弱，有意于古，下车期年，人用休息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158965_comment'></div>乃曰：「山为州镇，厥名尤著。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158965_comment'></div>自秦开五岭，迄今千载，凭轼之使，泛舟之宾，大麓之下，往还如织，不知观瞩之地，以为山荣，岂守土者详近而略远哉」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158965_comment'></div>遂按郡谍而相之，背山东渡五里而近，得地曰灵溪，即道左建亭，而山之奇秀，森然在目矣，伻来以图，授之矩画。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158965_comment'></div>先是，赐紫僧法崇者，推诚导募，众所钦信，尝于康衢构榭以壮州邦，既勤基缔，将贲髹雘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158965_comment'></div>太守曰：「吾以敦朴化人，无事于侈，可去华就实，移其用于兹亭」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158965_comment'></div>崇曰：「明使君之言，非唯集事，兼存为政之体」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158965_comment'></div>繇是舍饰画之浮费，市楩梓之美材，持畚筑、运斧斤者，子来而乐成矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158965_comment'></div>越再胐魄而亭就，则兹山具美，纤芥无隐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158965_comment'></div>屹者如阙，阛者如庾，平者如台，呀者如谷，向者如斗，背者如逃，人立鸟跂，霞明雾暗，碧玉千仞，青螺万叠，殊形诡制，纷不可名，驱鬼投物，巧不能备，信尘外之绝区也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158965_comment'></div>既而请名，太守曰「亭以山搆，而能尽山之美，其名韶」云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158965_comment'></div>岁月日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1158965_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1047&endYear=1047')">1047年5月</a>　江秀才从吉州来探视，与同游南华寺，临别为诗赠之。作品：游宝林精舍。<div id='poem_99469' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99469' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99469?labeling=true' target='_blank'>同黄宰游宝林精舍书祐长老壁</a><span "poem_title_99469")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_99469_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99469'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99469'>浮生万虑日营营，同访禅居耳目醒。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99469_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99469'>寻胜已穷烟霭外，谈空应有鬼神听。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99570'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_99570_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1047&endYear=1047')">1047年</a>　秋，广南东路转运使祖无择来探好友，靖有诗。作品：谢祖太博见访西园。<div id='poem_99531' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99531' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1047&endYear=1047')">1047年</a>　与祖无择聚，靖有诗。作品：答祖太博借山居要术。<div id='poem_99451' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99451' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a
