id='poem_sentence_2_99451_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1047&endYear=1047')">1047年9月9日</a>　时值重阳，知州潘凤、曲江知县邀祖无择、余靖同游韶石山，祖无择有《游韶石》，靖亦作诗赞美韶石。<div id='poem_99576' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99576' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99576?labeling=true' target='_blank'>游韶石</a><span class='authorDate'>（1047年9月9日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99576")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_99576_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99576'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99576'>世务常喧嚣，物外有真赏。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99576'>结友探胜槩，放情谐素想。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99576'>韶山南国镇，灵踪传自曩。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99576'>双阙倚天秀，一径寻云上。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_99576'>长江远萦带，众峦疑<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_99576", 99576, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>负襁</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_4_99576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_99576'>千里眇平视，万形罗怪象。<div id='poem_sentence_5_99576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_99576'>日影避昆崙，鳌头冠方丈。<div id='poem_sentence_6_99576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_99576'>青螺佛髻高，群玉仙都敞。<div id='poem_sentence_7_99576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_99576'>霞城晴煜爚，桃溪春浩荡。<div id='poem_sentence_8_99576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_99576'>仰攀霄汉近，俯瞰神魂恍。<div id='poem_sentence_9_99576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_99576'>涧深溜如织，岩虚动成响。<div id='poem_sentence_10_99576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_99576'>造化与真质，妙画胡能仿。<div id='poem_sentence_11_99576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_99576'>贱子生海隅，逢辰辱朝奖。<div id='poem_sentence_12_99576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_99576'>靡成彝鼎勋，甘从丘壑往。<div id='poem_sentence_13_99576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_99576'>惊禽恋故林，困骥畏羁鞅。<div id='poem_sentence_14_99576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_99576'>兹游得幽深，同怀乐清旷。<div id='poem_sentence_15_99576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_99576'>世言帝有虞，朔南声教广。<div id='poem_sentence_16_99576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_99576'>丹冥卜巡幸，翠华临苍莽。<div id='poem_sentence_17_99576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_99576'>箫韶曾此奏，钟石无遗像。<div id='poem_sentence_18_99576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_99576'>但觉薰风存，翛然天籁爽。<div id='poem_sentence_19_99576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_99576'>姬公著治典，历代所遵仗。<div id='poem_sentence_20_99576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_99576'>九野奠山川，万灵通肸蚃。<div id='poem_sentence_21_99576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_99576'>医闾与吴岳，半列戎夷壤。<div id='poem_sentence_22_99576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_99576'>四时迎气祠，犹烦礼官掌。<div id='poem_sentence_23_99576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_99576'>况乃祝融区，群物资含养。<div id='poem_sentence_24_99576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_99576'>来仪威凤居，乐育菁莪长。<div id='poem_sentence_25_99576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_99576'>肤寸起成霖，崇高一方仰。<div id='poem_sentence_26_99576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_99576'>跻之佐衡霍，无惭公侯享。<div id='poem_sentence_27_99576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_99576'></div><div id='poem_sentence_28_99576_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1047&endYear=1047')">1047年10月22日</a>　接敕诰授靖以左神武大将军、雅州刺史，靖辞不就。作品：让南班第一状。<div id='poem_1158758' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158758' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158758?labeling=true' target='_blank'>让南班第一状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1047年10月22日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158758")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158758_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158758'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158758'>臣今月二十二日，准韶州送到敕诰，蒙恩授臣左神武大将军、雅州刺史者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158758_comment'></div>窃以国家弃瑕用人，含垢御物，毁废之迹，再赐甄收。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158758_comment'></div>仰荷天恩，罔知纪极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158758_comment'></div>伏念臣往年知吉州日，以父年老，乐在乡土，曾乞解官侍养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158758_comment'></div>适会朝廷恩命，授臣分司，外议虽若弃捐，于臣实为私便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158758_comment'></div>官无曹事，月有俸钱，内奉旨甘，聊亦温足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158758_comment'></div>近者就家增秩，已出非望，今兹再宣成命，复缀通班，待遇至优，岂宜辞让？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158758_comment'></div>臣又闻之前典，事亲之礼，八十者一子不从政，九十者其家不从政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158758_comment'></div>盖谓高年之家，亲属虽众，当留子男，常在左右也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158758_comment'></div>切缘臣父年近八十，臣独一弟翊，已授惠州归善县主簿，违去膝下，惟臣旦暮亲侍膳羞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158758_comment'></div>今来既授右职，便须远赴边任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158758_comment'></div>奉亲而往，则有道路之劳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158758_comment'></div>委亲而行，又阙晨昏之养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158758_comment'></div>况今方隅无警，贤俊至多，不乏一臣，以济众务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158758_comment'></div>伏望圣慈，察臣诚请，许臣且守旧官，依前分司、韶州居住，所图就养，少裨孝治之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158758_comment'></div>干渎冕旒，无任惶惧待罪之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158758_comment'></div>所有递到敕诰，已牒送韶州，听候朝廷回降指挥缴纳。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1158758_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1047&endYear=1047')">1047年11月11日</a>　又接敕诰，改授寿州，兵马钤辖，靖再呈状，以父年事已高，本身抱病，力辞不就。作品：让南班第二状。<div id='poem_1158759' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158759' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158759?labeling=true' target='_blank'>让南班第二状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1047年11月11日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158759")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158759_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158759'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158759'>臣昨蒙恩，除授左神武军大将军、雅州刺史，充寿州兵马钤辖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158759_comment'></div>寻以父年老，具状奏闻，乞守旧官，依前分司侍养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158759_comment'></div>今月十一日，准中书劄子，奉圣旨不许辞让者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158759_comment'></div>伏念臣昨以毁废南归，因得侍亲之便，终身农亩，实所甘心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158759_comment'></div>忽蒙异恩，再加录用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158759_comment'></div>荷国家含养之德，同天地更生之仁，仍蒙圣慈，不许辞让。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158759_comment'></div>岂不知出身事主之节，受命忘家之忠，图后效可以涤前非，履荣途胜于处穷巷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158759_comment'></div>况君亲之恩至厚，而忠义之心弗忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158759_comment'></div>但缘父年衰老，先患上气，每风露所触，则喘嗽尤甚，迎侍艰难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158759_comment'></div>有此不便，须至再披肝胆，干冒朝廷，乞依前来所奏，只守旧官，依前分司侍养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158759_comment'></div>伏望圣恩，特赐俞允，违拒诏命，甘俟除削。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1158759_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1047&endYear=1047')">1047年</a>　是年，第四女适章惇裕。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年</a>　春，应知浔州杜应之函请，作记。作品：浔州新成州学记。<div id='poem_1158970' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158970' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158970?labeling=true' target='_blank'>浔州新成州学记<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历七年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1048年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158970")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158970_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158970'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158970'>桂林之南，州郡以十数，浔为善地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158970_comment'></div>郁江东注，上无氛恶，蛮溪獠洞，不际其境，民之从化，岂间然哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158970_comment'></div>国家题期敷佑，丕冒岭海，偃革櫜弓，七纪于兹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158970_comment'></div>亦尝诏牧守立庠序，以崇化厉贤为本，而吏喜文法自进，故于教育之道缺然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158970_comment'></div>庆历纪元之七祀，京兆杜君应之被诏守土，下车三日，进谒先圣祠宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158970_comment'></div>既而笏立周视，见其庭堂卑隘，像设堕剥，冕皇服章，不中程式，瑚簋之制，亵杂常用，摄齐抠衣，居无容席。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158970_comment'></div>乃喟然叹曰：「明经进士之科，其待贤也久矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158970_comment'></div>州人未尝预太常之第者，盖教之不至也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158970_comment'></div>乃大相厥土而营学宫，卜郛之东，龟则食焉，肆命从事刁君纾以董其劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158970_comment'></div>鸱屋衮服，正厥王礼，配食从祀，各列像次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158970_comment'></div>为堂乎东，尊师教也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158970_comment'></div>筑宫于西，洁斋祠也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158970_comment'></div>翼以二序，布为校舍，旦坐塾门，人知所观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158970_comment'></div>庙学既成，明年仲春，行释菜之仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158970_comment'></div>爵坫俎房，罍云洗海，丹髹矩雘，一范之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158970_comment'></div>奠币饮福，仰登俯退，相者肄习，其容济济，诸生袍鞟，陪列终事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158970_comment'></div>越翌日，经师执帙，以正厥位，听徒就席，坐立以齿，出规入矩，启愤发悱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158970_comment'></div>州人观者，知邦君以齐鲁周孔之教而为政先，与夫束刑名、争寻常以图进者异矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158970_comment'></div>先是，邦之秀士白玘等聚而议曰：「君之丕训于我，而广其黉，乐育俊民，俾邦其昌，我不可以不赞其成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158970_comment'></div>愿以私钱十万佐官之费」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1158970_comment'></div>故是役也，不发帑金，不诛民财，而人用休息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1158970_comment'></div>已事，俾以状来谒记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1158970_comment'></div>予谓杜君，上以宣朝廷向学之意，下以成州里兴贤之本，能使远邦学者，异时取名爵于朝，当自今始，真善教者，可记也哉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1158970_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年</a>　为补植常青树，有五言绝句。作品：寄韶石长老求柏栽。<div id='poem_99448' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99448' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99448?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄韶石长老求柏栽</a><span class='authorDate'>（1048年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99448")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_99448_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99448'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99448'>森然桃李阴，当春皆手植。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99448_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99448'>更求青青枝，要见岁寒色。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99448_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99448'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_99448_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年</a>　接淮南运使来函劝慰，有文。作品：答淮南转运使段学士启。<div id='poem_1158929' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158929' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158929?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答淮南转运段学士启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1048年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158929")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158929_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158929'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158929'>右，某启：某向以琐材，滥跻通籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158929_comment'></div>无沉默之量，而克从于众；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158929_comment'></div>慕耿介之节，而不得其宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158929_comment'></div>天子以法冠弹非，诤臣缝阙，过是疏远，不预谋议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158929_comment'></div>况黜陟之际，喜怒难回，辄陈囊封，果触天宪，投弃南服，列为冗官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158929_comment'></div>螗螂奋臂，诚不量力；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158929_comment'></div>鹪鹩一枝，亦返其分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158929_comment'></div>自惟生长草野，性仍寡合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158929_comment'></div>进无左右之容，退非丘园之秀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158929_comment'></div>幸得垂缨抱椠，趋走台阁，远方之人，宁复他望？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158929_comment'></div>且据权之与失宠，孰为轻重；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158929_comment'></div>当国之与孤臣，孰为势利？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158929_comment'></div>苟曰树党以营其私，则匹夫僮妇，犹之所向，区区之诚，岂在身计？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158929_comment'></div>而朝奏暮逐，坐为比周，痛哀疾首，自明无路，冉冉贬所，亦既逾年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158929_comment'></div>庭闱千里，不遑三釜之乐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158929_comment'></div>忠贤盈朝，未赐一言之佑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158929_comment'></div>然则舍生取义，尚欲为之，荣通丑穷，固非本志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158929_comment'></div>但恐陷此罪罟，不为正人所怜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158929_comment'></div>此盖伏蒙运使学士敦树风义，远锡书教，靡诮狂狷，猥形贲饰，如在寒谷，得逢阳春，免为妄人，自今日始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158929_comment'></div>傥得天下贤士共持此谈，则虽终身穷贱，不自深耻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1158929_comment'></div>某无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1158929_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年</a>　夏秋间，与潘凤知州唱和。作品：谢伯恭篆屏蟾砚。谢送篆文屏风因次来韵。谢伯恭重阳惠酒。再简伯恭。答伯恭招棋。<div id='poem_99453' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99453' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99453?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢伯恭篆屏蟾砚</a><span class='authorDate'>（1048年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99453")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_99453_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99453'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99453'>古砚蟾蜍滴，文屏薤叶书。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99453_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99453'>世间多倚伏，休叹橐中虚<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：来诗云橐中奇物为棋输。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99453_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99453'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_99453_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_99454' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99454' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99454?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢送篆文屏风因次来韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1048年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99454")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_99454_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99454'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99454'>一局聊将万境袪，非同得兔守枯株。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99454_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99454'>北窗枕畔添奇物，却想渊明旧日无。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99454_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99454'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_99454_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_99452' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99452' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99452?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢伯恭重阳惠酒</a><span class='authorDate'>（1048年9月9日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99452")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_99452_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99452'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99452'>早霜新菊谩葳蕤，寇过人家空酒卮<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99452_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99452'>多谢使君怜病废，免教寂寞倚东篱。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99452_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99452'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_99452_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_99452'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_99452_0'>⑴ 自注：俗重老酒，去冬盗入州境，居人奔避，（原作逆，据四库本改）今岁绝无旧酝。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_99452_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_99443' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99443' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99443?labeling=true' target='_blank'>再简伯恭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1048年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_content_99443'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99443'>十载京华九日期，帝家园苑醉金卮。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99443_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99443'>今朝郭外寻僧话，坐听寒泉绕竹篱。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99443_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99443'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_99443_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_99450' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99450' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99450?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答伯恭招棋</a><span class='authorDate'>（1048年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99450")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_99450_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99450'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99450'>谁知坐隐妙通仙，国手那能得万全。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99450_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99450'>对面机关难测度，临危一著谩争先。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99450_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99450'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_99450_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年</a>　秋，应好友祖无择之请，撰记，但因病未去海州。作品：海州社稷坛记。<div id='poem_1158963' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158963' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158963?labeling=true' target='_blank'>海州社稷坛记<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历八年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1048年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158963")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158963_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158963'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158963'>古之言社稷者，其尊与宗庙等，诸侯始封，授以茅土，归其国而立社，上以尊天子之命，下以教民美报也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158963_comment'></div>汉制，郡县置社，太守、令长侍祠，牲用羊，著于祠令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158963_comment'></div>则知郡国虽异，而祀事无改，春求秋赛，未之废也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158963_comment'></div>东海郡社稷旧坛，藐在孤山之麓，地形险迫，仪度草略，素亡坛壝高卑之式，绝无畛域外内之限，牛羊所践，刍牧弗禁，慢神渎礼，阙莫甚焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158963_comment'></div>范阳祖君择之，庆历戊子由兰台丞佩郡印，既下车之三月，以为群神之在祀典者众矣，惟社稷得用笾豆，奠贽币，以修万民之报，而祠所弗严，何以示教？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158963_comment'></div>乃相美土，改而筑之，去旧址五十步，得平壤焉，广轮数亩，命以官田易之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158963_comment'></div>封土为坛，升降有陛，袭今据古，一本于礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158963_comment'></div>树以所宜之木，敞以门墙，奉祠执事者，斋有宫，侍有次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158963_comment'></div>又阅章圣皇帝所颁崇器制度，未如制者，咸俾新之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158963_comment'></div>于是政礼具举，人祇交感，风雨以时，田谷顺成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158963_comment'></div>秋八月，行事于新坛，以报神福，民心熙熙，觇盛仪而乐嘉应也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158963_comment'></div>于戏！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158963_comment'></div>择之以通材远识，屈在外补，观其临民赋政，先于典礼，得古君子之风焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158963_comment'></div>修淫祀以求庇者，得不愧乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158963_comment'></div>督役者，朐山令李良辅云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1158963_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年</a>　居住西园，种植花草树木，并着手整理个人著述，汇编为武溪集，子仲荀及其他孙子辈亦来帮忙謄抄。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年</a>　是年孙惠光出世。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1049&endYear=1049')">1049年</a>　春，广南东路提举常平仓孙抗驻韶州，新居落成，靖有诗庆贺。作品：贺孙抗员外春昼端居。<div id='poem_99488' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99488' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99488?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺孙抗员外春昼端居</a><span class='authorDate'>（1049年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99488")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_99488_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99488'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99488'>万事皆从适意休，何须快马骋长楸。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99488_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99488'>高人鼓吹鸣蛙<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>地，当世神仙笑躄楼。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99488_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99488'>燕到捲帘如<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_99488", 99488, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>旧分</span>，花开逢雨最闲愁。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99488_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99488'>僧来更学尝茶诀，白乳枪旗带露收。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99488_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1049&endYear=1049')">1049年</a>　刑部尚书钱象先来广南东路察访，经韶州探望，余靖以七律酬之。作品：和钱学士见谢新栽竹。<div id='poem_99482' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99482' class='poemTitle ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1049&endYear=1049')">1049年</a>　余靖对乡居生活悠然自得，有诗。作品：山馆。寄袭长老。和伯恭自造新茶。<div id='poem_99462' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99462' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1049&endYear=1049')">1049年11月28日</a>　接敕诰授卫尉卿，有谢表。作品：谢转卫尉卿。<div id='poem_1158760' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158760' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158760?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢转卫尉卿表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1049年11月28日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158760")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158760_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158760'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158760'>臣某言：十一月二十八日，准进奏院递到敕诰各一道，蒙恩授臣卫尉卿，依前分司南京、韶州居住，散官、勋、封、赐如故者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158760_comment'></div>举稀阔之典，方治于隆平；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158760_comment'></div>广渗漉之仁，遽沾于枯瘁<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158760_comment'></div>窃以古之哲后，皆建合宫，体房心布政之名，行祖宗侑食之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158760_comment'></div>周同庙制，盖严配之所先；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158760_comment'></div>汉比郊仪，故精禋之为重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158760_comment'></div>汶上之图太简，国南之议未工，允俟圣朝，裁定彝矩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158760_comment'></div>伏惟皇帝陛下，顺稽古训，祗答灵心，即路寝之正居，讲总章之大挚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158760_comment'></div>百神胥悦，歆至治之馨香；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158760_comment'></div>万国欢呼，荷湛恩之汪濊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158760_comment'></div>如臣者孤危得罪，摈废累年，岂期蓬荜之遐，均蒙雷雨之施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158760_comment'></div>睚眦之辞未塞，何意叨荣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158760_comment'></div>支离之粟愈多，敢忘图报？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158760_comment'></div>惟怀渊谷之惧，更增斗极之瞻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158760_comment'></div>但臣无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1158760_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1049&endYear=1049')">1049年12月</a>　内弟孙洧致函，约靖为其兄亿撰墓志。作品：宋故大理寺丞前知白州孙公墓表。<div id='poem_1159035' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159035' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159035?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宋故大理寺丞前知白州孙公墓表</a><span class='authorDate'>（皇祐元年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1159035")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159035_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159035'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159035'>君讳亿，字廷龄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159035_comment'></div>其先周文王之子康叔，封于卫，为诸侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159035_comment'></div>卫武公之孙食采于戚，曰孙氏，世为上卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159035_comment'></div>楚有叔敖，三仕至令尹，封于寝丘，号为循吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159035_comment'></div>汉有坚父子，开国于吴，以有江淮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159035_comment'></div>故其世系繁衍于南方，而望于富春之族，土著于袁之分宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159035_comment'></div>曾祖某、祖某、考某，累叶高蹈，恬退自守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159035_comment'></div>君幼挺奇节，资性温厚，博览广记，不为章句之学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159035_comment'></div>弱冠能属文，举进士上第，选注桂阳监判官、虔州节度推官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159035_comment'></div>荐其材者章交公车，擢授大理寺丞、知吉州永新县，徙知白州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159035_comment'></div>丁先府君忧，服阙，符召还台，道卒于宿州，享年四十一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159035_comment'></div>桂阳地产五金，诤盗日积；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159035_comment'></div>南康土沃民繁，郡多滞讼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159035_comment'></div>君连佐二幕，率以和易守职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159035_comment'></div>进则启迪嘉谋，以裨邦君之阙，退接民吏，一无异言，故直道得行，而上下悦之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159035_comment'></div>其宰永新也，予时忝典城之寄，共为亲民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159035_comment'></div>吉民岁配和市缣素六万馀匹，主外计者籍收帑钱，以供他费，第给海盐偿其缣直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159035_comment'></div>前政又以邑豪入粟得爵者，准官户免其征，细民由是重困。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159035_comment'></div>君发其弊，予得奏停邑官，且藏镪于县以酬民缣，外台不能诘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159035_comment'></div>吉之田租，岁收四十万斛，必择廉干司庾之入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159035_comment'></div>漕臣意在聚歛，预戒庾吏定收什二以充羡馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159035_comment'></div>专其局者，惟君能守州约，拒台命，出纳一用仓式，其公正皆此类也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159035_comment'></div>俾其克寿而贵，善政岂可量哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159035_comment'></div>其居丧也，不历姻娅之门，不知盐酪之味，三年无改，邦域称焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159035_comment'></div>君初以艺文知名，故枢密成纪文宪李公咨特加称赏，妻以兄子，实多内助。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159035_comment'></div>生二女三男：长女适李氏，予以弱息仲荀娶其幼女；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159035_comment'></div>男之邵、之翰、之问，皆未冠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1159035_comment'></div>君以皇祐元年四月二十九日，捐馆舍于扶离。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1159035_comment'></div>诸孤扶其柩归，以其年十二月二日，葬于分宜县某乡某原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1159035_comment'></div>其弟洧以书来索文，不及掩圹之期，故表诸阡而铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_1159035'>天生吉人，付之正性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1159035_comment'></div>胡不与全，而薄其命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1159035_comment'></div>瘠贤肥佞，亦天之病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1159035_comment'></div>表诸墓道，以图惟永。</div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1159035_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1050&endYear=1050')">1050年</a>　春，与孙抗游芙蓉山，有诗。作品：谢孙抗员外惠酒。<div id='poem_99529' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99529' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99529?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢孙抗员外惠酒</a><span class='authorDate'>（1050年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99529")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_99529_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99529'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99529'>白衣远远到江楼，报道携壶助胜游。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99529_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99529'>醉眼便堪终日富，离肠先破一春愁。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99529_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99529'>梅梢背岭开犹晚，雪片当风舞未休。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99529_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99529'>此景满觞<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>方得意，不须<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_99529", 99529, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>千酿</span>敌封侯。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99529_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_99529'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_99529_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_99529'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_99529_0'>⑴ 原作肠，据四库本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_99529_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1050&endYear=1050')">1050年</a>　宗亲整理《余氏宗谱》，靖为作序。作品：下邳余氏世谱序。<div id='poem_1158951' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158951' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158951?labeling=true' target='_blank'>〔附录〕下邳余氏世谱序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1050年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158951")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158951_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158951'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158951'>按余氏之先世，出自黄帝之子玄嚣，又三世至弃，掌后稷之官，有功，封诸侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158951_comment'></div>自弃十六世至文王昌、武王发、成王诵，封同母弟叔虞于晋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158951_comment'></div>后三十馀世有苗裔曰由余，因晋不振，大臣恣横，惧祸及身，去晋入戎，戎主佐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158951_comment'></div>使秦，秦穆公问国之得失，对曰：「恭俭则昌，骄奢则亡」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158951_comment'></div>又论五帝三王盛衰之本，穆公惧曰：「邻国有圣人，可无忧乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158951_comment'></div>由余其圣人矣，奈何！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158951_comment'></div>我国之安危未定」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158951_comment'></div>由余出，芮史入，穆公曰：「卿为之谋」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158951_comment'></div>芮史曰：「但报戎君，缓遣由余，君臣反目即在尔」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158951_comment'></div>后戎主骄奢，荒于酒色，由余谏不行，遂归复于秦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158951_comment'></div>穆公闻由余归，喜而郊迎之，拜上卿，遂大用由余之计策，并国十二，辟地千里，皆由余之力，寻相秦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158951_comment'></div>而后世子孙有曰余瑞，仕秦中散大夫，居河洛间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158951_comment'></div>厥后两汉、魏、晋、齐、隋、秦之间，析居流裔，簪缨不绝，而禄卑，不得纪于国史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158951_comment'></div>至于大唐开元八年，有余钦为太学博士，居歙之休宁，历数世而至戭者，因黄巢之乱，徙居邵武之光泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158951_comment'></div>戭长子曰从，避五季寇乱，居韶之曲江；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158951_comment'></div>次曰咸，居洪州之分宁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158951_comment'></div>又其次曰衮，徙杭州之钱塘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158951_comment'></div>予即戭之五世孙也，以天圣甲子登进士第，寻擢集贤校理，与欧阳修同居谏职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158951_comment'></div>斯时也，奸心佞舌，充满朝廷，但进不能兴唐虞，退不能补三代之馀风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158951_comment'></div>迩因黔镇广南，道经故邑，祀享馀力，特书家谱，以遗后代云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1158951_comment'></div>皇祐二年庚寅岁正月望日，赐进士第、朝散大夫、授工部尚书、充集贤院校理学士、知广州军事、兼广南东路兵马都钤辖、按抚使、柱国、始兴郡开国公、食邑二千六百户、食实封二百户、赐紫金鱼袋、赠刑部尚书五世孙余靖撰<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1158951_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_1158951'>黄慈博校云：「按此文结衔有身后追赐者，疑为后人羼入，文气亦不甚类，或伪托也」。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1158951_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1158951'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_20_1158951_12'>⑴ 《武溪集补佚》引《余氏族谱》卷一上。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1158951_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1050&endYear=1050')">1050年5月</a>　应邀作记。作品：韶州新建永通监记。<div id='poem_1158962' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158962' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158962?labeling=true' target='_blank'>韶州新置永通监记</a><span class='authorDate'>（皇祐二年五月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158962")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158962_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158962'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158962'>古之建国者，义以制事，材以聚人，八政之先，曰食与货，即山鼓铸，三代而然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158962_comment'></div>禹铸历山之金以御水祸，汤造庄山之币以拯旱虐，周以金钖之利分隶虞衡，唐以郴桂之郡并建炉冶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158962_comment'></div>货之所产，本无定处，兴造之谋，期于便事而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158962_comment'></div>国家平一诸夏，宠绥四海，开宝、兴国之际，收复江闽，因其故区，作为泉布。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158962_comment'></div>时移岁积，地产靡常，比年已来，冶民几废焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158962_comment'></div>今天子嗣位之二十七年，特诏翰林学士叶公清臣、宋公祁经度山泽之禁，以资国用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158962_comment'></div>乃佥作奏曰：「谨校郡国产铜和市之数，惟韶为多，而夐处岭阨，由江淮资本钱以酬其直，实为迥远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158962_comment'></div>谓宜即韶置监，分遣金工以往模之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158962_comment'></div>岁用铜百万斤，可得成币三百万，三分其一以上供，馀复市铜，几得二百万，如是则其息无穷矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158962_comment'></div>诏下其议于广东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158962_comment'></div>于时转运使、直太史傅公某知韶州，比曹副郎栾公某协恭承诏，以经厥始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158962_comment'></div>郡有故堞，号为西州遗址，高平宛出郛外，乃相厥土，墨则食焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158962_comment'></div>凡栋宇之制，管库之严，询于故实，继以心匠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158962_comment'></div>模沙冶金，分作有八；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158962_comment'></div>刀错水蓥，离局为二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158962_comment'></div>并列关钥，互有堤防，当其中扃，控以厅事，谁何警察，自无逃形。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158962_comment'></div>其铅错之备用，薪炭之兼蓄，别藏异室，布于两序，出内谨密。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158962_comment'></div>前为大闳，冶官列署于闳之南，群工屯营于垣之外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158962_comment'></div>市材于山，市甓于陶，雇工于巧，凡手指之勤，筋力之用，率平价而与之金，不发帑赀，不徭民籍，而功用成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158962_comment'></div>为屋八百楹，最材、竹、铁、石、陶瓬之用一百四十万，惟材木六千资于连山，钉口十万出自真阳，馀悉办于韶之境，而民不知役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1158962_comment'></div>乃知循良之政，诚自有体哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1158962_comment'></div>以皇祐冠年龙集己丑三月甲午始筑其基而饬其材，八月辛酉，栋宇完，范镕备，物有区，工有居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1158962_comment'></div>九月己亥，大合乐以落之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1158962_comment'></div>董旧巧，募新习，勖怠励惰，绶以程准，日课千缗，不愆于素。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1158962_comment'></div>初，郡之铜山，五岁共市七万，前太守潘君一岁市百万，及栾公继之，乃市三百万，明年又差倍之，岁运羡铜三百万，以赡岭北诸冶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1158962_comment'></div>茍非主计者通其神，提纲者扬其职，守土者宣其力，则何以协规创模、成效之速如是哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1158962_comment'></div>且韶被山带海，杂产五金，四方之人，弃农亩，持兵器，慕利而至者，不暇十万，穷则公剽，怒则私斗，轻生抵禁，亡所忌惮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1158962_comment'></div>缓其羁绁，则鹰挚而陆梁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1158962_comment'></div>急其衔勒，则兽骇而踶齧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1158962_comment'></div>故境壤虽狭，而狱犴寇抄常倍他境，必资威肃惠和，兼被于物，乃成善政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1158962_comment'></div>观此图功赋事，精至详简，则民之受赐，其可知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1158962_comment'></div>初以远方置监，议者不一，故朝廷有以待之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1158962_comment'></div>明年四月，乃下敕赐名「永通」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1158962_comment'></div>时天子亲享明堂之岁五月记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1158962_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1050&endYear=1050')">1050年</a>　应桂林友人谭伯愿之请，作文。作品：书谭氏东斋。<div id='poem_1159007' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159007' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159007?labeling=true' target='_blank'>书谭氏东斋</a><span class='authorDate'>（皇祐二年七月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1159007")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159007_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159007'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159007'>人之志于道者，在乎去烦释累，静虑和衷，视听动息，不汩不诱，然后以居者则安，以学者则专，自非离尘绝俗，不能至于是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159007_comment'></div>吾友谭君伯顾，自桂林佐邑，遭私艰还第，素冠弥时，不营他务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159007_comment'></div>乃相厥居之东二里而近，出氛杂，卜岑寂，面江倚阜，披云跻险，廓地数亩，作为斋舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159007_comment'></div>上以屏去人事，下以训励子姓，己得其安，子姓得其专，有志于道者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159007_comment'></div>屋不加饰，地不祈广，蓺林驾泉，自适而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159007_comment'></div>图史机案，旁无长物，所谓不见异物而迁者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159007_comment'></div>丘垄不遐，日得瞻睇，不忘其亲者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159007_comment'></div>吾友之意也深矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159007_comment'></div>一日，携僧泛舟而谒之，爱其清旷，又嘉其子弟甥侄翼翼如也，因书其壁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159007_comment'></div>皇祐二年七月日题。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1159007_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1050&endYear=1050')">1050年</a>　少时之师张伯端已为道士，云游来韶州，后归赣，有诗。作品：送岳师归赣川。<div id='poem_99498' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99498' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99498?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送岳师归赣川</a><span class='authorDate'>（1050年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99498")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_99498_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99498'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99498'>千里起归思，翛然物外身。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99498_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99498'>海山经处雾，梅岭到时春。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99498_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99498'>药更开新楮，庭应长旧筠。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99498_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99498'>年衰重方术，聊此送行人。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99498_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_99498'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_99498_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1050&endYear=1050')">1050年</a>　同僚好友王子野卒，赋七律。作品：哭王子野待制。<div id='poem_99511' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99511' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99511?labeling=true' target='_blank'>哭王子野待制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1050年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99511")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_99511_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99511'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99511'>赤墀趋步近相陪，邸吏俄传远讣来。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99511_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99511'>方冀君心辨忠义，岂知天意夺贤材。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99511_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99511'>堪伤棣萼同时葬<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：闻与浙东兄同日襄事。）</span>，空想铭旌此日回。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99511_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99511'>谪宦无缘亲渍酒，江边长恸独徘徊。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99511_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_99511'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_99511_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1050&endYear=1050')">1050年</a>　秋冬间赋五言古诗。作品：南斋新植牡丹初冬忽开数朵爱玩不已因而感詠呈知郡中舍。<div id='poem_99561' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99561' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99561?labeling=true' target='_blank'>南斋新植牡丹初冬忽开数朵爱玩不已因而感咏呈知郡中舍</a><span class='authorDate'>（1050年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99561")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_99561_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99561'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99561'>峤南足暄候，秋叶不凋霜。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99561_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99561'>孤根自北来，绣蕊忽葩张。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99561_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99561'>嗟尔本国艳，秀色含天香。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99561_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99561'>淑气入春萼，园苑生辉光。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99561_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_99561'>豪家走钿车，珠翠妍新妆。<div id='poem_sentence_4_99561_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_99561'>贵门陈广宴，金碧开华堂。<div id='poem_sentence_5_99561_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_99561'>惟恐风雨至，不羞歌舞狂。<div id='poem_sentence_6_99561_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_99561'>意态占韶景，众媚曷能妨。<div id='poem_sentence_7_99561_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_99561'>今兹植荒圃，空斋围短墙。<div id='poem_sentence_8_99561_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_99561'>节物寒蝉后，林木野梅傍。<div id='poem_sentence_9_99561_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_99561'>胡为吐奇卉，特此昧温凉。<div id='poem_sentence_10_99561_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_99561'>祇知逢日暖，岂测非春阳。<div id='poem_sentence_11_99561_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_99561'>蜂蝶不尔采，坏栏啼夜螀。<div id='poem_sentence_12_99561_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_99561'>伊予久杜门，荆榛三径荒。<div id='poem_sentence_13_99561_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_99561'>独酌难成醉，徙倚徒徬徨。<div id='poem_sentence_14_99561_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_99561'>怜尔守常性，幽丛不改芳。<div id='poem_sentence_15_99561_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_99561'></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_99561_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1050&endYear=1050')">1050年</a>　秋冬间赋七言律诗。作品：先赏牡丹寄提刑考功。又和提刑太保。<div id='poem_99466' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99466' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99466?labeling=true' target='_blank'>先赏牡丹寄提刑考功</a><span class='authorDate'>（1050年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99466")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_99466_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99466'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99466'>花期何事早追陪，莺未迁乔燕未来。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99466_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99466'>曲槛为逢春日暖，香苞先逐晓风开。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99466_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99466'>旋邀歌舞同侪乐，却叹光阴急景催。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99466_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99466'>可惜韶妍莫虚掷，馀芳留待使车回。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99466_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1052&endYear=1052')">1052年6月20日</a>　朝廷命余靖停丧次，以秘书监知潭州，领韶州府特支赐钱三百贯文赴任，靖呈状。作品：乞不请支赐添支状。<div id='poem_1158784' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158784' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158784?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞不请支赐添支状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1052年6月20日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158784")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158784_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158784'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158784'>右，臣昨奉敕免持服，特授秘书监，就差知潭州兼本路安抚使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158784_comment'></div>准中书劄子，奉圣旨，令韶州特支赐钱三百贯文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158784_comment'></div>寻赴任次，在路奉敕改差知桂州、广南西路都钤辖兼经略安抚使，已于七月十六日到任上讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158784_comment'></div>伏缘臣昨者起就潭州差遣，所以不敢辞免者，盖欲因朝廷之命，起湖南兵甲，往广州策应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158784_comment'></div>寻奉敕命改差，其任益重，非臣本志所贪权宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158784_comment'></div>臣今只候杨畋到西路商量边机了日，却乞终丧持服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158784_comment'></div>兼臣居丧中已奉圣旨，支给前官料钱，所有特支赐钱，见寄韶州军资库，并桂州合请添支钱物，并乞不请领。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158784_comment'></div>其原受中书劄子一道，谨具封纳。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1158784_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年</a>，62岁</div><div id='84a3d089c77c4af8b0b98768528853a6' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年</a>　遣返荆湖路兵马，为妻奔丧，在韶州小住至年初。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='77b25d67e918477f85179ed2d0d9e60b_label'><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1064&endYear=1064')">1064年</a>　在韶州小住。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1064&endYear=1064')">1064年6月19日</a>　敕授工部尚书，充集贤院学士、加柱国、始兴郡开国公、食邑二千六百户、食实封二百户。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1006&endYear=1006')">1006年</a>　在耽石院与王陶来从学于王式。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1007&endYear=1007')">1007年</a>　余庆带次子希翊来耽石院，梅鼎臣亦带儿子梅佐来探王式，余靖与王陶、梅佐相处甚欢。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1008&endYear=1008')">1008年4月9日</a>　余庆举荐梅鼎臣、王式试礼部未中，二人回耽石院刻苦研读，严加督促余靖等四小辈读书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1008&endYear=1008')">1008年</a>　三弟余希端生。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1009&endYear=1009')">1009年</a>　父余庆改知海阳，仍留二子由王式、梅鼎臣执教。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1009&endYear=1009')">1009年</a>　耽石院檀越巢公供余靖兄弟生活费用，其子巢迪亦参加攻读。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1009&endYear=1009')">1009年</a>　黄正时来看望并授以辞赋知识，并与王式、梅鼎臣结为莫逆之交。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1010&endYear=1010')">1010年</a>　梅氏父子回翁源梅岩，余靖与弟希翊、王式父子攻读于耽石院，不久黄正加入。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1011&endYear=1011')">1011年</a>　王式父子丁母忧，黄正带余靖兄弟回韶州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1011&endYear=1011')">1011年</a>　余靖三妹出世。<br /><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1011&endYear=1011')">1011年</a>　父余庆陞潮州长史，因丁母忧归家守制。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='ad4adce3332c4aae972d1d4a70f69b6d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("33d7dc4c4ab74d7b805c753b005dfae6");'><span id='33d7dc4c4ab74d7b805c753b005dfae6_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1049&endYear=1049')">1049年</a>，50岁</div><div id='33d7dc4c4ab74d7b805c753b005dfae6' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1049&endYear=1049')">1049年8月</a>　应邀回翁源一行，作记。作品：翁源县净源山耽石院记。<div id='poem_1158981' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158981' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158981?labeling=true' target='_blank'>韶州翁源县净源山耽石院记</a><span class='authorDate'>（皇祐元年八月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158981")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158981_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158981'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158981'>古之学佛者，内乐空寂以照自性，外作饶益以济群动，故行脩于己而功施于物，虽岩居穴处，草衣木食，委去浮累，超然独往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158981_comment'></div>而万家之城、十室之聚，率有信向，仰为开导。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158981_comment'></div>由是攀萝蹑霭，栈险梁深，异人所居，必立精舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158981_comment'></div>耽石院者，翁川之列刹也，山川葱郁，杳绝纷嚣，泉石幽奇，足以耽玩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158981_comment'></div>唐大中三年，有僧法光，爰此剪茅，众为筑室，去华摭实，遂以耽石为名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158981_comment'></div>刘氏瓜剖，乱离斯瘼，钟呗之声，几乎息矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158981_comment'></div>开宝初，因其故号，迁于上潭，香火仅在，风幡无托。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158981_comment'></div>不有废也，其何以兴？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158981_comment'></div>天圣中，今住持慧周同檀越巢迪等相与谋曰：「佛之示权也大矣，人之起信也久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158981_comment'></div>察荣悴者知其果，视祸福者存乎应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158981_comment'></div>崇善者有精进以笃其修，畏罪者有忏悔以寡其过，多藏者有布施以破其惑，念往者有追奉以广其孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158981_comment'></div>是知民之闾井，不可一日而违塔庙也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158981_comment'></div>既而同焉者募，异焉者劝，富焉者资，巧焉者力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158981_comment'></div>其相土也，则叠岫宾挹，澄溪带附；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158981_comment'></div>其度材也，则百堵云搆，四阿翚飞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158981_comment'></div>其设像也，则金璧睟容，天龙善卫；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158981_comment'></div>其据境也，则珍木弥望，佳气袭人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158981_comment'></div>真崇福之秘宇，绝尘之幽致也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158981_comment'></div>茍非智者创谋，善人协规，孰能与于此哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158981_comment'></div>巨石如屏，泉淙于下，可以爽情灵，可以涤尘虑，命名之始，其在兹乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1158981_comment'></div>就崖砻琢，传之不朽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1158981_comment'></div>皇祐元年八月日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1158981_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
潮阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='641ddb8d8fc8456f854210f0579d57f5_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("641ddb8d8fc8456f854210f0579d57f5");'><span id='641ddb8d8fc8456f854210f0579d57f5_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1013&endYear=1013')">1013年</a>，14岁</div><div id='641ddb8d8fc8456f854210f0579d57f5' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1013&endYear=1013')">1013年</a>　父余庆因潮州海涌受灾停丧起复，携余靖赴潮州，林从周见其一表人材，以次女许之，余靖订婚。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='66a2f870705a497c81f20be31d0448da_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("66a2f870705a497c81f20be31d0448da");'><span id='66a2f870705a497c81f20be31d0448da_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1025&endYear=1025')">1025年</a>，26岁</div><div id='66a2f870705a497c81f20be31d0448da' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1025&endYear=1025')">1025年5月30日</a>　岳父林从周病逝，余靖赴海阳奔丧数天。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='b682dd22feb24d4faf80ce9c946a3a7b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b682dd22feb24d4faf80ce9c946a3a7b");'><span id='b682dd22feb24d4faf80ce9c946a3a7b_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年</a>，42岁</div><div id='b682dd22feb24d4faf80ce9c946a3a7b' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年</a>　夏，往潮州拜谒岳丈林从周墓及看望长子一家。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='40312627a5254694ae78054750b4d556_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("40312627a5254694ae78054750b4d556");'><span id='40312627a5254694ae78054750b4d556_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1064&endYear=1064')">1064年</a>，65岁</div><div id='40312627a5254694ae78054750b4d556' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1064&endYear=1064')">1064年</a>　至本路各州县察访，曾到海阳祭拜其岳丈林从周、长子伯庄墓。<br /></div>
-----end

-----title
杭州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='e8dc9a7d00ae4de2b46b14f60da2d272_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e8dc9a7d00ae4de2b46b14f60da2d272");'><span id='e8dc9a7d00ae4de2b46b14f60da2d272_link' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1015&endYear=1015')">1015年</a>　石介奉父命，苏舜钦由其父送来，俱拜林逋为师，与余靖、石介同室相处，最为要好。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1015&endYear=1015')">1015年</a>　曾去钱塘探望曾叔祖余衮后裔。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1017&endYear=1017')">1017年</a>　父余庆以年迈乞回韶州，获准迁韶州府学正，常去府庠讲学。<br /><a href="javascript: -----title
苏州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='7fa757c3db00487691647f3571053a42_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("7fa757c3db00487691647f3571053a42");'><span id='7fa757c3db00487691647f3571053a42_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1020&endYear=1020')">1020年</a>，21岁</div><div id='7fa757c3db00487691647f3571053a42' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1020&endYear=1020')">1020年</a>　奉师命至江苏吴县藏书乡天池山吴中书屋，从胡瑗学经济。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1020&endYear=1020')">1020年</a>　适孙复亦带石介、祖无择来访胡瑗，瑗喜邀孙复同讲学。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1020&endYear=1020')">1020年9月</a>　秋末，孙复携石介、祖无择回鲁。<br /></div>

-----title
开封
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='7d23e46f9c144372aaa8876a39c57c80_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("7d23e46f9c144372aaa8876a39c57c80");'><span id='7d23e46f9c144372aaa8876a39c57c80_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1024&endYear=1024')">1024年</a>，25岁</div><div id='7d23e46f9c144372aaa8876a39c57c80' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1024&endYear=1024')">1024年3月4日</a>　余靖参加礼部贡举人殿试，御试撰人判词十首。作品：甲为学官教国子以六艺或讥其艺成而下不伏。乙为太常请复乡饮酒御史以为其礼久废不可复行。丙为大夫浣衣濯冠以朝或讥其隘辞云俭德之恭也。丁盛服谒使者门下令其解剑辞云剑者君子武备不可解。戊为御史大夫泣封具狱或讥其过。甲为京尹耕者让畔行者异路或云无益。乙为刺史荐门下吏或以为当得山泽隐滞辞云山泽不必有异士。丙越度官府垣篱官司罪之辞云随甲而往。甲私行入驿驿官拒之辞云职事五品以上。辛捕罪人丁过而不救辞云家有急事救疗。<div id='poem_1158865' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158865' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158865?labeling=true' target='_blank'>甲为学官教国子以六艺或讥其艺成而下不伏<span class='inlineComment2'>（御试判词之一）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1024年3月4日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158865")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158865_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158865'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158865'>立身之道，虽鄙异端；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158865_comment'></div>进学之方，必资善教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158865_comment'></div>盖严师而育益，岂执艺以同讥？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158865_comment'></div>甲德比圭璋，才堪模范。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158865_comment'></div>东序上庠之地，素号人师；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158865_comment'></div>五礼六乐之文，敢忘国典？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158865_comment'></div>至于和容执辔，夙著彝章，会意差分，悉有成训，咸资博谕，式励多能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158865_comment'></div>何哉或者之谈，罔识先儒之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158865_comment'></div>且夫治民安上，不专于揖让周旋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158865_comment'></div>易俗移风，可以察存亡治乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158865_comment'></div>习于襄尺，爰摽选士之规；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158865_comment'></div>舞彼交衢，再纪鸣銮之节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158865_comment'></div>偃波成字，取法于奎躔；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158865_comment'></div>回箸穷微，能知于府实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158865_comment'></div>安可比之贱技，固当励彼兼才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158865_comment'></div>鄙事自谦，虽闻尼父之语；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158865_comment'></div>嘉猷可采，盍遵保氏之仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158865_comment'></div>固难诘以他规，宜见嘉于善诱。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1158865_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1158866' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158866' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158866?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乙为太常请复乡饮酒御史以为其礼久废不可复行<span class='inlineComment2'>（御试判词之二）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1024年3月4日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158866")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158866_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158866'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158866'>教民以礼，诚欲从时；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158866_comment'></div>观乡有仪，岂妨行古？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158866_comment'></div>将举治邦之典，必先几圣之谋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158866_comment'></div>况乎事著前修，议非独见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158866_comment'></div>太常以礼存沿革，请颁尚齿之仪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158866_comment'></div>御史云政贵因循，难复兴贤之制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158866_comment'></div>虽是非之互列，在白黑以宜分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158866_comment'></div>顺彼世机，岂五礼之必废？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158866_comment'></div>知其王道，亦三代之可追。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158866_comment'></div>何则？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158866_comment'></div>旧典攸存，鸿仪具举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158866_comment'></div>宾王取象于天地，长幼以伦；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158866_comment'></div>介僎立法于阴阳，登降有数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158866_comment'></div>俾其成俗，可以制中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158866_comment'></div>三揖而后升，所期教让；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158866_comment'></div>五十者立侍，式冀明尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158866_comment'></div>匪独扬觯以为容，抑亦荐能而垂范。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158866_comment'></div>严凝温厚，体仁义而有经；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158866_comment'></div>西北东南，正衽席而无乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158866_comment'></div>式稽典故，诚可遵行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1158866_comment'></div>请从宗伯之言，庶协先王之训。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1158866_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1158867' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158867' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158867?labeling=true' target='_blank'>丙为大夫浣衣濯冠以朝或讥其隘辞云俭德之恭也<span class='inlineComment2'>（御试判词之三）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1024年3月4日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158867")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158867_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158867'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158867'>车服有章，诚难偪下；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158867_comment'></div>衣冠无僭，当许谨身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158867_comment'></div>在全德而或亏，于常情而何过？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158867_comment'></div>丙也，名先淑慎，志谢纷华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158867_comment'></div>趋表著以思恭，方期率励；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158867_comment'></div>服浣濯而从俭，式诫奢淫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158867_comment'></div>盖质朴而自居，奚固陋而相罪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158867_comment'></div>且三梁垂制，用辨于尊卑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158867_comment'></div>百袭矜豪，未惭于侈汰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158867_comment'></div>所期见伟，何乃云非？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158867_comment'></div>贵而能贫，尝睹子张之戒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158867_comment'></div>富而好礼，式遵尼父之谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158867_comment'></div>俾有节于身章，宁妄加于首饰？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158867_comment'></div>平津布被，诚或虑其矫诬；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158867_comment'></div>子臧鹬冠，终亦招于祸败。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158867_comment'></div>盖俗奢而示俭，非诈善而近名，忘九仪之有差，信一节之可尚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158867_comment'></div>虽义存《戴礼》，狐裘为卿佐之讥；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158867_comment'></div>而《诗》美《周南》，《葛覃》有后妃之化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158867_comment'></div>式昭恭德，无愧前脩。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1158867_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1158868' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158868' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158868?labeling=true' target='_blank'>丁盛服谒使者门下令其解剑辞云剑者君子武备不可解<span class='inlineComment2'>（御试判词之四）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1024年3月4日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158868")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158868_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158868'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158868'>皇华宣命，虽喜登门；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158868_comment'></div>武备饰身，宁宜解剑？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158868_comment'></div>必许兼人之勇，难从索客之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158868_comment'></div>丁也，修谒驷车，入趋墙仞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158868_comment'></div>仰其符采，未逢躧履之迎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158868_comment'></div>佩彼干将，遂致解衣之拒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158868_comment'></div>过既彰于下吏，礼将阙于上宾，揖让未修，侮慢可耻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158868_comment'></div>且绣衣美秩，诚欲尊崇，而玉具盛容，难轻去就。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158868_comment'></div>所宜与进，胡莫肆仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158868_comment'></div>虽列郡宣风，汉守布佩牛之化；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158868_comment'></div>况公门异礼，鲁人有脱缞之嫌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158868_comment'></div>事茍失于典彝，义宁甘于进退？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158868_comment'></div>代逢吴子，设诸或止于膝行；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158868_comment'></div>名重霍光，萧傅亦羞于露索。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158868_comment'></div>固当从俗，奚独乱常？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158868_comment'></div>持斧自矜，暴胜之既闻失节；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158868_comment'></div>抚斋无茍，隽不疑终亦抗辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158868_comment'></div>勿疑披露之心，在焕干星之彩。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1158868_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1158869' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158869' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158869?labeling=true' target='_blank'>戊为御史大夫泣封具狱或讥其过<span class='inlineComment2'>（御试判词之五）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1024年3月4日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158869")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158869_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158869'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158869'>黄沙具狱，虽贵哀矜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158869_comment'></div>丹笔正刑，何烦感泣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158869_comment'></div>苟原心而无滥，谅承睫以胡为？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158869_comment'></div>戊名冠鸳行，任隆乌府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158869_comment'></div>国章明启，每色听而得情；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158869_comment'></div>奏章初成，必面封而流泪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158869_comment'></div>详观所履，未协大中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158869_comment'></div>何则？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158869_comment'></div>自速其辜，人既彰于凶德；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158869_comment'></div>不失有罪，法但诫于深文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158869_comment'></div>傥能察必无冤，何用痛其不免？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158869_comment'></div>且明德慎罚，虽存审克之规；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158869_comment'></div>而议狱缓死，岂有涟洳之象？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158869_comment'></div>况自专于决谳，亦可辨其重轻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158869_comment'></div>若徽纆之妄施，虽涕洟而何益？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158869_comment'></div>惠奸有意，所谓妇人之仁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158869_comment'></div>疾恶无私，宜惭君子之器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158869_comment'></div>但可精于慎恻，固应绝彼放纷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158869_comment'></div>悲对室家，盛吉未为得义；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158869_comment'></div>哀生棘木，张敞无乃近名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1158869_comment'></div>将示小慈，终亏大体。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1158869_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1158870' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158870' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158870?labeling=true' target='_blank'>甲为京尹耕者让畔行者异路或云无益<span class='inlineComment2'>（御试判词之六）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1024年3月4日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158870")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158870_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158870'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158870'>威严御下，诚曰有权；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158870_comment'></div>礼让移风，孰云无益？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158870_comment'></div>虽浩穰之难理，惟渐染而克成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158870_comment'></div>甲以德服人，所居必化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158870_comment'></div>大田千耦，咸敦让畔之诚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158870_comment'></div>广陌三条，尽识异途之教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158870_comment'></div>式期成俗，非欲邀名，何乃或人，旁生横议？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158870_comment'></div>且仁政必始于经界，自协和平；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158870_comment'></div>善教不争于丑夷，爰资诱导。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158870_comment'></div>治可孚于绳木，事且异于米盐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158870_comment'></div>学校如林，既飞声于蜀郡；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158870_comment'></div>羔豚去饰，尝阐化于中都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158870_comment'></div>实仓廪而有知，奉诏条而无失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158870_comment'></div>岐山布德，遂悛虞芮之心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158870_comment'></div>冯翊推诚，终息弟兄之讼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158870_comment'></div>咸裨治体，绰著民彝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158870_comment'></div>必世后仁，备闻往谍；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158870_comment'></div>一国兴让，宁愧前修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158870_comment'></div>岂唯知稼穑之难，不复竞险易之利，但可励其谦退，无宜督以科绳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158870_comment'></div>黄霸虽已失中，张敞未为知义。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1158870_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1158871' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158871' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158871?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乙为刺史荐门下吏或以为当得山泽隐滞辞云山泽不必有异士<span class='inlineComment2'>（御试判词之七）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1024年3月4日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158871")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158871_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158871'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158871'>择贤而任，诚恤滞淹；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158871_comment'></div>惟才是求，何必幽隐？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158871_comment'></div>但器能而可采，岂薖轴以为先？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158871_comment'></div>乙束带立朝，剖符出守，心既精于求瘼，道固协于援能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158871_comment'></div>千骑长人，任且隆于藩翰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158871_comment'></div>百石补吏，器不问于山林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158871_comment'></div>爰推体国之忠，允协知人之善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158871_comment'></div>岂资遗逸，方俟甄收？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158871_comment'></div>且风鉴既精，文子或升于管库；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158871_comment'></div>官联茍序，卫青犹奋于庸奴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158871_comment'></div>所贵立贤无方，庶协适时之用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158871_comment'></div>戋戋之帛，徒欲贲于丘园；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158871_comment'></div>森森之材，自可择其翘楚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158871_comment'></div>吴祐尝交于小吏，夷吾亦举于僻游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158871_comment'></div>采彼虚名，卢毓终羞于画饼；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158871_comment'></div>取其大节，郑《诗》无弃于采葑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158871_comment'></div>奚必絇兰之人，方今推毂而仕？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158871_comment'></div>虽鲁儒言教，当举于逸民；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158871_comment'></div>而汉守援贤，止求于佳器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158871_comment'></div>式谐举类，无或执迷。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1158871_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1158872' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158872' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158872?labeling=true' target='_blank'>丙越度官府垣篱官司罪之辞云随甲而往<span class='inlineComment2'>（御试判词之八）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1024年3月4日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158872")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158872_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158872'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158872'>协谋抵禁，法有减论；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158872_comment'></div>冒度干刑，理无从坐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158872_comment'></div>既投足而同往，岂原心而或殊？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158872_comment'></div>丙德之弗修，动而有悔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158872_comment'></div>不如己者，方踰数仞之墙；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158872_comment'></div>因而从之，遂惟三尺之法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158872_comment'></div>自疏明慎，犹启薄言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158872_comment'></div>况穴隙以相从，惟蔇茨而是履。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158872_comment'></div>前王著令，徒攀共犯之条；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158872_comment'></div>君子向儒，盍守独行之节？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158872_comment'></div>矧府寺之攸设，惟藩屏而是崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158872_comment'></div>不得其门，同临蔽恶之地；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158872_comment'></div>必求诸道，当惭由径之非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158872_comment'></div>虽曰比之匪人，实亦动而过则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158872_comment'></div>原其发虑，遽云职汝之由；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158872_comment'></div>详彼治躬，岂可效人之僻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158872_comment'></div>咎将谁执，戚实己招。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158872_comment'></div>视篱落之具存，当跬步而为过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158872_comment'></div>别冒汉家之网，或异首科；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158872_comment'></div>自绝蒲人之袪，谅难降等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1158872_comment'></div>三千之条备纪，七十之杖何逃？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1158872_comment'></div>罪必甘心，词奚苦诉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1158872_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1158872_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1158873' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158873' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158873?labeling=true' target='_blank'>甲私行入驿驿官拒之辞云职事五品以上<span class='inlineComment2'>（御试判词之九）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1024年3月4日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158873")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158873_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158873'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158873'>出非君命，难入息于野庐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158873_comment'></div>名重官联，当即安于公馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158873_comment'></div>既纡朱而表贵，虽按辔以何伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158873_comment'></div>甲锡爵王朝，改辕私役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158873_comment'></div>名司其局，张旌且异于輶軿；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158873_comment'></div>驾言出游，秣马遂登于馆舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158873_comment'></div>何哉主吏，罔识彝仪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158873_comment'></div>况银章之自崇，岂金车而见困？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158873_comment'></div>地分亭堠，亦既高其闬闳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158873_comment'></div>位列簪缨，焉可止于逆旅？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158873_comment'></div>官已差其品秩，人合辨于尊卑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158873_comment'></div>伯宗之传弗乘，诚难假道；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158873_comment'></div>子产之垣未毁，姑可安身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158873_comment'></div>必体置邮之规，且殊授粲之费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158873_comment'></div>汉朝典故，自存予告之条；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158873_comment'></div>周卿职司，宜谨守涂之役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158873_comment'></div>岂谓治其家事，即欲异于王人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158873_comment'></div>不遑宁居，驷牡虽非于驿骑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158873_comment'></div>各有攸处，一宿当就于蘧庐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158873_comment'></div>但可容其寝兴，无或给其委积。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1158873_comment'></div>式符唐令，勿乱周行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1158873_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1158873_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1158874' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158874' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158874?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辛捕罪人丁过而不救辞云家有急事救疗<span class='inlineComment2'>（御试判词之十）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1024年3月4日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158874")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158874_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158874'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158874'>逋播未擒，宜同掩袭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158874_comment'></div>弥留待救，安可邅回？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158874_comment'></div>苟或责其容奸，姑合先于拯患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158874_comment'></div>辛事当祗役，职在追逃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158874_comment'></div>力而拘之，饥鹰之效未展；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158874_comment'></div>势不足者，困兽之斗方劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158874_comment'></div>眷彼遵涂之人，式冀执兵之助。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158874_comment'></div>备其越逸，此望惠然肯来；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158874_comment'></div>忧在族姻，彼乃往而不返。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158874_comment'></div>诚或虑其饰诈，谅合原其执心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158874_comment'></div>网恐漏于吞舟，固宜并力；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158874_comment'></div>病方深于易箦，安得忘情？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158874_comment'></div>徒欲诘其图全，未可罪其为己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158874_comment'></div>囚其亡命，虽追捕以攸先；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158874_comment'></div>人各有亲，当患难而自救。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158874_comment'></div>纵云行迈，殊匪坐观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158874_comment'></div>逋逃之党未除，遽令谪我；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158874_comment'></div>瞑眩之求不济，则欲怒谁？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158874_comment'></div>职且异于追胥，罚难加于行路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158874_comment'></div>是则彼有词矣，姑合宥而舍之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1158874_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1158874_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1024&endYear=1024')">1024年3月</a>　应试后游京郊，赋诗。作品：暮春。<div id='poem_99538' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99538' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99538?labeling=true' target='_blank'>暮春</a><span class='authorDate'>（1024年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99538")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_99538_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99538'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99538'>草带全<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>铺翠，花房半坠红。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99538_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99538'>农家<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_99538", 99538, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>榆荚雨</span>，江国鲤鱼风。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99538_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99538'>堤柳绵争扑，山樱火共烘。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99538_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99538'>长安少年客，不信有衰翁。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99538_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_99538'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_99538_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_99538'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_99538_0'>⑴ 原作金，据四库本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_99538_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1024&endYear=1024')">1024年</a>　秋，余靖次女惠卿生。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1024&endYear=1024')">1024年</a>　余靖与黄正、梅鼎臣、王式以及石介、宋咸等进士及第。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='712bcc2ecc0c4012acc4356827224f72_label'><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1033&endYear=1036')">1033-1036年</a>，34-37岁</div><div id='712bcc2ecc0c4012acc4356827224f72' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1033&endYear=1033')">1033年7月</a>　余靖迁秘书丞，掌管典籍，起草文书，忙于公务，甚少应酬，李柬之为馆阁校勘，吕公绰为集贤校理，靖常请教焉。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1033&endYear=1033')">1033年</a>　进京后，应侍御史高弁之请，撰文。作品：祭高待制太君。<div id='poem_1159048' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159048' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159048?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭高待制太君文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1033年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1159048")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159048_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159048'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159048'>惟灵柔明素称，懿恭自饬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159048_comment'></div>惟龆及艾，终始一德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159048_comment'></div>结悦留范，诞光女式。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159048_comment'></div>采蘩承祀，克勤妇职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159048_comment'></div>卜邻教子，遹骏家则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159048_comment'></div>集此圣善，刑于燕翼。<div class='inline'
