id='poem_sentence_5_1159048_comment'></div>金华劝讲，训成忠翊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159048_comment'></div>石窌启封，庸酬慈力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159048_comment'></div>福未盈皆，寿胡不克？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159048_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159048_comment'></div>脩短之策，岂其偕极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159048_comment'></div>吉凶之会，曷无常域？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159048_comment'></div>积善之厚，享年不亿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159048_comment'></div>造物之意，终天罔识。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159048_comment'></div>輴轖启途，铭旌惨色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159048_comment'></div>执绋奠斝，横涕沾轼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159048_comment'></div>言瞻蒿里，莫知冥默。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1159048_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1034&endYear=1034')">1034年</a>　余靖再陈请校勘史籍，被命为校书郎，与王洙并校《汉书》《后汉书》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1034&endYear=1034')">1034年</a>　任校书郎，有诗。作品：咏史。读车千秋传。<div id='poem_99559' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99559' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99559?labeling=true' target='_blank'>咏史</a><span class='authorDate'>（1034年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99559")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_99559_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99559'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99559'>王氏席世宠，垂组驰朱轮。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99559_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99559'>五侯同日拜，四塞黄雾昏。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99559_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99559'>妖气徒勃勃，爵王各终身。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99559_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99559'>富贵若在天，祸淫真谬云。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99559_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_99559'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_99559_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_99569' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99569' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99569?labeling=true' target='_blank'>读车千秋传</a><span class='authorDate'>（1034年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99569")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_99569_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99569'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99569'>汉武好迂诞，江充专险贼。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99569_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99569'>引对大台宫，君臣自相得。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99569_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99569'>世乱谗人胜，奸谋多造饰。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99569_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99569'>元良天下本，掘蛊遭荧惑。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99569_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_99569'>春坊一动摇，前星冷无色。<div id='poem_sentence_4_99569_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_99569'>恐为扶苏诛，掘节储君侧。<div id='poem_sentence_5_99569_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_99569'>屈氂亡庙谋，转战同昏蚀。<div id='poem_sentence_6_99569_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_99569'>臣心无以明，野死不容息。<div id='poem_sentence_7_99569_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_99569'>千秋初奏疏，翩翩举其直。<div id='poem_sentence_8_99569_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_99569'>一言能悟主，破怒成悽恻。<div id='poem_sentence_9_99569_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_99569'>归来及望思，层台起东域。<div id='poem_sentence_10_99569_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_99569'>徒步取卿相，分茅非旧德。<div id='poem_sentence_11_99569_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_99569'>因思壶关老，先此陈奇策。<div id='poem_sentence_12_99569_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_99569'>嘉言若时用，生归当有益。<div id='poem_sentence_13_99569_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_99569'>徙薪不蒙赏，焦头为上客。<div id='poem_sentence_14_99569_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_99569'>汉道用人轻，取笑羞夷狄。<div id='poem_sentence_15_99569_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_99569'></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_99569_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1034&endYear=1034')">1034年</a>　任校书郎，有文。作品：汉论。汉武不能称宗论。<div id='poem_1158953' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158953' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158953?labeling=true' target='_blank'>汉武不宜称宗论</a><span class='authorDate'>（1034年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158953")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158953_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158953'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158953'>创帝基，革天命，济率土于涂炭者，祖之盛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158953_comment'></div>恢声教，同文轨，纳蒸民于富寿者，宗之最。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158953_comment'></div>存则咏其德，没则观其谥，所以叙昭穆于百世之下，配禘郊于群庙之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158953_comment'></div>亲虽尽而不毁者，祖宗之隆也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158953_comment'></div>昔武皇之抚运，绍炎汉之重熙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158953_comment'></div>拓蛮夷之境，则卫青、去病之勋立，而民疲于干戈矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158953_comment'></div>惑神仙之谈，则少翁、乐大之宠崇，而吏烦于祠祀矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158953_comment'></div>悦韩嫣之佞而处以副车，则君臣之位失矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158953_comment'></div>信江充之谮而诛及戾园，则父子之恩绝矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158953_comment'></div>举其大概，何昏如之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158953_comment'></div>至于即世之日，群臣加谥，曾不为灵若厉，而反壮其武，庙为世宗，亏周公之法，败三王之制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158953_comment'></div>当时洪儒硕生如夏侯胜、黄次公议其乐章，遽抵诏狱，不亦甚乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158953_comment'></div>且祖有功，宗有德，若夏之少康，商之太戊、武丁，皆废而复兴，不失旧物，然始谓之宗也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158953_comment'></div>周人自文、武而下，虽德如成康，刑措不用，宣王中兴，姬道再盛，庙在迭毁，亦无异号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158953_comment'></div>暨乎汉室高帝，以英武特起，绁婴刃籍，戴之曰祖，斯固宜矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158953_comment'></div>孝文崇仁义、省刑罚、弭兵革、服节俭，而囹圄空虚，县内太平，庙称太宗，斯又宜矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158953_comment'></div>孝武虽廓地斥境，而亡德及民，不加恶谥，固亦幸矣，尊之为宗，无乃失其正乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158953_comment'></div>或曰：孝武雄才远略，高出百王，西开夜郎之境，东建朝鲜之郡，匈奴徙庭，瓯越请吏，修典礼，向儒学，登封告成，而汉之制度，于是乎备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158953_comment'></div>若如所论，不亦过乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158953_comment'></div>曰：邦土虽辟，兵已黩矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1158953_comment'></div>远夷虽服，民已耗矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1158953_comment'></div>乐府虽盛，雅亦乱矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1158953_comment'></div>泰山虽封，制亦侈矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1158953_comment'></div>文、景之俗，由是而惫，可胜道哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1158953_comment'></div>末年下哀痛之诏，进筦榷之术，有富民之心，而不能得其道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1158953_comment'></div>世谓汉家杂以霸道，愚于武帝观之，曾霸者之不及，代庙弗毁，后嗣何以观乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1158953_comment'></div>西汉称宗者四，而东汉无复区别，至于安、桓，亦有庙号，其失自武帝始，故著论云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1158953_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1034&endYear=1034')">1034年9月</a>　右正言范仲淹因反对废郭妃事，触帝怒，被贬知睦州。九月，靖呈奏。作品：乞纳后元礼稍缓其期。<div id='poem_1158803' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158803' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158803?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞纳后之礼稍缓其期奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（景祐元年九月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158803")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158803_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158803'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158803'>臣伏睹景祐元年八月十五日诏敕：「顷以中闱有亏善道，降处次妃之位，仍从别馆之居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158803_comment'></div>郭氏宜令于外宅居止，更不入内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158803_comment'></div>美人尚氏，令于洞真宫披戴，亦不入内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158803_comment'></div>美人杨氏于别宅安置」者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158803_comment'></div>此盖皇帝陛下广示忧勤，摈去声色，割情断爱，以从典礼，虽尧舜无以加之，天下幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158803_comment'></div>诏旨又云：「长秋之重，阴教是宣，顾厥位以难虚，必惟贤而是择。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158803_comment'></div>将行聘纳，式助烝尝」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158803_comment'></div>臣谨按《春秋》，君举必书，以示后嗣，固当谨重，用存规法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158803_comment'></div>切以庄献明肃皇太后预闻朝政，托在母仪，保佑圣躬，安固宗社，钦奉慈旨，备尽孝诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158803_comment'></div>先太后登遐方踰祥练，陛下虽行易月之制，而心丧未除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158803_comment'></div>古者三年之丧，自天子达于庶人，其礼一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158803_comment'></div>所有纳后之礼，乞候先太后服纪阕日，然后审选世阀，登进贤淑，兴理内教，统领六宫，必允众望，始议册立，不宜频有改易，以骇四方，乃陛下孝治天下之本也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158803_comment'></div>昔者鲁文公居丧纳币以娶夫人，《春秋》非之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158803_comment'></div>《公羊传》曰：「娶在三年之外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158803_comment'></div>此何讥尔？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158803_comment'></div>曰：三年之内，不图婚也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158803_comment'></div>是皆孔子书之，以为世法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158803_comment'></div>伏望陛下谨兹举措，以示后代，稍缓其期，则臣缱绻之愿也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1158803_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1158803'><span class='label'>按：</span>《余襄公奏议》卷上，广东丛书本。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1158803_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1034&endYear=1034')">1034年</a>　三子叔英生，职方司事董赟来贺，有诗。作品：和董职方贺诞子诗。<div id='poem_99484' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99484' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99484?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和董职方见贺诞子诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（1034年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99484")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_99484_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99484'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99484'>天幸依仁守列藩，佳篇为贶荷谦尊。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99484_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99484'>固惭彝鼎无勋阀，且喜桑弧有子孙。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99484_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99484'>岂比芳兰庭下秀，预知苦李道傍繁。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99484_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99484'>日临庶狱虞阴谴，敢望高开纳驷门。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99484_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_99484'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_99484_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1034&endYear=1034')">1034年</a>　应右侍禁卞世长之请为其父母归葬兴仁府，撰文。舍人卞楚材过府谢之。作品：宋故礼宾副使知邵州卞府君墓志铭。<div id='poem_1159031' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159031' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159031?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宋故礼宾副使知邵州卞府君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1034年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1159031")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159031_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159031'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159031'>公讳日华，字某，曹州冤句人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159031_comment'></div>昔武王既克商，崇树亲亲，藩屏周室，母弟振铎，建邦于曹，诗存《国风》，谱在史简。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159031_comment'></div>别子之为大夫者，因食采之邑，命为卞氏，仲尼称卞庄子之勇，盖曹大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159031_comment'></div>魏晋已降，粹、壸世继清德，兄弟六龙并登宰府，乡邦坟垄，至今存焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159031_comment'></div>苏峻之难，壸为航东都督，王师不利，父子俱殒，义士嘉叹，国书褒美，以为忠孝之道，萃于一门，英风凛然，千古所仰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159031_comment'></div>曾祖讳某，举进士不第，终于家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159031_comment'></div>祖讳某，用卜河南之术以丰其才，羊畜蹄叫满野，而不尚豪汰，淡于荣味，卒以素风自乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159031_comment'></div>考讳某，专经成名，以廉谨称，丞相太师吕公蒙正、丞相太尉王公旦咸加慰荐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159031_comment'></div>历潭州决曹掾，卒官，累赠比部员外郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159031_comment'></div>公幼孤，倜傥有奇节，初修进士业，众推强记，以善诗著名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159031_comment'></div>既而曰：「吾母戴白而恃吾养，岂宜博习以自私于名？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159031_comment'></div>当就速成之术，冀得禄以为亲荣耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159031_comment'></div>乃夙宵砥砺，专诵《春秋》经传数十万言，果以明年一举登第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159031_comment'></div>解褐，除陕州平陆主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159031_comment'></div>惟陕郊虽名近辅，而介在崤渑之间，被山带河，盗贼据为囊橐，负甲持矛以剽掠为业者，岁常有之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159031_comment'></div>公到官，权总尉事，境上强寇，朝廷以名捕者十三辈，于是训练爪牙，多设筹略，悉擒之亡噍类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159031_comment'></div>府以状闻，太宗览奏大怿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159031_comment'></div>时广西溪洞反侧始安，方择守以绥之，即日降旨，急召赴阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159031_comment'></div>廷见之日，德音奖劝，擢授大理评事、知宾州军州事，即淳化四年也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159031_comment'></div>俄而交趾犯境，专诏陈公尧叟调度兵食，安抚南鄙，奏公治绩尤著，有诏特记姓名，别听任使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159031_comment'></div>居无何，永熙升遐，真皇登极，例进秩光禄丞，权开封府掾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159031_comment'></div>寻迁三门发运判官，将漕最。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159031_comment'></div>进丞大理，仍领漕事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159031_comment'></div>咸平三年，以北虏未宾，诏文臣有方略者，许两府荐名，或投牒自举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159031_comment'></div>公自计理效，恐见推择，若王命临门，则不得以亲为先事陈之，遂表乞解官侍养，朝旨未允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159031_comment'></div>太夫人果即世，居丧不胜衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159031_comment'></div>景德二年服阙，参政尚书赵公昌言援前诏，举公右职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1159031_comment'></div>上使人问曰：「朕下诏急人时不自进，若后之矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1159031_comment'></div>公对曰：「昔之不敢临桴鼓，以亲存也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1159031_comment'></div>今母亡能葬，得以捐躯报国，臣无所让」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1159031_comment'></div>上嘉之，遂除内殿崇班、知博州，恩赐加等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1159031_comment'></div>三年，河东用兵，移忻州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1159031_comment'></div>宿弊未刬，力欲绳政，遂为奸人中伤，左授考城兵马都监。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1159031_comment'></div>明年，徙太康。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1159031_comment'></div>天子东封之年，改内殿承制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1159031_comment'></div>当是时，太尉马公知节知枢密院事，屡称其材，上亦记之，遂授礼宾副使、知邵州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1159031_comment'></div>以大中祥符五年十二月壬辰终于官舍，享年五十二，州民为之罢市而行哭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1159031_comment'></div>公性端方，守名节，敦信重义，孝爱尤笃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1159031_comment'></div>自筮仕至于投笔，率以亲为进退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1159031_comment'></div>家之积粟，周赡族姻，而俸禄尽于宾客，捐馆之日，室无羡资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1159031_comment'></div>两朝遇知己之主，不克寿而展其才，可嗟也已！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1159031_comment'></div>公之兄楚材，今为春宫舍人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1159031_comment'></div>弟日就，举进士，景祐初释褐，未官而卒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1159031_comment'></div>季弟日新，亦举进士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1159031_comment'></div>公娶某氏，封某县君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1159031_comment'></div>生一男一女，男世长，右侍禁，恪勤以涖官，饬理以检身，咸有所称，以守先训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1159031_comment'></div>孙二人尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1159031_comment'></div>初，公之丧也，侍禁君羁贯，既扶服，以柩归，而厝于郡郛，今乃卜以某年某月，襄事于大茔，礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1159031_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1159031_comment'></div>卜其兆宅而安其体魄，又能论撰懿美以为子孙识，皆孝之大者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1159031_comment'></div>葬而有铭，古也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1159031_comment'></div>乃铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_51_1159031'>曹大侯邦，卞乃公族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1159031_comment'></div>赋邑命氏，并蒙其福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1159031_comment'></div>他姓奠居，数世则迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1159031_comment'></div>卞守本国，其绍绵绵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1159031_comment'></div>公之翼翼，生子积德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1159031_comment'></div>杰然起家，实惟茂识。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1159031_comment'></div>一尉之卑，遽为帝知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1159031_comment'></div>抱器遭时，当代所稀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1159031_comment'></div>亲存守常，以养其志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1159031_comment'></div>亲亡激节，有死不避。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1159031_comment'></div>进退之仪，必本于义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1159031_comment'></div>行道固难，卒多留滞，禀命不融，半途而陨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1159031_comment'></div>清名有馀，高才未尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1159031_comment'></div>九原苍苍，体魄所藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1159031_comment'></div>子孙不忘，以嗣其光。</div><div id='poem_sentence_65_1159031_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1034&endYear=1034')">1034年</a>　年初，应越东节度推官毛洵之请，为其父毛应佺作铭。作品：宋故国子博士通判太平州毛君墓志。<div id='poem_1159037' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159037' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159037?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宋故国子博士通判太平州毛君墓铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1034年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1159037")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159037_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159037'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159037'>公讳应佺，字子贞，其先荥阳人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159037_comment'></div>昔者武王剪商而造周，以介弟毛伯既亲且贤，乃裂地而爵之，与康叔居关东为诸侯，与聃季入寰内为卿士，胙土得姓，善善相继。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159037_comment'></div>其后领袖儒林、丹青史笔者，代有之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159037_comment'></div>玠仕魏为尚书仆射，以清公廉节自任，后嗣仰之，为万世法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159037_comment'></div>渡江而后，晋者世吏二千石，遂为江南著姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159037_comment'></div>今占籍于庐陵之吉水焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159037_comment'></div>曾祖讳让，祖讳休，仕南唐为侍御史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159037_comment'></div>烈考讳澄，赠大理寺评事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159037_comment'></div>妣高氏，赠南昌县太君，繇公之请也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159037_comment'></div>僖皇东迁，朱梁篡夺，版荡幅裂，称尊号者非一姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159037_comment'></div>李氏阻江为国，自绍唐统，御史府君忠于所奉，遂为天子之外臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159037_comment'></div>于时庐陵大郡，毛为右族，官于霸朝，卒以法进丞寺署、坐郡曹者，咸绰绰有名，国人韪之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159037_comment'></div>御史府君藏书数千卷，辟田数百顷，尝与人曰：「欲仕者可以识废兴，欲隐者可以实仓廪，吾于子孙计足矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159037_comment'></div>乃玉笥之阳，有终焉之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159037_comment'></div>公幼丧所天，刻意自立，砥名励行，文为闻人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159037_comment'></div>真宗皇帝得祥符之始年举进士，御前解褐，授杭州临安尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159037_comment'></div>负海名邦，古称都会，探丸仇吏，人或轻扬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159037_comment'></div>公广为方略，多设耳目，罻罗所得，囊橐皆空，人被其仁，至今称诵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159037_comment'></div>选部调补江陵府司理参军，以情察狱，宽而能断，所经讯谳，民自不冤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159037_comment'></div>秩满，迁万州军事推官，坐棠缺守，权董郡事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159037_comment'></div>束缚奸吏，按摩疲人，威凌秋霜，惠温冬日，荐绅立朝之士，状其绩用闻于廷者十一人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159037_comment'></div>归朝，擢授大理寺丞、知筠州高安县，平心御物，曲直立分，箕歛尽除，嚚讼自止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159037_comment'></div>期年，移知窦州军州事，转太子中舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159037_comment'></div>郡在合浦之东千里而近，地多珠、贝、犀、象、沉檀之产，前之剖符者，往往舳舻衔尾，竭其土物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159037_comment'></div>公北归之日，尽室一舟，无铢锱南国之货。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159037_comment'></div>入朝，授殿中丞、国子博士，历通判虔、筠、太平等军州事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159037_comment'></div>公性宽厚，守撝损，当官不示圭角，以沽赫赫之誉，所去民皆思之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1159037_comment'></div>信爱朋友，未尝斥人之非，故朝士多其长者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1159037_comment'></div>监郡之职，与刺史权均而势逼，固禄位者率以将迎守意，临事不自可否，屏气低首，趋府如幕吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1159037_comment'></div>吏持案牍立前，山叠波委，搦管署纸尾，不敢议其是非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1159037_comment'></div>及狷者为之，则刚而犯上，相持短长，缺士大夫之行者多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1159037_comment'></div>公处以中和，不茹不吐，三赞郡事，人亡间言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1159037_comment'></div>自筠之移姑孰也，抗遗荣之志，将归旧隐，乃白奏奉身而请老焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1159037_comment'></div>朝命以本官致仕，一子授太庙斋郎，以美其冥冥之节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1159037_comment'></div>诏未下，不幸属疾，以明道二年三月丁丑，考终命于当涂之官署，享年六十有七。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1159037_comment'></div>夫人高氏，封某县君，夙奉姆教，恪修妇式，婉容淑范，为闺房之秀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1159037_comment'></div>府君列朝著理郡务，遗清白于子孙者，夫人实有内助焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1159037_comment'></div>公即世既逾月，帷堂哭昼，未亡之叹方深；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1159037_comment'></div>同穴感义，溘至之期共尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1159037_comment'></div>以某月日终于池阳舟次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1159037_comment'></div>越明年某月日，合而祔之于某原，礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1159037_comment'></div>三子：长曰渐，太室斋郎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1159037_comment'></div>次曰溥，以毁卒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1159037_comment'></div>次曰洵，擢进士第，调判入四等，授越东节度推官、知宣城县事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1159037_comment'></div>三女：长适进士陈敏中，次适进士习遵路，次适进士艾琚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1159037_comment'></div>六孙：伯奋、伯达、伯玉，馀尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1159037_comment'></div>将葬，洵以状来乞铭，而掩诸幽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1159037_comment'></div>乃铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_47_1159037'>周之懿亲，魏之名臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1159037_comment'></div>越有裔孙，生兹德门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1159037_comment'></div>行为士则，才为世贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1159037_comment'></div>所治七官，遗爱存焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1159037_comment'></div>身羁绂绶，志在林泉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1159037_comment'></div>公既知止，时方引年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1159037_comment'></div>乞身西归，朝恩霈然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1159037_comment'></div>未被出綍，俄惊逝川。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1159037_comment'></div>哀陨庭兰，悲摧无鸾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1159037_comment'></div>灵轮筮宅，相随九原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1159037_comment'></div>令嗣执丧，戚容栾栾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1159037_comment'></div>泣状遗绩，乞铭𡑞埏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1159037_comment'></div>呜呼荥阳，府君之阡。</div><div id='poem_sentence_59_1159037_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1034&endYear=1034')">1034年</a>　年初，应越东节度推官毛洵之请，为其兄毛溥作铭。作品：荥阳毛君墓志铭。<div id='poem_1159038' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159038' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159038?labeling=true' target='_blank'>荥阳毛君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（明道二年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1159038")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159038_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159038'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159038'>君讳溥，字之祖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159038_comment'></div>于周为姬姓，文王之子国于毛，子孙以国为氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159038_comment'></div>春秋之际，世为王卿士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159038_comment'></div>在汉时，苌及亨皆为《鲁诗》，各以其家名学，儒者至今宗之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159038_comment'></div>晋永嘉之乱，士族南徙，宝有战功，为庐江守，名著竹帛，而毛宗益兴在南夏矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159038_comment'></div>宋齐而降，代有瑰杰，家牒阙坠，不复殚纪，今为吉州吉水人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159038_comment'></div>大王父讳某，侍御史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159038_comment'></div>王父讳某，赠大理评事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159038_comment'></div>考讳某，国子博士，终于姑孰同守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159038_comment'></div>以文学起家，所理七官皆著治效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159038_comment'></div>闺门肃肃，若居宫庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159038_comment'></div>妣曰高氏，封寿春县君，奉舅姑以礼，训诸子以严，里闬称之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159038_comment'></div>姑孰府君三子：伯曰渐，季曰洵，君即中子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159038_comment'></div>渐，太室斋郎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159038_comment'></div>洵，镇东府从事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159038_comment'></div>君幼聪悟，博览群籍及子史百家之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159038_comment'></div>与人交，不茍合，孝谨友爱，发于天性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159038_comment'></div>自从事君未仕时，君已能为进士业矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159038_comment'></div>吉于江西治最剧，其士人倍他郡，而岁贡俊选，偪以限人之制，褒博臂凑，歌《鹿鸣》而送之，十不取一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159038_comment'></div>衣冠家有令子弟，雁行而进求乡先生之荐者，郡中正往往畏钳忌之口，不克偕举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159038_comment'></div>从事君既冠，则与君并在宾兴籍中，君曰：「吾才不如季，脱不幸而顺吾长，以我先举，则为夺吾季之名也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159038_comment'></div>让不乞试，退而脩家人产业，季果得荐取太常第，邦人义之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159038_comment'></div>从事君既上第，君始有仕进之意，行益淳，学益勤，声名流四方，而禄未及之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159038_comment'></div>以明道二年五月十六日卒，享年三十有八。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159038_comment'></div>初，姑孰府君属疾，君尝药而后进，不去冠带者三月，昼夜不寐，两目尽疮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159038_comment'></div>府君弃世未逾月，母夫人寿春君亦亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159038_comment'></div>君哀号恸绝，勺饮不入口，并侍两丧，全柩归葬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1159038_comment'></div>途次钟陵，柴毁越制，终于舟中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1159038_comment'></div>其弟洵扶护其父、母、兄及己之妻之丧以归，哀感行路，以某月日葬于某府君之茔次，礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1159038_comment'></div>君娶刘氏，柔嘉之德，冠于族姻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1159038_comment'></div>子男三人：长曰伯奋，始志于学，馀尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1159038_comment'></div>女二人，皆未笄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1159038_comment'></div>于戏！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1159038_comment'></div>君之行可以激薄俗、窒奔竞，宜寿而贵者，乃以荼毒灭性，不享永年，可哀也哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1159038_comment'></div>故为之铭，铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_34_1159038'>生于德门，言淳行实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1159038_comment'></div>让弟以仕，哭父而没。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1159038_comment'></div>义而孝兮，胡不终吉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1159038_comment'></div>吁嗟毛君，居此窀窟。</div><div id='poem_sentence_37_1159038_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1034&endYear=1034')">1034年</a>　年末，又接毛溥之长子毛伯奋函告，其叔毛洵病故，余靖哀极又为撰铭。作品：宋故镇东军节度推官毛君墓志铭。<div id='poem_1159039' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159039' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159039?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宋故镇东军节度推官毛君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（景祐二年九月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1159039")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159039_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159039'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159039'>景祐元年十一月戊辰，故镇东军从事毛君卒于家，明年九月壬午，葬于庐陵吉水之仁寿乡南华原先府君之茔次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159039_comment'></div>君之兄遣使持书走京师，谓其友余某曰：「渐之弟才未尽施，抱恨入土，恐其名之易漫灭也，请铭而久之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159039_comment'></div>某于君游最厚，熟其行，故得书而无让焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159039_comment'></div>君讳洵，字子仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159039_comment'></div>世居吉水，业儒，为冠族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159039_comment'></div>曾祖讳休，侍御史；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159039_comment'></div>祖讳澄，赠大理评事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159039_comment'></div>考讳应佺，国子博士；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159039_comment'></div>母曰寿春县君高氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159039_comment'></div>君器度方正，动自修尚，幼精敏，能属辞，及冠，举进士，试秘书省校书郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159039_comment'></div>性笃于孝，视荣利泊如也，凡守四官，再以亲解。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159039_comment'></div>初，补抚州司法参军，先府君适知窦州，窦在南海南千里，遣人问起居者死于道，信不得通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159039_comment'></div>君喟然叹曰：「恶能以担石禄割亲之爱，经时阒然，不知息耗而自安」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159039_comment'></div>乃因郡邮言状，不待报，弃官去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159039_comment'></div>暨府君归朝，君再调洪之新建簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159039_comment'></div>以书判拔萃，天子御便殿试之，所对入等，改试大理评事、迁镇东军节度推官、知宣州宣城县事，政有绳墨，民咸宜之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159039_comment'></div>未逾岁，江淮制置使器其能，奏监扬州榷盐仓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159039_comment'></div>诏既下，留侍亲疾，不就职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159039_comment'></div>执药调膳，尝而后进，积三月不之寝室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159039_comment'></div>亡何，府君暨母夫人相继卒，君与兄渐奉丧归葬，持畚荷土，手胝面黔，亲友不能识。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159039_comment'></div>茔外松柏，皆所自树，遂结庐墓所而居之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159039_comment'></div>居忧凡二十一月，朝夕哭踊如初丧之仪，所食才脱粟，不加姜桂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159039_comment'></div>同闬诸生数十人日凑庐旁，执弟子之礼，请君敷辩经义，君对之流涕，未尝言文庐中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159039_comment'></div>非号泣时，则写佛书、读丧礼而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159039_comment'></div>自庐次得疾，归家数日卒，享年三十二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159039_comment'></div>郡以孝行闻，诏赐其家粟帛百以旌显之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159039_comment'></div>君二昆：伯曰渐，太庙斋郎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1159039_comment'></div>仲曰溥，先以毁卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1159039_comment'></div>夫人生一男一女，皆夭夫人前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1159039_comment'></div>君卒别葬，不祔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1159039_comment'></div>其铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_1159039'>文行俱，家世儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1159039_comment'></div>力孝弟，恬进趋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1159039_comment'></div>再弃官，为亲谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1159039_comment'></div>失怙恃，返丘墟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1159039_comment'></div>饭脱粟，居倚庐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1159039_comment'></div>不终丧，陨厥躯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1159039_comment'></div>位未充，材有馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1159039_comment'></div>祔无妇，哭无孤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1159039_comment'></div>善罔报，天何如。</div><div id='poem_sentence_38_1159039_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1035&endYear=1035')">1035年</a>　集中精力校刊史书，有奏。作品：上校正汉书。<div id='poem_1158805' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158805' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158805?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上校正汉书奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（景祐二年三月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158805")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158805_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158805'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158805'>案颜师古《叙例》云：班固《汉书》旧无注解，唯服虔、应劭等各著音义，自名其家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158805_comment'></div>至西晋晋灼集为一部，凡十四卷，又颇以意增益，时辨二家当否，号曰《汉书集注》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158805_comment'></div>永嘉之乱，此书不至江左。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158805_comment'></div>有臣瓒者，莫知氏族，考其时代，亦在晋初，又总集诸家音义，稍以己见续厕其末，掎摭前说，多引汲冢《竹书》，凡二十四卷，分为两帙，凡称《集解》、《音义》，即其书也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158805_comment'></div>蔡谟全取此书，散入众篇，自是以来，始有注本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158805_comment'></div>至唐太宗时，皇太子承乾命颜师古更加以刊正，删繁补略，裁以己说，儒者服其详博，遂成一家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158805_comment'></div>总先儒注解名姓可见者二十有五人，而爵里年代史阙载者殆半。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158805_comment'></div>考其附著及旧说所承注释源流，名爵年次，谨条件以闻，望行刊于本书之末，庶令学者启卷具知。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1158805'></div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1158805_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1035&endYear=1035')">1035年</a>　汇集《汉书刊误》三十卷，与校正后的《汉书》《后汉书》同刊印，靖因擢为集贤校理，有谢启。作品：谢帖职启。<div id='poem_1158918' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158918' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158918?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢帖职启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1035年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158918")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158918_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158918'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158918'>右，某启：伏奉敕命，蒙恩充前件职者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158918_comment'></div>天奖曲成，宠典过厚，内省鄙薄，荣惧交至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158918_comment'></div>伏念某本惟庸浅，生在遐陬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158918_comment'></div>弱岁就学，则经无师范；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158918_comment'></div>长年力行，而才非老成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158918_comment'></div>常构霿而自知，加钻励而忘倦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158918_comment'></div>且以有道之士，樵夫笑其诙谐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158918_comment'></div>安平之时，君子耻乎贫贱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158918_comment'></div>期慷慨以有立，乃徒步而西游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158918_comment'></div>属皇德休明，崇尚儒术，广求俊秀，延及幽陋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158918_comment'></div>谨乡遂之举，旅登仕途；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158918_comment'></div>择群萃之材，首膺嘉命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158918_comment'></div>越在官次，固亡治声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158918_comment'></div>徒稽吏资，屡进荣秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158918_comment'></div>间者以迁、固旧学，贯穿博乎群书；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158918_comment'></div>范、谢所录，撰述推其良史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158918_comment'></div>向在先代，摹于上庠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158918_comment'></div>虽千金置市，淮南莫之能改；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158918_comment'></div>而五经在黉，卢生得以裁定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158918_comment'></div>咨于前训，释以所闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1158918_comment'></div>归赴未央之朝，杂上公车之奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1158918_comment'></div>敢期震瞩，择用狂言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1158918_comment'></div>不遗一介之善，以广同文之化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1158918_comment'></div>石渠平议，总以钜儒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1158918_comment'></div>中秘旧藏，采其通说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1158918_comment'></div>再易岁月，仅终缉缀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1158918_comment'></div>纰缪毕去，固周于参检；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1158918_comment'></div>蠹文未辨，犹示于传疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1158918_comment'></div>重纡绨几之观，颇愧云台之议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1158918_comment'></div>岂谓荐言屡上，睿泽猥加，录其微勤，升之华贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1158918_comment'></div>伏惟昭文仆射相公，秉惠和之德，辅钦明之君，宣百王未举之政，扶万世不倾之业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1158918_comment'></div>裁成庶务，明昭百辟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1158918_comment'></div>薪槱克充于用，白黑不逃其形。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1158918_comment'></div>而况承明之庭，汉儒列于侍从；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1158918_comment'></div>东璧之府，唐制专乎刊脩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1158918_comment'></div>所宜推择俊髦，收集英乂，博求济理之具，以永无穷之闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1158918_comment'></div>必若望实外著，器识兼远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1158918_comment'></div>属词典赡，知礼乐而能述；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1158918_comment'></div>立行端方，敦名教而为乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1158918_comment'></div>茍中兹选，则惟其人，夫何鲰生，玷是荣命？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1158918_comment'></div>傥以稽合同异，绪正舛忤，此而可褒，谓之必称，则蔡邕壁池之本，镌刻以为劳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1158918_comment'></div>郑默兰台之经，嘉叹而尤著，未闻前世，推以厚恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1158918_comment'></div>揆兹非次之荣，迥出常均之外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1158918_comment'></div>盖由熙宁在运，明哲主谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1158918_comment'></div>譬阳春之和，土靡硗埆，大明之照，物无幽隐，用致矿顽，亦被光渥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1158918_comment'></div>敢不勤服素履，祗率攸闻，黄卷之中，稍研治体，一官之守，无隳国经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1158918_comment'></div>庶答己知，以逃群谤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1158918_comment'></div>某无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_47_1158918_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1035&endYear=1035')">1035年</a>　继续校勘《史记》，后汇集三史校勘成果，着手写《三史勘误》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1035&endYear=1035')">1035年</a>　任集贤校理，有史论。作品：尧舜非谥论。秦论。正瑞论。姚畴论。<div id='poem_1158952' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158952' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158952?labeling=true' target='_blank'>尧舜非谥论</a><span class='authorDate'>（1035年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158952")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158952_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158952'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158952'>迹骤五帝，德规百王者，有尧、舜焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158952_comment'></div>言常道，尼父首之于《书》；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158952_comment'></div>大一统，马迁列之为《纪》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158952_comment'></div>释者云：尧、舜，谥也，翼善传圣曰尧，仁圣盛明曰舜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158952_comment'></div>后之学者，罔不宗焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158952_comment'></div>愚尝考世系之端，辨质文之变，颇疑是说，请试明之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158952_comment'></div>粤自邃古，圣人迭兴，真淳乍散，制度未备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158952_comment'></div>尊庐、赫胥以前，未有氏姓，皆以教民之事而名之，钻燧改火则曰燧人，穴处巢居则曰有巢是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158952_comment'></div>迨及三皇，颇推五胜，乘火德者曰炎帝，应土运者曰黄帝，少昊、金天，亦袭其故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158952_comment'></div>迭观兴废，渐有兵战。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158952_comment'></div>自颛顼以来，天下之号，则因其名，颛顼与喾，则其名也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158952_comment'></div>帝挚，帝尧、帝舜，亦其名也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158952_comment'></div>以国言之，则颛顼称高阳氏，帝喾称高辛氏，帝尧称陶唐氏，帝舜称有虞氏，皆以所兴之地为国号也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158952_comment'></div>帝挚非改姓易代之主，故不称氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158952_comment'></div>以名言之，则颛顼、喾、挚、尧、舜皆名也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158952_comment'></div>顼，正也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158952_comment'></div>喾，极也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158952_comment'></div>挚，大也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158952_comment'></div>尧，高也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158952_comment'></div>舜，华也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1158952_comment'></div>古虽敦朴，知以美字为称，固不疑矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1158952_comment'></div>夫《谥法》者，著于周公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1158952_comment'></div>盖三代之际，世有僻王，嗜音酣酒者有之，荒禽冒色者有之，饰非愎谏者有之，剖忠害贤者有之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1158952_comment'></div>欲使闻美号而知劝，见恶谥而思惧，垂易名之典，为观行之则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1158952_comment'></div>此周公之制也，岂以周制而逆观尧、舜之世耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1158952_comment'></div>且尧之《典》曰：「有鳏在下曰虞」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1158952_comment'></div>舜当群臣举善之初，釐降试难之善未显，宾门纳麓之功未著，安有对万乘而不称其名，在侧陋而先定其谥哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1158952_comment'></div>斯固知其不然也明矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1158952_comment'></div>释者又云：受禅成功曰禹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1158952_comment'></div>岂舜受尧禅而不能成功乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1158952_comment'></div>夏商之王，以名为号者多矣，仲康、太甲之类是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1158952_comment'></div>禹之保邦，莫非尧、舜之制，而加以繁文缛礼，乌有舍诫劝而就质略哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1158952_comment'></div>若以夏道尚质，则禹非夏耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1158952_comment'></div>愚谓周公之著《谥法》也，特取尧、舜、禹、汤之名以为训解，将后之下武守文者，慕其名而袭其行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1158952_comment'></div>周人以讳事神，讳其名而称其谥者，周道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1158952_comment'></div>谥兴于周，为得弥文之实。</div><div id='poem_sentence_35_1158952_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1158958' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158958' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158958?labeling=true' target='_blank'>正瑞论</a><span class='authorDate'>（1035年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158958")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158958_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158958'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158958'>夫上古明王，言为天下法，动为后世则，犹恐怠惰，故立左右史以规之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158958_comment'></div>是则史之设，所以谨言行于一人，正褒贬于千古，不独纪岁月、辨赴告而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158958_comment'></div>三皇《坟》、五帝《典》，记言之史也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158958_comment'></div>楚《梼杌》、鲁《春秋》，记事之史也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158958_comment'></div>训诰誓命之词，得失存亡之迹，发简可见，未闻祥瑞之言焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158958_comment'></div>迨于两汉，则有赤芝、白雁、醴泉、甘露、卿云、宝鼎之应，岂古史阔略而后史该备乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158958_comment'></div>盖有司失为史之本意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158958_comment'></div>敢谓国之兴也，在乎德，不在乎瑞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158958_comment'></div>国之亡也，在乎乱，不在乎妖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158958_comment'></div>故尧以敦九族、和万邦而兴，舜以举十六相、去四凶则又兴，禹以平水土兴，汤以行仁政兴，周人以积行累德兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158958_comment'></div>夫是者，虽无祥瑞，可不谓圣且治乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158958_comment'></div>癸以侈奢亡，辛以暴虐亡，厉王以聚歛亡，幽王以女色亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158958_comment'></div>夫是者，虽无妖怪，可不谓昏且乱乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158958_comment'></div>桑谷生朝，高宗复商；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158958_comment'></div>荧惑守心，景公安宋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158958_comment'></div>此则明君在上，妖不为害矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158958_comment'></div>鲁获麒麟，哀公出奔；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158958_comment'></div>汉鸣凤凰，平帝失国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158958_comment'></div>此则闇主在上，瑞不为美矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158958_comment'></div>仲尼笔削《春秋》，书日食地震、山隤星陨、蝝生鹢飞之变者，非广乎异闻也，盖欲人君责躬修德，见灾思惧，而臻于治也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1158958_comment'></div>特于篇末，因麟之无应，以明述作之意耳，其他瑞则无闻焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1158958_comment'></div>鹤舞晋庭，龙见洧水，不由德至，斥而弗叙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1158958_comment'></div>若是之比，求名而亡，则圣人微旨可见矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1158958_comment'></div>子长、孟坚，推论怪谍，其启国也，以斩蛇大泽为受命之符，而英雄之略弃矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1158958_comment'></div>其定制度也，以龙见成纪为易服之感，而古人之象隳矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1158958_comment'></div>及乎蔚宗，患其失实，则云某郡上言某瑞，以示微意，与其疑而列之，曷若正而削之之为愈乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1158958_comment'></div>今之郡县，时报祥瑞，以为纪事之瑞，愚谓非良直之法也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1158958_comment'></div>必若德施于民，效易其俗，赏不僭，刑不滥，则四灵为畜，日游于君之宫沼郊薮矣，又何用索异传怪，惑天下之耳目哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1158958_comment'></div>苟荐绅者默而不言，则示之后嗣，得无惧乎？</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1158958_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1158959' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158959' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158959?labeling=true' target='_blank'>姚畴论</a><span class='authorDate'>（1035年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158959")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158959_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158959'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158959'>古者天子之立史官也，不独纪岁月远近，辨朝会同异而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158959_comment'></div>盖以王者居亿兆之上，喜似阳春，怒如雷霆，予夺生杀，无不从也，故立史以谨其言动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158959_comment'></div>动则左史书之，言则右史书之，以示后嗣，欲其畏后世之名而不敢过举者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158959_comment'></div>窃见两汉而下，有唐制度最为详备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158959_comment'></div>而史官废置，未臻大中，敢试论之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158959_comment'></div>唐之修史，其术有二：武德故事，小省之官更直近陛，执笔对仗，随而撰录，书之方册，谓之「起居注」；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158959_comment'></div>姚畴建议秉钧之臣吁谟便殿，嘉猷善经，退必编次，送之史馆，谓之「时政记」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158959_comment'></div>于是《周官》六史之职不复甄叙矣，累朝著作之局不复刊修矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158959_comment'></div>畴议既行，而起居之官立于外朝，仗退之后，迹便疏远，虽延英数刻之对，圣人有泣辜解网之言，应机成务之谋，不可得而闻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158959_comment'></div>若非宰臣撰述，则军国政要，何由知之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158959_comment'></div>繇是而言，有不可者三焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158959_comment'></div>古者帝王不得见当代之史，何则？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158959_comment'></div>史之为书，不隐恶，不虚美，谓之实录。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158959_comment'></div>史而可见，则其臣不敢以实书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158959_comment'></div>书而不实，为己诬矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158959_comment'></div>实而不讳，为己戮矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158959_comment'></div>不得见史者，以此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158959_comment'></div>宰臣监修，是使自司其过者也，其不可者一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158959_comment'></div>昔者成王尚幼，与唐叔戏剪桐叶而与之曰：「以是封汝」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158959_comment'></div>明日，太史上舆地图请封唐叔，自是成王终身无戏言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1158959_comment'></div>夫是则史官常在左右也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1158959_comment'></div>今史臣随仗出入，则是用史臣于顷刻之间耳，戏言过行，尚奚史之畏哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1158959_comment'></div>其不可者二也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1158959_comment'></div>古者大臣不掌注记，故董狐得以直笔于晋，南史氏得以执简于齐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1158959_comment'></div>设有史官，外朝既罢，则目不见帝王之容，耳不闻帝王之言，近臣奏对，孰邪孰正，孰谀孰诤，咸莫之辨也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1158959_comment'></div>用他人注记为己之笔削，夫是则史官失职，莫甚如此，其不可者三也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1158959_comment'></div>语曰：「使廉士守藏，不如扃钥之固也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1158959_comment'></div>使义士分财，不如投钩之平也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1158959_comment'></div>何则？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1158959_comment'></div>有情之与无情也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1158959_comment'></div>夫以广渊之谋，居翊亮之位，缉熙庶绩，裁成万机，而复代史臣撰述，固亦劳矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1158959_comment'></div>向使房、杜、姚、宋击毂轨而自序策略，人犹疑之，脱不幸而有元载、卢杞当其任，则安所取信哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1158959_comment'></div>太宗文皇帝贞观中所论政体，皆可冠冕古今，粉泽王度，著在方册，昭昭然者，史臣得侍于内朝故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1158959_comment'></div>姚畴虽知注记之详，未知先王立史之意，一失其源而莫之敢议，惜哉！</div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1158959_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1035&endYear=1035')">1035年</a>　任集贤校理，有酬赠王沿之作。作品：送峡州推官。<div id='poem_99499' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99499' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99499?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送峡州推官</a><span class='authorDate'>（1035年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99499")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_99499_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99499'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99499'>决科雠汉策，佐郡得荆关。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99499_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99499'>地胜诗锋锐，兵销檄笔闲。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99499_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99499'>路岐高鸟外，城郭白云间。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99499_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99499'>婉画应馀刃，何人荐祢还。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99499_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_99499'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_99499_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1035&endYear=1035')">1035年</a>　任集贤校理，有酬赠杨日严之作。作品：送杨学士益州路转运。<div id='poem_99496' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99496' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99496?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送杨学士益州路转运</a><span class='authorDate'>（1035年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99496")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_99496_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99496'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99496'>芝函新命直仙蓬，又见岷山叱驭忠。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99496_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99496'>玉佩晓班辞日下，水牛秋粟转褒中。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99496_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99496'>花时井邑蚕丛富，徼外人家栈道通。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99496_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99496'>奇技刺文频诏约，此行应更变民风。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99496_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_99496'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_99496_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1035&endYear=1035')">1035年</a>　任集贤校理，有酬赠凌浩之作。作品：送凌屯田知和州。<div id='poem_99501' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99501' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99501?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送凌屯田知和州</a><span class='authorDate'>（1035年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99501")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_99501_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99501'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99501'>粉署仙郎守一麾，都门别岸柳依依。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99501_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99501'>定知春雨随车至，且喜秋风破浪归。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99501_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99501'>仁政便当闻虎渡，治声犹在隔牛矶<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：君前宰芜湖县。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99501_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99501'>侬今亦恳怀章请，假道尚应鲈正肥。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99501_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_99501'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_99501_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1036&endYear=1036')">1036年</a>　春，同僚施昌言以屯田郎中知太平州，靖赠诗。作品：送施屯田知太平州。<div id='poem_99500' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99500' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99500?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送施屯田知太平州</a><span class='authorDate'>（1036年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99500")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_99500_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99500'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99500'>天阁汉郎居，新荣刻兔符。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99500_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99500'>趋曹兰在握，到境弩先驱。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99500_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99500'>地望遥分楚，州封半入吴。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99500_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99500'>仙科存俊望，归路约蓬壶。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99500_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_99500'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_99500_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1036&endYear=1036')">1036年3月</a>　是年三月，开始校定李照所奏乐议。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1036&endYear=1036')">1036年4月</a>　夏初，呈校正《史记》与《三史勘误》。擢天章阁待制。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1036&endYear=1036')">1036年5月</a>　范仲淹上《百官图》，言谓讥讽吕夷简，由是落职贬知饶州。靖越班呈奏，贬监筠州酒税。尹洙、欧阳修论救，亦同时被贬、蔡襄为作《四贤一不肖诗》作品：论范仲淹不当以言获罪。<div id='poem_1158807' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158807' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158807?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论范仲淹不当以言获罪奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（景祐三年五月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158807")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158807_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158807'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158807'>臣闻位疏而言深者罪也，知浅而谋深者妄也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158807_comment'></div>臣故抵罪妄，辄有开陈者，怀忠事君，不敢自爱，万一益国，死无所恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158807_comment'></div>伏闻今月十九日，以吏部员外郎、天章阁待制范仲淹落职守本官差知饶州者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158807_comment'></div>臣窃谓仲淹秉朴忠之心，怀直谏之节，不识忌讳，有可矜悯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158807_comment'></div>观其临事不茍，言必忤上，竭忠奉国，夫岂私其身哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158807_comment'></div>去岁起自贬所，召居顾问之职，尔时正人端士，酌酒相贺，盖喜陛下纳善思治，招来忠谠，真圣帝哲王聪明之政也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158807_comment'></div>今兹遽闻以言获罪，左降僻远，事出不意，惊骇耳目，何其进之太暴而逐之太速乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158807_comment'></div>然则仲淹若以官政阙失，自取罪戾，国有常典，谁敢议之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158807_comment'></div>今以刺讥大臣，指讦时政，而不示含恕，重加谴谪，臣深为陛下不取也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158807_comment'></div>昔尧舜之帝，商周之王，尝云谔谔以昌，不闻诽谤为罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158807_comment'></div>况仲淹前所言事，在陛下母子夫妇之间，犯颜逆耳，最其大者，以其言合典礼，尚加优奖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158807_comment'></div>正人端士，所以相贺者，以陛下屈情恂道，超越前古若是者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158807_comment'></div>今因进对之际，言大臣长短，纵令谋论疏浅，褒贬过当，未必尽合圣虑，此则断在陛下听与不听耳，安可与谗邪同罪乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158807_comment'></div>至如汲黯在廷，毁平津之多诈；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158807_comment'></div>张昭论将，以鲁肃为粗疏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158807_comment'></div>汉帝吴主，熟闻此议，两用无猜，岂损令德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158807_comment'></div>臣今越职而言者，非不知百官内外，各有职分，但以谏官御史畏罪而未言，遂恐庶人之议，不得上达，故敢区区不避诛放。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158807_comment'></div>臣之所言，亦非营救仲淹，何者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158807_comment'></div>仲淹自大理寺丞，四五年间，至吏部员外郎，比于常流，此乃踰涯之宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158807_comment'></div>今虽落职，于仲淹之身，未有所损，但所论者，国家大体耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1158807_comment'></div>古者斥去直臣，皆玷累盛德，故多含垢忍怒，以示容纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1158807_comment'></div>彼非不能快意行事，盖惜千古之名耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1158807_comment'></div>陛下自亲政以来，三逐言事者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1158807_comment'></div>若习以为常，不甚重惜，则恐书于史册，亏玷太平之政，钳天下之口，塞陛下之聪，在此举矣，不可不谨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1158807_comment'></div>故臣披沥肝胆，冀陛下察之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1158807_comment'></div>伏望陛下以舜察迩言为念，以汉招直谏为谋，常以壅塞而是忧，不以诽谤而加罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1158807_comment'></div>追改前命，无重过举，则天下幸甚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1158807_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='dc26c06f1e054d0ea93901474e477188_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("dc26c06f1e054d0ea93901474e477188");'><span id='dc26c06f1e054d0ea93901474e477188_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1043')">1042-1043年</a>，43-44岁</div><div id='dc26c06f1e054d0ea93901474e477188' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年</a>　进京后，有奏状。作品：论常平仓。三统论。论文彥博知秦州状。<div id='poem_1158809' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158809' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158809?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论常平仓奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历二年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1042年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158809")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158809_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158809'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158809'>臣闻天下无常安之势，无常胜之兵，无常足之民，无常丰之岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158809_comment'></div>由是古先圣王，守之有道，制之有术，傥有缓急，不可无备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158809_comment'></div>伏睹真宗皇帝景德中，诏天下以逐州户口多少量留上供钱，起置常平仓，付司农寺系帐，三司不问出入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158809_comment'></div>每年夏秋两熟，准市价加钱收籴，其出息本利钱，只委司农寺专掌，三司转运司不得支拨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158809_comment'></div>自后每遇灾伤赈贷，使国有储蓄，民无流散者，用此术也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158809_comment'></div>前三司使姚仲孙，今春已来于京东等处，借支司农常平钱，以给和买。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158809_comment'></div>虽然借支官钱以充官用，循常视之，似无妨碍，若于经远之谋，深所未便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158809_comment'></div>臣窃惟真宗皇帝圣虑深远，臣敢梗概言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158809_comment'></div>当今天下金谷之数，诸路州军年支之外，悉充上供及别路经费，见在仓库更无馀羡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158809_comment'></div>所留常平本钱及斛㪷等，若以赈赡饥荒，此固常虑所及矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158809_comment'></div>万一不幸，方隅小有缓急，常给资粮，应卒可备，岂非先皇暗以数百万之资蓄于四方者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158809_comment'></div>今若先为三司所支，则天下储蓄尽矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158809_comment'></div>伏乞特降指挥三司，先借支常平本钱去处，并仰疾速拨还，今后不得更有支拨，并依景德先降敕命施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158809_comment'></div>又闻昨来遭旱州军，司农寺至今未曾指挥出粜斛㪷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158809_comment'></div>伏乞指挥司农寺遍牒诸路州军，应合出粜斛㪷去处，并仰疾速开仓，减价出粜，无使人民失所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158809_comment'></div>此实惠民之急、经国之要者也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1158809_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1158960' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158960' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158960?labeling=true' target='_blank'>三统论</a><span class='authorDate'>（1042年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158960")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158960_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158960'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158960'>夫王者受命，必先改正朔、易服色者，盖示民之有初也，故三统之义于是彰焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158960_comment'></div>然而先儒所论止及三王之世，是以夏之寅而黑，商之丑而白，周之子而赤，可得以述也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158960_comment'></div>至于尧、舜以上，则虽仲尼之说，亦无闻焉，岂非旨深而意远乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158960_comment'></div>而郑康成之徒，则据此而逆推，以为舜与周同，尧与商同，高辛氏乃与夏同，正朔三而止，文质再而复，自古而然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158960_comment'></div>非但不经，抑亦于帝王之道有所昧焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158960_comment'></div>尝试论之：夫帝王步骤不同，文质亦异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158960_comment'></div>三皇正历，岁准摄提。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158960_comment'></div>古之为君，因民而治，故唐虞已上无变易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158960_comment'></div>逮夏后之继统也，自以德衰，不及二帝，又知夫时将醨矣，必示之以制度，故其沿革，颇渐于文，是以《小正》之说、尚黑之义，于是著焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158960_comment'></div>然而服色有所尚而正朔不必改也，但纪之于政令而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158960_comment'></div>故仲尼称述三代则曰「行夏之时」，盖以其合于古而得天数也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158960_comment'></div>礼因于虞而不言其所损益者，盖谓此乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158960_comment'></div>及汤武之革命，既以兵胜，俗又寖弊，欲示民以改作，而新其耳目，俾知夫令出诸己，故有服色之变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158960_comment'></div>又以服色之制，本象于正朔，商人以建丑而易寅，新其令也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158960_comment'></div>尚白而变黑，象其朔也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158960_comment'></div>周之尚赤，而建子由是兴焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158960_comment'></div>然三王之易服改正，必取三微之月，盖以君之出令，象岁功阳气之始也，足以垂训于百王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158960_comment'></div>文质制度于斯备矣，后王虽兴，制作不出于此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158960_comment'></div>故仲尼曰：「其或继周者，百世可知」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158960_comment'></div>其此之谓矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1158960_comment'></div>夫谓正朔三而止者，月过三微不可以垂法也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1158960_comment'></div>斯亦王者之制耳，安可及于上古哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1158960_comment'></div>且五帝之书，二《典》存焉，其尧之书则曰「敬授人时」，顺历数也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1158960_comment'></div>又曰：「日中星鸟，以正仲春；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1158960_comment'></div>日短星昴，以正仲冬」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1158960_comment'></div>此则分至之候，正在四仲，契古历而符夏正也，又乌闻建丑之说乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1158960_comment'></div>舜在璿玑，以齐七政，审己之德，当天心与不尔，至于历数，亦不异于尧，又曷睹建子之言乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1158960_comment'></div>及其制服，则曰观古人之象，故出龙日月之度较然可知也，又何服色之改乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1158960_comment'></div>然则五帝之德淳，三王之俗薄，德淳则制简，俗薄则政备，故三统之义，起于三代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1158960_comment'></div>而虽自太昊，或推五德之运，盖顺天之数也，正朔则无所更焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1158960_comment'></div>至三王则政有偏矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1158960_comment'></div>夫有偏则有弊，故后之兴者，必举其偏而救其弊也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1158960_comment'></div>若谓文质可推于上古，是则夏尚忠、商尚质、周尚文，此三正者，又可行于帝王之代乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1158960_comment'></div>斯见其不然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1158960_comment'></div>自秦汉以下，服色但依于五胜，此又不可推于三王亦明矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1158960_comment'></div>康成既已失之，而杜佑、孔颖达之徒复引为證，疑误后学，甚矣夫！</div><div id='poem_sentence_35_1158960_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年</a>　是年，有诗。作品：送温陵庄君崇班赴长乐都尉。送舒太博通判眉州。<div id='poem_99506' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99506' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99506?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送温陵庄君崇班赴长乐都尉</a><span class='authorDate'>（1042年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99506")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_99506_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99506'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99506'>新命升鹓序，办严辞浚都。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99506_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99506'>去乘关吏传，归握戍兵符。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99506_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99506'>云阔逢乡树，风和见海桴。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99506_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99506'>南枝羡君乐，遣我忆莼鲈<span class='inlineComment2'>（以上《武溪集》卷一）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99506_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_99506'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_99506_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_99507' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99507' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99507?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送舒太博通判眉州</a><span class='authorDate'>（1042年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99507")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_99507_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99507'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99507'>通守方忻再命新，东风疏雨拂行尘。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99507_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99507'>封疆远入鱼凫国，岐路正逢蚕市春。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99507_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99507'>彭岫晓岚迎画隼，锦江晴绿照朱轮。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99507_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99507'>归期不待更书至，旧有清名在缙绅。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99507_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_99507'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_99507_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年9月27日</a>　接虞部府君之状，为作铭。作品：宋赠大理寺丞朱府君墓志铭。<div id='poem_1159024' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159024' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159024?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宋赠大理寺丞朱君墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（并序　庆历二年闰九月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1042年9月27日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1159024")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159024_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159024'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159024'>君讳信，其先邾人，战国时并于楚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159024_comment'></div>汉初以任侠闻，季布归之，以解主仇，名熏灼于天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159024_comment'></div>孝武徙山东甲族实诸陵，遂移名数长安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159024_comment'></div>云自平陵以峭直显名，博居杜陵以材敏称职，为汉名臣焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159024_comment'></div>世祖南阳，浮与祐俱自南阳为佐命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159024_comment'></div>晋、宋之际，龄石以权勇辅义，集勋疆埸，世有英特，发闻京辇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159024_comment'></div>唐室之季，遂家大梁，今占籍开封府阳武县户牗乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159024_comment'></div>曾祖讳洪，五代俶挠，仕涂榛梗，与道沉浮，不嗅骄饵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159024_comment'></div>祖讳敬安，郑州别驾，生一男一女：女适陕府右司马、赠少府少监陇西李咸，秩封河南县君；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159024_comment'></div>男讳昭泽，应《毛诗》学究举，不第，早亡，即君之文考也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159024_comment'></div>自曾门以来，以气义自守，君以奇节终之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159024_comment'></div>河南君之子李公穆，以谏议大夫参知政事，于君为外兄弟，终不于此时屈节，一图进取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159024_comment'></div>尝署计台右职，以劳当迁供奉禁庭矣，子友直明经及第，君即自解去，从容子舍，其淡泊荣味如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159024_comment'></div>然疏财好义，重许可，广交募，其游皆英俊有名之士也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159024_comment'></div>友直历官至虞部员外郎，要津提擢，繄君之旧，其知人之明又如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159024_comment'></div>卒以子登朝，再赠大理寺丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159024_comment'></div>女二人：长适孔氏，次适东染院副使赵承谔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159024_comment'></div>孙男二人：长曰济，中书堂后官、检校尚书水部员外郎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159024_comment'></div>次曰从政，早亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159024_comment'></div>孙女三人：长适左班殿直路昭吉，其次亦早亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159024_comment'></div>济字伯仁，少孤而倜傥，多识当世典故，复广交契，克绍祖烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159024_comment'></div>卜葬，得庆历二年太岁壬午闰九月二十七日丁酉，凡八柩同迁于开封府祥符县开府乡东韩村之大茔，君与夫人吴氏同窆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159024_comment'></div>朝廷以恩赙钱五万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159024_comment'></div>将葬，即以虞部府君之状托天章阁侍讲王洙撰次其美，复以君之状伻来索辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159024_comment'></div>济之游皆在朝闻人，籍籍居显仕矣，襄事，孝诚之极，而以文见属，故不克让。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159024_comment'></div>乃为铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_1159024'>猗与君子，韬光抱器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159024_comment'></div>进退以道，交游以义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1159024_comment'></div>不茍势荣，不屑禄累。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1159024_comment'></div>起家有承，拂衣无愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1159024_comment'></div>时人蹈道，身蒙其利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1159024_comment'></div>明哲树善，世福其嗣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1159024_comment'></div>乌经卜吉，牛眠善地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1159024_comment'></div>铭以掩幽，为子孙识。</div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1159024_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年10月</a>　九月，天武四厢都指挥使、镇戎军副总管葛怀敏御西夏之敌，陷重围遇害，仁宗嗟悼良久，赠太尉，赐谥忠隐。十月，靖作文。作品：葛怀敏谥议。<div id='poem_1158864' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158864' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158864?labeling=true' target='_blank'>葛怀敏谥议</a><span class='authorDate'>（1042年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158864")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158864_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158864'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158864'>赠太尉葛公，生于将门，资性明锐，束发从官，即以能称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158864_comment'></div>彤墀赞导，五符监督，屡更器使，人推其才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158864_comment'></div>御下不苛，接士以礼，轻赀好与，重器贵诺，官有所底，善声日闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158864_comment'></div>朝廷宠嘉，付以边事，易京之治，至今为最。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158864_comment'></div>属西羌怙远，辜我含育，率其犬羊，触齧保障。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158864_comment'></div>烽燧初举，即有肤施之役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158864_comment'></div>鉴其覆轨，寤寐材隽，是用起于谪籍，授之次将，画野增戍，以固封略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158864_comment'></div>氐孽孔炽，举国兴师，来如猬毛，屯逼城砦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158864_comment'></div>言奋其旅，出当贼锋，乘锐急战，卒用屠溃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158864_comment'></div>忘躯徇节，殒于旗鼓，诏赠旄钺，以旌死事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158864_comment'></div>祖载易名，式参前典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158864_comment'></div>谨案谥法：临患不忘国曰忠，隐拂不成曰隐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158864_comment'></div>若其远当勍寇，师无从继，势寡力屈，义不茍生，可不谓忠乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158864_comment'></div>肃将王怒，志清戎丑，众怫其令，投戈莫保，闻憿痛悼，雅意无成，可不谓隐乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158864_comment'></div>昔者流矢在马，鲁侯诔之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158864_comment'></div>握节陨命，晋策褒尚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158864_comment'></div>咸用加等，式彰义烈，繄公勤死，宜谥忠隐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158864_comment'></div>谨议。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1158864_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年</a>　同判太常礼院事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年</a>　入春，又为右正言。时欧阳修、王素知谏院。蔡襄赠诗赞曰：“御笔亲除三谏官，传喧朝野竞相欢，自古忠良得路难，必有谋献裨帝右。世间万事俱尘土，进取功名久远看； 当年流落丹心在，更加风采动朝端。”三人列名荐蔡襄，帝遂为知谏院，是为四直谏。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年</a>　会吕夷简罢相，章得象、晏殊贾昌朝、韩琦、范仲淹、富弼同时执政，仁宗采用范仲淹《十事疏》，任用贤达，推行新政。靖更是竭尽全力，为新政大造舆论，运用直谏手段，推进新政实施。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年1月</a>　正月，吴奏。作品：论皇子服罢开宴用乐。<div id='poem_1158810' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158810' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158810?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论皇子服罢开宴用乐奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历三年正月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1043年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158810")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158810_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158810'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158810'>臣伏见阴阳尅择官状申：皇子故鄂王大殓破服，并取今月十四日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158810_comment'></div>又伏见每年正月五日，紫宸殿开宴管领契丹贺正人使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158810_comment'></div>切恐有司循故事申举，以戎使为重，依例作乐开宴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158810_comment'></div>臣身为礼官，故敢先事言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158810_comment'></div>切以故鄂王虽在襁褓，是为无服之殇，其如已赐爵命，当同成人之例。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158810_comment'></div>父子天性，岂能无戚？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158810_comment'></div>今日服之，而明日宴乐，情何以安？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158810_comment'></div>且臣寮之家遭此丧，尚当给假，况万乘之主，因戎狄之使，不得申其私恩，深可痛也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158810_comment'></div>臣以为若不得已，宣召与礼食，而彻去声乐，亲遣大臣告谕戎使，以皇帝有嗣续之痛，故罢去声乐，非有轻重于北朝也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158810_comment'></div>戎狄虽同禽兽，不敢以此为恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158810_comment'></div>昔周景王以子丧既葬而与宴，《春秋》讥之，以为失礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158810_comment'></div>古者卿佐之丧，虽在祭祀，尚犹废乐，况其亲父子乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158810_comment'></div>臣不胜区区之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1158810_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年2月</a>　西夏元昊上书媾和，靖上疏。作品：论元昊请和当令权在我。<div id='poem_1158811' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158811' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158811?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论元昊请和当令权在我奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历三年二月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1043年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158811")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158811_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158811'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158811'>臣窃闻昊贼差私署官入境，相次到阙，欲与朝廷通和事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158811_comment'></div>伏以息兵减费，番人顺命，国家大臣，至于边将，咸欲息肩，以休士卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158811_comment'></div>臣愚料之，以谓挫北朝之气，折西羌之锐，不如不和，最为得策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158811_comment'></div>假如元昊贪我财货，其心臣伏，此之为祸大于今日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158811_comment'></div>臣请别白言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158811_comment'></div>伏自国家用兵以来，五年之间，三经大战，军覆将死，财用空虚，天下嗷嗷，困于供给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158811_comment'></div>今乃因胡人入一介之使，驰其号令，遂使二国通好，君臣如初，吾数年之辱，而契丹一言解之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158811_comment'></div>若胡人又遣一介有求于我，以为之谢，其将何词以拒之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158811_comment'></div>若使国家又有所惜，必将兴师责我，谓之背约，则北鄙生患，二境受敌矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158811_comment'></div>矧西戎自僭名号，未尝挫折，何肯悔祸，轻屈于人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158811_comment'></div>今若因其官属初来，未有定约，但少许之物，无满其意，坚守名分，以抑其僭，虽赐以甘言，彼必不屈，则吾虽西鄙受敌，而北胡未敢动也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158811_comment'></div>何以知之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158811_comment'></div>昨梁适使胡之时，国主面对行人，遣使西迈，意气自若，自言指呼之间，便令元昊依旧称臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158811_comment'></div>今来贼昊不肯称臣，则是北朝之威，不能使西羌屈伏，彼自丧气，岂能来责？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158811_comment'></div>故臣谓今之不和，则吾虽西鄙受敌，而北朝未敢动也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158811_comment'></div>若使与西戎结盟，则我之和好，权在番人，中国之威，于是尽矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158811_comment'></div>契丹责我，则二鄙受敌，其忧深矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158811_comment'></div>伏愿陛下与执政大臣，密谋而深思之，无令陷敌计中，则天下社稷幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158811_comment'></div>必不得已而与货财，须作料钱公使名目，便将灵盐、银夏作两镇，则赐与倍于往时，而君臣名分不改矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158811_comment'></div>或欲速成和好而屈名分，则天下共耻之，虽强兵在境，有血战而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1158811_comment'></div>若他年贼自有衅来求和者，权在于我，则不必拒之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1158811_comment'></div>惟陛下裁之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1158811_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年</a>　上疏。作品：请定献官冕服。禘郊论。请小祠献官以祭服行事。论河北榷盐。<div id='poem_1158825' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158825' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158825?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请定献官冕服奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历三年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1043年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158825")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158825_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158825'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158825'>《周礼》司服，掌王之吉凶衣服，所祀鬼神大小，以为制度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158825_comment'></div>今大中祠所遣献官，用上公九旒九章冕服为初献，馀公卿皆七旒冕，制无差降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158825_comment'></div>小祠则公服行事，乖戾旧典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158825_comment'></div>谓宜详《周礼》，因所祭鬼神，以等献官冕服之制。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1158825_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1158961' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158961' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158961?labeling=true' target='_blank'>禘郊论</a><span class='authorDate'>（1043年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158961")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158961_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158961'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158961'>先儒之所以解经者，盖欲导前圣之渊源，启后学之钤键，援古有据，垂世不惑者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158961_comment'></div>祭祀之仪，国之大典，今之礼经，以郑注为正，而康成释禘祭之文，前后驳杂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158961_comment'></div>《大传》曰：「礼不王不禘，王者禘其祖之所自出」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158961_comment'></div>郑云：「谓祭感生帝于南郊也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158961_comment'></div>《祭法》曰：「有虞氏禘黄帝而郊喾，祖颛顼而宗尧」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158961_comment'></div>郑云：「谓，谓祭昊天于圜丘也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158961_comment'></div>祭上帝于南郊曰郊，祭五帝五神于明堂曰祖宗，皆谓祭祀以配食也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158961_comment'></div>观郑所释，似有未悟，尝试论之：夫禘者，宗庙大祭之名也，「王者禘其祖之所自出」，谓虞氏之祖，出自黄帝，不立庙祧，故五年盛祭则及之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158961_comment'></div>夏亦禘黄帝，商周禘喾，盖姓氏所出，是为远祖也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158961_comment'></div>诸侯之禘，则降于王者，止祭始封之君，不得禘姓氏所出之祖，故曰「诸侯及其太祖」是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158961_comment'></div>而郑谓太微五帝递王，而王者之兴，必感其一，因其所感，别祭以尊之，故以感生之帝祭于圜丘，而祀上帝于南郊，唯据纬书以释经义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158961_comment'></div>太微亦为星象，昊天亦谓北辰，苍穹之号，遂有六天、郊丘之名，分为二祀，斯皆舛谬，深用轸惜，何则？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158961_comment'></div>郊与圜丘，俱是祭天之所，王肃所谓犹王城之内，与京师异名而同处也，岂可郊丘分为二祀，祖宗合为一祭乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158961_comment'></div>康成俱以禘文在郊祭之前，其祀必尊，当为圜丘，皆罔研经意，肆其臆说耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158961_comment'></div>又以祖宗、五帝、五神于明堂，小德配寡，大德配众，郑之此说，殊为失旨，误取《孝经》宗祀之名，以解祖宗之义，乃以二主泛配五帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158961_comment'></div>若谓太微五帝耶，则郑说太微与昊天上帝为六天矣，天尚无二，安得有六？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158961_comment'></div>按《天官书》，太微宫有五帝者，自是五精之神，不在穹苍之例。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158961_comment'></div>若以为太昊、炎帝之属耶，则又非仲尼配天之意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158961_comment'></div>《周礼》曰：「王将旅上帝，张毡案，设皇邸；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158961_comment'></div>祀五帝，张大次」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1158961_comment'></div>由此言之，上帝之与五帝，自有差殊，岂可混而为一乎？<div class='inline'
