ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1025&endYear=1026')">1025-1026年</a>，26-27岁</div><div id='b29b37846fc24fc2914bf75886fb3761' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1025&endYear=1025')">1025年</a>　从海阳返赣县。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1026&endYear=1026')">1026年9月</a>　改任江南东路湖口县丞，赴任途中赋五言古诗。作品：山寺独宿。<div id='poem_99552' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99552' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99552?labeling=true' target='_blank'>山寺独宿</a><span class='authorDate'>（1026年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99552")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_99552_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99552'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99552'>柴车走县封，穷途秋耿耿。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99552_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99552'>急雨带溪声，残灯背窗影。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99552_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99552'>驱驰下士身，凄凉旅人景。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99552_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99552'>山寒梦不成，愁多知夜永。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99552_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_99552'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_99552_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1026&endYear=1026')">1026年</a>　余靖三女梅卿出世。毛应佺调任江州通判。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='374212c2405c41e692dff68d935d9728_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("374212c2405c41e692dff68d935d9728");'><span id='374212c2405c41e692dff68d935d9728_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1032&endYear=1032')">1032年</a>，33岁</div><div id='374212c2405c41e692dff68d935d9728' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1032&endYear=1032')">1032年</a>　秋，改知江陵府松滋县，赴任前归家。作品：庐山栖贤宝觉禅院石浴室记。<div id='poem_1158993' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158993' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158993?labeling=true' target='_blank'>庐山栖贤宝觉禅院石浴室记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1032年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158993")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158993_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158993'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158993'>大雄氏之为教也，即空无著之谓性，摄心自持之谓修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158993_comment'></div>植因成果之说，所以道迷也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158993_comment'></div>施财获福之论，所以破贪也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158993_comment'></div>兹道坦明，各随所證。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158993_comment'></div>自像法东被，诸华向风，塔庙庄严，遍我国土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158993_comment'></div>凡所经始，人皆乐成者，非它也，彼既未悟于心，姑欲弛贪而出迷，当有导师掖而趋善使其然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158993_comment'></div>栖贤寺新成石浴室，募众而植因也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158993_comment'></div>浴室在寺之西南隅，寺在庐山之阳，山在浔阳郡之左，郡在大江之阴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158993_comment'></div>山川佳丽，栋宇轮奂，梵刹废兴，则寺记存焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158993_comment'></div>寺之始创于齐，盛于唐，赐名于皇朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158993_comment'></div>居之者不以昭穆伯仲相继，自智常至澄諟，皆海内有名高僧统其众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158993_comment'></div>故建刹启基，布金流银，日月天宫，琉璃地界，霞鲜翼张，翕赩相照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158993_comment'></div>唯兹温浴，屋老不支。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158993_comment'></div>一之日，澄諟言于众曰：「六时赞唱，当务洁斋，若尘垢未除，则七福何聚？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158993_comment'></div>欲求精进比丘，备其七物，不亦善乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158993_comment'></div>时则有浙僧希昱、能湛，行为上首，愿集其事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158993_comment'></div>用因缘相，一唱而就，募得缗钱二百万，凿山筑基，砻石构堂，仍市美材，续成外室，凡十一楹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158993_comment'></div>其浣濯之所、苏膏之器，罔不具焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158993_comment'></div>自天禧庚申岁矢谋，至乾兴改元之初，用浮图旧法饭僧以赞其成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158993_comment'></div>壬申岁，昱师会某于豫章，求文而志之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1158993_comment'></div>噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1158993_comment'></div>佛之性也，开示悟人，各有所因，则知昱、湛二开士，当于水因悟最上乘、入三摩地，岂独使洗涤前尘、除去七病而已哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1158993_comment'></div>按《十诵律》云：「昔舍利弗隆暑行化，执恼所著，有灌园者溉馀之水，请以为浴，此人获报，生忉利天」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1158993_comment'></div>由是观之，同捐货财，成此浴具，功又胜彼，如佛所说，其获福报，可思量哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1158993_comment'></div>其靡丽宏壮，则简而不书，聊记岁时而已。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1158993_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='a4f417f6a2954630ae80321bc76e50c9_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a4f417f6a2954630ae80321bc76e50c9");'><span id='a4f417f6a2954630ae80321bc76e50c9_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年</a>，52岁</div><div id='a4f417f6a2954630ae80321bc76e50c9' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年9月10日</a>　到任，呈谢表。作品：虔州谢上表。<div id='poem_1158761' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158761' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158761?labeling=true' target='_blank'>虔州谢上表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1051年9月10日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158761")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158761_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158761'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158761'>臣某言：九月六日，进奏院递到敕牒壹道，蒙恩落分司南京，守本官，就差知虔州军州事，已于今月十日到任上讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158761_comment'></div>仰望云天，起于久废；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158761_comment'></div>重沾雨露，恩比再生<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158761_comment'></div>伏念臣出自寒微，素无才识，幸逢明主，擢在近班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158761_comment'></div>本期名教之敦崇，冀正朝廷之黜陟；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158761_comment'></div>不悟怨仇交搆，毁訾百端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158761_comment'></div>尚蒙洪覆之仁，移隶别都之籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158761_comment'></div>退居田里，坐变炎凉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158761_comment'></div>前岁被以言纶，授之勇爵，宣君命而见召，在臣义之必行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158761_comment'></div>盖以弟任远官，父方卧病，委之遐适，心所难安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158761_comment'></div>寻沥血诚，再干天听，果回睿旨，许遂家居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158761_comment'></div>免朝虽远于宸廷，夺禄不从于吏议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158761_comment'></div>享无名之厚奉，久愧冗闲；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158761_comment'></div>乘一障以先登，亦惟驱策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158761_comment'></div>岂谓不离卿寺，就委郡章，既同死灰之复然，俾展铅刀之一割。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158761_comment'></div>亲有旨甘之便，民当攘劫之馀，得奉宽条，庶成后效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158761_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下，尧天广覆，汤网宏开，遗弃咸收，幽隐必察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158761_comment'></div>皇明下烛，同日月之无私；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158761_comment'></div>惠泽所沾，匝乾坤而共泰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158761_comment'></div>永言朽瘁，育以阳春，特推簪履之旧恩，无使田园之虚老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1158761_comment'></div>敢不佩服光宠，罄竭疲驽，询疾苦之所先，遵简易之成理，不忘官守，上报主知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1158761_comment'></div>但臣无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1158761_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年</a>　友人李定以殿中丞差通判洪州，途经虔州探靖，李定以词知著，靖遂填词赠行。作品：玉楼春。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年</a>　应约为李定父作诗序。作品：朝贤赠行诗总序。<div id='poem_1158942' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158942' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158942?labeling=true' target='_blank'>朝贤赠行诗总序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1051年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158942")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158942_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158942'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158942'>古之贤士大夫，尚冲退而轻进取者，无他焉，盖所以敦止足，远奔竞，激贪冒，励风俗也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158942_comment'></div>陇西李氏，奕世清德，某守庐陵日，今致政驾部尝以诗序一编见寄，乃朝贤赠行之为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158942_comment'></div>首则先正尚书以蓬丘佐著辞荣就养，次则令元贰卿以霜台独坐避权请郡，末则传政驾曹以春宫属僚解组归休，皆未及引年之典，而挂冠勇退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158942_comment'></div>故三朝夙德，二府名臣，台阁清贤，搢绅伟望，率用揄扬高趣，歌咏素风，或诗或序，共美行色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158942_comment'></div>又其豫章所居，构阁东湖之涘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158942_comment'></div>不杂嚣滓，有云泉之致；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158942_comment'></div>不出户庭，杂鱼鸟之乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158942_comment'></div>朝廷文雅之士，闻其风而慕之，咸寄英词，刻在翠琰，欲俾总序，录之以为子孙之藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158942_comment'></div>适会某负谤去官，不克从命，越十稔矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158942_comment'></div>今兹驾部文洎令子比部、司门二君，悉以书见贻，复叙前意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158942_comment'></div>且司门之书曰：「大门世父诗序，各在一石，今欲合而传之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158942_comment'></div>且予兄弟执先妣之丧已终矣，兄当僶俛还台，定乞便官奉养，旦夕侍立，未尝不议及此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158942_comment'></div>况老父十年之意，不为不勤矣，吾友之文，不可靳也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158942_comment'></div>某伏自惟念，当世儒宗，故司空李公昉、故翰林宋公白、故宫保晁公迥皆有诗，故翰林杨公亿、前相国晏公殊皆有序，于李氏世德，非不光矣，岂假鄙拙，乃益其重耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158942_comment'></div>幸而获交其父子间，今勤如是，虽久废笔砚，敢怠于词哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158942_comment'></div>于戏！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158942_comment'></div>求之旧史，累代华显、传龟袭紫者多矣，至于习守退静，脱去荣利，并踵其高者尤难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158942_comment'></div>其人可尚矣哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158942_comment'></div>故直书而序之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158942_comment'></div>凡序五首、记一首、诗一百三十二首，列之于石，传无穷焉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1158942_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年</a>　原虔州通判萧固移官湖南，赠留茉莉花栽，喜赋七律。作品：酬萧閤副惠末利花栽。<div id='poem_99536' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99536' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99536?labeling=true' target='_blank'>酬萧阁副惠末利花栽</a><span class='authorDate'>（1051年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99536")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_99536_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99536'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99536'>素艳南方独出群，只应琼树是前身。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99536_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99536'>自缘香极宜晨露，勿谓开迟怨晚春。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99536_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99536'>栏槛故将宾榻近，丹青重整画图新。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99536_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99536'>移根得地无华裔，从此飞觞不厌频。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99536_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_99536'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_99536_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年</a>　以父丧，去官归家守制。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='fb9af9d39be4474e8d951e39c872573f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("fb9af9d39be4474e8d951e39c872573f");'><span id='fb9af9d39be4474e8d951e39c872573f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1052&endYear=1052')">1052年</a>，53岁</div><div id='fb9af9d39be4474e8d951e39c872573f' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>回虔州交任。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>由赣州桂源镇西北行过湘，有诗。作品：桂源晓别秦珏河隄。桂源早行。<div id='poem_99515' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99515' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99515?labeling=true' target='_blank'>桂源晓别秦珏河湜</a><span class='authorDate'>（1052年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99515")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_99515_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99515'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99515'>回馆逢清论，长亭惨别襟。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99515_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99515'>亡羊南北路，跃马利名心。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99515_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99515'>酒市摇风帜，花村锁雾林。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99515_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99515'>行行俱得意，结绶有知音。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99515_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_99515'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_99515_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_99514' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99514' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99514?labeling=true' target='_blank'>桂源早行</a><span class='authorDate'>（1052年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99514")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_99514_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99514'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99514'>闻鸡已行迈，策马更徘徊。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99514_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99514'>月色依山尽，秋声带雨来。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99514_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99514'>自堪悲<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_99514", 99514, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>玉璞</span>，谁复筑金台。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99514_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99514'>薄宦空羁束，西斋长绿苔。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99514_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_99514'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_99514_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='ef3ded4f81de4534aef77919f7e69c69_label'><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1064&endYear=1064')">1064年</a>　登州城楼，回忆昔时在桂源与友人分别，有七绝。作品：感旧。<div id='poem_99456' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99456' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99456?labeling=true' target='_blank'>感旧</a><span class='authorDate'>（1064年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99456")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_99456_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99456'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99456'>醉吟曾共倚江楼，秾艳清香万柄秋。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99456_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99456'>荡子再归时已暮，暮鸿惊散水悠悠。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99456_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99456'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_99456_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
湖口
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='180b1270211646a2a234cf3d1e8f273a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("180b1270211646a2a234cf3d1e8f273a");'><span id='180b1270211646a2a234cf3d1e8f273a_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1027&endYear=1028')">1027-1028年</a>，28-29岁</div><div id='180b1270211646a2a234cf3d1e8f273a' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1027&endYear=1027')">1027年3月25日</a>　梅佐、邓戡、苏舜钦预殿试，擢进士第，余靖专柬贺之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1027&endYear=1027')">1027年</a>　岳父母合葬海阳，家人来告，撰文由家人带回。作品：宋故两浙提点刑狱尚书度支员外郎林公墓碣。<div id='poem_1159020' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159020' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159020?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宋故两浙提点刑狱尚书度支员外郎林公墓碣铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（并序　宝元二年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1027年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1159020")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159020_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159020'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159020'>公讳从周，字某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159020_comment'></div>其先西河人，问礼孔子，显名诸侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159020_comment'></div>七世祖自南安徙居潮州，宗族盘互，为海阳著姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159020_comment'></div>曾大父讳某，大父讳某，丘园贲素，咸以冲旷终焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159020_comment'></div>父璨，少以节惠称于乡党，复谨义方训子，遂起其家，四进秩，太子洗马致仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159020_comment'></div>公即长子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159020_comment'></div>景德二年，由进士上第敕除泉州南安主簿，郡以符召为掾，日持手板，与刺史廷辩曲直，凛然有国士之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159020_comment'></div>主计者闻其材，俾莅剑州银冶，半岁，入银铜七十一万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159020_comment'></div>第其最以闻，天子嘉之，擢授大理评事，筦榷永嘉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159020_comment'></div>复以课迁本寺丞、知开封考城县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159020_comment'></div>遭母丧解官，柴毁过礼，闾里指为标准。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159020_comment'></div>服阙，又丞殿中，勾当诸司粮料院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159020_comment'></div>大司徒王公钦若镇馀杭，奏辟公为副，诏授太常博士、通判杭州军州事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159020_comment'></div>司徒故相，长于智术，处事与朝廷约束不能无异同，公悉力牵挽，归于绳墨而后已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159020_comment'></div>司徒公初怒中悔，命一府惟公之听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159020_comment'></div>入朝久之，以屯田员外郎充开封府推官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159020_comment'></div>议不己同，锱铢不移，事或闻上，帝独可公奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159020_comment'></div>寻转度支员外郎、提点浙江东西刑狱公事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159020_comment'></div>以天圣三年五月癸巳卒官，享年五十一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159020_comment'></div>公孤进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159020_comment'></div>以材称，故自南安二考特转京城官，非列也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159020_comment'></div>司徒公之出镇，精择本朝望士为佐，故内阁段公少连时为观察判官耳，公乃通判其府，事无巨细，一决于公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159020_comment'></div>初，大司徒与丁晋公谓久以势位相倾，俄而弃节，于洛得罪，其尝所厚者，悉坐左迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159020_comment'></div>公在馀杭，以抗直不党闻于朝，故得免戾，然亦格不用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159020_comment'></div>晋公败，乃为天府佐，司徒再秉国钧，犹以前佐郡时持正不能屈，终亦疏之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159020_comment'></div>在府三年，凡易四尹，太后、帝知名，而终不迁，止以平例外补，遂卒，岂命也哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159020_comment'></div>公性耿介，不容人私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1159020_comment'></div>京邑浩穰，压于权贵请托，不得循理可否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1159020_comment'></div>公锐意痛绝私谒，所得权贵人翰墨，都不省视，至夕聚而焚之，由此势益失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1159020_comment'></div>上初即位，富于春秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1159020_comment'></div>庄献皇太后五日一垂帘，御长春殿，共断天下事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1159020_comment'></div>故事，大尹上殿，职官一员同陟殿陛，与大尹东西立黼扆前，腰笏对展奏牍，听上裁决。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1159020_comment'></div>一日，奏事退，庄献指公语上曰：「此林某也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1159020_comment'></div>近侍咸闻焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1159020_comment'></div>公之奏事，常出文法之外，故两宫多之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1159020_comment'></div>府民有杀其兄之二子以规其财者，长被疮即死，其幼走以免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1159020_comment'></div>事发狱成，以母年八十，法当留侍，公乃建言，使无状子居母侧，以凌其幼孤，必无全理；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1159020_comment'></div>且孤孙虽稚，亦能为祖母养，留之惠奸，不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1159020_comment'></div>读奏未毕，太后遽颔之曰：「人情当如此」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1159020_comment'></div>即命配海外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1159020_comment'></div>公之持平固执，皆此类也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1159020_comment'></div>其在南安、考城之政，至今民歌颂之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1159020_comment'></div>故天章阁待制刘公随，考城人也，尝与某言：王府属邑，多以材望奏请，然自公罢去二十馀年，耆旧言父母官无及林公者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1159020_comment'></div>闻公亡时，或至沾泣，其政感人心如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1159020_comment'></div>公属文不茍为华媚，遣言指事，必根政道，再献赋颂，悉以规诫为本，上亦再以手诏褒之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1159020_comment'></div>公之弟五人：其长曰从善，先公卒，次曰从式，次曰从变，次曰从义，次曰从道，皆良士也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1159020_comment'></div>上之初奠玉于圜丘也，公以府僚侍祠，例授一子出身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1159020_comment'></div>公之二子皆白身未仕，独念母弟早亡，嗣续未光，遂先奏其孤以慰藉之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1159020_comment'></div>言行义者，咸共推伏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1159020_comment'></div>公娶乡里张氏，封清河县君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1159020_comment'></div>公之存，以妇顺助其内；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1159020_comment'></div>公之没，以母道严其家，宗族奉之如师保焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1159020_comment'></div>生二男三女：长子东乔，光禄寺丞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1159020_comment'></div>次子东美，举进士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1159020_comment'></div>长女嫁大理寺丞许因；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1159020_comment'></div>其次女封德安县君；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1159020_comment'></div>幼女嫁进士魏庚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1159020_comment'></div>孙几人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1159020_comment'></div>公之卒也，弟从庆及其孤扶其柩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1159020_comment'></div>逾闽岭以归，而洗马府君亦以其年四月壬戌卒，遂以天圣五年某月，举二丧同域葬于某乡某里某原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1159020_comment'></div>妣曰临颍县太君钟氏，前葬某乡某原，卜人曰吉，遂不克祔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1159020_comment'></div>某幸得娶公中女，公既窆十五年，乃克拜于松槚之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1159020_comment'></div>于是聚其族姻，询访遗懿在人之闻者，书之于石以为表云尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1159020_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_63_1159020'>鹑火耀芒，重离协光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1159020_comment'></div>下生俊杰，发为端方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1159020_comment'></div>俗尚软熟，视如坚刚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1159020_comment'></div>君子居之，不易其常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1159020_comment'></div>仁义内修，我知克举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1159020_comment'></div>爵禄外至，委于所遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1159020_comment'></div>万乘知名，身犹龃龉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1159020_comment'></div>才乎命乎，天不兼予。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1159020_comment'></div>未伸明谟，弗克中寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1159020_comment'></div>善之所报，将在于后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1159020_comment'></div>惟石言言，立于松阡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1159020_comment'></div>直书不文，庶乎长存。</div><div id='poem_sentence_74_1159020_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1028&endYear=1028')">1028年3月</a>　接孙复书柬与赠诗，得悉石介将妻子久安置于师处，戏以友人妻填词寄石介。作品：南歌子。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1028&endYear=1028')">1028年3月</a>　奉和孙复五律。作品：次韵孙明复见寄。<div id='poem_99472' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99472' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99472?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵酬孙明复见寄</a><span class='authorDate'>（1028年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99472")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_99472_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99472'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99472'>门外车尘绝，樽前俗虑无。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99472_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99472'>轻身脱羁绊，曳尾得泥涂。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99472_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99472'>出处天真在，炎凉物性殊。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99472_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99472'>寄言钦雅意，相望隔江湖。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99472_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_99472'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_99472_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1028&endYear=1028')">1028年</a>　余靖四女莲卿出世。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1028&endYear=1028')">1028年</a>　王仝善因助余靖报考制举科，被韶州知州革职，闲居处州；林逋病逝于孤山。二事使余靖非愤不已，因林逋追谥和靖，遂改名为靖，呈改名条陈由毛通判转递交吏部。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='9ce2bdb50c8c4dcdba6892e2cd10221e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("9ce2bdb50c8c4dcdba6892e2cd10221e");'><span id='9ce2bdb50c8c4dcdba6892e2cd10221e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1060')">1060年</a>，61岁</div><div id='9ce2bdb50c8c4dcdba6892e2cd10221e' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1060')">1060年8月</a>　行军途中，作五言诗。作品：湖乡检旱入南路夜宿江寺对望郛郭。<div id='poem_99577' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99577' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99577?labeling=true' target='_blank'>湖乡检旱回入南路夜宿江寺对望郛郭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1060年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99577")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_99577_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99577'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99577'>高城锁夕霭，远水浮秋空。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99577_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99577'>此时行役心，展转如飞蓬。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99577_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99577'>路入浅沙断，堪恸车辙穷。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99577_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99577'>岂无舟楫利，枉道非所从。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99577_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_99577'>虽有泉石趣，暂到徒匆匆。<div id='poem_sentence_4_99577_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_99577'>儿啼不入门，敢辞身徇公。<div id='poem_sentence_5_99577_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_99577'>梦归身未归，薄宦真池龙。<div id='poem_sentence_6_99577_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_99577'>披衣复起坐，惊鸿鸣西风。<div id='poem_sentence_7_99577_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_99577'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_99577_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
修水
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='f272b422862e4f23a5363a0898c72d7f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f272b422862e4f23a5363a0898c72d7f");'><span id='f272b422862e4f23a5363a0898c72d7f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1028&endYear=1028')">1028年</a>，29岁</div><div id='f272b422862e4f23a5363a0898c72d7f' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1028&endYear=1028')">1028年</a>　秋，改任宣州司理参军。有诗。作品：松门守风。<div id='poem_99560' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99560' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99560?labeling=true' target='_blank'>松门守风</a><span class='authorDate'>（1028年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99560")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_99560_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99560'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99560'>彭蠡古来险，汤汤贯侯卫。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99560_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99560'>源长云共浮，望极天无际。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99560_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99560'>传闻五月交，兹时一阴至。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99560_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99560'>飓风生海隅，馀力千里曀。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99560_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_99560'>万窍争怒号，惊涛得狂势。<div id='poem_sentence_4_99560_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_99560'>涌恐楚山拔，声疑夏鼎沸。<div id='poem_sentence_5_99560_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_99560'>妖蜃吐浓烟，层台誇壮丽。<div id='poem_sentence_6_99560_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_99560'>奔雷鸣大车，连鼓声粗厉。<div id='poem_sentence_7_99560_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_99560'>岂诚阴阳争，长忧天地闭。<div id='poem_sentence_8_99560_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_99560'>孤舟一叶轻，飘如斿在缀。<div id='poem_sentence_9_99560_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_99560'>所以溯沿人，未尝贪既济。<div id='poem_sentence_10_99560_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_99560'>逆犹上坂丸，顺比飞鸿翅。<div id='poem_sentence_11_99560_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_99560'>直待浮云收，乾坤廓然霁。<div id='poem_sentence_12_99560_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_99560'>湖光百里平，波色连天翠。<div id='poem_sentence_13_99560_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_99560'>然后榜兰桡，以避蛟龙害。<div id='poem_sentence_14_99560_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_99560'>进退甘迟留，克保无祇悔。<div id='poem_sentence_15_99560_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_99560'>我愿修身者，体此操舟态。<div id='poem_sentence_16_99560_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_99560'>动静惟时几，畏慎存纤芥。<div id='poem_sentence_17_99560_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_99560'>跬足虽平易，尽心防暧昧。<div id='poem_sentence_18_99560_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_99560'>长如履险时，终身不危殆。<div id='poem_sentence_19_99560_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_99560'></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_99560_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
九江
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='304d7f4d2ccc465c91d770b72fd223bf_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("304d7f4d2ccc465c91d770b72fd223bf");'><span id='304d7f4d2ccc465c91d770b72fd223bf_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1028&endYear=1028')">1028年</a>，29岁</div><div id='304d7f4d2ccc465c91d770b72fd223bf' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1028&endYear=1028')">1028年</a>　过大孤山，有诗。<div id='poem_99555' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99555' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99555?labeling=true' target='_blank'>过大孤山</a><span class='authorDate'>（1028年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99555")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_99555_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99555'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99555'>有形天地分，设险山河壮。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99555_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99555'>孤山镇南服，峨峨楚之望。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99555_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99555'>中立亡所倚，屹然怪其状。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99555_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99555'>石嵾入春空，翠柱支秋浪。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99555_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_99555'>片时起雪痕，万顷排霜杖。<div id='poem_sentence_4_99555_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_99555'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_99555", 99555, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>噫气</span>专呼吸，横流以溟涨。<div id='poem_sentence_5_99555_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_99555'>行人多躁进，那解明得丧。<div id='poem_sentence_6_99555_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_99555'>不顾风涛险，半就江鱼葬。<div id='poem_sentence_7_99555_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_99555'>挂席经其<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>旁，往往乞灵贶。<div id='poem_sentence_8_99555_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_99555'>遂因孤独名，塑立轻盈像。<div id='poem_sentence_9_99555_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_99555'>绰约姑射姿，梦魂巫峡想。<div id='poem_sentence_10_99555_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_99555'>如何方面祠，终古承其妄。<div id='poem_sentence_11_99555_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_99555'>五岳视三公，降杀不过两。<div id='poem_sentence_12_99555_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_99555'>不然为子男，何以通祀享。<div id='poem_sentence_13_99555_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_99555'>四气均分风，条融各有掌。<div id='poem_sentence_14_99555_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_99555'>避其狂<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作吼）</span>怒势，亦可利攸往。<div id='poem_sentence_15_99555_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_99555'>亭育天地心，凭险恣荡漾<span class='inlineComment2'>（二字原缺，据四库本补）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_16_99555_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_99555'>正直鬼神德，非名奚独飨。<div id='poem_sentence_17_99555_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_99555'>不使悔吝侵，庶几忠信仗。<div id='poem_sentence_18_99555_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_99555'>在人不在神，勿为虚稽颡。<div id='poem_sentence_19_99555_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_99555'></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_99555_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_99555'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_8_99555_0'>⑴ 原作典，据四库本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_99555_comment'></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
宣城
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='b0486b386e1744f0b16fbd96d678478b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b0486b386e1744f0b16fbd96d678478b");'><span id='b0486b386e1744f0b16fbd96d678478b_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1028&endYear=1030')">1028-1030年</a>，29-31岁</div><div id='b0486b386e1744f0b16fbd96d678478b' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1028&endYear=1028')">1028年</a>　淮河有灾民南下流徙，余靖动员地方予以救济安置，处置得当，湖口、宣州均无灾民与当地民众械斗纠纷事件。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1029&endYear=1029')">1029年</a>　宰相张士逊罢为刑部尚书、知江宁府，充江南东路安抚使，巡察宣州，对余靖赈灾得力甚为赞赏，支持他报考制举科。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1029&endYear=1029')">1029年</a>　薛长孺来探访，赋诗送归。作品：送薛秀才归乡。<div id='poem_99509' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99509' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_content_99509'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99509'>半岁接高论，一朝归故关。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99509_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99509'>道存惭设醴<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：主礼不腆，深愧前哲。）</span>，别易忍登山。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99509_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99509'>进即龟龙瑞，退当江海闲。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99509_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99509'>无为牵俗趣，碌碌利名间。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99509_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_99509'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_99509_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1030&endYear=1030')">1030年</a>　应制举科试，得书判拔萃科第一，改知新建县。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='ff53c5ac6b6e4013b14e6f5ab59095e4_label'><a href='javascript: gray;'>▪</span>过江宁府考试途中于宣州作诗。作品：送僧惠勤归乡。赠青林庵主。<div id='poem_99508' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99508' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99508?labeling=true' id='poem_sentence_0_99508'>旧国起归兴，三江一棹轻。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99508_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99508'>夜吟逢月白，晓渡趁潮平。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99508_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99508'>楚岸云藏寺，吴宫水绕城。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99508_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99508'>羡师尘外去，何日濯吾缨。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99508_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_99508'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_99508_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_99575' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99575' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99575?labeling=true' target='_blank'>游山五题<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span>赠青林庵主</a><span class='authorDate'>（1030年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99575")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_99575_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99575'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99575'>佛性深如海，中边见各异。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99575_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99575'>道在有无间，语论皆儿戏。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99575_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99575'>几多名利僧，妄习诸家气。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99575_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99575'>贪嗔尚缠牵，生灭何由离。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99575_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_99575'>三世古今佛，岂离根本智。<div id='poem_sentence_4_99575_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_99575'>舍此觅菩提，谁證<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>菩提位。<div id='poem_sentence_5_99575_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_99575'>吾师识自心，有为皆委弃。<div id='poem_sentence_6_99575_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_99575'>冥坐不知年，了了忘言意。<div id='poem_sentence_7_99575_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_99575'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_99575_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_99575'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_5_99575_0'>⑴ 原作正，据四库本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_99575_comment'></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1030&endYear=1030')">1030年6月</a>　六月赴任，作诗。作品：新建县西山记。<div id='poem_1159004' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159004' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159004?labeling=true' target='_blank'>新建县西山记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1030年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1159004")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159004_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159004'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159004'>西山在县西四十里<span class='inlineComment2'>（《舆地纪胜》三十六。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159004_comment'></div>初济江十里有盘<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>石，名石头津。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159004_comment'></div>自石头西行有梅岭，即梅福学仙处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159004_comment'></div>岭之南有葛仙峰，下有葛仙坛，上有丹井及鸾冈，乃洪崖先生乘鸾所憩处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159004_comment'></div>西山鹤岭，王子乔控鹤所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159004_comment'></div>又有大萧、小萧二峰，世传萧史尝游其侧，旁有萧仙坛，又有水出山椒，名吕源，水高下十堰，溉田万馀顷<span class='inlineComment2'>（《大明一统志》四十九。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159004_comment'></div>岩岫四出，千峰北来，岚光染空，连属三百里，其所经行，尽西山之景<span class='inlineComment2'>（《舆地纪胜》三十六。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159004_comment'></div>西山之势与庐岳<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>等，而不与之接<span class='inlineComment2'>（此句据《江西通志》增。）</span>，馀山则支附耳。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1159004_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1159004'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_1159004_0'>⑴ 《古今图书集成·山川典》引《江西通志》作磬。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_7_1159004_0'>⑵ 光绪《江西通志》五十岳作阜。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1159004_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1030&endYear=1030')">1030年6月</a>　在新建，作诗。作品：西山。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1031&endYear=1031')">1031年</a>　岳父故交、原韶州知州、江南西路转运使许申陪九华山隐士许亮山人来游西山，有诗。作品：许申工部招九华许亮山人因有和赠。<div id='poem_99474' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99474' id='poem_sentence_1_99474'>中真久待茅君会，密信频教鹤使催。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99474_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99474'>玉斧祖风应共继，琼酥宾宴更谁陪<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99474_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99474'>西山五色从兹得，脱略浮名薄似埃。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99474_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_99474'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_99474_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_99474'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_2_99474_0'>⑴ 自注：《南岳夫人传》云夫人觞王子乔琼酥渌酒。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_99474_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1032&endYear=1032')">1032年</a>　春夏间，于新建赋诗。作品：送林秀才归南海。送任秘丞知长兴县。<div id='poem_99567' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99567' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99567?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送林秀才归南海</a><span class='authorDate'>（1032年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99567")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_99567_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99567'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99567'>红尘倦客游，䌽衣归故山。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99567'>凛凛朔风劲，携手江之干。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99567'>江声万雷震，帆影孤鸿翻。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99567'>修途南尽海，冰雪凄人肝。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_99567'>不但川陆险，所思在承颜。<div id='poem_sentence_4_99567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_99567'>亲膳足甘滑，家居<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>富林泉。<div id='poem_sentence_5_99567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_99567'>怀安实败名，无为乐丘园。<div id='poem_sentence_6_99567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_99567'>好爵縻英贤，早奋冲天翰。<div id='poem_sentence_7_99567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_99567'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_99567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_99567'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_5_99567_0'>⑴ 原作足，据四库本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_99567_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_99491' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99491' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99491?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送任秘丞知长兴县</a><span class='authorDate'>（1032年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99491")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_99491_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99491'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99491'>懿文通籍气飘飘，二十年来困下僚。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99491_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99491'>吾道本将忠许国，世途休叹老登朝。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99491_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99491'>囊装冷落堆青简，衙署幽深枕画桥。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99491_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99491'>预想吴人蒙美化，海鸥桑雉共逍遥。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99491_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_99491'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_99491_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='4c164896dfb846159348de94d7527df3_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("4c164896dfb846159348de94d7527df3");'><span id='4c164896dfb846159348de94d7527df3_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1036&endYear=1036')">1036年</a>，37岁</div><div id='4c164896dfb846159348de94d7527df3' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1036&endYear=1036')">1036年10月</a>　应洪州通判施元长之请，到洪州小住休憩，并在洪州州学讲述三史校正情况颇受学正赞许，暂缓到任。作品：洪州新置州学记。<div id='poem_1158971' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158971' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158971?labeling=true' target='_blank'>洪州新置州学记</a><span class='authorDate'>（景祐三年十月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158971")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158971_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158971'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158971'>三代之制，天子之学曰辟廱，诸侯曰泮宫，党遂所居，必有庠序，释菜之奠，其来旧矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158971_comment'></div>盖孔子之道，万世师表，故昔唐氏尊之以王爵，奉之以时祀，而礼用祭菜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158971_comment'></div>夫祭菜之义，本于太学，存庙而废学者，礼之失也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158971_comment'></div>大江之西，处都会而山水佳者，洪为率，郡之造秀，以文获仕，岁有人焉，固宜兴学校以宠其俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158971_comment'></div>景祐改元之明年，天水赵槩叔平，以祠曹副郎兼东壁图书之职来守是邦，剪弊擿蠹，树立群善，和气被境，庭无宿奸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158971_comment'></div>乃思本朝一祖二宗，承平八十年，垂白耇老不识攻守之器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158971_comment'></div>今上复好文以守成业，而学校之风未甚流布，殆于守臣之阙请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158971_comment'></div>遂露奏：豫章介在江左，为支郡准的，援南西二都暨上始封之国为比，即其祠宫，愿建黉舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158971_comment'></div>诏从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158971_comment'></div>繇是葺旧模新，补败增卑，广其壖垣，峻其廉陛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158971_comment'></div>或易椽而朽，或筑基而营，起桡为隆，变蔀为丰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158971_comment'></div>寝殿奕奕，俨然南面，龙衮珠旒，备乎王章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158971_comment'></div>自高第弟子至汉魏大儒，坐而侍，壁而立，于堂于庑，列像有次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158971_comment'></div>考室百楹以处生徒，凡大夫、士、庶人之子为俊士者，皆许游焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158971_comment'></div>仍乞上庠镂版书以赋其时习，给閒田五百亩以充其日廪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158971_comment'></div>选文行之士观察推官陈肃总其众而谨其号令，事由中覆，咸得请焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158971_comment'></div>又俾设色之工，以夏、商、周车服、圭璧、梡俎、彝斝之器见于经礼者，绘之讲论之堂，使朝夕观焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158971_comment'></div>孟子所谓「乐得英才而教育之」者，其是之谓乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158971_comment'></div>鸠工于三月庚子，告成于八月庚申。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158971_comment'></div>役用卒徒，不劳于民，赋以羡材，不歛于众，而克成焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1158971_comment'></div>噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1158971_comment'></div>汉袭秦令，以太守领郡，而泮宫之制阙焉，其或著理效，称循吏，大抵谨绳墨、挟钩距、尚威刑以束缚人耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1158971_comment'></div>能知学校为教民之本者，惟文翁唱之于蜀，故司马相如、王褒之徒，用文章揄扬汉美，与三代相照耀于先后者，文翁之力也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1158971_comment'></div>后人复声而和者亡几焉，盖学校之益人也缓，威刑之取名也速，故为政者有所趋焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1158971_comment'></div>今叔平以文学举进士而升鼎科，以器识居宦途而历显仕，复能敦大教之本，储诗书而萃英髦，以尊圣育贤为事，夫其远大，安可量哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1158971_comment'></div>与夫徼福于神、盛祠庙者异矣，又岂知洪人戴之不若文翁之于蜀耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1158971_comment'></div>某以上书忤旨，贬筠州，道出大府，目是懿绩，故为之记云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1158971_comment'></div>皇宋景祐丙子岁十月日建。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1158971_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1036&endYear=1036')">1036年</a>　在洪州，有诗。作品：留题许国博申申堂。送邓秘丞知德安县。思寿阳寓居高氏园亭。<div id='poem_99517' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99517' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99517?labeling=true' target='_blank'>留题许国博申申堂</a><span class='authorDate'>（1036年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99517")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_99517_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99517'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99517'>宴居潇洒一斋宽，每到高谈暮忍还。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99517_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99517'>境胜自容巢燕托，时清谁顾卧龙闲。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99517_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99517'>桥前水石纷华外，窗下琴书寂寞间。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99517_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99517'>兼济未成归有地，羡君因此转思山。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99517_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_99517'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_99517_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_99490' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99490' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99490?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送邓秘丞知德安县</a><span class='authorDate'>（1036年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99490")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_99490_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99490'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99490'>里闬俊游心久降，越台成政俗敦庞。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99490'>香炉山下重为县，阊阖风高还渡江。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99490'>且喜恩威长及物，莫嫌功业未经邦。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99490'>公斋更近渊明宅，寄傲情应卧北窗。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_99490'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_99490_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_99486' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99486' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99486?labeling=true' target='_blank'>思寿阳寓居高氏园亭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1036年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99486")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_99486_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99486'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99486'>尝借芳园石友家，幽栖无复羡<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>纷华。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99486_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99486'>敞扉气爽云生栋，卷箔香微露泫花。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99486_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99486'>桂向淮山分月魄，桃从秦洞得仙葩。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99486_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99486'>别来追想清闲境，悔褫方中走栈车。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99486_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_99486'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_99486_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_99486'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_99486_0'>⑴ 原作美，据四库本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_99486_comment'></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='6bf31186560a434fb3828f3d792d30f9_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("6bf31186560a434fb3828f3d792d30f9");'><span id='6bf31186560a434fb3828f3d792d30f9_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1064&endYear=1064')">1064年</a>，65岁</div><div id='6bf31186560a434fb3828f3d792d30f9' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1064&endYear=1064')">1064年</a>　溯赣江而上，至洪州，与同榜进士好友知洪州施元长欢叙，撰铭。此乃绝笔之作。作品：庐山归宗禅院妙圆大师塔铭。<div id='poem_1159042' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159042' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159042?labeling=true' target='_blank'>庐山归宗禅院妙圆大师塔铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（嘉祐四年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1159042")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159042_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159042'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159042'>禅师讳自宝，庐州合肥人，姓吴氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159042_comment'></div>生有奇相，幼不同俗，弱龄出家寿州普宁禅院，智柔大师授以经律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159042_comment'></div>初具戒腊，已抱出群之见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159042_comment'></div>蹑履游方，遍参知识，靳州五祖山戒禅师、驸马都尉李公遵勖，素所友善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159042_comment'></div>丛林匠石，禅流所宗，见师之来，则曰大乘器也，许其入室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159042_comment'></div>置水投针，理存默识，得彼心要，声问翕然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159042_comment'></div>寻至筠州洞山，自唐而来谓之洞上，长老晓聪，有名江左，韪师通悟，堪嘱后事，乃白于州，愿以法度传之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159042_comment'></div>四方禅学，闻风远至，户外待次，每至宵分，檀施委积，库司常馀百万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159042_comment'></div>黄檗山者，唐相裴休所施庄田，旧赡五百馀众，近岁僧才数十，而饘粥弗充，移师总之，清众日增而资用丰足，其为人信向如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159042_comment'></div>江南号为江山佳丽甲于天下，其岩岫峻拔，磅礴千里者，庐阜为最。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159042_comment'></div>梵刹相照，其间名古佛道场者，山之阳则曰归宗，据云水之都要；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159042_comment'></div>山之西则有云居，览泉石之幽邃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159042_comment'></div>皆学佛者之所辐凑，统领茍非其人，则去者半矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159042_comment'></div>今丽正直院祖君无择、河东部宪程君师孟并著好贤乐善之名，继守南康军，祖召师临归宗，程徙师主云居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159042_comment'></div>咸率群官列名而邀之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159042_comment'></div>所至选择名僧自随，为其羽翼，故学徒加众，厨廪加丰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159042_comment'></div>提唱宗乘，言出意表，啐啄之机，不涉名相，或纵或夺，遂至无言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159042_comment'></div>嗣其法而居师席、处名山者，不可胜数，其服人心如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159042_comment'></div>厥后以舟楫往来，衣冠之士至星子者，咸欲见之，故再涖归宗，从众愿也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159042_comment'></div>其在洞山时，尝自甓寿藏，为终焉之计矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159042_comment'></div>后二十岁，凡四徙禅席，而终于归宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159042_comment'></div>乃知有才德者，无意于隐显，而人自归之，名自从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159042_comment'></div>观师之出处，真无求于人，古之有道者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159042_comment'></div>初以驸马李公荐其名而赐紫方袍，皇祐中，特恩赐号妙圆大师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159042_comment'></div>至和元年十月二十八日示疾，十一月一日斋毕，辞众端坐示寂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159042_comment'></div>十八日全身入塔，俗寿七十七，僧腊五十一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159042_comment'></div>既没六年，门人松思以状来乞铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1159042_comment'></div>乃铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_1159042'>彼上人者，丛林独步。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1159042_comment'></div>激扬宗旨，慈心广度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1159042_comment'></div>言发其机，俾之自悟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1159042_comment'></div>人得其要，直趋觉路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1159042_comment'></div>横杖而来，舍筏而去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1159042_comment'></div>吁嗟妙圆，人天仰慕。</div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1159042_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

-----title
松滋
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='1fd53b6d691a41a4bd70d61d3904be70_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("1fd53b6d691a41a4bd70d61d3904be70");'><span id='1fd53b6d691a41a4bd70d61d3904be70_link'
