href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1032&endYear=1032')">1032年12月</a>　到任，与江陵府胡旦唱和，有诗。作品：和胡学士馆中庭树。<div id='poem_99481' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99481' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99481?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和胡学士馆中庭树</a><span class='authorDate'>（1032年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99481")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_99481_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99481'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99481'>仙材封植九重深，苒苒何年别故林。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99481_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99481'>晓色半笼青琐闼，春光长在玉山岑。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99481_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99481'>静临高阁翻清吹，坐见羁禽息密阴。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99481_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99481'>休羡井梧能待凤，凌霜坚守岁寒心。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99481_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_99481'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_99481_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1032&endYear=1032')">1032年12月</a>　为汉成帝时期浈阳（广东英德）进士何丹题诗。作品：句（要知当日循良吏）<div id='poem_99580' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99580' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99580?labeling=true' target='_blank'>句<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1032年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99580")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_99580_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99580'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99580'>要知当日循良吏，留得松南堕泪碑<span class='inlineComment2'>（松滋令何丹墓）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99580_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99580'></div><div id='poem_sentence_1_99580_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_99580'><span class='label'>按：</span>何氏《庐江书院通谱》<br /></div><div id='poem_note_99580_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1033&endYear=1033')">1033年</a>　许申回京在刑部任职，向参知政事薛奎举荐余靖《修三史奏议》作品：撰修三史奏议。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1033&endYear=1033')">1033年4月</a>　仁宗亲政，召还宋绶、范仲淹，罢吕夷简等，以李迪为相。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1033&endYear=1033')">1033年</a>　进京前，余靖应邀撰文。作品：楚州团练推官厅壁记。宋故峡州军事推官赠太常博士魏公墓志并序。<div id='poem_1158979' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158979' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158979?labeling=true' target='_blank'>楚州团练推官厅壁记</a><span class='authorDate'>（明道二年五月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158979")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158979_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158979'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158979'>汉制：部从事佐刺史提政纲而舒卷之，其编氓劳逸，群吏善否，钱刀盈缩，狱犴邪正，无虑朱出墨入，咸得婉美其画，白府而损益焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158979_comment'></div>有唐天宝之后，宿兵四郊，分建元戎以屏王室，大者拥旄而制数郡，其次持节而颛一州，各立监佐辅其条教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158979_comment'></div>然郡曹掾不得闻军谋，军尉于民事亦如之，兼而赞者，必求文雅之士为其上宾，故参谋幕府，沿使名而命之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158979_comment'></div>山阳，楚之东都，北缭淮，东负海，漕渠贯中，天下辐辏者半，四达用武之国，南走广陵为大府，故持节者不得制旁郡，团练之名，得于此矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158979_comment'></div>皇朝命文吏领州，将惩诸侯之专也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158979_comment'></div>宾佐之任委于选部，累资计考，不由辟召，而主礼轻矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158979_comment'></div>先是，团练推官受署之馆，位得其表，接宾客，分曹局，列厨厩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158979_comment'></div>容妻子，各有攸处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158979_comment'></div>前居是官者，才谫而权不足，郡都尉缘隙而豪夺之，徙居河亭，才庇风雨，近市而嚣，焚巢而危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158979_comment'></div>孰谓宫庭，返隘民舍，枝梧湫底，何以观政？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158979_comment'></div>兰陵萧君，江左之秀，由进士擢第，再命而佐楚，会某人为太守，仁贤协赞，纲领克振，民得和气，军无怨声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158979_comment'></div>议政之暇，谋及居室，乃根源前事，上白廷中，愿迁爽垲，以正民之瞻视，诏可其奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158979_comment'></div>乃择地于子城之东南隅，出帑金、市山材、兴卒徒、利工器，一毫不取于民间，费府缗若干万，考室若干。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158979_comment'></div>上栋下宇，可以避燥湿；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158979_comment'></div>高闳厚垣，可以卜清旷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158979_comment'></div>噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158979_comment'></div>世之处官局者，茍非因循卑陋，则兴役动众，疲劳下民矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158979_comment'></div>今萧君革因循之弊，绝罢劳之役，而安厥居，愈见其兼济之能也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158979_comment'></div>异时享大名器，佐王之国，则观其佐东诸侯之政，斯得之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158979_comment'></div>若乃楶棁轮奂，亭圃嘉美，本无意于华侈，故略之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1158979_comment'></div>明道二年五月日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1158979_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1159040' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159040' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159040?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宋故峡州军事推官赠太常博士魏公墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（并序　明道二年十二月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1033年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1159040")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159040_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159040'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159040'>公讳清，字友置，洪州南昌县灌城乡龙沙里人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159040_comment'></div>毕万始赏，世为晋卿；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159040_comment'></div>韩、赵协力，终践侯爵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159040_comment'></div>因国命氏，子孙繁焉，相曹公族，蝉联于汉晋矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159040_comment'></div>曾祖玭、祖爽、考谠，并以唐祚衰季，帅臣专兵，割裂土壤，喋血为纵横之业，进则私署，耻为陪臣，繇是潜德丘园，不食其粟，家世以财雄州党。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159040_comment'></div>公昆仲四人，求分父产，人人自佔其膏腴，公悉以服玩田宅让之，脱身而去，独取犀带一条，市书力学，退居西山，名溢人口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159040_comment'></div>李氏窃据江左，自称后唐，封拜予夺之柄自专之，我宋开国，始授正朔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159040_comment'></div>公闻其顺命，乃萌筮仕之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159040_comment'></div>开宝三年，犹以礼部侍郎张洎私掌贡籍，公以进士中其选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159040_comment'></div>李主批云：「魏某励志谨行，学有馀文，与二三子不同，可特放及第」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159040_comment'></div>释褐授饶州馀干尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159040_comment'></div>艨艟东下，青盖入洛，公授王命为滑州灵河尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159040_comment'></div>将漕臣樊知古上殿奏公富文达学，吏材干敏，中旨召赴阙，将加显秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159040_comment'></div>引对之日，逆气并喘，口噤不能语，诏授散官以就土地之医，除陈州参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159040_comment'></div>二年，疾愈，州将奏公云：「烦而使之，屡观错节，文长笺奏，政兼威惠，愿加擢用，以励能者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159040_comment'></div>顷之，中旨复令诣阙，学士院召试，授许州临颍主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159040_comment'></div>公以江南擢第，非王室之命，故授官不复以科名为叙，仍自临颍再应进士举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159040_comment'></div>京辅近藩，尤重举首，公就试，群士亡出其右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159040_comment'></div>明年，殿廷覆试，中甲科，时端拱二年也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159040_comment'></div>御试前一日，公肺忓胸喘，坐卧艰苦，呻吟危笃之际，沈然而寐，梦一道士谓公曰：「姓名定矣，勿复忧之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159040_comment'></div>中夕痊平，诘早赴赤墀之试，亡恙焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159040_comment'></div>初，礼部籍奏公名在九十一，暨临轩唱第，名次如旧，事与梦叶，闻者异之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159040_comment'></div>授保信军节度推官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159040_comment'></div>两川地险，人心如之，宾筹幕画，咸择声称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159040_comment'></div>移阆州观察推官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159040_comment'></div>居亡何，黄巾窃发，军城失守，民溃其上，力所不支，郡无良将，遁以避难，降资授峡州军事推官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159040_comment'></div>秩满归阙，咸平四年季夏五月十三日，以疾终于辇下，享年六十三岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1159040_comment'></div>散官至给事郎，兼官至大理评事，累赠至太常博士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1159040_comment'></div>公简而不倨，廉隅自守，在官三十年，俸给之外，秋毫无横入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1159040_comment'></div>性宽厚，未尝失色于人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1159040_comment'></div>即世之日，家无馀财，识者称之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1159040_comment'></div>夫人乐氏，以屯田君贵，封河南县太君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1159040_comment'></div>生五子：长曰英、次曰蒙，并遗名好遁，混迹闾里；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1159040_comment'></div>次曰庄，咸平三年进士及第，即屯田君也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1159040_comment'></div>次曰旧、次曰芳，皆早世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1159040_comment'></div>二女：长适进士刘觉，次适进士尹中正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1159040_comment'></div>屯田君羁贯之岁，公即器之，尝谓亲旧曰：「待第三子成名，吾死无憾矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1159040_comment'></div>果以屯田君登第之明年而卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1159040_comment'></div>知子莫若父，岂虚语哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1159040_comment'></div>明道二年，屯田君罢守晋康郡，乃曰：「有父不葬，终身之戚」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1159040_comment'></div>遂露章乞告便道归营窀穸之事，朝旨从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1159040_comment'></div>以其年十月抵豫章，兆有日矣，河南君寻以寿终，乃祔焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1159040_comment'></div>府君自咸平辛丑岁卒，明道癸酉岁始克襄事，而河南君发纼同归蒿里，死生之会期有数欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1159040_comment'></div>以是年十二月十九日，皆窆于新建县善政乡罗埇里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1159040_comment'></div>乃为铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_44_1159040'>弈世潜德，运遘衰微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1159040_comment'></div>丁年筮仕，识照安危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1159040_comment'></div>项灭归汉，吴亡得机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1159040_comment'></div>才高命蹇，毕世早飞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1159040_comment'></div>乌经卜宅，鸾鉴同归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1159040_comment'></div>死生离合，各有其期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1159040_comment'></div>西山巍巍，铭旌依依。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1159040_comment'></div>此焉壤树，行路兴悲。</div><div id='poem_sentence_51_1159040_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
寿阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='5d01b207432f49be944b0cca44f96dbb_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("5d01b207432f49be944b0cca44f96dbb");'><span id='5d01b207432f49be944b0cca44f96dbb_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1036&endYear=1036')">1036年</a>，37岁</div><div id='5d01b207432f49be944b0cca44f96dbb' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1036&endYear=1036')">1036年5月</a>　自此，余靖名声大振朝野。其友石介闻靖贬，曾约靖到山西寿阳其岳丈家亭园小住叙旧。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
阳新
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='811ba25f20c74a9cabca9651147ca151_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("811ba25f20c74a9cabca9651147ca151");'><span id='811ba25f20c74a9cabca9651147ca151_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1036&endYear=1036')">1036年</a>，37岁</div><div id='811ba25f20c74a9cabca9651147ca151' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1036&endYear=1036')">1036年9月</a>　应兴国军知军事王以道邀请，由长江入富水到永兴县，作记。作品：兴国军重修文宣王庙记。<div id='poem_1158975' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158975' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158975?labeling=true' target='_blank'>兴国军重修文宣王庙记</a><span class='authorDate'>（景祐三年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158975")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158975_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158975'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158975'>孔子抗帝王之法于六经，而百世宗之，故其血食与学校无穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158975_comment'></div>然教之兴衰，存乎其时，惟至治之代，其道乃大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158975_comment'></div>在汉四叶，始建郡国之学而进儒术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158975_comment'></div>在唐六帝，乃克用王礼而尊夫子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158975_comment'></div>五代兵革，虽祀典不废，羽籥弦颂之音盖寝矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158975_comment'></div>圣宋在宥，七纪于兹，今上纂三圣之丕烈，综御大器，息武行文，泽浸八荒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158975_comment'></div>常以只日视朝，双日讲学，间岁程文擢多士，故天下靡然知所向焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158975_comment'></div>郡诸侯独大府剧部能以营葺黉舍为请，率报闻从之，馀或专于督狱赋政而未遑暇，朝廷亦置之不问，在其自视何如耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158975_comment'></div>兴国军者，本隶武昌，以摘山鼓铁之利，遂建军壁，故庙学草创而不完。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158975_comment'></div>景祐受册之明年，太原王君以成均博士知军事，刚断柔惠，敷和于下，剔去蠹螫，民怀其生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158975_comment'></div>柅车期年，简肃成政，乃谓其僚曰：「古之善教，自学校始，家塾党庠，职在乡老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158975_comment'></div>况今领县立社，以有兹土，人不知学，何以示教？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158975_comment'></div>先圣先师之祠，而不若淫昏之鬼，何以示德？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158975_comment'></div>二者皆为政所当先也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158975_comment'></div>惟旧祠在牙城之西，风隤雨隙，不自撑梧，先生弟子，居无容席之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158975_comment'></div>岁率常祀，俯仰其间，实所病焉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158975_comment'></div>于是度费饬材，以萃百工，罢不急之用而用之，不疮于民，不割于公，而霈然馀力，以克有成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158975_comment'></div>露寝奕奕，负阴向明，龙卷玉璪，颙昂其象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158975_comment'></div>廉陛严峻，庭序闳廓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158975_comment'></div>凡爵于唐、赞于先朝，作配从祀，及得图形太学者，塑坐绘立，咸备其制，向之不如制者，悉俾新之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1158975_comment'></div>筵开<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_20_1158975", 1158975, "Clauses/83/Comments/0")'>黉堂</span>，以登师儒，局列校室，以来隽秀，是焉者，处于东偏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1158975_comment'></div>又为二库，藏赐书以勖生徒之业，椟礼器以谨春秋之祀，是焉者，居于西偏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1158975_comment'></div>学之稽古，先乎制度，乃案三代车旂器服，图之屋壁，使来者观之，焕然在前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1158975_comment'></div>祀之有斋，致其虔恭，复筑斋室于宫之南，湖光上照，山翠欲滴，太虚之庭，垢虑可涤，事神诲人之道备矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1158975_comment'></div>新宫既就，而行礼其中，邦人怡然知学校之所以为教也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1158975_comment'></div>宾僚以书来俾为记，将伐石而刻之，以永其寿年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1158975_comment'></div>昔鲁人美僖公遵伯禽之法，能修泮宫，播在《诗·颂》，盖以能修其宫，又修其化，故国人思乐泮水而往观之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1158975_comment'></div>礼有饮酒养老之仪，兵有受成告克之事，咸在泮焉，则化民成俗之道，舍此宜何先哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1158975_comment'></div>王君能尊仲尼无穷之教，宣当世所宜之治，修祠宫，建学馆，知为政之本，故不敢让而记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1158975_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
高安
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='7e636279e6744301b91c0897a28c1c2b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("7e636279e6744301b91c0897a28c1c2b");'><span id='7e636279e6744301b91c0897a28c1c2b_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1036&endYear=1038')">1036-1038年</a>，37-39岁</div><div id='7e636279e6744301b91c0897a28c1c2b' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1036&endYear=1036')">1036年</a>　同榜进士周尧卿知高安县，靖为筠州酒税后，周相迎叙旧。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1037&endYear=1037')">1037年</a>　筠州荒僻，以产酒闻。靖到任后，除恪守本职外，还协助周尧卿整治街道，作记。作品：筠州新砌街记。<div id='poem_1158980' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158980' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158980?labeling=true' target='_blank'>筠州新砌街记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1037年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158980")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158980_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158980'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158980'>予至筠州之明年，道者僧体谦袖谒及门，既坐，遂言本永嘉人，寓筠二年，去居庐山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158980_comment'></div>筠之崇善者曰吴太元命之复来，募众得钱一千万，召工凿山陶土，得石与塼若干千万，砌成大道，北断于江，其南西缭于阛阓，凡若干万尺；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158980_comment'></div>横渠暗窦，为桥以通之，凡若干所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158980_comment'></div>喜舍之士以道计者，自五百尺至百尺，凡若干人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158980_comment'></div>以钱计者，自三十万至一万，凡若干人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158980_comment'></div>一万而下，不可胜计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158980_comment'></div>所得钱不以簪毫自私，皆寄某氏之帑，朱出墨入，悉某氏主之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158980_comment'></div>麻衣草屩，以董众役，暮宿甄舍，饥食于施者家，凡若干年而工毕，乞书其事而志之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158980_comment'></div>吁！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158980_comment'></div>今夫地征物赋，官司列榜笞，谨期会，上监下督，民犹有靳固而逋负者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158980_comment'></div>至以西方之教，一呼于众，则发畜积割珍爱，欣然无所惜，其故何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158980_comment'></div>盖儒以礼法御当世，使人迁善而去恶；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158980_comment'></div>佛以因果诲未来，使人修福而避祸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158980_comment'></div>然世有积善而遇祸，积恶而蒙福者，虽有仁智，无如之何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158980_comment'></div>释之徒则曰：彼前世之所为，今获其报耳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158980_comment'></div>今世之脩，报在来世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158980_comment'></div>又言：没有天堂、地狱、苦乐之趣，次序纤悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158980_comment'></div>故无刑而威，无爵而劝，归之者如川之流，壅之不停，去之不竭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158980_comment'></div>其为教大抵若是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158980_comment'></div>其有窃佛之权，愚弄于众，财未入手，先营其私，衣华暖，居宏丽，瞰甘脆，极力肆意无畏惮者，十六七焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1158980_comment'></div>彼上人者，独弊衣粝食，苦其行而外其利，又能得开信同心，成此利益，使夫趋官曹、游旅肆者，出滓泥、入清净之境，真奉佛事、励戒行而好方便者也，志之无愧词。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1158980_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1037&endYear=1037')">1037年</a>　去年在集贤校理任期间，审乐律未了，至此始上奏，转呈有司。作品：议李照所定乐。<div id='poem_1158808' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158808' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158808?labeling=true' target='_blank'>议李照所定乐奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（景祐四年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158808")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158808_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158808'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158808'>臣闻道路传言，已降指挥：今月十六日皇帝御后殿，令中书、枢密院及修书臣僚同于上前详议李照、胡瑗所定乐是非事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158808_comment'></div>臣窃谓乐者因声以布其和，声者因器以宣其用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158808_comment'></div>故假金石以为器，然后声得其和；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158808_comment'></div>分宫商以为音，然后乐可以审。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158808_comment'></div>今李照之说，形器可辨；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158808_comment'></div>胡瑗之议，音律未传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158808_comment'></div>以此而欲定优劣，不亦难乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158808_comment'></div>又况言有辨讷，意有巧拙，又安能顷刻之间定之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158808_comment'></div>臣又以为古之作乐者，知声有清浊，故吹律以制其中；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158808_comment'></div>恐久而失传，故累黍以存其法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158808_comment'></div>后世增损，不能识其本声，若以古法求之，尚或得其髣髴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158808_comment'></div>疑古而不用，未知凭何可从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158808_comment'></div>况胡瑗所定，颇有经据，何不试令造钟磬一编，与李照之乐，更可迭奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158808_comment'></div>取其丝竹之声，谐和而不相夺者，定以为优，而后行用，彼时集议，亦未为晚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158808_comment'></div>臣顷闻谈者云云，并言李照学无师法，自传损益，又挟阎文应以为内助，故得纷然恣其偏见，而律度疏长，钟声振作，不守古制，不可垂法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158808_comment'></div>察于众言，照未全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158808_comment'></div>若以乐为政之大者，当谨重改作，则宜谨于李照未改之前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158808_comment'></div>今既改而未定，又宜详考律吕，审酌制度，以防其失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158808_comment'></div>臣故谓当令胡瑗作为钟磬，而与照乐两辨其声，然后是非灼然，如在衡鉴，不辨而可知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158808_comment'></div>臣不任区区瞽言待罪之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1158808_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1037&endYear=1037')">1037年</a>　同榜进士李之才知福清县，路经筠州探靖，靖作五律送。作品：送李廷评知福清县。<div id='poem_99495' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99495' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99495?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送李廷评知福清县</a><span class='authorDate'>（1037年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99495")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_99495_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99495'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99495'>世阀茂<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_99495", 99495, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>儒绅</span>，瓯闽宠命新。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99495_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99495'>县图遥尽海，乡树密藏春。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99495_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99495'>供帐莺将老，登车雉已驯。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99495_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99495'>行闻趋召节，旧美政如神。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99495_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_99495'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_99495_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1037&endYear=1037')">1037年</a>　长孙尧臣生，家人千里迢迢来报喜。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1038')">1038年</a>　弟希翊之子仲华、孙嗣隆出生，靖六女德卿生。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1038')">1038年1月</a>　作记，凿之于壁。作品：筠州洞山普利禅院传法记。<div id='poem_1159000' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159000' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159000?labeling=true' target='_blank'>筠州洞山普利禅院传法记</a><span class='authorDate'>（景祐五年正月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1159000")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159000_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159000'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159000'>近世分禅、律为二学，其所居之长，禅以德、律以亲而授之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159000_comment'></div>以德者选于众，而归之者亦众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159000_comment'></div>夫言德者，非世所谓德也，以其等空妄、超渐次、出死生，可以为天人师者耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159000_comment'></div>故祖祖孙孙，称佛嗣焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159000_comment'></div>筠之望山曰新丰，洞有佛刹曰普利禅院，唐咸通中，悟本大师始剪荆而居之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159000_comment'></div>悟本得心印于药山俨，俨得于云岩晟，晟得于石头迁，迁得于青原思，思得于曹溪能，是为六祖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159000_comment'></div>自释迦如来二十九世而至达摩传中国，五世而至曹溪，又五世而至悟本，凡三十九世矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159000_comment'></div>及悟本之即世也，得法而去者，道全居中山，道虔居青林，相继来嗣之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159000_comment'></div>悟本又传曹山寂，寂传道延，居鹿头。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159000_comment'></div>及道虔卒，鹿头又续之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159000_comment'></div>鹿头延卒，其门人惠敏袭之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159000_comment'></div>惠敏卒，嗣和尚自净业来继之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159000_comment'></div>李氏之称国主也，觉海国尊师启大道场于金陵之报恩，其嫡曰文坦，被黄纸诏书，赐号大沙门，来统之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159000_comment'></div>云门真禅师之上足曰清禀，亦奉主命来后之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159000_comment'></div>禀卒，而豫章彦闻因之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159000_comment'></div>及彦闻而衰矣，辄以院付其徒，檀越不可，乃疏请九峰守诠绍之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159000_comment'></div>九峰亦本境之名蓝也，移法席至是山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159000_comment'></div>五年，复为庐山栖贤所请而去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159000_comment'></div>诠传曲江晓聪，聪传合淝自宝，宝又传曲江鉴迁，绳绳兴之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159000_comment'></div>宝师得法于黄梅聪，与迁皆云门之嗣孙，自悟本主迁，或绝或承，凡十三代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159000_comment'></div>诠徙栖贤，宝徙黄檗，自聪已上，皆终焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159000_comment'></div>悟本讳俍价，越州诸暨人，姓俞氏，年十二，师事五泄；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159000_comment'></div>二十一，受具于嵩山睿律师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159000_comment'></div>慕南宗之学，南游江湘，得云岩而事之终其身，毕丧而后去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159000_comment'></div>遇武宗之诏，遂民服隐于箕州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159000_comment'></div>及宣皇御宇，乃复僧仪，南至高安之所丰洞，邑豪雷衡之山也，见其泉石幽奇，乃曰：「此大乘所居之地」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159000_comment'></div>言于雷氏，雷氏施之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1159000_comment'></div>初，山多蛇虎，师庵居一宿，蛇虎尽去，至今山无虎焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1159000_comment'></div>留居十八年，名声四传，来学者五百馀众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1159000_comment'></div>坐谈立悟，虚来实去者，不可胜数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1159000_comment'></div>名闻京师，天子赐咸通广福寺额并一钟焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1159000_comment'></div>寻以咸通十年三月顺世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1159000_comment'></div>先期其日，期至而去，徒众环泣，师瞑而复觉曰：「心无所依，是真修行，何有悲喜？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1159000_comment'></div>勿惊吾也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1159000_comment'></div>复令为斋七日，乃具师食讫，沐浴安坐，歛容而化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1159000_comment'></div>葬于山之阳，敕谥悟本大师，塔曰惠觉之塔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1159000_comment'></div>师能攻苦率众，衣无䌽，卧无褥，炉无炭，室无烛，故后世以简约相承焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1159000_comment'></div>集《大乘经要》一卷，行于世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1159000_comment'></div>中山全姓宣氏，常州人，以其尝居隽水之中山，故号中山和尚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1159000_comment'></div>中和二年，镇南节度使钟传实召以来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1159000_comment'></div>景福二年，避寇于分宁，制置戴尚书迎居龙安院，明年坐亡于龙安，归葬寺之东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1159000_comment'></div>青林虔姓陈氏，杭州馀杭人，初谒悟本，悟本曰：「此子向后走杀天下人」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1159000_comment'></div>广明初抵南郑，遇贼巢之乱，驾幸梁、洋，时有中贵人姓第五者，见师，瞻视良久，曰：「此是法王，非同龙象也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1159000_comment'></div>自汉东之青林，亦钟镇南召之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1159000_comment'></div>天祐元年灭度，门人录其语三百节，为《玄机示诲集》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1159000_comment'></div>鹿头延姓刘氏，福州长乐人，江南武义二年，自鹿头至，凡三年而示寂，全身瘗于寺南，赐谥洪果大师，塔曰惠光之塔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1159000_comment'></div>敏姓李氏，蜀之华阳人，从洪果来，及其终而代焉，保大六年，迁化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1159000_comment'></div>嗣姓周氏，同郡高安人，金陵召见，深加信重，乾德二年顺寂，塔于惠光之北。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1159000_comment'></div>坦姓吴氏，建州建阳人，李主以其国命命之，凡四年而终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1159000_comment'></div>禀姓李氏，泉州仙游人，李主召入澄心堂，集诸方语要，凡十年，又俾来继坦焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1159000_comment'></div>彦闻以疾而间其位，故衰，凡三年而卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1159000_comment'></div>诠，金陵人，自九峰来居，五年，大壮其栋宇而新之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1159000_comment'></div>既赴栖贤之请，以首座聪嘱檀那及其众，众从之，请于州，州从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1159000_comment'></div>聪姓杜氏，大中祥符三年，实应是命，于山之东北，手植松可万株，凡植一株，坐诵《金刚经》一卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1159000_comment'></div>常自称栽松比丘，今号其地为金刚岭云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1159000_comment'></div>聪临终而让宝，如聪之始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1159000_comment'></div>聪之终也，遗诫于其众，无服衰绖，哭泣吊慰，一切绝之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1159000_comment'></div>其寺之再兴也，诠始缉之，聪又能经纬，至宝而纪纲大备焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1159000_comment'></div>宝姓吴氏，开堂十六年，未尝出院门，自江湖之南及岭之南，二十馀州闻其名者，岁奉钱共数十万以供其堂，其为人信向如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1159000_comment'></div>亦种杉万株，皆手自培斸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1159000_comment'></div>同郡有黄檗山某院，唐裴丞相休之功德院也，岁入丰而主者侵牟之，众食不足，思有德者为之长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1159000_comment'></div>景祐四年，自太守而下，列名请其行，又俾其自择人而付之，得迁焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1159000_comment'></div>居黄檗未十日，四方至者仅百人，盖其道可师者邪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1159000_comment'></div>迁姓某氏，亦能守宝之规而不敢加焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1159000_comment'></div>某上书失职，来是郡，得其传法之次叙而记之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1159000_comment'></div>景祐五年龙集戊寅正月日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_65_1159000_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1038')">1038年2月</a>　转官，因去年十二月京师及并、代、忻州皆地震，有官员劝仁宗“深自咎责”，大理评事苏舜钦言“修已以御人，洗心以鉴物，劝听断，舍燕安，放弃优谐近习之纤人，亲刚明鲠直之良士，以思永图”，范仲淹等皆得近徙，靖改监泰州酒税。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
泰州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='fa4c168d43bb4749bcf2d367a9ae7747_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("fa4c168d43bb4749bcf2d367a9ae7747");'><span id='fa4c168d43bb4749bcf2d367a9ae7747_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1038')">1038年</a>，39岁</div><div id='fa4c168d43bb4749bcf2d367a9ae7747' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1038')">1038年7月</a>　王式病逝，靖为作铭。作品：宋故大理寺丞知梅州王君墓碣铭。<div id='poem_1159027' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159027' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159027?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宋故大理寺丞知梅州王君墓碣铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1038年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1159027")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159027_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159027'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159027'>王氏之盛于天下旧矣，以望别族者，秦之郡五、汉之郡一十六。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159027_comment'></div>公之望实出太原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159027_comment'></div>自司马氏南渡，而诸王世为辅弼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159027_comment'></div>梁永宁郡公、侍中、尚书令僧辩生顗，顗生圭，唐贞观中宰相，以亮直称为名臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159027_comment'></div>圭子敬直，尚南平公主，拜驸马都尉，坐事贬死岭南，子孙留者，因为曲江著姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159027_comment'></div>虽世袭簪绅不绝，而禄卑不得谱于国史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159027_comment'></div>曾大父讳某，大父讳当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159027_comment'></div>刘氏自即尊号，族人仕者皆得美官，独父子幅巾高蹈，不嗅其饵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159027_comment'></div>考讳临，字嘉谋，皇朝以乡邑器望署潮州司理参军，卒官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159027_comment'></div>公讳式，字用之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159027_comment'></div>十四而孤，耿介自立，以学行见称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159027_comment'></div>举进士，得秘书省校书郎，历广州、虔州、南安军司理参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159027_comment'></div>入朝，除大理寺丞、知吉州永新县，以能闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159027_comment'></div>明年，移知梅州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159027_comment'></div>景祐五年七月卒于治所，享年六十五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159027_comment'></div>公沉厚方直，敦尚名教，自幼孤至白首，贯以一节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159027_comment'></div>旧制：岭表按察官岁调郡县掾佐，阙员，取进士再举、明经三举下入太常第者试摄其事，三载不瘝厥职，乃送吏部为品官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159027_comment'></div>邦人自为南选，常才趋之唯恐不及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159027_comment'></div>公尝喟然曰：「曲江自文献公后，士大夫鲜复以科第取显爵于朝，岂南方以此选诱人为卑耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159027_comment'></div>吾为州党项领，期于展力从官，讵宜碌碌齿其间」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159027_comment'></div>由是自弱冠捧乡老书游场屋三十年，终不屈意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159027_comment'></div>暨上第，时母夫人犹在堂，升堂拜嘉，闾里始归其高焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159027_comment'></div>今天子初践祚，在谅闇，不待祥禫，即临轩，急于采撷天下俊异，而曲江联翩六人中第，皆公之力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159027_comment'></div>六人即公及子陶，馀若靖辈，悉尝趋函丈焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159027_comment'></div>郡守嘉尚，缕陈其事，乞改公所居之乡曰兴文、里曰折桂，诏可其奏，邦邑荣之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159027_comment'></div>三为决曹掾，以清慎自守，发擿奸伏、湔洗良善，期于详允，狱无隐情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159027_comment'></div>虽苛吏把其上，狡胥穴其下，不敢簪毫夺其理，卒以雪枉改官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1159027_comment'></div>其宰永新也，俗固好讼，而当官者复侵涣之，公一皆痛刮其弊，民戴之如父母焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1159027_comment'></div>公始掾南海，遭内难解官，在始衰之年而致毁过制，遂以气恙，到梅之三月，疾作，不及成政而捐馆舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1159027_comment'></div>公志尚高洁，义不茍合，训子弟有常检，接僚友无戏言，闻人之善，谈不虚口，其不善者，疾如仇雠，真所谓古之君子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1159027_comment'></div>夫人余氏，乡邦令望，明淑贤懿，上奉其姑，下抚其族，于公内助为多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1159027_comment'></div>二子：长曰陶，信州军事推官；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1159027_comment'></div>次曰防，亦举进士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1159027_comment'></div>孙男六人、孙女五人，皆幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1159027_comment'></div>公之初丧也，引柩西还，藁葬其郊居之侧，至某年某月某日，以礼襄事于兴文乡折桂里厚富原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1159027_comment'></div>以靖幸而交其父子间，兼师友之重，使来索铭，以表其墓，乃铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_35_1159027'>韶山之秀，发为俊茂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1159027_comment'></div>清识懿文，南州领袖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1159027_comment'></div>人趋禄仕，不羞茍得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1159027_comment'></div>公独夷由，决于翰墨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1159027_comment'></div>五试文昌，晚成之光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1159027_comment'></div>三掾决曹，罔私毫芒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1159027_comment'></div>明照隐诋，民不冤死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1159027_comment'></div>入奏天子，乃丞大理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1159027_comment'></div>试政蒲芦，五柳双凫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1159027_comment'></div>锄强息弱，百里以苏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1159027_comment'></div>期年成绩，部符岭阨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1159027_comment'></div>车茵未温，卧篑已易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1159027_comment'></div>旌旐西还，霜凄露漙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1159027_comment'></div>福不盈皆，俄归九原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1159027_comment'></div>惟公之德，倜傥殊特。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1159027_comment'></div>身虽云亡，留为轨则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1159027_comment'></div>词学起家，义方教子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1159027_comment'></div>有诏旌之，文乡桂里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1159027_comment'></div>胡为石彦，累世弗显。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1159027_comment'></div>才不谁知，卒于遐远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1159027_comment'></div>势薄地寒，不贵不年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1159027_comment'></div>廷尉高门，在于后昆。</div><div id='poem_sentence_56_1159027_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='4dbb525d30624ffea45c7c6bd6ab41d3_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("4dbb525d30624ffea45c7c6bd6ab41d3");'><span id='4dbb525d30624ffea45c7c6bd6ab41d3_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1039&endYear=1039')">1039年</a>，40岁</div><div id='4dbb525d30624ffea45c7c6bd6ab41d3' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1039&endYear=1039')">1039年1月</a>　应邀作文。作品：韶州新修望京楼记。韶州光运寺重修证真照寂大师塔铭。<div id='poem_1158967' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158967' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158967?labeling=true' target='_blank'>韶州新修望京楼记<span class='inlineComment2'>（宝元□年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1039年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158967")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158967_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158967'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158967'>广之旁郡一十五，韶最大，在楚为边邑，在越为交衢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158967_comment'></div>治城居武水东，真水西<span class='inlineComment2'>（古名虎溪，唐讳虎字曰武。）</span>，境压骑田、大庾二岭，故地最善而名著。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158967_comment'></div>均之远官，得名城暨善地，故其择守于等夷，阅人最贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158967_comment'></div>唐、汉之西都也，繇湘、衡而得骑田，故武水最要；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158967_comment'></div>今天子都大梁，浮江、淮而得大庾，故真水最便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158967_comment'></div>骑田虽乘驲旧途，而王官往来太平水道，是以风亭水馆、高台上舍，徙在真水，不视溪山巧拙，而偏诊左臂者，势使之然耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158967_comment'></div>今郡守河内常公承命而典城也，心乐易而政悉精力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158967_comment'></div>先是，郡岁课丁夫刺船南海，馈盐数十万石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158967_comment'></div>俗固绵力而薄产矣，又重之以困扰，日益窘急，而繁狱讼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158967_comment'></div>公之下车，适遇主计集贤张公温之，乃谋所以息民之策，斥工巧占名之卒以代之，故民释重负，邦事亦简。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158967_comment'></div>人和于下，嘉气应之，风雨以时，百谷用登，政有馀力，而废堕兹缉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158967_comment'></div>惟虎溪浮航之道带绕闉下，揵闭仅存，而雉堞楼橹之制弛然莫具，前所谓偏诊左臂之失也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158967_comment'></div>公因暇日，抚睥睨而四顾，则山川郁葱之气，森然满目，既叹且喜其久蔽而有待乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158967_comment'></div>乃命畚颓土，完缺甃，饬美材，籍士伍，顺启塞之训，以门其下，因临观之美，以台其上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158967_comment'></div>民不瘠，公不匮，而厥功以成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158967_comment'></div>飞轩缭砌，一望四野，重峦复岫，周遭万形，烟颜雨态，远近异色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158967_comment'></div>溪流浼浼，逗碧洄清，鸟声渔唱，出入杳霭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158967_comment'></div>君子谓其访境也皆绝，其命名也必古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158967_comment'></div>身居江海之上，心存魏阙之下，故额其西楼曰望京之楼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158967_comment'></div>饮醇酒者不忘于狱市，褰车帷者能广其视听，故署其入之门曰通阓之门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1158967_comment'></div>除道梁川，而邻国先交，故标其出之门曰郴阳之门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1158967_comment'></div>登高怀古，而舜祠在望，故题其北台曰闻韶之台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1158967_comment'></div>目与心俱适，心与境俱远，浩然之气，来栖人身，如蹑壶中，而眄物休也，非守臣之贤，此景孰为来哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1158967_comment'></div>檐庑环合，凡二十楹，其形胜之游，目观之美，甲于邦城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1158967_comment'></div>智者创物，夫岂徒然！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1158967_comment'></div>又况登陴之际，民瘼可询，乘传而来，郊劳为便，亦所以辅官成而尊王命也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1158967_comment'></div>时宝元□年正月日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1158967_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1159044' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159044' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159044?labeling=true' target='_blank'>韶州光运寺重修證真照寂大师塔铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（宝元三年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1039年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1159044")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159044_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159044'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159044'>世称佛为浮图氏，盖即其塔而名之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159044_comment'></div>释迦在世说法时云：「有过去多宝佛塔，从地踊出」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159044_comment'></div>则知塔之名制尚矣，所以严事古佛之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159044_comment'></div>佛去世后，舍利之塔遍于大千；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159044_comment'></div>祖师西来，全身之塔布在中土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159044_comment'></div>且夫气聚而形全，神散而体坏，有生之同患也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159044_comment'></div>佛以自在冥其心，故湛而常寂；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159044_comment'></div>以定力持其身，故没而不朽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159044_comment'></div>此其所以示至虚无著之性，成金刚坚固之体者欤，何其千百年间，造化寒暑，不能夺而变之耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159044_comment'></div>光运寺塔者，奉安照寂大师坐亡之全身也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159044_comment'></div>大师郴人，朱姓，讳道广。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159044_comment'></div>真性等空，大慈利物，愿力深广，存亡以之，含识蒙其润泽，故归仰亡替。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159044_comment'></div>唐天宝二年，禅坐而终，门人瘗而异香满室，乃奉其全体，覆以香泥，龛而藏之，建塔于寺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159044_comment'></div>岁或大旱，民往诚请，则获嘉澍，如远壑之应声也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159044_comment'></div>是寺以隋初建刹，故名仁寿台，及大师居之，世呼广和尚院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159044_comment'></div>至广明中，刺史谢公恶其斥贤者之号，遂以年名加之曰广明院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159044_comment'></div>刘氏专制南海，谥大师曰辅圣，又命其塔曰宝元，寺曰光运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159044_comment'></div>每岁同六祖真容，并以龙舟迎至广内，又益其谥曰證真照寂焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159044_comment'></div>开宝中，王师既克广州，遂迁其卒于京师，不乐北迁者，相率为叛，寺塔罹郁攸之祸，而晬容独存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159044_comment'></div>厥后虽构缉遗宇，力不足而屋之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159044_comment'></div>天禧初，寺僧尝欲募众，兴复兹塔，始基之而不克缔构。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159044_comment'></div>二十馀年，风隳雨蠹，栋干斯坏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159044_comment'></div>曲江素号山川奇秀，而复熏以南宗之风，由是占形胜、依邑落而树刹构舍为精庐者，差倍他境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159044_comment'></div>缁衣之徒，渡江而来，不之衡庐，则之曹溪，故其挈瓶锡、动道路、探幽深者，亦差众诸部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159044_comment'></div>郡人根性好善者，复以谈空乐施为胜，其缁徒之守戒行、兴佛事、了宗乘者，各以其气相亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159044_comment'></div>今天子以宝元受册之明年，郡郭耆寿等列名请晋康郡僧德诚、南康郡僧智润，共主营造之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159044_comment'></div>诚、润二开士，游方十馀岁，常以率导喜舍，所至开信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1159044_comment'></div>既允众诚，四方闻义，乐出财货，唯恐在后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1159044_comment'></div>凡为塔三级，藻井黼帐，髹柱绘梁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1159044_comment'></div>层檐之上，响以金铃；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1159044_comment'></div>䌽疏之外，周以庑序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1159044_comment'></div>越一岁而工毕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1159044_comment'></div>其告成也，乞词书之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1159044_comment'></div>予观大师石刻行状云：「持盂所得，同之一器，先饲贫病，然始自餐，均以精粗，等其丰鲜」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1159044_comment'></div>又曰：「吾食于人，得不同病」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1159044_comment'></div>于是感通致雨，以救岁旱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1159044_comment'></div>集是二美，推之于仁义之途，则古之博施高行君子，何以尚之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1159044_comment'></div>岂独以佛事为佞乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1159044_comment'></div>因序而铭之，不惮烦以示于后人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1159044_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_39_1159044'>施无贵贱，饭先贫病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1159044_comment'></div>慈悲普济，十地齐圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1159044_comment'></div>仰食于人，即同其忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1159044_comment'></div>言行相副，千古扬休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1159044_comment'></div>性如虚空，无住无去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1159044_comment'></div>晬容俨然，金刚坚固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1159044_comment'></div>黼座照日，宝铎鸣风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1159044_comment'></div>深诚感众，开士之功。</div><div id='poem_sentence_46_1159044_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1039&endYear=1039')">1039年</a>　苏舜钦以礼部郎中通判洪州，赴任途中，先到泰州探靖，靖作诗。作品：送苏祠部通判洪州。<div id='poem_99497' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99497' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99497?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送苏祠部通判洪州</a><span class='authorDate'>（1039年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99497")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_99497_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99497'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99497'>天家顿网极详延，果见鸿风颂得贤。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99497_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99497'>庭拜外官聊试治，史分新策入编年。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99497_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99497'>江淹赋笔虽伤别，郭泰归舟只恐仙。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99497_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99497'>南国勿思终计最，蓬丘番直即和铅。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99497_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_99497'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_99497_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1039&endYear=1039')">1039年</a>　希昱长老亦由京来探靖，作诗。作品：送希昱上人永嘉觐亲。<div id='poem_99564' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99564' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99564?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送希昱上人永嘉觐亲</a><span class='authorDate'>（1039年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99564")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_99564_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99564'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99564'>阊阖西风高，振锡吴门去。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99564_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99564'>三江碧浸天，惟持一杯渡。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99564_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99564'>败叶梧桐秋，云中永嘉树。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99564_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99564'>借问何言归，亲齿桑榆暮。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99564_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_99564'>再怀生育仁，聊为馨洁具。<div id='poem_sentence_4_99564_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_99564'>聆师金石词，郑重加钦慕。<div id='poem_sentence_5_99564_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_99564'>陆梁原上兽，群居先识母。<div id='poem_sentence_6_99564_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_99564'>嗷嗷林中乌，敛翼受子哺。<div id='poem_sentence_7_99564_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_99564'>云何蚩蚩辈，胜衣复能语。<div id='poem_sentence_8_99564_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_99564'>口腹徒自丰，骨肉如行路。<div id='poem_sentence_9_99564_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_99564'>师本谈空人，浮云无去住。<div id='poem_sentence_10_99564_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_99564'>未出轮回身，归心应有悟。<div id='poem_sentence_11_99564_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_99564'>临岐索赠言，愧乏雕章句。<div id='poem_sentence_12_99564_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_99564'>愿达采诗官，当令不孝惧。<div id='poem_sentence_13_99564_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_99564'></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_99564_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1039&endYear=1039')">1039年</a>　听朝野人士透露，当朝对范仲淹等人仍以朋党论，加以排斥贬逐。靖以父母年事已高为由呈外任状，请求南还。两浙转运副使叶清臣欲挽留，靖回启谢绝。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1039&endYear=1039')">1039年6月</a>　调知英州，有谢状。作品：谢知英州状。<div id='poem_1158919' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158919' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158919?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢知英州状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1039年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158919")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158919_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158919'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158919'>右，某伏奉圣恩，授前件差遣者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158919_comment'></div>祗荷宠光，不任感惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158919_comment'></div>伏念某才非出类，智不适时，始怀铅而备官，遽越俎而蒙罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158919_comment'></div>三迁岁历，再食门征，既无状以昭明，固甘心于弃逐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158919_comment'></div>岂谓自天洒泽，解网均恩，眷言乔木之邻邦，付以小侯之全壤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158919_comment'></div>光生里闬，便为竹马之期；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158919_comment'></div>荣被亲闱，仍遂兰陔之便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158919_comment'></div>此盖某官素垂抆拭，力掩瑕疵，致此颛愚，复沾甄录。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158919_comment'></div>敢不励精士检、祗率郡条，上答天慈，旁酬恩造。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1158919_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
湖州

-----title
大余
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='fe192a02cab344a592998d4ad3444aa6_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("fe192a02cab344a592998d4ad3444aa6");'><span id='fe192a02cab344a592998d4ad3444aa6_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1039&endYear=1039')">1039年</a>，40岁</div><div id='fe192a02cab344a592998d4ad3444aa6' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1039&endYear=1039')">1039年7月</a>　南下，途经大庾岭，作诗。作品：双松。<div id='poem_99465' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99465' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99465?labeling=true' target='_blank'>双松<span class='inlineComment2'>（在故县）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1039年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99465")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_99465_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99465'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99465'>自古咏连理，多为艳阳<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作阳艳）</span>吟。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99465_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99465'>谁知抱高节，生处亦同心。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99465_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99465'>风至应交响，禽栖得并阴。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99465_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99465'>岁寒当共守，霜雪莫相侵。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99465_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_99465'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_99465_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='e623d03e72574b02a9758cfb76d2b7b9_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e623d03e72574b02a9758cfb76d2b7b9");'><span id='e623d03e72574b02a9758cfb76d2b7b9_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年</a>，43岁</div><div id='e623d03e72574b02a9758cfb76d2b7b9' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年3月</a>　暮春，应邀到江西大庾县，作铭。作品：南安军兴福院慈氏观音堂阁碑铭。<div id='poem_1159018' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159018' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159018?labeling=true' target='_blank'>南安军兴福院慈氏观音堂阁碑铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1042年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1159018")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159018_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159018'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159018'>上古圣人，以中道御物，反于经制，然后济之以权；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159018_comment'></div>西方之教，以大权诱俗，涉其津涯，然后受之于道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159018_comment'></div>西教所以浸淫国土，千载弥盛者，以其权胜者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159018_comment'></div>且复巧于方便，起人信心，其言过去未来、祸福环转，显作而冥报，习异则业殊，故有大人之乐、诸趣之苦，盖所以警贪痴、悟颠倒也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159018_comment'></div>又所说诸佛菩萨世界名号，咸表行而著称，见名而知證，河沙算数，不能穷尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159018_comment'></div>独以慈悲愿力，推贤文殊、普贤、观音、弥勒四菩萨，能入生死海中，极度群有，同佛智见，登佛果位，超然于无学之徒，为其上首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159018_comment'></div>观音以甚深般若，克證圆通；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159018_comment'></div>弥勒以最初三昧，故名慈氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159018_comment'></div>或自在神力，能施无畏，使大千众生，免诸苦恼；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159018_comment'></div>或一生补处，受记成佛，与百亿天子，同其安稳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159018_comment'></div>由是赞叹获福，瞻仰蒙祐，闻名而不堕金刚，系念而咸生兜率，著在经具，流为善谈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159018_comment'></div>华都夷聚，罔不归向，损货竭哀，靡所悭吝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159018_comment'></div>虽事存视听之表，难以实求，纷起是非之端，或生异论，然而信心所启，不谋同听，先已胶固于中矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159018_comment'></div>南安军浮石院者，江南李氏保大年中闻僧行高结庵之地也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159018_comment'></div>振锡云游，乐兹奇胜，剪荆山麓，以卜终焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159018_comment'></div>麻麦仅充，风雨才庇，百年过隙，八世相承，皆卷道岩壑，休心息迹者耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159018_comment'></div>今住持智应，祥符年中乃结前绪，以谓独觉小善，皆声闻之果，洪愿普济，寔如来之乘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159018_comment'></div>况今天下至大，含生至众，十室之邑，必有塔庙以奉薄伽之遗像，一刹所建，必据溪山以先邑落之胜处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159018_comment'></div>钦崇虽广，废兴在人，不有庄严，何以示教？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159018_comment'></div>不有导募，谁能同心？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159018_comment'></div>当勤摄受，共令成熟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159018_comment'></div>遂倾私楮，得钱十万，命工计费，作为层构。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159018_comment'></div>上之为阁，下之为堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159018_comment'></div>其上望慈氏菩萨，拟天宫次补楼阁重重之体；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159018_comment'></div>其下为观自在菩萨，肖宝陀海岸人龙隐见之状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159018_comment'></div>皆以大悲含物，万行利生，大愿坚固，佛所称叹，将举教以劝修，俾见像而思果者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159018_comment'></div>散召檀施，共树福田，群言响答，量力出货。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1159018_comment'></div>堂皇门序，四轩环合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1159018_comment'></div>且是院也，楚岭之通衢，章江之上津，前瞰回波，却视层阜，修篁丛布，粉解玉立，真物外之绝境也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1159018_comment'></div>香火之缘，泉石之乐，居然两适矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1159018_comment'></div>工既毕，遣介赍书乞铭，旌其远诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1159018_comment'></div>乃铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_1159018'>章江之源，楚岭之通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1159018_comment'></div>粤有名蓝，字之浮石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1159018_comment'></div>开榛百年，制度翛然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1159018_comment'></div>今得其传，规模乃全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1159018_comment'></div>广示慈力，众所悲仰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1159018_comment'></div>三十二应，观音之像。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1159018_comment'></div>脱门空阔，愿海淀深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1159018_comment'></div>利益世间，慈氏之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1159018_comment'></div>睟容并列，遗芳克振。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1159018_comment'></div>庶几来者，虔恭起信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1159018_comment'></div>实义难穷，权言易从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1159018_comment'></div>违恶竦善，繄权之功。</div><div id='poem_sentence_42_1159018_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='8e8dc3748084421588303b98cc8a1a34_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("8e8dc3748084421588303b98cc8a1a34");'><span id='8e8dc3748084421588303b98cc8a1a34_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1064&endYear=1064')">1064年</a>，65岁</div><div id='8e8dc3748084421588303b98cc8a1a34' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>登大庾岭，喜见蔡氏兄弟重修梅岭关新貌，应关吏之请，欣然赋诗。作品：叱馭樓。來鴈亭。通越亭。<div id='poem_99542' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99542' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99542?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题庾岭三亭诗<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>叱驭楼</a><span class='authorDate'>（1064年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99542")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_99542_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99542'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99542'>山巅层搆与云平，贤者新题叱驭名。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99542_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99542'>为要澄清归治道，不辞艰险表忠诚。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99542_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99542'>南枝初见梅林秀，九折遥思剑栈横。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99542_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99542'>若使当时嫌远宦，海隅何得有欢声。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99542_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_99542'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_99542_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_99543' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99543' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99543?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span>来雁亭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1064年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_99543_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99543'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99543'>南方旧说无燕雁，岁序严凝亦暂来。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99543_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99543'>天外每随寒雨过，春前先逐暖风回。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99543_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99543'>人稀弋射矰休避<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：岭南射生者少。）</span>，俗厌鱼餐网莫猜。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99543_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99543'>况是弟兄封境接，登临因此几徘徊。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99543_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_99543'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_99543_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_99544' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99544' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99544?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span>通越亭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1064年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_99544_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99544'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99544'>行尽章江庾水滨，南踰梅馆陟嶙峋。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99544_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99544'>城中绍祚千年圣，海外占风九译人。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99544_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99544'>峤岭古来称绝徼，梯山从此识通津<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：蔡学士弟兄新砌岭路相接。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99544_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99544'>舆琛辇赆无虚岁，徒说周朝白雉驯。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99544_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_99544'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_99544_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

-----title
仁化
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='523ac0ee9e6842f7a6747e0a9dd4c764_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("523ac0ee9e6842f7a6747e0a9dd4c764");'><span id='523ac0ee9e6842f7a6747e0a9dd4c764_link' style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>遵母遗言，代母到仁化深山寺院还愿，有诗。作品：仁化錦石巖。游水南寺。游临江寺。晚至松门僧舍怀寄李太祝。<div id='poem_99441' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99441' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_content_99441'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99441'>巉岩绚烂倚云隈，万玉无香结作堆。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99441_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99441'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_99441_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_99524' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99524' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99524?labeling=true' target='_blank'>游水南寺</a><span class='authorDate'>（1040年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_content_99524'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99524'>双刹耸浮云，层轩绝世尘。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99524_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99524_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99524'>暂来犹永日，堪羡白莲人。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99524_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_99524'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_99524_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_99526' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99526' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a
