-----title
曲江
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='4dcc14cf7245483cb5ebf4fd8dcb0c56_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("4dcc14cf7245483cb5ebf4fd8dcb0c56");'><span id='4dcc14cf7245483cb5ebf4fd8dcb0c56_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年</a>，42岁</div><div id='4dcc14cf7245483cb5ebf4fd8dcb0c56' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年6月</a>　经翁源，应寺院之约作铭。作品：净源山定慧禅院思长老寿塔铭。<div id='poem_1159041' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159041' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159041?labeling=true' target='_blank'>韶州净源山定慧禅院思长老自造寿塔铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1041年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1159041")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159041_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159041'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159041'>夫鸿鹄翔于青云之上，鱼龙潜于深泉之下，安其性也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159041_comment'></div>人之处林野、乐闲旷，栖神养和，保终性命，得其适也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159041_comment'></div>古之达士者，皆自为秘器寿室，以卜返真之宅，《周官》有冢人、墓大夫掌其禁令与其位数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159041_comment'></div>然世人尚以死为讳，独蒙庄氏昌言矫俗，云：「富者苦身疾作，多积财而不尽用，贵者夜以继日，思虑善否，不若死者无君于上、无臣于下，虽南面王之乐，不能过也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159041_comment'></div>庄生之言，盖犹佛氏所云厌生死苦乐涅槃乐者欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159041_comment'></div>佛之去世，天下之国，分其齿骨爪发舍利而藏之，为塔于其上，奉之如其存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159041_comment'></div>后之学佛而终者，皆塔而不坟，从象教也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159041_comment'></div>今净源长老名邵思，姓李氏，曲江都渚人，于曹溪南华寺出家受具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159041_comment'></div>既而叹曰：「身居曹溪，漫不知其门域，当自愧其名」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159041_comment'></div>遂起游方之念，天台南岳，无不之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159041_comment'></div>最后见洞山聪和尚，得悟入之要以归焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159041_comment'></div>州以近郭名蓝宜择知宗乘者统领其众，遂召师居之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159041_comment'></div>昼登师座，夕启虚室，以延学徒，各以其仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159041_comment'></div>寺之西数百步，有岗蜿蜒盘屈，左右峰峦拥抱，其前平敞可爱，乃即岗之南麓为竁穴，陶甓以累其傍上，而侧设隧道以入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159041_comment'></div>又于其上屋之为塔之形，曰：「吾将归骨于此」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159041_comment'></div>前搆草堂数楹，署曰宝福之庵，日自策杖往来其间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159041_comment'></div>又熂其西北原，树以松柏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159041_comment'></div>仍得土之可垦者数十亩垦之，取其苗子为香火之用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159041_comment'></div>屡登吾门乞词，将伐石而镵之以自志云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159041_comment'></div>尝与朋友私议：今夫啖声利、争寻常者，桑榆末光，彯撇其气，然尚身恋圭组，手握牙筹，计生兴利，不知止息；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159041_comment'></div>茍能解擿外累，以死为归而休其心者，亦足嘉矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159041_comment'></div>孟坚书裸葬，有为为之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159041_comment'></div>自汉已来，文士或自志以掩幽室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159041_comment'></div>今思师不攻外典，且畏予之去而固求先铭其侧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159041_comment'></div>某亡叔葬其西原，故尝登是岗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159041_comment'></div>乃为铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_1159041'>生灭无本，是为佛性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159041_comment'></div>心境皆遣，同归于静。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1159041_comment'></div>不讳其死，是达真理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1159041_comment'></div>性同虚空，体魄归此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1159041_comment'></div>《武溪集》卷七。</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1159041_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
惠州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='6074a9b6cacd4673b3f0939b7d056a23_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("6074a9b6cacd4673b3f0939b7d056a23");'><span id='6074a9b6cacd4673b3f0939b7d056a23_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年</a>，42岁</div><div id='6074a9b6cacd4673b3f0939b7d056a23' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年6月</a>　上罗浮山，应邀作记。作品：罗浮山延祥寺记。<div id='poem_1159001' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159001' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159001?labeling=true' target='_blank'>惠州罗浮山延祥寺记</a><span class='authorDate'>（康定二年六月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1159001")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159001_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159001'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159001'>名山大川，方域之镇，必藉异人以光其图谍；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159001_comment'></div>达才通识，稠众之表，必托有为以播其绩用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159001_comment'></div>二美胥副今为难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159001_comment'></div>罗浮山者，越之望也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159001_comment'></div>蓬莱一峰，尧波所荡，附丽于此，《水经》之怪录也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159001_comment'></div>良常诸洞，吴郊之秀，岫穴相通，真㖟之秘谈也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159001_comment'></div>曰浮屠西来，蔓延中国，塔庙严饰，遍宅形胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159001_comment'></div>兹山精蓝十馀，而延祥之基最古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159001_comment'></div>梁朝有头陀僧景泰，不知何许人，薙草屋之号焉，朝游南海，暮宿罗浮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159001_comment'></div>大同中始建寺额，以其峰顶二石，望之如楼布金，所居适在南峰之下，故以南楼命之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159001_comment'></div>唐开元二十六年，西域僧乾末多罗以铁肖释迦真像，浮海而去番禺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159001_comment'></div>天宝二年，中贵人何行成以祠事将命，遂迎其像置山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159001_comment'></div>归，以珍柑入贡，因得御署其门曰延祥之寺，仍开明月戒坛于寺之右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159001_comment'></div>凡岭之南，落发坏衣者，悉受具于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159001_comment'></div>武宗朝例削其籍，咸通恢复，而地归中阁，别揭南楼之名于山之西。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159001_comment'></div>延祥再造苦晚，故久不竞，然亦不敢父子私自相传，必择什方名德尸之，以俟来学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159001_comment'></div>初，铁像之来也，扶土以具其四体，及祥符初，住持僧彦课乃购金雇工易之以铁，而像始完。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159001_comment'></div>彦课卒，州以舆议请今长老云达绍隆禅席。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159001_comment'></div>达师桂州阳朔人，幼聪悟，师事同郡禠禅师，既削发，即游方至筠州洞山，宝禅师付以大乘之要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159001_comment'></div>既而曰：「生本无物，何有本乡；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159001_comment'></div>悟在于心，岂须戏论」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159001_comment'></div>遂优游南行，至于海上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159001_comment'></div>有黄龙洞者，山灵绝境，人迹罕到，可以逃声名，去思虑，于是结茅而居，期于自得而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159001_comment'></div>俄而学徒推戴以登师座。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159001_comment'></div>既尸其徒，则专其忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159001_comment'></div>括囊而来者，居于我乎安；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159001_comment'></div>持盂而求者，食于我乎仰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1159001_comment'></div>于是募信心以施其财，召匠指以利其器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1159001_comment'></div>审高卑，面平旷，凿户牖，陶瓴甓，取于坚完，不务华丽，日廪岁资，悉得其度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1159001_comment'></div>康定元年，达公自袖其状至于曲江，俾予书之，归为福地之识。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1159001_comment'></div>明年，予因经途诣山，于其南得张鸑之碑，而知其名之始；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1159001_comment'></div>于其侧见明月之坛，而知其制之古；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1159001_comment'></div>于其堂闻达师之问答，而知其言之当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1159001_comment'></div>乃曰：「道如是，书之无愧词」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1159001_comment'></div>康定二年六月日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1159001_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年6月</a>　在罗浮山，应邀作序。作品：宫师陈相公（尧佐）留题罗浮山诗序。<div id='poem_1158940' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158940' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158940?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宫师陈相公留题罗浮山诗序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1041年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158940")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158940_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158940'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158940'>道家品天下名山，称洞天者三十六，号福地者七十二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158940_comment'></div>罗浮籍在洞天之七，而岫穴北通金坛，盖蓬莱之一洲，神仙之聚窟，岂独荣公侯之祀、擅登临之美乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158940_comment'></div>彼嵩少、终南、中条、太华，枕乎名利之场，故吟咏者日争，咀嚼含嗽，以买名声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158940_comment'></div>而兹山磅礴海上，寂寥千载，自非安恬愉、乐幽静者，孰肯于名外摛为不世之观乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158940_comment'></div>今宫师致政相君，尝于咸平中领郡来此，帅其属而游焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158940_comment'></div>稚川炼药之区，景泰冥心之地，咸有留咏，共成四章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158940_comment'></div>观夫大君子之存诚也，卷道而远迹，不羞于窘；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158940_comment'></div>遭时而调元，不谓之泰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158940_comment'></div>所以托言寄意，安于适而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158940_comment'></div>故其解相印如脱屣，岂不素乐于闲旷哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158940_comment'></div>博罗令黄君，以曳裾之旧而希其高，惜其粉字尘蠹，恐湮没而不纪，遂买石而移之，以永其传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158940_comment'></div>某蹑屐来游，会其錾刻，因书岁月于右。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1158940'></div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1158940_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年6月</a>　在罗浮山，作诗。作品：五色雀。<div id='poem_99440' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99440' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99440?labeling=true' target='_blank'>五色雀</a><span class='authorDate'>（1041年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99440")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_99440_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99440'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99440'>五方纯色俨衣冠<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>，应是山灵寄羽翰。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99440_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99440'>多谢相逢殊俗眼，谪官犹作贵人看。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99440_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99440'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_99440_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_99440'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_99440_0'>⑴ 自注：尤可爱者，朱蓝正色若朝服焉。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_99440_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年7月</a>　六、七月间，抵惠州作记。作品：惠州开元寺记。<div id='poem_1158998' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158998' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158998?labeling=true' target='_blank'>惠州开元寺记</a><span class='authorDate'>（康定二年六月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158998")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158998_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158998'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158998'>自汉迄今仅千祀，天下郡国之胜游、云泉之绝境，精庐居之，迨且遍矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158998_comment'></div>盖名僧高士，无世无之，或潜光丘壑，洗心閒旷，山林所以栖息；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158998_comment'></div>或应现度人，随机示化，国邑之所归仰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158998_comment'></div>日联岁续，人去迹存，此乃钟梵相闻，不为多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158998_comment'></div>有唐开元，天子号令，翔于四海，每为新制，以自张大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158998_comment'></div>乃命祠曹，州择一最胜寺，易以年名冠之，俾后世知声教之广被也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158998_comment'></div>故天下寺以开元名者，必基爽垲、据形便，祠宇最壮，像设最严，纲维最亲而不苛，制度最古而有序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158998_comment'></div>惠州治城之南二里，则所谓最胜之寺也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158998_comment'></div>古者邑而未郡，山犹林莽，虎狼宅之，肆害民里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158998_comment'></div>东汉之末，有僧曰文简，挂锡栖此，猛兽驯伏，因为伏虎台云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158998_comment'></div>郡本百越之地，汉隶南海，晋为东管郡，晋武帝咸宁元年，太社青气属天，占者云东管有帝王之祥，于是以东管王胄徙封琅琊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158998_comment'></div>是岁，元帝始生，胄即其祖，中兴纂绍，实启祥应，于此建刹，锡名龙兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158998_comment'></div>隋文帝削平江左，南北一统，因得西域舍利，遍置名山，俾筑塔而藏之，又改曰舍利道场。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158998_comment'></div>至开元二十八年，乃赐今号，奉安睿宗皇帝御容，至今存焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158998_comment'></div>兹寺重岗复阜，隐映岩谷，长溪带盘，湖光相照，探幽赏异，一郡之绝，故累朝诏择名蓝，锡以嘉号，而常在其选；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158998_comment'></div>郡廷精拣经论名德，署为僧职，以总领缁衣，亦多其人，乃知其名实不相浮矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158998_comment'></div>咸平三年，以郁攸之灾，悉为煨烬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158998_comment'></div>不有废也，其何以兴？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158998_comment'></div>于是即其旧基，沿同革异，或出自私楮，或募于檀信，凡为栋宇若干间，堂殿若干所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158998_comment'></div>扶土设色，肖像而争勤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1158998_comment'></div>捐金弛具，不谋而同力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1158998_comment'></div>禅徒律学，各有攸居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1158998_comment'></div>初，寺之名舍利道场也，有石刻以志其本末，昆岗之焚，字无完点。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1158998_comment'></div>及其再造，四十馀年矣，遗缁故老，存亡相半，陵谷之变，将无纪焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1158998_comment'></div>以某尝登东壁之府，倦游而归，佥来乞词，以为后观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1158998_comment'></div>由是询邦志，采耆言，笔之于石，以备遗逸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1158998_comment'></div>康定二年龙集辛巳六月日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1158998_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年7月</a>　六、七月间，抵惠州作诗。作品：留题澄虚亭。<div id='poem_99518' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99518' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99518?labeling=true' target='_blank'>留题澄虚亭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1041年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99518")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_99518_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99518'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99518'>湖光湛寒碧，帘影拂莓苔。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99518_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99518'>鱼戏应同乐，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_99518", 99518, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>鸥闲</span>亦自来。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99518_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99518'>雨馀轻霭合，竹外杂花开。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99518_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99518'>久欲留诗去，惭无绮靡才。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99518_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_99518'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_99518_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年7月</a>　在潮州，赋诗。作品：荔香亭。<div id='poem_99487' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99487' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99487?labeling=true' target='_blank'>荔香亭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1041年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99487")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_99487_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99487'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99487'>虚亭何所赏，为爱果中奇。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99487_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99487'>气禀南方秀，生当火王时。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99487_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99487'>渡淮嫌橘变，经庾笑梅衰。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99487_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99487'>不共花争艳，残莺莫傍枝。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99487_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_99487'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_99487_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年7月</a>　在潮州，应邀作序。作品：海潮图序。<div id='poem_1158949' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158949' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158949?labeling=true' target='_blank'>海潮图序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1041年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158949")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158949_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158949'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158949'>古之言潮者多矣，或言如橐籥翕张，或言如人气呼吸，或云海䲡出处，皆亡经据。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158949_comment'></div>唐世卢肇著《海潮赋》，以谓日入海而潮生，月离日而潮大，自谓极天人之论，世莫敢非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158949_comment'></div>予尝东至海门，南至武山，旦夕候潮之进退，弦望视潮之消息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158949_comment'></div>乃知卢氏之说，出于胸臆，所谓盖有不知而作者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158949_comment'></div>夫阳燧取火于日，阴鉴取水于月，从其类也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158949_comment'></div>潮之涨退，海非增减，盖月之所临，则水往从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158949_comment'></div>日月右转而天左旋，一日一周，临于四极，故月临卯酉则水涨乎东西，月临子午则潮平乎南北，彼竭此盈，往来不绝，皆系于月，不系于日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158949_comment'></div>何以知其然乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158949_comment'></div>夫昼夜之运，日东行一度，月行十三度有奇，故太阴西没之期，常缓于日三刻有奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158949_comment'></div>潮之日缓，其期率亦如是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158949_comment'></div>自朔至望，常缓一夜潮；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158949_comment'></div>自望至晦，复缓不昼潮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158949_comment'></div>若因日之入海，激而为潮，则何故缓不及期常三刻有奇乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158949_comment'></div>肇又谓月去日远，其潮乃大，合朔之际，潮始微绝，此固不知潮之准也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158949_comment'></div>夫朔望前后，月行差疾，故晦前三日潮势长，朔后三日潮势极大，望亦如之，非谓远于日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158949_comment'></div>月弦之际，其行差迟，故潮之去来亦合沓不尽，非谓近于日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158949_comment'></div>盈虚消息，一之于月，阴阳之所以分也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158949_comment'></div>夫春夏昼潮常大，秋冬夜潮常大，盖春为阳中，秋为阴中，岁之有春秋，犹月之有朔望也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158949_comment'></div>故潮之极涨，常在春秋之中；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158949_comment'></div>涛之极大，常在朔望之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1158949_comment'></div>此又天地之常数也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1158949_comment'></div>昔窦氏为记，以谓潮虚于午，此候于东海者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1158949_comment'></div>近燕公著论，以谓生于子，此测于南海者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1158949_comment'></div>又尝问于海贾，云潮生东南，此乘舟候潮而进退者耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1158949_comment'></div>古今之说，以为地缺东南，水归之，海贾云潮生东南，亦近之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1158949_comment'></div>今通二海之盈缩，以志其期，西北二海所未尝见，故阙而不纪云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1158949_comment'></div>尝候于海门<span class='inlineComment2'>（通州海门县。）</span>，月加卯而潮平者，日月合朔，则旦而平，日缓三刻有奇，上弦则午而平，望已前为昼潮，望已后为夜潮<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1158949_comment'></div>月加酉而潮平者，日月合朔，则日入而潮平，上弦则夜半而平，望则明日之旦而平，望已前为夜潮，望已后为昼潮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1158949_comment'></div>此东海之潮候也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1158949_comment'></div>又尝候于武山<span class='inlineComment2'>（广州望船之处。）</span>，月加午而潮平者，日月合朔，则午而潮平，上弦则日入而平，望则夜半而平，上弦已前为昼潮，上弦以后为夜潮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1158949_comment'></div>月加子而潮平者，日月合朔，则夜半而潮平，上弦则日出而平，望则午而平，上弦已前为夜潮，上弦已后为昼潮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1158949_comment'></div>此南海之潮候也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1158949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1158949'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_26_1158949_0'>⑴ 此皆临海之候也，远海之处则各有远近之期。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1158949_comment'></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
广州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='6743bbd4ab954795bc420bdd240c06d8_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("6743bbd4ab954795bc420bdd240c06d8");'><span id='6743bbd4ab954795bc420bdd240c06d8_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年</a>，42岁</div><div id='6743bbd4ab954795bc420bdd240c06d8' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>秋，抵广州，知州段少边是年四月改知渭州，病逝于赴任途中，靖悲极作祭文。时知广州方慎言亦相陪遥祭，闻者为之泪下。作品：祭段待制文。<div id='poem_1159047' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159047' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159047?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭段待制文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1041年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1159047")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159047_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159047'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159047'>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159047_comment'></div>天之间气，是生俊德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159047_comment'></div>特禀粹精，蕴为才识。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159047_comment'></div>应物成务，代王脩职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159047_comment'></div>皇图所倚，譬诸轮翼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159047_comment'></div>试之以渐，终将康国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159047_comment'></div>量既未充，寿胡不克？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159047_comment'></div>呜呼天乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159047_comment'></div>世于禄仕，不羞茍得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159047_comment'></div>或枉道以容身，或买声而借力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159047_comment'></div>公之立朝，侃然正色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159047_comment'></div>孤根竦干，古之亮直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159047_comment'></div>母后专制，戚里滥恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159047_comment'></div>千官结舌，喑过天阍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159047_comment'></div>公俦抗愤，方幅建言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159047_comment'></div>雷霆震怒，甘心黜去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159047_comment'></div>委吏冗员，处之如傃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159047_comment'></div>乘骢宪府，和铅书殿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159047_comment'></div>智略再伸，周行改观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159047_comment'></div>外台主计，国无贫岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159047_comment'></div>揽辔观风，钝顽咸砺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159047_comment'></div>南床执法，官宿其业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159047_comment'></div>簪豸伏墀，权豪共慑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159047_comment'></div>粤佐金谷，旋登侍从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159047_comment'></div>竭诚纳忠，言行策用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159047_comment'></div>暂拥麾幢，殿此海邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159047_comment'></div>锄奸树善，民夷以康。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1159047_comment'></div>天胡不憖，歼我忠良。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1159047_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1159047_comment'></div>人之怀才，不遭于世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1159047_comment'></div>或结隙而被诬，或抱忠而见弃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1159047_comment'></div>既饮痛而莫伸，甘捐躯而自誓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1159047_comment'></div>犹有生还故都，此去遐裔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1159047_comment'></div>公今于时，不为不遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1159047_comment'></div>直道守官，自结明主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1159047_comment'></div>暂斥复还，帝其玉汝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1159047_comment'></div>扬历清显，勤劳靡盬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1159047_comment'></div>旦夕顾问，其仕则膴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1159047_comment'></div>众推周才，可以镇远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1159047_comment'></div>抚封半载，帝亦悔遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1159047_comment'></div>紫泥赐书，追锋给车。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1159047_comment'></div>俾公受代，归侍玉除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1159047_comment'></div>代公者谁，在湘之湄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1159047_comment'></div>抗旌即道，朝露先晞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1159047_comment'></div>公之未去，励精愈苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1159047_comment'></div>遂使忠魂，沦丧兹土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1159047_comment'></div>公之才良，无愧庙堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1159047_comment'></div>亲逢旦暮，而死炎方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1159047_comment'></div>物理难晓，徒怨苍苍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1159047_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1159047_comment'></div>蛮酋海客，乘风浮舶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1159047_comment'></div>明月犀象，岁至日积。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1159047_comment'></div>昔人北归，不能弭谤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1159047_comment'></div>竹简薏珠，方舟兼量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1159047_comment'></div>公之戒行，朝以俟夕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1159047_comment'></div>尽室轻装，十夫之役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1159047_comment'></div>天若有知，延其漏刻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1159047_comment'></div>俾我后人，观之为则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1159047_comment'></div>庶乎无憾，以叶柔克。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1159047_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1159047_comment'></div>脩短之期，盖有常数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1159047_comment'></div>逝川不息，藏舟靡固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1159047_comment'></div>人生至此，胡其艰茹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1159047_comment'></div>哀公之丧，不得其常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1159047_comment'></div>弱息乳齿，孺妇空房。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1159047_comment'></div>远托故国，未知存亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1159047_comment'></div>哭无由而凭柩，歛不及于帷堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1159047_comment'></div>谓暂时之一别，遂隔生而可伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1159047_comment'></div>昔紫服兮乘驷，今丹旐兮还乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1159047_comment'></div>瞻灵輀之祖载，痛川途之阻长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1159047_comment'></div>陈絮酒兮一酸，泪沾襟兮浪浪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1159047_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！</div><div id='poem_sentence_71_1159047_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>应宋咸之请作序。作品：广州南海罗汉院记。<div id='poem_1158983' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158983' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158983?labeling=true' target='_blank'>广州南海县罗汉院记</a><span class='authorDate'>（康定二年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158983")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158983_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158983'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158983'>孔子曰：「可与适道，未可与权」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158983_comment'></div>则知道者，圣人之中正也，守常而不可变；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158983_comment'></div>权者，圣人之轻重也，应变而邻于谲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158983_comment'></div>权之时用大矣哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158983_comment'></div>佛氏生于西域，与诸华土壤断绝，殆将万里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158983_comment'></div>其灭度后且千岁，摩腾、竺法兰始持其书逾葱岭，东土当时未之识也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158983_comment'></div>乃绎汉明秘梦以肖其像，复筑鸿胪外馆以居其徒，䌷其梵音以通华言，讽诵讲说，日渐月清，自是迄今又且千岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158983_comment'></div>天下之俗，云蒸波委。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158983_comment'></div>秀眉之老，毁齿之童，服役其事，惟恐在后；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158983_comment'></div>百户之邑，十家之乡，铙鼓梵呗，未尝可阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158983_comment'></div>其故何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158983_comment'></div>盖佛以大权宠万化归于至理而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158983_comment'></div>其为教也，禁杀伐，断淫妄，崇布施，重忏悔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158983_comment'></div>性命之说，付之通博之士；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158983_comment'></div>因果之论，精入鬼神之域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158983_comment'></div>使贤者务修，愚者生怖，同归于善也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158983_comment'></div>且夫蠉飞蠕动，含生之伦，莫不畏苦而趋乐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158983_comment'></div>圆手方足，最灵之品，莫不跂高而好胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158983_comment'></div>而况血气充于内，嗜欲诱于外，不足而后争，有馀而后肆，欺诬巧伪，皆欲勿为而不能已也，非权曷以诱之哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158983_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1158983_comment'></div>人羊相啖，生死循环，一念作恶，流入胎卵，有知之所同惧也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1158983_comment'></div>高赀厚产，逐利不休，暂持所爱，则获福报，常情之所乐为也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1158983_comment'></div>欺天罔上，造恶者众，摄心自悔，罪即消灭，众人之所愿闻也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1158983_comment'></div>死丧之哀，五情溃乱，闻有遗教，俾其熏修，能饷亡者，往生善处，则虽损躯破产，无所靳吝，孝子之不忘其亲也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1158983_comment'></div>乃知浮屠塔庙相望于野，不为过矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1158983_comment'></div>南海，诸越之冠邑也，番禺大府，节制五岭，秦汉已来，号为都会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1158983_comment'></div>邑即郡治，俗杂五方，史谍志之，此无预焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1158983_comment'></div>邑之南有里曰丰衍，村曰平洲，山曰莠罗，院曰萝汉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1158983_comment'></div>自刘氏归命，里落荒榛，院之馀基，郁为茂草，然而名在郡图，未削也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1158983_comment'></div>至天禧中，圣化翔洽，逾五十载，国无横赋，民有常业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1158983_comment'></div>生聚既众，仓廪既实，亡者必有悼也，而不知其所之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1158983_comment'></div>存者必有修也，而不知其所向。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1158983_comment'></div>耋艾同议，香火为归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1158983_comment'></div>尔时檀越麦延绍等五十馀人，列名请今住持僧法宗建刹奠居，以奉西方之教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1158983_comment'></div>繇是相山林，视原隰，基爽垲，宅闲旷，令元龟而协谋，仰定星而考室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1158983_comment'></div>罄己所有，惟力是视，募众所得，一簪不私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1158983_comment'></div>饰土以寄虔，故斲砻缥碧以极尊崇之数；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1158983_comment'></div>倚席以待众，故节棁轮奂以开讨论之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1158983_comment'></div>一饭之约，击钟而示严；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1158983_comment'></div>四方之来，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_39_1158983", 1158983, "Clauses/139/Comments/0")'>折床</span>而勿拒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1158983_comment'></div>茂松嘉树，莫非手植，缔构缮完，其亦勤矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1158983_comment'></div>却视城阙，尘嚣不来，前瞻海潮，法音如在，真物外之幽绝也，人地相高，众所推择，遂选为县僧首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1158983_comment'></div>凡僧之董领教门者，国曰统、曰录，郡曰正，县曰首，茍非才出辈类，孰能得之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1158983_comment'></div>法宗师本郡人，姓陈氏，幼以经业自进，长以戒行自守，遂能阐扬佛事，化其聚落，咸使信向，称为一邑之首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1158983_comment'></div>噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1158983_comment'></div>彼上人者，僻居海屿，不求闻达，至于志有所立、行有可取，人则戴之，以为领袖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1158983_comment'></div>自修者可以劝人，其信矣乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1158983_comment'></div>康定辛巳岁，予以缟冠南来，得其状而书之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1158983_comment'></div>既志佛之权，且警夫怠者云耳。</div><div id='poem_sentence_48_1158983_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>容州知州杜杞任满回京述职，游罗汉院，二人相见甚欢，有诗送杜杞。作品：送容州杜秘丞。<div id='poem_99502' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99502' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99502?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送容州杜秘丞</a><span class='authorDate'>（1041年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99502")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_99502_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99502'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99502'>官满一舟归，高怀俗背驰。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99502_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99502'>家藏唯翰墨，民政在声诗<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：秀才陈生为诗言政甚详。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99502_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99502'>气劲秋霜并，吟多夜月知。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99502_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99502'>知贤无路荐，何以报明时。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99502_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_99502'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_99502_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='e4e5d75b1e96485ebadd24f2cfdb1aac_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e4e5d75b1e96485ebadd24f2cfdb1aac");'><span id='e4e5d75b1e96485ebadd24f2cfdb1aac_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1063')">1061-1063年</a>，62-64岁</div><div id='e4e5d75b1e96485ebadd24f2cfdb1aac' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年7月18日</a>　到任， 有谢表。作品：广州谢上表。<div id='poem_1158780' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158780' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158780?labeling=true' target='_blank'>广州谢上表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1061年7月18日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158780")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158780_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158780'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158780'>臣某言：奉敕差知广州军州事、兼管内劝农市舶使、提点银铜场公事、充广南东路都钤辖、兼本路经略安抚使，已于今月十八日到任上讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158780_comment'></div>斗筲器小，方面任隆，海国虽遐，圣恩尤厚<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158780_comment'></div>伏念臣禀生卑薄，赋性颛愚，误蒙当宁之知，殊乏防闲之虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158780_comment'></div>三聘未羁之虏，终以左迁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158780_comment'></div>一弹不孝之人，遭其返噬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158780_comment'></div>既不虞而致毁，固无望于复燃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158780_comment'></div>就丧次以家居，属侬蛮之寇境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158780_comment'></div>愚谓古之卿士，退处乡闾，或遇凶荒之期，贼盗为梗，则必同坚堡壁，用庇族姻，谋与守臣，共伸此议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158780_comment'></div>朝廷因其急病，误谓知兵，起于缞绖之中，委其金革之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158780_comment'></div>以至绝交夷唇齿之援，擒寇魁子母之亲，正军刑于藁街，憺国威于铜柱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158780_comment'></div>在见闻之或异，亦谗谤之互兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158780_comment'></div>上赖天慈，屡更藩寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158780_comment'></div>去岁邕边失策，纳彼逋逃，峒獠恃强，遂成侵扰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158780_comment'></div>逻司丧元而溃败，列郡闻风而震惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158780_comment'></div>因驿骑以召臣，俾单车而谕指。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158780_comment'></div>虽岛夷听命，愿诛首恶之人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158780_comment'></div>而寨将贪功，未绝交争之患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158780_comment'></div>亦既与之约束，各守封疆，茍邦令之必行，谅吾圉之能固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158780_comment'></div>犹以岭服之外，越徼相通，俾临此州，以办边事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158780_comment'></div>窃惟兵火之后，疮痍未平，力役尚繁，生业犹困。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1158780_comment'></div>将祈存恤，当择循良，再具表陈，莫回恩旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1158780_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下乾刚下济，离照旁罗，傥寸有所长，则使之必报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1158780_comment'></div>轮翮无遗于木雁，潢污或荐于王公，致此非才，亦叨重任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1158780_comment'></div>敢不率励愚虑，勉守孤忠，察蕃汉险易之情，宣陛下忧勤之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1158780_comment'></div>庶乎萌隶，同被休明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1158780_comment'></div>臣无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1158780_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年7月18日</a>　有谢启。作品：谢知广州启。<div id='poem_1158927' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158927' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158927?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢知广州表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1061年7月18日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158927")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158927_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158927'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158927'>右，某启：叨膺睿渥，出布藩条，祗荷宠光，不任感惧，已于今月十八日到任上讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158927_comment'></div>伏念某器非适用，智不逮人，初既谢于才升，中亦罹于毁废，间蒙驱策，频易炎凉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158927_comment'></div>谋无补于临戎，宠屡叨于进律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158927_comment'></div>去岁载驰驿骑，重见阙庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158927_comment'></div>猥当谕指之行，殊乏绥边之略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158927_comment'></div>暨于复命，惟俟黜幽，遽升纲辖之司，仍领藩宣之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158927_comment'></div>下惭猛士，徒字于四方；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158927_comment'></div>仰愧文昌，甫联于八座。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158927_comment'></div>此盖某官义敦与善，德极包荒，密为敷扬，致兹忝冒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158927_comment'></div>敢不体国家忠厚之化，究邦俗利害之源，无露才以近名，冀顺民而成政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158927_comment'></div>茍能逃于官谤，期勿负于己知。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1158927_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年7月27日</a>　接敕诰，加上护军，进开国公、食邑五百户，赐银二百两，呈谢表，赐银上纳军资库。作品：谢加勳邑表。<div id='poem_1158781' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158781' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158781?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢加勋邑表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1061年7月27日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158781")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158781_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158781'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158781'>臣某言：今月二十七日，进奏院递到敕牒官诰各一道，伏蒙圣恩，授臣依前守尚书左丞、充集贤院学士，加上护军，进封开国公，食邑五百户，散官、实封、赐如故者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158781_comment'></div>合宫礼成，绵区泽普，不遗遐远，咸被冲瀜<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158781_comment'></div>恭惟皇帝陛下，昭事上穹，丕承洪绪，遍举累朝之阔典，再修宗祀之盛仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158781_comment'></div>即露寝以达诚，御端闱而涣号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158781_comment'></div>旁周覆载，罔不欢呼，下逮缙绅，咸加命数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158781_comment'></div>臣器能无取，礼秩兼优，护诸将以书勋，冠五等而疏爵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158781_comment'></div>仍增稍食，备极宠灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158781_comment'></div>敢不荷生育之恩，勤简惠之政，誓全苦节，上答宸慈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158781_comment'></div>但臣阻守外藩，不获奔诣阙庭，臣无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1158781_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年</a>　三子叔英以大理评事知潭州军监，孙舜臣陞南雄州知州。孙嗣隆中第。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年</a>　支持转运使栾沂修建英州至韶州江崖栈道，整治矿场、盐场。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年</a>　是年，占城国遣使顿琶尼来广州，向宋朝廷进贡方物，从所求赐其王施里律茶盘麻常杨溥白马一匹。顿巴尼曾在广州蕃学讲学，留住一年，靖礼遇之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1062&endYear=1062')">1062年1月</a>　驾部郎中、广南东路转运使栾沂赴京述职，靖作诗。作品：送栾驾部。闻栾驾部度岭见寄。<div id='poem_99548' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99548' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99548?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送栾驾部</a><span class='authorDate'>（1062年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99548")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_99548_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99548'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99548'>赋政古循良，恩威著一方。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99548_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99548'>疲民恋冬日，黠吏畏秋霜。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99548_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99548'>直道经摧折，公心愈激昂。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99548_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99548'>米盐躬细务，绳墨谨周防。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99548_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_99548'>度岭囊装简，攀辕父老忙。<div id='poem_sentence_4_99548_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_99548'>采诗如有诏，持此续甘棠。<div id='poem_sentence_5_99548_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_99548'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_99548_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_99510' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99510' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99510?labeling=true' target='_blank'>闻栾驾部度岭见寄</a><span class='authorDate'>（1062年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99510")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_99510_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99510'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99510'>久接贤规见准绳，还朝犹听颂声腾。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99510_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99510'>安民虑远疆封静<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>，富国材高帑藏增<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99510_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99510'>野老赓歌除横敛<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑶</sup>，侍臣交表荐殊能<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：近闻侍从诸公累表荐导。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99510_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99510'>岭头若著关官籍，可察孤清节似冰<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑷</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99510_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_99510'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_99510_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_99510'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_99510_0'>⑴ 自注：祐计司以徭寇酋豪三十馀人在州境，君拒而不留，民乃安堵。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_99510_0'>⑵ 自注：君二岁市铜八百万斤、银二十万两，一岁铸钱三千万贯。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_2_99510_0'>⑶ 自注：三溪盐场并草虚量子，岁出钱千缗以供徭人，君皆罢之。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_99510_0'>⑷ 自注：国家于岭道未著检察过岭之事，制若行之，则清污可分。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_99510_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1062&endYear=1062')">1062年1月</a>　蔡抗为广南东路转运使，其弟蔡挺知安南军提举虔州盐兼江西提刑，兄弟商议修复梅关驿道事，靖大力支持，知照南雄州、韶州抽调人力财力开筑驿道，方便南北驿道。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1062&endYear=1062')">1062年2月</a>　广州通判黄师道之父殿中丞黄珙卒，靖为作墓表。作品：宋故殿中丞黄公墓表。<div id='poem_1159026' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159026' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159026?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宋故殿中丞黄公墓表</a><span class='authorDate'>（嘉祐七年十一月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1159026")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159026_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159026'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159026'>公讳珙，字希珍，其先楚人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159026_comment'></div>春申之后，世居江夏，或系为公辅，或时号奇童，前史详之，此不复叙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159026_comment'></div>占名数于衡阳有年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159026_comment'></div>曾门讳璠，大门讳承禄，潜德不显，高蹈林泉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159026_comment'></div>考讳徘，乐道奉佛，中年戒杀，遂绝荤血，乡曲称为居士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159026_comment'></div>公以清素自励，兼通内外典，而留意篇咏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159026_comment'></div>尝云：「圣世右文兴治，旁罗寒俊，家有令子弟，不可不训之以学，而起其家」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159026_comment'></div>当是时，子侄四人，悉趋党塾，义方之教，劘琢有成，公喜而为诗曰：「门兰自有子孙荣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159026_comment'></div>章献太后上仙之明年，二子同年进士擢第；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159026_comment'></div>越再榜，犹子师尹继捷词科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159026_comment'></div>既而二子升朝，以禋祀恩及让官回授，五被命至殿中丞，朱衣银鱼，湖外向儒盛矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159026_comment'></div>德门贤范，遂为称首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159026_comment'></div>公尝谓儒术以饰躬，佛法以理性，故其崇奉西教逾于先君，诵《金刚般若经》四万卷，虽资质方直，而好行阴德，每以善行诲人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159026_comment'></div>尝自吟曰：「但将贫作富，祇以道为怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159026_comment'></div>有欲休持戒，无欺便是斋」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159026_comment'></div>君子谓之知言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159026_comment'></div>公以嘉祐七年二月辛丑，考终命于衡之私馆，享年七十五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159026_comment'></div>疾病弥年，精爽不乱，其奉行众善、无忘正念者欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159026_comment'></div>太夫人许氏，其寿九十。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159026_comment'></div>夫人许氏，累封长寿县君，内助于公，下训诸子，主蘋蘩之祀，著闺闱之则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159026_comment'></div>长子师道，屯田郎中、通判广州；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159026_comment'></div>仲子师说，举进士不第，先公二年卒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159026_comment'></div>季子师旦，屯田员外郎、桂阳监使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159026_comment'></div>并承公积善，以取科级，谨于率履，咸以清白材干闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159026_comment'></div>大司田君复深于佛性，栖心事外，有高世之风焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159026_comment'></div>缘公及夫人年高，偕不乐远去庭闱，朝议韪而从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159026_comment'></div>女适同郡郴州司法李日宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1159026_comment'></div>孙五人：长镇，次钧，太庙斋郎，广城、启期、锜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1159026_comment'></div>女孙九人，重孙四人，重女孙三人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1159026_comment'></div>以其年十一月庚申，葬公于东郊里墅之东五里虎龙山先茔之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1159026_comment'></div>方葬有日矣，嗣子走其中亲进士罗友谅，持其郡倅都官莫君及所撰行状，伻来乞铭，表于墓阡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1159026_comment'></div>顷岁某经制广西，大司田君时为桂倅，婉谋正论，日蒙开益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1159026_comment'></div>公及夫人，皆板舆迎侍至郡，升堂获见，折节相欢，一日之素，于兹久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1159026_comment'></div>及今经略广东，君复倅南海，盖以便于定省，故十年之间连倅二郡，不自以为滞，非孝诚发中，孰能如此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1159026_comment'></div>秩满既归，罹此荼毒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1159026_comment'></div>湖湘之间，岂无文士，特缘雅故，见托斯文，然虽藻思荒落，其敢辞哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1159026_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_1159026'>为善致祥，乃天之常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1159026_comment'></div>其身用光，其家用昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1159026_comment'></div>忠恕之贤，后裔绵绵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1159026_comment'></div>立石松阡，以永其传。</div><div id='poem_sentence_39_1159026_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1062&endYear=1062')">1062年</a>　待制田况来广州，并携宋咸《忧余集》，求靖为序，靖为作序。作品：宋职方忧余集序。<div id='poem_1158948' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158948' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158948?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宋职方忧馀集序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1062年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158948")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158948_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158948'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158948'>君子之道，行之当世以为范，言之后世以为稽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158948_comment'></div>词章之作，寄谋赏而明教化也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158948_comment'></div>同年贯之，自登第以来，莅政退公之暇，朋游独处，悲欢荣悴，未尝不发于文，故于著撰为多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158948_comment'></div>今论思近臣侍读龙图宋君子京、侍讲龙图赵君祐之、搢绅闻人王子元岩、穴高士李泰伯并为君之集序，其言文之体要、道之用舍极矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158948_comment'></div>皇祐四年，以溪獠干纪，侵轶郡县，某自丧次中起为桂林守，兼总师政，贯之自曲江守移倅广西漕军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158948_comment'></div>明年，蛮事平息，得还郡治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158948_comment'></div>剧谈之次，贯之复出居艰所著文集，命曰《忧馀》，索序于某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158948_comment'></div>读玩数四，惟增感叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158948_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158948_comment'></div>古之君子，居丧读《丧礼》，既葬读《祭礼》，不欲馀事乱哀思也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158948_comment'></div>某不幸执亲之丧，不得终其哀，违坟墓，去几筵，驱驰疆埸万里之外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158948_comment'></div>贯之丧中所著，则改葬议及斋文、青词而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158948_comment'></div>后世之楷，岂不高哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158948_comment'></div>故泣而叙之云耳。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1158948_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1062&endYear=1062')">1062年</a>　待制田况来广州，余靖有诗。作品：寄题田待制广州西园。<div id='poem_99549' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99549' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99549?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄题田待制广州西园</a><span class='authorDate'>（1062年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99549")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_99549_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99549'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99549'>善政遍修举，增完池馆清。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99549_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99549'>地含春气早，月映暮潮生。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99549_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99549'>石有群星象<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：庭际罗立，旧名九曜石。）</span>，花多外国名<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99549_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99549'>与民同雉兔，邀客醉蓬瀛。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99549_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_99549'>翰墨资吟兴，云泉适野情。<div id='poem_sentence_4_99549_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_99549'>镇应持左蟹，快欲鲙长鲸。<div id='poem_sentence_5_99549_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_99549'>积霭藏楼阁，驯鸥识旆旌。<div id='poem_sentence_6_99549_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_99549'>甘棠留美荫，高倚越王城。<div id='poem_sentence_7_99549_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_99549'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_99549_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_99549'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_2_99549_0'>⑴ 自注：异花皆舶上所来，岭北无之。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_99549_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1062&endYear=1062')">1062年</a>　余靖整顿吏治严惩贪官；视察蕃坊，兴办蕃学，公平对待外商；呈请减免流民田赋，减番舶装船税，从而使被焚的农桑复甦，外国来经商的人日益增多，广州市舶收入有大幅增长，市面繁荣。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1062&endYear=1062')">1062年</a>　大食国首领蒲沙乙来广州进贡方物，于广州蕃学讲学，靖为之迎送。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1062&endYear=1062')">1062年</a>　末孙嗣祖出世，孙嗣昌贡举人。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1062&endYear=1062')">1062年</a>　到端州察访，喜购墨砚一方。察访途中，撰文阐明为政之道。作品：书去虎。<div id='poem_1159008' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159008' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159008?labeling=true' target='_blank'>书去虎</a><span class='authorDate'>（1062年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1159008")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159008_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159008'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159008'>禺山之阴曰翁永，水之源有居邑，去刺史府五百里而近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159008_comment'></div>山富毒草，水蒙毒雾，雾昏草黄，夏日瘅热，历者生疾，故州人惮之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159008_comment'></div>邑老吏恃远且崄，肆诋欺以成俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159008_comment'></div>亡何，丞尉飞书白府云：境中三虎暴自踣，请以状闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159008_comment'></div>本朝彰太守服猛击强之应，太守贪伪名，欲市其矫，乃召他邑掾往验之，以成其诈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159008_comment'></div>邑掾到境得疾，繇是怒而以实对：虎坠阱而死，言自踣者非是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159008_comment'></div>邑掾返，卧疾且死者久之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159008_comment'></div>野史氏闻之，废书而叹曰：「罪由古史，非丞尉太守之罪也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159008_comment'></div>昔者刘琨、宋均以循良著治理效，史氏有猛虎渡河之说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159008_comment'></div>向使政仁且明，虎虽在境，机埳可制；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159008_comment'></div>政昏且暴，虎虽出境，其害被于千里，岂特一虎哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159008_comment'></div>则知虎之去，不若暴之去，太史氏以异闻惑中智，甚矣哉！</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1159008_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1063&endYear=1063')">1063年1月</a>　应邀撰文。作品：广州鸟龙山觉性禅院草堂记。<div id='poem_1158987' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158987' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158987?labeling=true' target='_blank'>广州乌龙山觉性禅院草堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（嘉祐八年正月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158987")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158987_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158987'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158987'>伽蓝之制，寝室曰方丈，十方皆然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158987_comment'></div>番禺之东，去郡郛十里而近，有山曰乌龙，院曰觉性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158987_comment'></div>长老僧曰法持，剪发为头陀，题其寝曰草堂，视其迹似好异者，察其所为，则禅心而戒行，衲中之隽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158987_comment'></div>不游聚落将十稔矣，语必诚愿，人多信向，不祈甘美而鼎饪常丰，不尚华侈而丹素无废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158987_comment'></div>夫道充诸己，伏之必众；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158987_comment'></div>行敦于内，闻之必远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158987_comment'></div>曰缁曰素，未有不始于修者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158987_comment'></div>或者谓无修无證，乃欲屏去因果，混同善恶，则与夫愚暗贪恚者，何以异哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158987_comment'></div>殊不知无散乱心是无思也，无染著心是无为也，故虽智空境寂而不舍方便，严饰佛刹，纳人于善，兹所以为众所归也，迹之同异可略矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158987_comment'></div>嘉祐八年正月丙寅，行春至此，既归而笔之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1158987_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1063&endYear=1063')">1063年3月8日</a>　仁宗驾崩，靖呈五律挽诗。作品：仁宗皇帝挽诗二首（其一）仁宗皇帝挽诗二首（其二）<div id='poem_99464' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99464' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99464?labeling=true' target='_blank'>仁宗皇帝挽诗二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1063年3月8日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99464")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_99464_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99464'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99464'>丕承三后绩，盛烈古难陪。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99464_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99464'>纳谏书囊集，谈经殿阁开。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99464_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99464'>御弧圆月满，宸翰舞鸾回。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99464_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99464'>冠剑虽归葬，英风万祀恢。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99464_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_99464'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_99464_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_99463' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99463' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99463?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1063年3月8日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_99463_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99463'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99463'>四十载居尊，勤劳涤化源。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99463_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99463'>精禋敦舜孝，至治布尧言。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99463_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99463'>武尚包戈节，刑宽解网恩。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99463_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99463'>遗弓初奉讳，雨泪遍乾坤。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99463_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_99463'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_99463_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1063&endYear=1063')">1063年4月9日</a>　英宗即位，赐百官一等。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1063&endYear=1063')">1063年4月19日</a>　敕授靖工部尚书、知广州。有谢表。作品：谢转工部尚书表。<div id='poem_1158782' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158782' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158782?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢转工部尚书表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1063年4月19日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158782")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158782_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158782'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158782'>臣某言：今月十九日，进奏院递到敕诰各一道，伏蒙圣恩，授臣工部尚书，依前充集贤院学士，加柱国、食邑五百户，散官、实封、赐如故者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158782_comment'></div>龙德飞天，萝图兴运，旷荡之泽，遐远不遗<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158782_comment'></div>伏念臣学谢兼明，器惭远到，夤缘孤进，遭遇先朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158782_comment'></div>亟登词翰之科，频居文史之任，遽繇谏路，擢掌王言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158782_comment'></div>常欲北屈匈奴，南羁劲越，未能胜任，每预遣行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158782_comment'></div>曾无横草之功，连被拔茅之宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158782_comment'></div>屡委临于戎律，久陪贰于文昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158782_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下嗣守丕基，涣发大号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158782_comment'></div>乾坤之造海岳，至大而必包；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158782_comment'></div>雷雨之恩动植，无微而不及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158782_comment'></div>致兹散拙，亦预甄升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158782_comment'></div>素乏羽仪之才，遽当喉舌之任，将何以根本万事，出纳主言？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158782_comment'></div>谨当祗畏简书，恪修条教，更励委珠之节，不忘曳履之忠，庶答天慈，以逃官谤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158782_comment'></div>但臣守远藩镇，不获奔诣阙庭，臣无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1158782_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1063&endYear=1063')">1063年4月19日</a>　敕授靖工部尚书、知广州。有谢启。作品：谢转工部尚书启。<div id='poem_1158928' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158928' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158928?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢转工部尚书启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1063年4月19日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158928")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158928_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158928'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158928'>右，某启：叨奉圣恩，擢迁官品，无从逊避，徒积忧兢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158928_comment'></div>伏念某才谢适时，器非经远，幸缘孤直，误记清衷，擢自书林，超居谏路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158928_comment'></div>以至殊邻专对，西掖代言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158928_comment'></div>谤箧将盈，遗簪罔弃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158928_comment'></div>尝亲临于矢石，幸免丧元；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158928_comment'></div>曾无纪于旂常，徒烦舍爵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158928_comment'></div>屡统绥于武节，久陪贰于文昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158928_comment'></div>比者上圣登遐，真人应运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158928_comment'></div>尧仁舜孝，百世承基，乾健离明，重熙继照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158928_comment'></div>俊德旁罗于百辟，惠泽广宣于八纮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158928_comment'></div>爰及疏蒙，亦叨甄叙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158928_comment'></div>此盖某官曲加题品，俯念衰残。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158928_comment'></div>列郡承流，已忝股肱之寄；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158928_comment'></div>六曹平奏，俾升喉舌之官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158928_comment'></div>谨当祗率政经，防弭官谤，惟图死节，上报国恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158928_comment'></div>过此以还，罔知所措。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1158928_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1063&endYear=1063')">1063年4月19日</a>　夏，至州县察访立学情况。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='31dc872a01334a0e871ad26c7ddcba15_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("31dc872a01334a0e871ad26c7ddcba15");'><span id='31dc872a01334a0e871ad26c7ddcba15_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1063&endYear=1063')">1063年</a>，64岁</div><div id='31dc872a01334a0e871ad26c7ddcba15' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1063&endYear=1063')">1063年</a>　同榜进士、职方员外郎宋咸来广州，靖与之游越秀山，有诗。作品：寄题宋职方翠楼。宋职方补注周易后序。<div id='poem_99521' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99521' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99521?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄题宋职方翠楼</a><span class='authorDate'>（1063年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99521")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_99521_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99521'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99521'>层楼幽趣称登临，望远凭高豁素襟。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99521_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99521'>棋酒等閒忘世虑，溪山最乐是家林。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99521_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99521'>松声带雨千峰外，潭影涵虚落照深。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99521_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99521'>此景为君珍赏甚，起余归兴欲抽簪。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99521_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_99521'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_99521_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1158946' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158946' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158946?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宋职方补注周易后序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1063年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158946")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158946_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158946'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158946'>《易》之道深矣，自汉兴有施孟、梁丘、京氏、费、高诸家之学，列于庠序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158946_comment'></div>而传异词、师异说，往往入于五行谶纬之术，故其学中绝焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158946_comment'></div>王氏之学，传自魏晋，盛于隋唐之际，大有言阴阳变化、人事得失，不悖于三圣，不荡于术数，故独为学者所宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158946_comment'></div>近世言《易》者，复以奇文诡说相高，自成一家之言，考之卦繇、爻、《象》、《彖》、《系》之微，有所不通矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158946_comment'></div>今广平宋君贯之《补注周易》，盖惩诸儒之失，而擿去异端，志在通王氏之说，合圣人之经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158946_comment'></div>字有未安，意有未贯，必引而伸之，用明文王、周公之旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158946_comment'></div>初著《易明》数十篇，后得唐郭京《举正》之说，意与己合，遂采郭氏《举正》与《易明》相参，缀于经注之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158946_comment'></div>辩坠简之所缺，启后人之未悟，朱墨发端，粲然可睹，其自叙详矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158946_comment'></div>于戏！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158946_comment'></div>古之儒者，以明经为本，两汉名臣，未尝不以经进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158946_comment'></div>自儒林、文苑派分已来，搢绅之士视经犹蘧庐耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158946_comment'></div>贯之学必稽古，言皆贯道，以词章取科第，以通博副名实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158946_comment'></div>皇祐五年岁在荒落，《补注》既成，闻于旒扆，俄颁中旨，附邮投进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158946_comment'></div>其明年，蛮事平息，因谈经义，遂得奏御副本为示，乃周而研之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158946_comment'></div>尝观刘氏《钩隐图》，言宓牺氏因龙图龟书之文以画八卦，又言天五地五，大衍之用，谓其深于数者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158946_comment'></div>及观贯之之释，以谓宓牺稽象于天，取法于地，观鸟兽之文，通万物之情以画卦，奚独取于龙马之图耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158946_comment'></div>又其言《乾》《坤》之策生于四象，其于尼父之经、辅嗣之注，亡所戾而有所明焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158946_comment'></div>固可秘之藏室、流之学宫，宁止是正文字而已哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158946_comment'></div>叹其言近旨远，故题而序之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1158946_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1063&endYear=1063')">1063年10月</a>　承天监寺僧松思上门求题记，喜作记。作品：庐山承天归宗禅寺重修寺记。<div id='poem_1158982' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158982' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158982?labeling=true' target='_blank'>庐山承天归宗禅寺重修寺记</a><span class='authorDate'>（嘉祐八年十月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158982")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158982_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158982'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158982'>佛氏之权大矣，三乘十二分之教，虽所说不同，同归于化人为善，人天龙鬼无不归仰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158982_comment'></div>故一一城邑、一一聚落、一一川原、一一岩岫，未尝无刹也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158982_comment'></div>俗无华裔，土无沃塉，十室之居，万里之远，钟梵之声相闻，世人不厌其多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158982_comment'></div>夫惟群动外诱，则其智昏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158982_comment'></div>一念内息，则其心寂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158982_comment'></div>习浮图者，定慧发光，以戒为本，故居城廓之愦吏，不若山林之闲旷也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158982_comment'></div>天下溪山之秀，江国为最；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158982_comment'></div>塔庙之严，庐阜为胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158982_comment'></div>近不接于尘坌，远弗托于岩崄，晓参夕问，无非佛事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158982_comment'></div>归宗田焉，本晋右将军王逸少之宅也，坛宇虽改，墨池犹存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158982_comment'></div>天竺耶舍尊者，振锡来居，遂作布金之所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158982_comment'></div>江左六代至于隋、唐，总以律仪，莫穷谱系。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158982_comment'></div>贞元中，江州刺史李勃与智常禅师为云霞之交，兼师友之契，爰开法席，革以禅规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158982_comment'></div>常禅师，马祖之嗣，风韵殊特。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158982_comment'></div>初，有日者言师相有异表，师闻之曰：「吾学佛者，异欲何求」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158982_comment'></div>遂以沙眯其目，辄有流星之应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158982_comment'></div>时人因其睑赤，呼为赤眼道人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158982_comment'></div>四方来学，不下千众，自是灯灯相继，于今二十三世矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158982_comment'></div>皇朝景德三年，以诞圣节名承天赐为寺额，仍冠归宗之号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158982_comment'></div>丛林之盛，少能比拟；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1158982_comment'></div>栋干之隆，几及千间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1158982_comment'></div>皇祐初，出饎之灾，郁为煨烬，长老慧南既痛己身逢此坏相，又思成性庄严，当由我兴，于是精勤再造，同于经始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1158982_comment'></div>未终厥志，奄先归寂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1158982_comment'></div>妙圆禅师自宝，昔尝众请在十八世矣，诸方道目推为禅伯，第以云居，久隳纲领，徙猊座而振之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1158982_comment'></div>及是缁黄共议，还师故处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1158982_comment'></div>人之求旧，群情胥悦，智者献谋，匠者献艺，富者献财，壮者献力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1158982_comment'></div>土毛所入，日用所资，众竭其诚，簪毫无隐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1158982_comment'></div>远者伐山，近者陶土，而绀宇巍然；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1158982_comment'></div>巧思铺金，寓形设色，而宝像俨然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1158982_comment'></div>惜其能事未终，倏亦避去；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1158982_comment'></div>道宜绍之，亦才数稔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1158982_comment'></div>今长老慧通嗣总清众，极力兴修，凡陂而未平，基而未构，器之未具，像之未完，月缀岁葺，工无暂舍，期于大备，又加饬焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1158982_comment'></div>素不至朴，严不及丽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1158982_comment'></div>香火所虔，宾主所止，经行作务，群居独息，各为区域，莫非僧仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1158982_comment'></div>愚尝谓臣庶之家，虽五世相韩，七貂仕汉，子孙能保故居者鲜矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1158982_comment'></div>至于禅宗佛宇，或时迁代易，而钟呗巾盖不绝者，何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1158982_comment'></div>选于众，择其能而授之，乃克起弊补废，而永厥世也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1158982_comment'></div>必因夫大患难、大灾害然后见哲匠之才谋、菩提之愿力，古今已然之势也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1158982_comment'></div>故十三年之间，继择开士而见寺制周焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1158982_comment'></div>监寺僧松思，宝师之门人也，遣价驰书数千里，丐词为记，不获让而志之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1158982_comment'></div>嘉祐八年十月日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1158982_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1063&endYear=1063')">1063年</a>　是年，有高僧智缘游方至广州，为靖把脉，云近体无恙，终官秦亭有凶兆。众谓秦亭在陕甘，靖遂畏西行。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='df6feaff54374774a46ad8184726cf0e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("df6feaff54374774a46ad8184726cf0e");'><span id='df6feaff54374774a46ad8184726cf0e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1064&endYear=1064')">1064年</a>，65岁</div><div id='df6feaff54374774a46ad8184726cf0e' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1064&endYear=1064')">1064年3月</a>　卢士宏继任知广州，余靖卸任。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
乐昌
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='cafac6bf6ae745a28f68f218ab198d99_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("cafac6bf6ae745a28f68f218ab198d99");'><span id='cafac6bf6ae745a28f68f218ab198d99_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年</a>，42岁</div><div id='cafac6bf6ae745a28f68f218ab198d99' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年9月</a>　应宝林禅院圆祐禅师之请，作记。作品：乐昌县宝林禅寺记。<div id='poem_1158984' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158984' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158984?labeling=true' target='_blank'>韶州乐昌县宝林禅院记</a><span class='authorDate'>（康定二年九月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158984")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158984_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158984'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158984'>上士冥心而履道，其次崇善以济物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158984_comment'></div>道充于内而迹彰于外，物应于迩而名闻于远，所以咨事而察其言，寻声而索其实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158984_comment'></div>一家之誉，必用之于乡；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158984_comment'></div>一乡之秀，必升之于国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158984_comment'></div>盖善恶起诸己，毁誉成诸<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>众，择贤采异，用此术也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158984_comment'></div>今夫推自稠人之中，升于高座之上，巍然当室之白，以师道自处，使同袍济济，北面就列，拜起趋揖，如事君父，若非深识悬解，领悟性相，舂容一音，发矇去惑者，众多之心，岂易伏哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158984_comment'></div>越人右鬼，而刘氏尤佞于佛，故曲江名山秀水、膏田沃野，率归于浮屠氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158984_comment'></div>郡之属邑曰乐昌，去县郛四十里，有院曰宝林，地灵境胜，一邑之冠，远郊近落，率来瞻仰，故常登延开士，主其熏修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158984_comment'></div>于戏！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158984_comment'></div>栖山林以遂其高，遁江海以安其闲，幽人奇士，所以击节而争往也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158984_comment'></div>又况有栋宇以资其偃息，有菑畬以奉其饘粥，果能择得闻人以付之，俾其发扬佛事，开导氓俗，奉行诸善，共避众恶，此乃因高閒之适，成兼济之利者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158984_comment'></div>今长老圆祐师，福州怀德人，姓陈氏，学顿放于黄梅山显宗禅师，服勤二十年，昼问夕参，遂探幽楗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158984_comment'></div>乃曰：「未脱自缚，安能度人」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158984_comment'></div>即谋南归，以卜终焉之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158984_comment'></div>惟兹宝林之众，屡易师长，而莫能兴葺以延四方，于是计使邹公覃远听博采，得师于虔之慈云，遂迎以来，俾尸其众，时景祐三年也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158984_comment'></div>先是，院制度狭小，不克称于其名，殿陛庳下，堂奥浅仄，居才数亩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158984_comment'></div>面临回照，影过亭午，则暑气郁勃，坐者挥汗，至于末光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158984_comment'></div>师以日廪之馀，悉付营造，易其堂殿，负阴向阳，增筑厥基，始逾百堵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158984_comment'></div>伐山、陶土、剞劂、圩墁之工，百役自具，不假外徇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158984_comment'></div>居者执畚而同力，来者挂锡而如归，夏开南荣，冬塞墐户，无复往时之陋也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1158984_comment'></div>乃知择得其人，为利自博，但无意侵渔，能守厥旧，已足佳矣，矧能指无修之要以悟自性，精有为之勤以励后学？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1158984_comment'></div>此而不记，将孰记哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1158984_comment'></div>康定二年九月日记<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_1158984'></div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1158984_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1158984'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_4_1158984_0'>⑴ 诸原作请，据四库本改。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_22_1158984_0'>⑵ 《武溪集》卷七。又见《广东文徵》卷五五。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1158984_comment'></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

大同

-----title
赤峰
-----detail

-----title
宁城
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='64847653c94e4db2b5860da3bca80299_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("64847653c94e4db2b5860da3bca80299");'><span id='64847653c94e4db2b5860da3bca80299_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年1月17日</a>　仁宗命靖以知制诰任贺国母正旦使，第三次使辽。抵中京，辽主允准与夏握手言和，商定三月换俘。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年2月6日</a>　边报西夏与辽约和，寻复犯边，请求朝廷派使干预。靖指出此乃元昊狡计，毋容置理。作品：奉使契丹时上言。<div id='poem_1158861' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158861' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158861?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉使契丹时上言<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历五年二月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1045年2月6日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158861")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158861_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158861'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158861'>昨闻西人与契丹约和，寻复侵掠，必恐契丹兵忿不解，前又遣使来以告西伐，则将命者不绝，蠹耗财用，无有尽时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158861_comment'></div>臣今奉使契丹，欲先谕以元昊反覆小臣，其去就不足为两朝重轻，设或携叛，亦是常事，彼此只边上关报，更不专遣使臣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_1_1158861_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年2月</a>　靖受命代朝廷出外主持祭典，有五律。作品：禋郊。<div id='poem_99550' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99550' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99550?labeling=true' target='_blank'>禋郊诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（1045年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_sentence_1_99550'>物兼明德荐，天以至诚通。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99550_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99550'>制度亲祠盛，威仪陟配崇。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99550_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99550'>戎容俨仙仗，霁色照郊宫。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99550_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_99550'>国典书昭事，神禧报屡丰。<div id='poem_sentence_4_99550_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_99550'>端闱宣大号，王泽浸无穷。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年2月</a>　代朝廷出外主持祭典，有五律。作品：新息道中遇雪。<div id='poem_99534' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99534' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a 保德
