-----title
吉安
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='d4d3afc2a570470dbec534531483e445_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d4d3afc2a570470dbec534531483e445");'><span id='d4d3afc2a570470dbec534531483e445_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年</a>，46岁</div><div id='d4d3afc2a570470dbec534531483e445' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年8月4日</a>　到吉州任，有谢表。作品：吉州谢上表。<div id='poem_1158754' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158754' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158754?labeling=true' target='_blank'>吉州谢上表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1045年8月4日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158754")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158754_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158754'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158754'>臣某伏奉五月十五日敕命，差知吉州军州事，放朝辞取便路，疾速发赴本任者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158754_comment'></div>天鉴素诚，特从轻典，星驰即道，已届所临，寻于某月某日，到州赴上讫<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158754_comment'></div>伏念臣生自边州，闇于时务，谬从科试，早玷书林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158754_comment'></div>陛下擢臣于迁谪之馀，置臣于谏诤之列，匪由言荐，特出宸衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158754_comment'></div>而又掌西掖之训词，执史官之汗简，推宠过分，非臣所堪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158754_comment'></div>自惟疏贱之中，孤直见进，思所以报，知无不言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158754_comment'></div>补朝政而未工，为身谋而已拙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158754_comment'></div>谗谤不恤，用酬主知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158754_comment'></div>论议所伸，寡与势合，常欲引去，以免众猜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158754_comment'></div>岂意发于枢机，自起瑕谪，然念间者夏台效顺，再禀正朔，虏帐怙强，沮我封拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158754_comment'></div>徇虏约则西戎怨，纳夏欸则北狄怒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158754_comment'></div>重师宿境，须我报音，人人异论，必有兵祸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158754_comment'></div>圣虑独断，柄臣佥谋，授以聘词，择于朝列，有死不避，见选于臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158754_comment'></div>单车即途，送者失色；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158754_comment'></div>握节以往，敢望生还？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158754_comment'></div>历阶而议，所期理夺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158754_comment'></div>王命既达，而国体获伸；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158754_comment'></div>胡兵自交，而戎盟两就。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158754_comment'></div>此乃庙堂成算，非臣之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158754_comment'></div>及乎单于罢兵，穹庐报聘，谓知前议，再伸理装。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1158754_comment'></div>臣亦让以非才，辞不获命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1158754_comment'></div>汉使荐至，虏中甚欢，迎劳尤勤，宴犒加等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1158754_comment'></div>盖重邻好，非私臣身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1158754_comment'></div>臣既频到虏庭，欲练胡事，上则接谈于宾主，下则访事于舆隶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1158754_comment'></div>示相亲狎，则务通其情；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1158754_comment'></div>所临机会，则未尝屈礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1158754_comment'></div>本谓六蕃之语，可以博之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1158754_comment'></div>岂料一言之失，不能免罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1158754_comment'></div>仰冀宸造，鉴无他肠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1158754_comment'></div>窃以臣素乏时名，猥遭天眷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1158754_comment'></div>出于孤官，而延登近班；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1158754_comment'></div>岂无群材，而专聘绝域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1158754_comment'></div>蒙此宠任，人所忌嫉，而不慎言语，自罹宪章，计其所犯，死有馀责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1158754_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下，至明御宇，广覆如天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1158754_comment'></div>凡曰近臣，非有大故，不忍遐弃，止除外官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1158754_comment'></div>含容之德，过于尧禹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1158754_comment'></div>况夫庐陵古郡，南近家庭，临民侍亲，不为失所，戴荷恩育，宁可赀度？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1158754_comment'></div>方今边警虽息，民力犹困。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1158754_comment'></div>赋歛加疾，而吏以为健；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1158754_comment'></div>刻削已甚，而上不能知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1158754_comment'></div>若得询其疾苦，思所施设，蠲去横取，率循旧规，朝廷听而从之，岂以地狭为恨？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1158754_comment'></div>体国安民，图所报效，臣之愿也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1158754_comment'></div>无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_42_1158754_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年8月4日</a>　到吉州任，有谢启。在任勤询疾苦，削去苛横，坚持亲民善政。作品：谢知吉州启。<div id='poem_1158922' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158922' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158922?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢知吉州启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1045年8月4日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158922")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158922_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158922'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158922'>右，某启：伏奉敕命，差知吉州军州事，已于八月四日到州赴上讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158922_comment'></div>伏念某起自寒官，本无远图，偶逢圣明，遂玷清近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158922_comment'></div>论人君之得失，正史氏之褒贬，典西掖之纶綍，领中台之衡鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158922_comment'></div>宠任皆过，毫发无裨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158922_comment'></div>伏况行人之官，列辟所选，衔君命以申信，歌《皇华》而戒途，四方式瞻，专对为重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158922_comment'></div>且以朝廷之大，髦彦比肩，至如识周古今，言穷治乱，蕴厚重之器，抱通博之才，可以出锋颖于囊中，畅威声于方外者，济济盈庭，不可胜数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158922_comment'></div>而偎辱佥议，独当重委。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158922_comment'></div>不能死请，以坚避让之诚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158922_comment'></div>偶得生还，果贻狃习之患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158922_comment'></div>原其所坐，当伏严刑，尚蒙宽恩，俾领便郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158922_comment'></div>此盖伏遇昭文相公燮调元化，开济万邦，思九德之咸事，虑一物之失所，特形敷奏，见轸孤危，遏弹射溢恶之词，敦国家驭吏之体，正从薄谪，庸示深仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158922_comment'></div>风波垂拯于畏涂，日月遂回于曲照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158922_comment'></div>再苏朽瘁，敢忘厚恩？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158922_comment'></div>然念方今甲兵渐息，赋歛必省，谨当奉朝廷宽大之诏，求古人简易之理，削去苛横，勤询疾苦，庶竭驽蹇，少答恩私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158922_comment'></div>往此以还，罔知所措。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1158922_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年9月</a>　在吉州，作记。作品：江州庐山重修崇胜禅院记。<div id='poem_1158988' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158988' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158988?labeling=true' target='_blank'>江州庐山重修崇胜禅院记<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历五年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1045年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158988")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158988_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158988'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158988'>夫万寓之大、群动之众，佛以溥博之教、渊泉之语，广譬善导，无不入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158988_comment'></div>其言含生有知之类，人人物物，皆蕴佛性，犹木中有火，本来无睹，方便钻凿，乃见光华，离暗得明，不从外至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158988_comment'></div>故无生之说，以去缠缚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158988_comment'></div>有为之法，以勖因果。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158988_comment'></div>二者并施于世，随所悟解，归之等觉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158988_comment'></div>佛去世后，持其说而化于一方者，信向远近，视其缘之厚薄云耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158988_comment'></div>大江之南，号为山水奇胜，庐阜又称诸方之最，自东晋已来，高人开士，蝉联不绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158988_comment'></div>山形磅礴三百里，宝刹之有名于天下者以十数，四方学心之人多归焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158988_comment'></div>学人之至，必又能以圆顿一音之教，举其机而惊于众者，以登法席，茍得其人，则一言顿解，出生死海刹那顷耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158988_comment'></div>崇胜禅院，江南李氏乾德二年所建也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158988_comment'></div>远公莲社，绝顶相望；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158988_comment'></div>渊明栗里，高风接秀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158988_comment'></div>左泉漱玉，可以涤昏烦；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158988_comment'></div>前林蔽空，可以乐閒旷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158988_comment'></div>真遗世观空者宴息之地也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158988_comment'></div>景祐初，久虚禅席，于是州将而下，佥谋列刹，广询法王之器，授之猊座，遂得今禅祖珂师焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158988_comment'></div>寺之故居庳陋，不足容四方之来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158988_comment'></div>一日，珂师言于众曰：「吾以诸法一味，离去世间染净，忻厌一切差别境界，无有少法可说，乃能入于如来难思智地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158988_comment'></div>然而一切诸善，皆由信起，不有庄严，何能起信？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158988_comment'></div>若寂然无营，则陷于因任止灭之病矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1158988_comment'></div>众闻是语，翕然从风，其堂皇殿闼、庑序管库之不如制者，一皆新之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1158988_comment'></div>筑基而饬材，陶土而砻石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1158988_comment'></div>肖像设色，众工攸聚，栋宇轮奂，见者起恭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1158988_comment'></div>师以善教而流其法，以信而募其货，以智而役其工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1158988_comment'></div>自丙子经营，至甲申落成，轩槛回合，凡三百馀楹，雕琢金碧，皆极研丽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1158988_comment'></div>无有远迩，宾到如归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1158988_comment'></div>其徒之至者，寝于斯，食于斯，闻于斯，思于斯，觉于斯，夫见宗祊而起孝，睹墟墓而生哀，视塔庙而增信，其理一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1158988_comment'></div>某故史官，且师之同郡人，故得其实而书之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1158988_comment'></div>珂师通学敏识，少厌荣进，坏衣削发而居丛林，不露头角。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1158988_comment'></div>游庐阜若干年，提唱宗乘，集《轴禅录》七卷，盛行于世，时人服其该洽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1158988_comment'></div>噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1158988_comment'></div>自祖法之东流，六世而居曲江，今珂师生曲江，复以心法名于名山，古言孔子之后，邹鲁多儒，信矣哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1158988_comment'></div>庆历五年某月某日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1158988_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年10月</a>　应端州梁揆之求为其父梁頵作墓志。作品：宋光禄寺丞梁君墓表。<div id='poem_1159036' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159036' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159036?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宋故光禄寺丞梁君墓表<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历五年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1045年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1159036")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159036_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159036'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159036'>梁与秦、赵同祖，绝于秦，续于晋，显于汉，故为京兆万年人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159036_comment'></div>祖讳旻，佐幕番禺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159036_comment'></div>属刘氏据有南海，耻非王命，不从所署，遁于东筦，世归其高焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159036_comment'></div>二子：长曰光运，署右职，捕贼遇害；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159036_comment'></div>少曰光远，即君之文考，亦佐戎政，皆刘氏官也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159036_comment'></div>君讳頵，字微之，幼秉奇节，强学笃行，信义称于朋友，词章秀于乡邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159036_comment'></div>国家削平僭伪，统壹函夏，君即占籍高要以从乡赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159036_comment'></div>旧制，岭南按察者皆专选补，州县吏员阙，即择前资及士之豪俊而署之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159036_comment'></div>试守三岁，克有成效，则荐于吏部而授真秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159036_comment'></div>君以故事召署，满三期，调于天官，得象之武仙簿、贵之郁林尉、封之司户参军，悉以能官有声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159036_comment'></div>年及悬车，抗止足之分，移疾请老，朝廷美之，迁光禄寺丞致仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159036_comment'></div>以景祐元年六月考终命于封水，享年七十三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159036_comment'></div>夫人陈氏，先府君二岁卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159036_comment'></div>其孤揆继岁衔恤，遂蓬首垢面，挈畚负土，由祖妣而下，封大莹而窆之，凡六坟，异藏同域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159036_comment'></div>以景祐二年十二月辛酉，掩圹于端州高要县归仁乡湖洲原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159036_comment'></div>乃筑庐居冢旁，朝夕哭泣，刺手取血，写佛书以祈冥报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159036_comment'></div>庐外植蔬树粟以给饘粥，不茹荤血，凡六岁，乃除丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159036_comment'></div>州闾耆旧缁素以其状白长吏，表闻，天子嘉之，诏郡县以时存抚，赐之粟帛，以旌其孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159036_comment'></div>专选补者以揆至行，夺而官之，窘于穷而从焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159036_comment'></div>庆历五年十月，患旧域卑湿，仍负土全茔，徙瘗宗崇原，加封树焉，从高显也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159036_comment'></div>既而乞铭以表之，铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_1159036'>哀无时而忘，服有时而终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159036_comment'></div>去庐立表，以寄哀于无穷。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1159036_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年</a>　是年石介卒，长子伯庄亦卒。第三女适宿州观察支使周熊。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='7d95b04eaf5f46429f477c04817f208f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("7d95b04eaf5f46429f477c04817f208f");'><span id='7d95b04eaf5f46429f477c04817f208f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年</a>，47岁</div><div id='7d95b04eaf5f46429f477c04817f208f' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年</a>　春，应知饶州张清河之请，作记。作品：饶州新建州学记。<div id='poem_1158972' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158972' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158972?labeling=true' target='_blank'>饶州新建州学记<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历六年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1046年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158972")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158972_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158972'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158972'>汉袭暴秦之馀，治定五世，乃刊著功令，建郡国之学以育隽秀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158972_comment'></div>文翁作守巴蜀，克变其风，比于齐鲁，褎然称为循吏之首者，谨诏令、善条教也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158972_comment'></div>国家承五朝之季，刬僭薙偪，祖功宗德，翱翔四裔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158972_comment'></div>今上兴葺治本，二纪于兹，乃诏郡县立学，详延褒博。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158972_comment'></div>是岁，都官副郎清河张君自南海倅车移守鄱阳，举遗修要，事亡不缉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158972_comment'></div>一日集其僚而谋曰：「今天子思得贤俊，基固太平，诏启黉校，以广声教，郡国当以新书从事，庸副上意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158972_comment'></div>且古之教者，以学校为本，卿佐修之于国，父老修之于乡，旦而里父坐塾上以视民之出，暮视其入，以勖怠者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158972_comment'></div>又师氏、保氏以德、行、书、射共训于民，乡之秀者移之于邑，邑移于国，国以闻于天子，皆学之制也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158972_comment'></div>善为政者，固当先之，矧奉天子之诏乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158972_comment'></div>先是，郡先圣祠宫栋干隳剥，前守亦尝相土，而未遑缔搆也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158972_comment'></div>君于是即其基，于东湖之北偏而经营之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158972_comment'></div>郡之秀民，闻是谋者，争出家以助其费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158972_comment'></div>乃命从事之贤曰胡宗尧、属城之良曰朱琬籍而司之，得资三百五十万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158972_comment'></div>于是令畚筑，购楩梓，利匠器，程工力，度堂室，谨储峙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158972_comment'></div>朱墨之督，一本规矩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158972_comment'></div>远枕城闼，取乎居国之阳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158972_comment'></div>傍睨湖光，象乎雍水之半。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158972_comment'></div>严俎豆之习以隆乎礼，正师资之位以传其经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158972_comment'></div>萃乎群贤，贯之六艺，悉三代之遗则也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158972_comment'></div>乙酉仲夏，始庀其役，越期年而有成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1158972_comment'></div>凡为屋百二十楹，昼讲夜习，各有攸居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1158972_comment'></div>又市美田三顷以赋其日廪，仍奏署属县宿儒胡宁以为其表率，真君子乐育英材之意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1158972_comment'></div>移其意以及于天下，其善岂可量哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1158972_comment'></div>文翁、范侯不得独擅美于前史矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1158972_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年</a>　闻蔡襄近故郡为官，侍养高堂，即呈乞外任状。<div id='poem_1158747' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158747' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158747?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞外任状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1046年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158747")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158747_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158747'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158747'>臣误被采擢，待罪谏垣，自揣空疏，无以上报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158747_comment'></div>去岁尝与蔡襄皆以亲老，愿除家便一官，庶就侍奉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158747_comment'></div>圣慈宽裕，悉蒙厚恩，蔡襄给假还乡，臣某特赐缣帛，仍令差人迎侍，归京奉养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158747_comment'></div>仰荷非常之恩，足为私门之幸，事出望外，捐驱不忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158747_comment'></div>今春得臣父书，候秋与孙男迎娶，乃能即路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158747_comment'></div>初领此讯，诚亦有待其来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158747_comment'></div>今闻蔡襄父母，不忍去乡国，惟襄独行还朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158747_comment'></div>伏缘蔡襄躬自奉迎，尚犹不至，微臣差人般侍，必更迁延，在臣私心，进退无措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158747_comment'></div>伏念臣备职谏诤，言多过差，老父衰年，远在南土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158747_comment'></div>上不能补国家之阙，下不能展庭闱之私，何颜自安，久玷清望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158747_comment'></div>陛下悯此远迹，谅其素心，俾臣先尽事亲之诚，徐图报国之效，在于出处，不陷宪章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158747_comment'></div>伏乞特授臣沿流家便一郡差遣，以便侍养，庶当孝理之朝，未缺人臣之行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158747_comment'></div>若谓臣兼领史职，不当差出，则叶清臣、杨察等差出，已有成例，但臣无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1158747_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年</a>　再呈乞外任状。作品：再乞外任状。<div id='poem_1158748' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158748' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158748?labeling=true' target='_blank'>再乞外任状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1046年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158748")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158748_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158748'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158748'>右，臣近有奏陈，愿授家便差遣，虽坚诚请，未蒙朝旨允从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158748_comment'></div>伏以国家之意，谓臣身忝谏官，日言国事，今一旦无故即除外任，恐四方传闻，以为不容谏诤，不忍遣去，盖惜朝廷之名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158748_comment'></div>伏念臣生长远方，不识忌讳，顷年得罪，但坐多言，再表乞归，乃得近乡小郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158748_comment'></div>曾未逾岭，母氏已亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158748_comment'></div>服终还台，即求外补，愿归江国，稍便家庭，庶因斗筲之禄，用勤晨夕之养，而国家权俾掌礼，因得奉朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158748_comment'></div>去春忽被命书，猥参谏列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158748_comment'></div>言不经务，尽忠无益于时；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158748_comment'></div>才非出人，论事不能无过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158748_comment'></div>寻沥私恳，仰干宸严，但缘偏亲向衰，乞以寸禄归养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158748_comment'></div>遽蒙天眷，特赉帑缣，俾为奉迎之资，不许脱然而去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158748_comment'></div>实逾半载，亲舆未来，寻已启陈，未奉俞允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158748_comment'></div>伏惟圣神在宥，俊乂如林，才过臣者，比肩叠迹，臣去此职，必当得奇士，开益聪明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158748_comment'></div>如或惜去朝之为重，恐外迁之差屈，则乞令臣带小省之官，为名城之守，上以昭陛下从谏之盛德，下以成微臣养亲之私荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158748_comment'></div>中外闻之，自为至美之事，固于朝廷无所亏损，但臣无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1158748_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年3月</a>　暮春，闻杜鹃鸣叫，触感而有诗。作品：子规。<div id='poem_99461' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99461' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99461?labeling=true' target='_blank'>子规</a><span class='authorDate'>（1046年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99461")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_99461_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99461'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99461'>一叫一声残，声声万古冤。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99461_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99461'>疏烟明月树，微雨落花村。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99461_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99461'>易堕将乾泪，能伤欲断魂。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99461_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99461'>名缰惭自束，为尔忆家园。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99461_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_99461'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_99461_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年</a>　夏，应海琳禅师持函之约，作记。作品：韶州开元寺新建浴室记。<div id='poem_1158985' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158985' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158985?labeling=true' target='_blank'>韶州开元寺新建浴室记<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历六年六月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1046年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158985")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158985_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158985'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158985'>释氏之为道也，兼济于人不待乎达，独善之乐不专于穷，以悲智为修者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158985_comment'></div>悲之为言，仁之端也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158985_comment'></div>能与众多作大饶益、去大患难、获大安稳，视物之累，如身之忧，建功而不祈赏，益善而不祈报，此悲者之为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158985_comment'></div>智之为言，介之徒也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158985_comment'></div>守静默，舍欣厌，居市朝而非显，宅山林而非晦，身同梦幻，性等空虚，离五蕴，超三有，此智者之为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158985_comment'></div>韶于岭外为望州，卢祖印心之域，故寺最众，僧最多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158985_comment'></div>然郛郭之居，初无众浴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158985_comment'></div>开元寺者，精蓝之甲也，比刍延吉，以头陁苦行劝募依信，量力出货，聿图胜果。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158985_comment'></div>乃于寺东南之外壝相善地，市美材，购梓人，售陶工，积勤营构，用成温室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158985_comment'></div>八桂僧道夔勾稽其簿，矢谟于康定，落成于庆历之某年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158985_comment'></div>五日为期，一具汤沐，熏修者得以涓洁，尘垢者得以涤荡，至者欣欣，真兼济之事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158985_comment'></div>先是，州跨二江，通以浮梁，夏潦暴怒，岁苦漂泆，人用艰涉，户烦科督。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158985_comment'></div>吉师居河之湄，极力纠率，伐材以横大航，冶铁以络连锁，新而维之，众获其便，方辀并辔，如履康庄，积霖涨波，不能冲齧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158985_comment'></div>非悲智所乐，何以及此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158985_comment'></div>月华琳禅师，丛林之宗工也，以书来抵庐陵，谒词为志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158985_comment'></div>吉师曹溪人，姓侯氏，十六受具，遍游名山，禅学通悟，琳师称之，今受众请为住持主云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158985_comment'></div>庆历六年六月日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1158985_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年7月</a>　初秋，应惠阳僧智清之求，作铭。作品：袁州仰山齐长老寿塔铭。<div id='poem_1159046' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159046' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159046?labeling=true' target='_blank'>袁州仰山齐长老寿塔铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1046年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1159046")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159046_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159046'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159046'>天下地有形胜，境有清旷，必建佛刹，以为民福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159046_comment'></div>盖自汉明已来，像教东被，日崇月衍，栋宇遂繁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159046_comment'></div>及乎心印密传，宗风寖盛，通人间出，学者云趋，所以名山奥壤，必安清众，又常推择人誉，以崇善继。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159046_comment'></div>凡寺之兴衰，众之多寡，系乎师德之厚薄耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159046_comment'></div>袁州仰山者，通智大师之法席也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159046_comment'></div>通智讳慧寂，曹溪之裔孙、沩山之嫡嗣，陆丞相云「仰山龙纵于江西」是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159046_comment'></div>蹑履来游者，不下千人，于时号为小释迦，学徒之盛，诸方莫比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159046_comment'></div>殆今长老智齐，十五世矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159046_comment'></div>齐师安州人，俗姓某氏，遍游名岳，得法于栖贤諟禅师，于是息心居庐阜三十七岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159046_comment'></div>庆历中，仰山虚坐，转运使齐公廓询于缁素，以师应选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159046_comment'></div>三空四病，示人以要，啐啄之机，间不容息，或纵或夺，至者忘归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159046_comment'></div>住山凡二十年，悟而去者亦多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159046_comment'></div>乃于集云峰下自为寿藏，而种松千株，且示世间之法，无所染著，皆如幻住，死生之理，无所厌苦，皆如梦觉，何必语言，然后为学？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159046_comment'></div>惠阳僧智清以其书及其真来，且言师之行也如此，因其归，以铭寄之：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_1159046'>圣凡一性，死生一息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159046_comment'></div>悟者一言，顿超凡域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159046_comment'></div>湛然常存，无丧无得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159046_comment'></div>千株松下，来者之式。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1159046_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年</a>　应邀撰文。作品：循州新修白云山普安寺记。曾太傅临川十二诗序。<div id='poem_1159002' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159002' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159002?labeling=true' target='_blank'>循州新修白云山普安寺记<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历六年七月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1046年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1159002")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159002_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159002'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159002'>大雄氏之教也，国无中边，俗无同异，人无耆幼，士无愚智，闻其名氏，率用信向，非役而随，非威而济，茍有唱导，亡不响答。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159002_comment'></div>万家之都，十室之鄙，必立塔庙以寄瞻仰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159002_comment'></div>谁其尸之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159002_comment'></div>选在贤者，稽其类，拔其萃，推之于众，无虚授焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159002_comment'></div>龙川郡者，汉之名部，越之沃野，地近鱼盐之饶，士多江海之乐，故其资奉易足，而怂恿易劝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159002_comment'></div>且浮图之道也，俾人出贪网，断爱缚，守净默，慎熏染，广方便，重忏悔，俗所以闻声而乐从者，以舍恶径而趣善途也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159002_comment'></div>古有兰若曰普安，居子城之西隅，州人之所崇植也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159002_comment'></div>天禧中，遇郁攸之灾，煨烬无馀，惟老释曰智珣，相土于闲旷之野，得白云山焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159002_comment'></div>掘地数尺，有古石像七十馀躯，亦精庐之故墓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159002_comment'></div>始鸠工，而珣即世，州将吁众，以今住持僧德广承其基焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159002_comment'></div>鸱其屋以藏像，猊其座以存法，列鬲而烹以示均，击钟而食以来众，皆古之制也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159002_comment'></div>尺椽片瓦，力所收焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159002_comment'></div>茂材修干，手所植焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159002_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159002_comment'></div>今夫士庶百族，以天性之笃，血食之重，鲜克数世恢隆丕烈者，亡他术焉，昵于亲耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159002_comment'></div>浮图氏则不然，邑择于邑，乡择于乡，超登其良，以绍耿光，绵世而益昌者，此其所长也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159002_comment'></div>广师本郡人，张姓，受业于圣寿寺，受具于南海之祖坛，出继珣师于白云山，择其良也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159002_comment'></div>岁在阉茂，抨图逾岭谒志，揽其实而书之云尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159002_comment'></div>庆历六年七月八日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1159002_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1158944' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158944' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158944?labeling=true' target='_blank'>曾太博临川十二诗序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1046年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158944")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158944_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158944'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158944'>古今言诗者，二《雅》而降，骚人之作，号为雄杰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158944_comment'></div>仆常患灵均负才矜己，一不得用于时，则忧愁恚憝，不能自裕其意，取讥通人，才虽美而趣不足尚，久欲著于言议而莫由也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158944_comment'></div>今兹得罪去朝，守土滨江，同年不疑曾兄惠然拿舟见顾，间日共言临川山水之美，因出十二诗以露其奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158944_comment'></div>其诗皆讽咏前贤遗懿、当代绝境，未尝一言及于身世，陶然有飞遁之想。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158944_comment'></div>通哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158944_comment'></div>不疑不以时之用舍累其心，真吾所尚哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158944_comment'></div>遂题其篇。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1158944_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年8月</a>　仲秋，御史茹孝标复职，以靖“少游广州，犯法受谤”罪名进谗。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年8月</a>　余靖左迁将作少监，时靖已积劳成疾，遂以病为名求朝廷分司南京解官侍养，有状。作品：乞分司状。<div id='poem_1158755' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158755' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158755?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞分司状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1046年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158755")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158755_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158755'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158755'>臣再沥血诚，上干天听，退量烦渎，甘俟诛夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158755_comment'></div>伏念臣生于鄙远，素无才识，束发从宦，二纪于兹，遭时见用，遂忝清近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158755_comment'></div>然念臣顷蒙擢在谏垣，累上七章，乞免谏职，出就外任，以便侍养，皆蒙朝廷不赐允许。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158755_comment'></div>及至去年得罪，不敢迂路归乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158755_comment'></div>又缘臣父年渐衰老，不乐远出，寻曾乞移便郡，愿解近职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158755_comment'></div>私诚虽切，未闻报可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158755_comment'></div>臣揆才至薄，负罪则深，上无补于国家，下阙奉于温凊，一身之责，万死何逃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158755_comment'></div>臣今欲乞落职分司，归乡侍养，伏望天慈，特赐矜允。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1158755_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年8月</a>　获准，有谢表。作品：谢分司表。<div id='poem_1158756' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158756' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158756?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢分司表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1046年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158756")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158756_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158756'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158756'>臣某言：与夺者朝廷之大柄，出处者人臣之大方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158756_comment'></div>成命自天，退身得地<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158756_comment'></div>伏念臣乡邦遐远，世系孤平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158756_comment'></div>偶自童观，即亲儒术，寻师千里，备历险艰，志学十年，乃得科第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158756_comment'></div>国家颁制目以求士，开文馆以待贤，臣之非才，咸预兹选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158756_comment'></div>每守孤直，不事贵权，盖尝忤旨而谪官，寻亦知名而见用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158756_comment'></div>降发中之诏，擢居谏诤之联；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158756_comment'></div>以出疆之勤，延登侍从之列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158756_comment'></div>愿宣忠力，以酬万乘之知；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158756_comment'></div>屡被国恩，自忘五羖之贱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158756_comment'></div>多所论列，罔畏仇嫌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158756_comment'></div>臣既拙于周身，毁者得以销骨，惟期退避，屡抗表章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158756_comment'></div>帝座虽处九重之深，皇明远照万里之外，预颁明命，克遂初心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158756_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下，天覆无私，乾刚独断。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158756_comment'></div>念臣尝经躯策，不避艰危；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158756_comment'></div>察臣本以公言，搆成私隙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158756_comment'></div>俾从散秩，归奉所天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158756_comment'></div>下以成微臣就养之勤，上以全陛下退人之道，丘山荷赐，冰炭在怀。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1158756_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年8月</a>　王子元已陞信州别驾，闻靖病即行告假，到吉州陪靖南下。<br /></div>
-----end

-----title
梧州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='4446143fb4d4489da68016c48f5b9598_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("4446143fb4d4489da68016c48f5b9598");'><span id='4446143fb4d4489da68016c48f5b9598_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1052&endYear=1052')">1052年</a>，53岁</div><div id='4446143fb4d4489da68016c48f5b9598' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1052&endYear=1052')">1052年</a>　是年，三子叔英中朝乡进士，是榜年最幼。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='091deec85b95428daffe043ebbb3717f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("091deec85b95428daffe043ebbb3717f");'><span id='091deec85b95428daffe043ebbb3717f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1052&endYear=1053')">1052-1053年</a>，53-54岁</div><div id='091deec85b95428daffe043ebbb3717f' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1052&endYear=1052')">1052年</a>　靖领兵追至西境，屯兵梧州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1052&endYear=1052')">1052年</a>　是年三子叔英中朝乡进士，是榜年最幼。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1053')">1053年</a>　朝廷任命狄青为宣徽南院使、宣抚荆湖路，提举广南经制贼盗事，并诏鄜延、环庆、泾原路择蕃兵广锐军各五千人赴广南行营，诏孙沔、余靖辅助，合兵剿灭。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1053')">1053年</a>　广南西路钤辖孙曙与叛军战于金城驿，兵败，死二千余人。狄青至宾州，数曙败军之罪，并军校数十人皆斩之。靖起拜曰：“曙之失律，亦靖节制之罪。”青曰：“舍人文臣，军旅之责，非所任也。”释不问，众将士遂听令，各自奋力为战。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1053')">1053年1月25日</a>　大败侬智高兵于归仁铺，伪侍郎黄师宓及其母嫁特磨道蛮酋侬夏卿，以重金贿其兄侬夏诚，遂得逃入特磨道。靖有贺表。作品：代狄宣抚贺捷表。<div id='poem_1158790' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158790' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158790?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代狄宣抚贺捷表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1053年1月25日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158790")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158790_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158790'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158790'>臣某言：正月十八日至邕州归仁铺，蛮贼侬智高徒党出城迎战，登时杀获首领黄师必等二千馀人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158790_comment'></div>当夜侬智高焚城将带残徒潜遁，寻差兵甲及溪峒壮丁袭逐，今月某日已出省地界者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158790_comment'></div>万里奉词，盖肃将于天讨；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158790_comment'></div>群蛮一战，遂收复于边城<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158790_comment'></div>窃以国家威叠四方，恩涵八表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158790_comment'></div>日月所照，悉解辫而来庭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158790_comment'></div>舟车所通，率辇赆而修贡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158790_comment'></div>蠢尔广源之部族，本惟交趾之附庸，自肆陆梁，招纳亡叛，乘边陲之失备，兴戈甲以内侵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158790_comment'></div>焚荡州闾，钞劫生聚，远浮江郁，直抵番禺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158790_comment'></div>自岭而南，忘战兹久，忽逢冲突，无不骛骚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158790_comment'></div>亦尝屡遣师徒，分命将帅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158790_comment'></div>军无部伍，人不齐同，勇者邀功而鲜谋，怯者贪生而先退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158790_comment'></div>贼既未经挫衄，愈恣猖狂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158790_comment'></div>臣忝预咨询，日亲机宥，睹兹丑类，能不疚心？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158790_comment'></div>久烦旰食之忧，敢怠请行之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158790_comment'></div>果蒙睿眷，见许愚忠，授成算以即途，加宠名而异数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158790_comment'></div>常虑虚叨边寄，不副主知，况彼窃据城池，图为巢穴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158790_comment'></div>守于九地之下，未易进攻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158790_comment'></div>御以七擒之奇，固无良策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158790_comment'></div>而乃敢率犬羊之众，前当貔虎之师，意拒辙而甚骄，势破竹而先解。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1158790_comment'></div>横尸满野，委甲如山，既触网以计穷，遂焚营而宵遁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1158790_comment'></div>系累者逸，老幼得以再生；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1158790_comment'></div>煨烬所馀，金帛积而无算。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1158790_comment'></div>再获金城之固，几还铜柱之封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1158790_comment'></div>非臣短材，能集兹事，此盖皇帝陛下宸机电发，睿略天成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1158790_comment'></div>事达其情，体汉光之远照；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1158790_comment'></div>师行以律，赐魏武之《新书》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1158790_comment'></div>故此凶强，遽然破碎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1158790_comment'></div>抚其彫瘵，浸惠泽于民心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1158790_comment'></div>歼彼狡顽，振天声于方外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1158790_comment'></div>臣无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1158790_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
长沙
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='3f874e2f1c3b4199b119c46f27ff4183_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("3f874e2f1c3b4199b119c46f27ff4183");'><span id='3f874e2f1c3b4199b119c46f27ff4183_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1052&endYear=1052')">1052年</a>，53岁</div><div id='3f874e2f1c3b4199b119c46f27ff4183' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1052&endYear=1052')">1052年6月23日</a>　急行赴任，途中接劄子三道，改知桂州。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='3398bb6efc8645b19e061a9fb9db121c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("3398bb6efc8645b19e061a9fb9db121c");'><span id='3398bb6efc8645b19e061a9fb9db121c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1057&endYear=1058')">1057-1058年</a>，58-59岁</div><div id='3398bb6efc8645b19e061a9fb9db121c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1057&endYear=1057')">1057年3月23日</a>　到任，卸任到任谢绝一切馈赠。有谢表。作品：潭州谢上表。<div id='poem_1158774' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158774' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158774?labeling=true' target='_blank'>潭州谢上表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1057年3月23日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158774")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158774_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158774'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158774'>臣某言：伏奉敕命，就差知潭州军州事、充荆湖南路安抚使，已于今月二十三日到任上讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158774_comment'></div>久居炎徼，忽荷天恩，虽尚远于阙庭，幸无虞于瘴疠<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158774_comment'></div>伏念臣素无学术，徒偶休明，宦路风波，艰危备历，君恩雨露，涓滴未酬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158774_comment'></div>顷罹栾棘之哀，尚浅期祥之制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158774_comment'></div>属溪蛮之叛涣，轶边戍以跳梁，攻围越台，侵逼庾峤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158774_comment'></div>虽微臣修完堡障，本期自固于家林；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158774_comment'></div>而朝廷夺去缞麻，遽俾分持于戎律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158774_comment'></div>惧薄材而败事，会元帅之成功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158774_comment'></div>假号渠魁，既远逃于夷域；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158774_comment'></div>主谋凶媪，俄就戮于天街。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158774_comment'></div>盖震叠于皇威，致敉宁于蛮落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158774_comment'></div>臣无纤芥之力，徒居戎旅之间，职是累年，空尸厚禄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158774_comment'></div>岂谓忽承丹诏，还抚旧封，再见昔时之山川，如全此生之首领。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158774_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下天慈广覆，日照无私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158774_comment'></div>公听并观，用臣于众毁必察之际；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158774_comment'></div>记功忘过，知臣有临危不避之诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158774_comment'></div>每遇急难，必蒙驱策，既臻平定，未忍弃捐，重施造化之恩，复委藩防之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158774_comment'></div>谨当率循政体，讲守邦经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158774_comment'></div>封内之民或未康，必询其庶隐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158774_comment'></div>境上之兵犹未戢，亟议于绥怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1158774_comment'></div>图报国恩，庶逭官责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1158774_comment'></div>臣无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1158774_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1057&endYear=1057')">1057年</a>　有谢启。作品：谢知潭州启。<div id='poem_1158925' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158925' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158925?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢知潭州启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1057年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158925")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158925_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158925'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158925'>右，某启：伏奉敕命，就移前件差遣，已于今月二十三日到任上讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158925_comment'></div>伏念某器非应务，才乏适时，盖识浅而虑昏，故毁多而誉少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158925_comment'></div>向以哀缠风树，归处丘樊，属当蛮事之兴，首预诏除之目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158925_comment'></div>三湘假守，初令备御于封陲；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158925_comment'></div>五筦董戎，遽俾亲临于矢石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158925_comment'></div>矧机筹之素惰，惧首领以难全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158925_comment'></div>所赖者元帅总其中权，迩臣定其远制，乃容无似，于此备员。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158925_comment'></div>以至大憝遐奔，子母不能全其族；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158925_comment'></div>外夷协比，斧钺得以正其诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158925_comment'></div>皆上禀于庙谋，致甫消于边患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158925_comment'></div>因之积岁，幸免瘝官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158925_comment'></div>念婚嫁之失期，愿圭符而易地，果蒙俞旨，还抚旧封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158925_comment'></div>顾忝窃以居多，实权衡之有托。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158925_comment'></div>此盖伏遇昭文相公明谟特出，广度并容，谓其尝辱于埏陶，未忍遐遗于林薮，过形敷奏，犹假宠名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158925_comment'></div>敢不祗畏简书，询求疾隐？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158925_comment'></div>蛮溪戍嶂，图销未弭之兵；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158925_comment'></div>士里农闾，期问未康之俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158925_comment'></div>庶展宣风之效，庸酬播物之恩。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1158925_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1057&endYear=1057')">1057年</a>　三月十日，狄青卒，家人遵遗嘱远道求靖撰墓铭。作品：宋故狄令公墓铭。<div id='poem_1159019' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159019' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159019?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宋故狄令公墓铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（并序　嘉祐四年二月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1057年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1159019")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159019_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159019'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159019'>惟宋四世嘉祐二年三月，陈州上言：护国军节度使、同中书门下平章事狄公，属疾于镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159019_comment'></div>诏遣国医驰视，未至，以薨闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159019_comment'></div>天子震悼，为之素服发哀，再不视朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159019_comment'></div>制赠中书令，厚赙其家，褒勋臣也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159019_comment'></div>公讳青，字汉臣，赠太傅讳应之曾孙，赠太师讳真之孙，赠中书令讳普之少子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159019_comment'></div>汾州西河人，远祖唐纳言梁文惠公仁杰，本家太原，危言直节，再复唐嗣，子孙或从汾晋，世为著姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159019_comment'></div>公谨重信厚，风骨异常，少以骑射为乐，期于功名自立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159019_comment'></div>弱冠游京师，系名拱圣籍中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159019_comment'></div>国家自北虏请盟，韬偃师节，息烽彻警，垂四十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159019_comment'></div>元昊世以河西称藩，常岁遣牙校贡方物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159019_comment'></div>胡贾往来，直抵都下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159019_comment'></div>奸人窥觇，知我虚实，一旦上还印节，僭盗名字，朝廷始增兵择将，以为戎备，时宝元元年也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159019_comment'></div>公初以散直为延州指使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159019_comment'></div>贼昊宿心苞藏，椎锋甚锐，吾边弭兵兹久，士不知战，他将遇之，靡不折衄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159019_comment'></div>延安最当贼冲，公以材武智略，频与贼较，未尝少沮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159019_comment'></div>四年之间，大小二十五战，中流矢者八，斩捕首虏万馀，获马、牛、羊、橐驼、驴、铠甲、符印、器仗以数万计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159019_comment'></div>攻贼金汤城及西南马市，至于杏林原，破其镇砦七，遂略宥州之境，屠龙咩、岁香等部落，燔其积聚数万、庐舍千馀，收其族帐二千三百、生口五千七百。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159019_comment'></div>又城穚子谷，筑招安、丰林、新塞、大郎堡，皆扼贼之要害，而夺其气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159019_comment'></div>朝恩懋赏，七迁至秦州刺史、泾原路兵马副部署。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159019_comment'></div>上奇公功，欲召见之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159019_comment'></div>无何，寇逼平凉，乃命公即趋泾原，俾图形以进，京师不呼公名而呼狄万，盖比之关、张也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159019_comment'></div>公在泾原数岁，贼不敢犯塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159019_comment'></div>复以夏国主称臣，由是边柝解严矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159019_comment'></div>遂以侍卫亲军职名宠公，徙真定府路部署，累迁至彰化军节度使、知延州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159019_comment'></div>羌人修贡，道出高奴，边事裁处，不遑中覆，故佥议帅臣，常为诸镇之首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159019_comment'></div>公当是任，边戎畏伏，乃召为枢密副使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159019_comment'></div>会蛮寇内侵，岭海警扰，公以疆埸之虞、廊庙之忧，抗章请行，宽上南顾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1159019_comment'></div>上嘉其诚，遂改宣徽南院使、荆湖南北路宣抚使、提举广南经制贼盗事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1159019_comment'></div>初，侬氏之蛮，世为酋豪，羁附交趾，智高趫勇而善用兵，因击并旁近州邑而统有之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1159019_comment'></div>拓地寖广，胜兵寖盛，交趾不能制，南方亡命者多归之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1159019_comment'></div>由是儗正朔，置百官，潜窥据窃峤南之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1159019_comment'></div>以皇祐四年五月，举兵攻邕州，陷之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1159019_comment'></div>乘郁江瀑流，连陷沿江九郡，杀逐其守臣，遂攻广州，围之，连月不尅，大掠而还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1159019_comment'></div>仍覆没四将，燔毁二郡，俘劫兵民数万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1159019_comment'></div>复据邕州城，诱略溪峒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1159019_comment'></div>江湘已南，为之骚然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1159019_comment'></div>朝旨以公大臣，既可其行，第令驻于桂、象之间，训练师旅，而指授方略于群帅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1159019_comment'></div>公以二广安危，在此一举，若偏裨失利，则兵气难振，自非躬亲，无以号令，先行后闻，朝议韪之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1159019_comment'></div>五年正月甲辰，三将之兵会于宾州，公接士大夫以礼，御下以严，临敌制变，众莫之测。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1159019_comment'></div>己酉下令，人赋十日之粮，谍者既去，诘旦遂行，故贼以师期尚缓，不克守险者以此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1159019_comment'></div>己未，至归仁铺，贼悉其众据高迎战，前锋遇之，少却，左第一将孙节死之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1159019_comment'></div>公亲执旗鼓，麾骑兵，左右驰出贼后，贼遂大败，驰骑追捕，斩首二千二百，贼之谋主黄师虙、侬志忠等腹心爪牙没于阵者五十七人，智高焚营而遁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1159019_comment'></div>明日，按兵入城，获金银器用二万，戎仗称是，伪符节十一、马牛千馀，老壮士女还城者三千馀人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1159019_comment'></div>再遣阅闉外创重归死者，复得尸三千二百。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1159019_comment'></div>翌日，分兵追袭贼之馀党，几歼焉，招复虏口七千三百。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1159019_comment'></div>其邕人也，俾奠其居；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1159019_comment'></div>非邕人者，振廪续食，还其本土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1159019_comment'></div>所得贼之遗物暨首级之赏，估直四千万，均给战士，仍筑京观，以志武功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1159019_comment'></div>二月丙子班师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1159019_comment'></div>辛巳，诏迁检校太尉、河中尹，召还枢府，遂曲赦广南，至于江西、湖南，咸宣布德音焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1159019_comment'></div>未几，进拜枢密使，领节如故，仍赐城南第一区，诸子悉增其秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1159019_comment'></div>职居机轴，势均台宰，外颁戎马之政，内参宫省之务，弼违顺美，动协厥中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1159019_comment'></div>越四年，愿去权宠，以辞盛满，遂兼相印出临辅郡，暴疾而终，享年五十。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1159019_comment'></div>公天赋明智，世推权勇，临事董众，识与几会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1159019_comment'></div>其行师也，所统步骑不以众寡，常取诸葛武侯八阵法以为模楷，宿息坐作，悉成部伍，故虽仓卒遇敌，而师徒无桡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1159019_comment'></div>其为偏裨时，每被发面铜，其从骑兵驰突贼阵，羌人识之，见则辟易，无敢当者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1159019_comment'></div>尝中流矢，创甚，闻寇至，裹创而行，帅不能止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1159019_comment'></div>公器度深远，今相国韩公、故资政殿大学士范文正公之为西帅也，公皆隶其节下，咸奇之曰：「此国器也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1159019_comment'></div>文正尝以《左氏春秋》授公曰：「熟此可以断大事，将不知古今，匹夫之勇，不足为也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1159019_comment'></div>公于是晚节益喜书史，既明见时事成败，尤好节义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1159019_comment'></div>其在泾原也，副起居舍人、知渭州尹洙与公同经略招讨安抚使事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1159019_comment'></div>洙字师鲁，有文武才略，博通古今，公与虑事，尤为精密。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1159019_comment'></div>师鲁尝称公：「古之名将，无以过也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1159019_comment'></div>公于交游，在亡不渝，师鲁后以贬死，公厚恤其孤，如至亲焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1159019_comment'></div>文正既没，其子纯礼服除还台，当莅吴中市征，公首为启陈，得署河南宾幕，以便坟垄，识者称之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1159019_comment'></div>其徙真定也，过家上冢，还谒县长，步趋令庭，以修桑梓之恭，然令不敢当，议者重其得体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1159019_comment'></div>遂留里中，与故老酾酒相欢，挥金而去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1159019_comment'></div>其征蛮也，上亲饯于垂拱，命釂者数焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1159019_comment'></div>当是时，衮国太夫人侯氏微疾，公朝服而入，戒家人无得言治兵事，第云「奉使江表」，故得不忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1159019_comment'></div>其纯孝如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1159019_comment'></div>公好以众整，又能分功与人，而令在必行，故师之所过，秋毫无犯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1159019_comment'></div>其为小校延安也，大里、南安、安远之功，初不自言，物议多之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1159019_comment'></div>其征南也，今观文殿学士孙公时经制贼盗，与公偕行，其军中之政，公实专之，至于南夏经久之制，多让孙公裁处，谈者嘉其谦挹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1159019_comment'></div>初，广西钤辖陈曙以步卒八千溃于昆崙关，公至，推首遁者殿直袁用而下并曙，诛三十一人，其下股慄，遂能一战而成大功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1159019_comment'></div>公历官自三班差使、殿侍迁左右班殿直、侍禁、閤门祗候、通事舍人、西上閤门副使，正除秦州刺史、遥领惠州团练、眉州防御使、保大军两使留后，真拜彰化、护国军节度使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1159019_comment'></div>职事自指使迁延州西路巡检、鄜延路都监、沿边都巡检、泾原仪渭兵马部署，遂总禁旅，历捧日天武四厢都指挥使、步军殿前都虞候、步军马军副都指挥使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1159019_comment'></div>其为兵马部署，以泾原部署知渭州、真定部署权定州、鄜延路经略安抚使知延州，皆著能政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1159019_comment'></div>一拜宣徽使，再践枢密副使，遂总机政，以兼相判陈州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1159019_comment'></div>临民统军，未尝少有差失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1159019_comment'></div>其征羌平蛮，名震夷狄，勋在竹帛，近代之良将也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1159019_comment'></div>公娶魏氏，封定国夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1159019_comment'></div>五男：长咨，西上閤门副使；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1159019_comment'></div>次咏，东头供奉官、閤门祗候；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1159019_comment'></div>譓、谏，皆内殿崇班；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1159019_comment'></div>说，东头供奉官，不幸以夭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1159019_comment'></div>二女，许嫁而未行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1159019_comment'></div>孙璋，左侍禁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1159019_comment'></div>瓙，尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1159019_comment'></div>同产兄素，右班殿直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1159019_comment'></div>兄子五人：询，左侍禁、閤门祗候；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1159019_comment'></div>诜，左班殿直；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1159019_comment'></div>諲、谆、䛆，皆左侍禁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1159019_comment'></div>从父兄靖，左班殿直，其子详，右侍禁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1159019_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1159019_comment'></div>戎夷旅距之际，公悉力捍御，以至平定，宜享遐福、而禀命不融，后世其有兴者乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1159019_comment'></div>公薨之年，归殡京师，明年，卜宅西河之太平乡刘村里，又明年二月十九日襄事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1159019_comment'></div>太常诔行，考功议绩，百僚佥允，乃赐谥曰武襄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1159019_comment'></div>诏给本品卤簿，送至都外，启攒掩圹，并辍其日视朝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1159019_comment'></div>仍诏所经道发卒卫送葬所，州县优假人牛车马，特恩也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1159019_comment'></div>其孤咨等既已砻石树碑神道之表，以靖尝从征南，复谒铭以志幽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1159019_comment'></div>遂铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_100_1159019'>天生哲人，康济斯民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1159019_comment'></div>不有屯难，何展经纶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1159019_comment'></div>眷言平夏，弈世称臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1159019_comment'></div>一旦陆梁，边鄙生尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1159019_comment'></div>公之忠勤，威名冠军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1159019_comment'></div>近斗远略，岁策其勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1159019_comment'></div>寇入萧关，即镇泾原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1159019_comment'></div>图形以进，百辟改观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1159019_comment'></div>入董卫卒，风清禁屯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1159019_comment'></div>出总边兵，霜凝塞垣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1159019_comment'></div>乃建高牙，以肃和门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1159019_comment'></div>延登枢府，式赞治源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1159019_comment'></div>蠢兹侬蛮，轻去巢穴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1159019_comment'></div>陷邕围广，图据全越。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1159019_comment'></div>公之善筹，成于庙谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1159019_comment'></div>愿得奋行，馘彼凶酋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1159019_comment'></div>帝念其诚，俾公专征。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1159019_comment'></div>岭海之区，傒公以宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1159019_comment'></div>收复边城，绥抚遗氓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1159019_comment'></div>南夏再平，繄公之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1159019_comment'></div>露布传呼，欢声九衢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1159019_comment'></div>曲赦岭表，德音江湖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1159019_comment'></div>乃陟太尉，乃尹河中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1159019_comment'></div>升总机务，言畴厥庸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1159019_comment'></div>枢极之柄，兵戎大政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1159019_comment'></div>弼谐有托，方隅以静。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1159019_comment'></div>致主推诚，辞权戒盈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1159019_comment'></div>乃锡相印，以镇陪京。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1159019_comment'></div>天胡不仁，夺我勋臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1159019_comment'></div>上心嗟悯，悼往抚存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1159019_comment'></div>輴车孰引，发卒三川。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1159019_comment'></div>铭旌改宠，卤簿宣恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1159019_comment'></div>佳城何在，汾河介山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1159019_comment'></div>勋书彝鼎，冢象耆连。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1159019_comment'></div>山西出将，天下称贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1159019_comment'></div>功名不朽，亿万斯年<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_135_1159019'></div><div id='poem_sentence_135_1159019_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1159019'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_135_1159019_0'>⑴ 《武溪集》卷一九。又见《广东文徵》卷六五。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1159019_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1057&endYear=1057')">1057年</a>　兼充荆湖南路经略安抚使，常微服私访州县，查处不法官吏豪绅，吏治一新。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1057&endYear=1057')">1057年</a>　夏间，有诗。作品：端午日事。端午日寄酒庶回都官。和邃卿张学士暑夕。<div id='poem_99457' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99457' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99457?labeling=true' target='_blank'>端午日事</a><span class='authorDate'>（1057年5月5日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99457")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_99457_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99457'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99457'>江上何人吊屈平，但闻风俗彩舟轻。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99457_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99457'>空斋无事同儿戏，学系朱丝辟五兵。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99457_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99457'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_99457_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_99458' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99458' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99458?labeling=true' target='_blank'>端午日寄酒庶回都官</a><span class='authorDate'>（1057年5月5日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99458")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_99458_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99458'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99458'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_99458", 99458, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>龙舟</span>争快楚江滨，吊屈谁知特怆神。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99458_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99458'>家酿寄君须酩酊，古今嫌见<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_99458", 99458, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>独醒人</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99458_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99458'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_99458_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_99485' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99485' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99485?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和邃卿张学士暑夕</a><span class='authorDate'>（1057年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99485")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_99485_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99485'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99485'>危坐空斋暝色低，三金才伏火将西。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99485_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99485'>烟蒙细草流萤度，月上疏林倦鹊栖。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99485_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99485'>荃葛野裳交羽扇，桔槔邻圃响蔬<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>畦。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99485_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99485'>中宵爽气夺炎热，却笑班姬谩惨悽。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99485_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_99485'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_99485_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_99485'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_2_99485_0'>⑴ 原作疏，据四库本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_99485_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1057&endYear=1057')">1057年</a>　惊闻好友孙抗卒，有祭文。作品：祭孙工部文。<div id='poem_1159050' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159050' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159050?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭孙工部文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1057年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1159050")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159050_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159050'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159050'>惟灵黟山之英，生为俊明，学探圣域，诗合雅声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159050_comment'></div>再以科进，列于王庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159050_comment'></div>豸冠霜简，凛凛持平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159050_comment'></div>绣衣朱旆，未足于外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159050_comment'></div>二易江城，直道无悔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159050_comment'></div>粤惟前载，寇攻南海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159050_comment'></div>烽火飞腾，岭隅震骇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159050_comment'></div>君乘使车，闻急惊呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159050_comment'></div>不俟王命，遽发铜符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159050_comment'></div>救兵先集，围城不孤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159050_comment'></div>番禺无虞，惟君之羭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159050_comment'></div>帝曰汝材，将漕来此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159050_comment'></div>盗据边关，旁无储峙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159050_comment'></div>元戎秉钺，貔貅千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159050_comment'></div>饷馈不续，许之以死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159050_comment'></div>君运心计，委粟流钱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159050_comment'></div>士免饥色，凯歌以旋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159050_comment'></div>幕府第劳，郎曹再迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159050_comment'></div>当享遐福，胡不永年？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159050_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159050_comment'></div>君于场屋，名出辈流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159050_comment'></div>作掾南昌，始与君游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159050_comment'></div>柔圆易安，刚方多滞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159050_comment'></div>假守庐陵，朱轮相继。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159050_comment'></div>生叨郡寄，君领监司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159050_comment'></div>再任相逢，哀乐是随。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159050_comment'></div>君哭吾父，我哭君身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1159050_comment'></div>嗟嗟世人，纠缠相因。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1159050_comment'></div>聊陈薄奠，以告营魂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1159050_comment'></div>茫茫九泉，孰听斯言？</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1159050_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1057&endYear=1057')">1057年</a>　应同榜进士屯田员外郎、广南西路转运使苏安世之请，为其祖作墓铭。作品：宋故殿直苏府君墓志铭。<div id='poem_1159028' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159028' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159028?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宋故殿直苏府君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（嘉祐二年十月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1159028")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159028_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159028'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159028'>府君讳继，字传之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159028_comment'></div>其先盖祝融之裔，为周寰内卿士，故为武功著姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159028_comment'></div>唐僖宗幸蜀，扈驾而西者，徙名数于成都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159028_comment'></div>祖讳厚，仕蜀至尚食使；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159028_comment'></div>考讳进之，为蜀牙兵校长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159028_comment'></div>蜀亡，孟氏之臣例署东宫官，得副率。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159028_comment'></div>府君以父任，累迁殿直，太平兴国中，授深州安平寨主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159028_comment'></div>是时北虏岁扰边，安平虽名堡障，宿兵不满数百，援师不集，则祸至常不测。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159028_comment'></div>或劝府君辞勿行，府君曰：「平时既食其禄，急辞其难，非人臣节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159028_comment'></div>吾不耻于死，而耻以此生」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159028_comment'></div>遂寓家他所，而独之安平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159028_comment'></div>明年，虏以兵夜袭寨城，果以无援，遂至陷没，享年七十五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159028_comment'></div>帅臣讳援兵稽期，诬以不备敌闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159028_comment'></div>繇是，虽死王事而赠典不及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159028_comment'></div>吁，忠义其难行哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159028_comment'></div>子咸熙，南京留守判官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159028_comment'></div>孙二人：长曰安世，尚书屯田员外郎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159028_comment'></div>次曰昌世，太庙斋郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159028_comment'></div>以嘉祐二年十月庚午，并举王父母考妣四丧，归葬于扬州江都县兴宁乡马坊原，府君与夫人许氏同藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159028_comment'></div>俾作铭于幽宫，铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_1159028'>常人宴安，唯禄与利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159028_comment'></div>君子所徇，曰忠与义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159028_comment'></div>既食其食，夷险一致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159028_comment'></div>履危忘难，虽死不避。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159028_comment'></div>守帅蒙上，唯善之蔽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159028_comment'></div>赠典不加，忠魂无愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159028_comment'></div>福不在身，在乎来裔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159028_comment'></div>吁嗟九原，古人之继。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1159028_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1057&endYear=1057')">1057年</a>　应同榜进士屯田员外郎、广南西路转运使苏安世之请，为其父作墓铭。作品：宋故南京留守判官赠都官郎中苏公墓志铭。<div id='poem_1159029' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159029' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159029?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宋故南京留守判官赠都官郎中苏公墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（嘉祐二年十月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1159029")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159029_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159029'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159029'>公讳咸熙，字太和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159029_comment'></div>其先胙土于苏，为周卿士，故代为武功人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159029_comment'></div>曾门讳厚，以唐末翠华西幸，避兵至蜀，仕蜀至尚食使，因为成都人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159029_comment'></div>祖讳进之，从孟昶归朝，授东宫副率。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159029_comment'></div>考讳继，殿直、深州安平寨主，契丹犯寨陷焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159029_comment'></div>公以太平兴国八年明经擢第，授邠州定平尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159029_comment'></div>会朔易帅，耻于援兵不出，痛诋安平失守，公缘坐谪澧州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159029_comment'></div>未几，义士疏其状，天子悯焉，诏释之，调绥州司法参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159029_comment'></div>太宗割绥、银畀夏国，徙隰川尉，秩满，迁建州松溪令，改宣州南陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159029_comment'></div>母丧去官，服除，授忻州秀容令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159029_comment'></div>州将转运使以治状闻，迁宁州军事判官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159029_comment'></div>历单州团练、均蕲防御、荆南节度、南京留守判官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159029_comment'></div>景祐二年七月辛卯，以疾终南京，享寿七十五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159029_comment'></div>公性淳气直，廉谨自守，所历十二官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159029_comment'></div>未尝一挂于法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159029_comment'></div>口不言人非，其有过者，款言谕之，人亦信伏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159029_comment'></div>常语子孙曰：「吾少孤无赀，徒力学，祈寸禄以养母。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159029_comment'></div>母终养矣，又得衣食尔子孙，吾自足矣，岂能以谄言谀色干权贵以求进乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159029_comment'></div>且贫无苞苴，耻学术数，何以取合于人？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159029_comment'></div>吾老于从事，不自愧也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159029_comment'></div>人虽不知，曾不一露锋颖，真吏隐君子哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159029_comment'></div>德之积而福不享于身者，将钟其后乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159029_comment'></div>夫人汝氏，封颍川县太君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159029_comment'></div>子二人：安世举进士，屯田员外郎、广西转运使；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159029_comment'></div>昌世太庙斋郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159029_comment'></div>女三人：长适黄州麻城尉费中黄，次适建州进士吴渊，次适合州进士袁务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159029_comment'></div>孙五人：台文举进士，永州推官；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1159029_comment'></div>详文太庙斋郎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1159029_comment'></div>懿文、炳文、彦文未仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1159029_comment'></div>公初自秀容令赴选，奏举引见，例进京秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1159029_comment'></div>一夕，子婿吴渊梦人呼公为判官，及见，果得宾幕，其从事六州皆为判官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1159029_comment'></div>公志本恬素，及事符梦寐，益加退让焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1159029_comment'></div>疾亟之际，自言吾梦于城北自择阴地，幽冥所安，无累后代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1159029_comment'></div>又言：「生平守官，未尝过误，惟邠州一狱有差，适梦之帝所，辨之得请矣，文字在吾怀中」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1159029_comment'></div>亲戚怪其谵言，就索文字，公曰：「七月十日来看」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1159029_comment'></div>至日果不禄焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1159029_comment'></div>及今卜葬之原果在城北。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1159029_comment'></div>以嘉祐二年十月庚午，与夫人汝氏合葬于扬州之江都县兴宁乡马坊里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1159029_comment'></div>屯田君以靖同年进士，又同官于洪、于桂，故托铭遗懿，以掩幽户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1159029_comment'></div>曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_39_1159029'>学行由己，穷通在命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1159029_comment'></div>人贪茍得，公惟守正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1159029_comment'></div>内修廉谨，外绝奔竞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1159029_comment'></div>识高位下，非德之病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1159029_comment'></div>嗣职炽昌，有家克盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1159029_comment'></div>九原可作，百代辉映。</div><div id='poem_sentence_44_1159029_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1057&endYear=1057')">1057年</a>　孙余舜臣贡举人。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1058&endYear=1058')">1058年</a>　孙余嗣襄出世。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1058&endYear=1058')">1058年10月17日</a>　改知青州，充东京东路安抚使。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='2fa18161ca6c436db9962a77ac5e079d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("2fa18161ca6c436db9962a77ac5e079d");'><span id='2fa18161ca6c436db9962a77ac5e079d_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年</a>，62岁</div><div id='2fa18161ca6c436db9962a77ac5e079d' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年</a>　至年初，北返，仁宗连派使臣拦余靖于湖湘境，诏以尚书左丞，依前守集贤学士知广州，充广南东路兵马钤辖经略安抚使，靖乞免，要求改差知潭州。作品：乞免转尚书左丞知广州状。<div id='poem_1158778' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158778' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158778?labeling=true' target='_blank'>免转尚书左丞知广州状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1061年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158778")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158778_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158778'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158778'>右，臣准阁门告报，蒙恩授臣尚书左丞，依前集贤院学士、知广州、充广南东路都钤辖、经略安抚使，替魏琰者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158778_comment'></div>伏念臣昨于庆历中，自知制诰分司南京，于韶州居住。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158778_comment'></div>是时蛮贼唐和走在岭表，已有臣僚言臣得罪，不合令居岭南，尚赖圣朝含容，免臣迁徙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158778_comment'></div>至皇祐中蛮贼侬智高俶扰二广，臣于父忧中，首被诏命，起知潭州，移知桂州，充广南西路经略安抚使，即与交趾公牒往来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158778_comment'></div>寻在狄青阵中战败蛮贼，收复邕州，俄又捉获侬智高母。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158778_comment'></div>累蒙圣恩迁官，屡曾陈乞依旧分司，不蒙俞允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158778_comment'></div>去岁甲峒作过，准中书劄子自青州召臣，差充广南西路体量安抚使，面奉圣旨，许令牒报交趾差官前来商量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158778_comment'></div>及至差费嘉祐等到钦州，犹差人前来体探是与不是臣亲身，仍言臣与先王有分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158778_comment'></div>今来差臣知广州，缘广州与交趾海道相通，切虑谈者易生构间，若言臣交通外夷，则于臣家族不便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158778_comment'></div>兼广州大市，居民元无城池围捍，近岁议者多欲修筑罗城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158778_comment'></div>若从群议，必须大兴力役，以民力凋弊之后，加臣才术短浅，当此重寄，必致旷败。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158778_comment'></div>臣今欲乞只守旧官，差知荆南潭州一次，庶免愆谤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158778_comment'></div>干冒冕旒，无任待罪惶恐之至，伏望圣慈特赐俞允<span class='inlineComment2'>（《武溪集》卷一五。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158778_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_1158778'>此状之后原附仁宗答诏，兹移入仁宗文。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1158778_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
桂林
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='fb7146b5e7a246e48883e2ca0aadeb66_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("fb7146b5e7a246e48883e2ca0aadeb66");'><span id='fb7146b5e7a246e48883e2ca0aadeb66_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1052&endYear=1052')">1052年</a>，53岁</div><div id='fb7146b5e7a246e48883e2ca0aadeb66' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1052&endYear=1052')">1052年7月16日</a>　到任，充广南西路兵马都钤辖，兼经略安抚使，知桂州。作品：桂州谢上表。<div id='poem_1158762' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158762' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158762?labeling=true' target='_blank'>桂州谢上表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1052年7月16日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158762")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158762_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158762'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158762'>臣某言：昨于六月二十日，准枢密院递到敕诰，蒙恩免持服，特授守秘书监，就差知潭州兼本路安抚使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158762_comment'></div>并准中书劄子，奉旨令臣次日起离，乘递马赴发本任，仍令韶州催促进发，不得收接辞免文状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158762_comment'></div>及在路，再奉敕改差知桂州，充广南西路都钤辖兼经略安抚使，准中书劄子三道，催促赴任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158762_comment'></div>臣寻于今月十六日到任上讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158762_comment'></div>事起金革，辞避无从，君父之恩，感深以泣<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158762_comment'></div>伏念臣生在遐徼，才识无取，自遭荼毒，未盈岁月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158762_comment'></div>近者侬蛮作梗，岭外骚然，悯彼远方，如在重病，思与诊疗，无有方术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158762_comment'></div>忽奉恩旨，令守长沙，非喜名爵之所加，自谓救兵之可出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158762_comment'></div>且古之列国，尚发恤邻之师；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158762_comment'></div>况今为王臣，岂有坐观之理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158762_comment'></div>由是遍檄境内，分起卒徒，本约一月之中，回至番禺城下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158762_comment'></div>朝命既改，人心不同，论议纷纭，师已减半。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158762_comment'></div>既违本志，进退不遑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158762_comment'></div>职多任重而可忧，就近辞远而非便，勉趋新任，自顾茫然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158762_comment'></div>官兵尽集于东南，狂寇岂忘于巢穴？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158762_comment'></div>当资锐旅，遏彼归途，而封疆阔远，守御虚寡，未知何计，可以逃责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158762_comment'></div>内惟愚暗，何堪差委？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158762_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下，敦二仪之仁，回万里之照，特怜孤露，误记寸长，擢自苫块之中，参于方面之寄，敢不捐躯竭虑，酬报皇恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158762_comment'></div>伏乞赫震天威，剪灭丑类，所以快四方之望，慑百蛮之心，臣之愿也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158762_comment'></div>候臣与杨畋处置广西边机了日，却乞缞麻私室，以终丧制。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1158762_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1052&endYear=1052')">1052年</a>　又令同提点广东刑狱李枢与陈曙讨智高，广东转运、钤辖司发兵援之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1052&endYear=1052')">1052年9月24日</a>　令余靖提举广南两路兵甲，经制贼盗事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1052&endYear=1052')">1052年</a>　冬，侬智高兵围广州，靖率两路兵马前往救援。侬智高攻广州五十六日不下，西折回邕州，沿途焚烧，片甲无存。靖领兵到广州城下。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='f8a415fd4f9e4ee39a8bf89c61d82917_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f8a415fd4f9e4ee39a8bf89c61d82917");'><span id='f8a415fd4f9e4ee39a8bf89c61d82917_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1054')">1053-1054年</a>，54-55岁</div><div id='f8a415fd4f9e4ee39a8bf89c61d82917' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1053')">1053年</a>　狄青率兵回朝，余靖迁给事中，留守桂州，有求免转及事中状，并建议朝廷大赦广南。作品：免转给事中。<div id='poem_1158765' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158765' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158765?labeling=true' target='_blank'>免转给事中状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1053年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158765")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158765_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158765'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158765'>右，臣今月二十日，进奏院递到敕诰各一道，授臣给事中者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158765_comment'></div>窃以赏为国典，必中事功，宠溢情涯，敢忘辞避。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158765_comment'></div>伏念臣揆材至薄，赋命多奇，幸偶休明，免居羁贱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158765_comment'></div>向以边臣失备，蛮寇内侵，越从缞绖之中，起亲金革之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158765_comment'></div>漫怀嫉恶，素匪知兵，所至面墙，几同学制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158765_comment'></div>贼锋尚锐，胜算无施，身负重而日增，民在溺而同窘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158765_comment'></div>果烦睿眷，特辍枢臣狄青以人杰之雄，总其师律；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158765_comment'></div>孙沔以国器之重，济以事机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158765_comment'></div>号令修明，士马奋励，故得凶丑败亡而绝迹，蒸黔苏复以息肩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158765_comment'></div>青所以定二广之阽危，沔所以正一方之经制，臣则幸于免戾，何止备员。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158765_comment'></div>今乃例被纶言，同增官秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158765_comment'></div>虽念劳劝善，国家宁厚于恩章；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158765_comment'></div>而揣分量能，私计实非于己力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158765_comment'></div>伏乞察臣诚请，追改命书，则朝廷无滥赏之讥，微臣免贪功之过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158765_comment'></div>干冒冕旒，臣无任待罪激切之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158765_comment'></div>所有降到敕诰，已送桂州军资库收管，听候朝廷指挥缴纳。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1158765_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1053')">1053年2月21日</a>　曲赦广南，靖呈状，请复终丧守制，不许。作品：乞解职行服状。<div id='poem_1158763' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158763' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158763?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞解职行服状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1053年2月21日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158763")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158763_comment'></div><div class='poemContent'
