id='poem_content_1158763'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158763'>右，臣去年六月二十日，枢密院递敕诰至韶州，蒙恩免持服，特授秘书监，就差知潭州兼本路安抚使；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158763_comment'></div>仍准中书劄子，奉圣旨限次日起发，不许辞免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158763_comment'></div>未到任间，再奉敕改差知桂州，充广南西路都钤辖兼经略安抚使，于七月十六日到任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158763_comment'></div>又准中书劄子，奉圣旨同杨畋等经制广南东西路盗贼事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158763_comment'></div>自授命已来，蒋偕等诸将败衄，臣亦累状，乞从追削归守丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158763_comment'></div>至今年正月十八日，宣徽使狄青部领三将兵甲，杀败蛮寇，收复邕州，贼首智高奔回巢穴，狄某、孙某、石某等各已发还京，臣今分屯兵马，即回本任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158763_comment'></div>伏念臣去岁授官，不敢辞免者，贼在方面，逼近乡里，欲因驱策，剪除凶丑，而绝无劳效，幸免追逐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158763_comment'></div>况今盗贼出境，贤俊满朝，何假墨缞以临民政？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158763_comment'></div>再念臣父存之日，尚容归侍，父没之后，不能终丧，乃是微臣事亲之不诚，朝廷置臣于有过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158763_comment'></div>臣若拂衣而先去，则似要君，抗章自陈，盖非虚饰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158763_comment'></div>伏乞朝廷悯臣持父之服有限，报国之日尚长，许臣解官归乡，终满丧制，则臣感天荷圣之诚，无有纪极。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1158763_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1053')">1053年2月21日</a>　又呈状，请復终丧守制，不许。作品：第二状。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1053')">1053年3月</a>　暮春，孙抗回京述职，靖为其诗集作序。作品：孙工部诗集序。<div id='poem_1158941' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158941' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158941?labeling=true' target='_blank'>孙工部诗集序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1053年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158941")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158941_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158941'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158941'>诗之源其远矣哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158941_comment'></div>唐、虞之际，君臣相得，明良赓载，书于帝典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158941_comment'></div>及周之兴也，姜嫄、后稷配天之基，公刘、亶父艰难之业，任、姒思齐之化，文、武太平之功，莫不发为声诗，荐于郊庙，被于弦歌，协于钟石者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158941_comment'></div>周、召没而王迹衰，幽、厉作而风雅变，然亦褒善刺过，与政相通，盖所以接神明，察风俗，道和畅、泄愤怒，不独讽咏而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158941_comment'></div>迨夫五言之兴，时更汉魏，而作者众矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158941_comment'></div>大抵哀乐之所感，情性之所发，虽丹素相攻，华实异好，其有乐高古，纵步骤，局声病，拘偶俪，为体不同，同归比兴，前哲论之详矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158941_comment'></div>某屏居岭服，北来交问殆绝，和叔继以三编见寄，自华原通守至庐陵典城七八年间，凡得千首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158941_comment'></div>观其励精篇翰，托情讽谕，目之所经，迹之所接，一事一物，亡虚闻览。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158941_comment'></div>其间藩辅大臣之美绩，道义良朋之荣问，泉石四时之嘉景，关河四方之行役，有美必宣，无愤不写。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158941_comment'></div>虽语存声律，而意深作用，固当远敌曹、刘，高揖颜、谢，兼沈、宋之新律，跨李、杜之老词，其他靡曼之作，不足方也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158941_comment'></div>且其取譬引类，发于胸臆，不从经史之所牵，不为文字之所局，如良工饬材，手习规矩，但见方圆成器，不睹斧斤之迹，于诗其深矣乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158941_comment'></div>世谓诗人必经穷愁，乃能抉造化之幽蕴，写悽辛之景象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158941_comment'></div>盖以其孤愤郁结，触怀成感，其言必精，于理必诣也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158941_comment'></div>和叔自关中用兵时，即佐华原，预闻边事，以材召入御史府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158941_comment'></div>属莫徭作梗于湖湘，奉诏安集，遇谗失职，守景陵，再谪倅汉阴，数年，徙沔上军壁，乃得剖符庐陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158941_comment'></div>其绵历周旋万里间，边风塞草，陇云江月，凄切羁孤，无不经涉，其为穷亦久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158941_comment'></div>今天子忧勤求治，四海无波，羌戎伏顺，祥应臻集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158941_comment'></div>既已修孝治、祀明堂矣，方将升中岱宗，告成天地，而寤寐英杰，讨论仪矩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158941_comment'></div>和叔当于此时扈从法驾，褒赞帝功，纪朱草、赤雁之瑞，赋《我将》、《时迈》之什，歌于圜坛，荐于太室，与吉甫清风之颂相照千古，乃诗之用也，岂独穷愁称工而已哉！</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1158941_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1053')">1053年</a>　夏，有诗酬唱黄都官。作品：酬黄都官舟次近坰见寄次韵。<div id='poem_99578' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99578' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99578?labeling=true' target='_blank'>酬黄都官舟次近坰见寄次韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1053年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99578")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_99578_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99578'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99578'>南州苦炎酷，薄宦淹翘隽。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99578'>怡然贤者心，五稔若一瞬。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99578'>归程江海遥，永日风波进。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99578'>屡经溪壑险，且乐帆樯顺。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_99578'>忽传邮驿音，雅什浑金振。<div id='poem_sentence_4_99578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_99578'>披襟许见过，握兰欣入觐。<div id='poem_sentence_5_99578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_99578'>衡门久索居，黄陂渴馀润。<div id='poem_sentence_6_99578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_99578'>觏止君子容，玉光窥千仞。<div id='poem_sentence_7_99578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_99578'>高谈尽今古，不独期廉蔺。<div id='poem_sentence_8_99578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_99578'>相逢勿惜醉，别去生蒙吝。<div id='poem_sentence_9_99578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_99578'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_99578_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1053')">1053年</a>　夏，作七律送友人。作品：送黄秘校南剑州司法。<div id='poem_99505' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99505' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99505?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送黄秘校南剑州司法</a><span class='authorDate'>（1053年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99505")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_99505_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99505'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99505'>早年援笔气飘飘，尚屈区区补郡寮。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99505_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99505'>苦<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作蒙）</span>掾去平三尺法，急贤期赴一封轺。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99505_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99505'>舟冲柳市吟春昼，帆卷江风宿暮潮。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99505_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99505'>及著莱衣过乡梓，循陔多羡撷兰苕。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99505_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_99505'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_99505_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1053')">1053年</a>　夏，作大宋平蛮碑，凿之郡壁。<div id='poem_1159016' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159016' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159016?labeling=true' target='_blank'>大宋平蛮碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（皇祐五年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1159016")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159016_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159016'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159016'>圣宋体天法道钦文聪武圣神孝德皇帝在宥之三十一年，天宇之内，海渚之外，毡裘卉服，罔不率俾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159016_comment'></div>粤五月，蛮贼侬智高寇邕州，陷其郛，贼虐衣冠，驱虏稚艾，遂沿郁江东下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159016_comment'></div>所过郡县，素无壁垒，倏然寇至，吏民弃走，因得焚荡剽钞，无所畏惮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159016_comment'></div>乃攻围广州五十馀日，不克，大掠其民而去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159016_comment'></div>然所存者官舍仓库而已，百年生聚，异域珍玩，扫地无遗矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159016_comment'></div>国家于岭南不宿重兵，故贼起三月而后师集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159016_comment'></div>蒋阶、张忠素号骁将，相继覆没，由是畏懦者望风溃走，贼锋益炽，逼连、贺，毁昭、宾，再穴于邕矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159016_comment'></div>驿骑继闻，上甚忧之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159016_comment'></div>枢密副使狄公青以为将帅之任，古难其才，若再命偏裨，事一不集，则二广之地，祸连而不解矣，亟自请行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159016_comment'></div>天子韪之，遂改宣徽南院使、荆湖南北路宣抚使、都大提举广南东西路经制盗贼事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159016_comment'></div>九月拜命，既授禁旅，仍启以旧镇骑兵、荆湖锐卒从行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159016_comment'></div>十二月，至桂林，督部伍，亲金鼓，然后兵知节制矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159016_comment'></div>明年正月甲辰，至宾州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159016_comment'></div>先是，钤辖陈曙领步兵八千溃于昆崙之关，公推其罪首，斩曙及佐吏已下三十一人，然后人知赏罚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159016_comment'></div>兵将股慄，咸思用命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159016_comment'></div>是月已来，引师至邕城一舍，贼悉其徒以逆战。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159016_comment'></div>公之行师，虽仓卒道途，皆有行列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159016_comment'></div>贼至，驻先锋以接之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159016_comment'></div>公凭高望，撝骑兵以翼焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159016_comment'></div>贼徒大败，追奔十五里，斩首二千二百馀级，生擒五百人，尸甲如山，积于道路，伪署将相死者五十七人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159016_comment'></div>是夕，智高焚营自遁，复入于蛮中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159016_comment'></div>先是，命湖南江西路安抚使、枢密直学士孙沔、入内押班石全彬过岭，与广西经略使余靖，同其经制东西路贼盗，故命公督大提举，然孙、石赞谋，而军中悉禀公之节制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159016_comment'></div>贼之再据邕也，农者辍耕，商者辍行，远迩惶惶，不聊其生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159016_comment'></div>及公之拜命也，朝野之论，中外欢然，以方、召之才，兼机轴之重，出剪狂蛮，无噍类矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159016_comment'></div>贼之巢穴曰广源州，交趾之附庸也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159016_comment'></div>父为交趾所戮，遂弃其州，奔南蛮界中渊薮，悖慠以僭称号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159016_comment'></div>自名其居曰云南道，又曰南天国，再名其年曰景瑞、曰启历，杂名其左右之人，自侍中、开府已下署之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1159016_comment'></div>其主谋者，黄师宓、侬廷侯、侬志忠等，战没于阵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1159016_comment'></div>未有剪其羽翼而能飞，刳其腹心而能全者也，故宵逍矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1159016_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1159016_comment'></div>智高之谋，十馀年间，招纳亡叛，共图举事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1159016_comment'></div>十馀月间，连破十二郡，所向无前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1159016_comment'></div>夫岂自知破碎奔走，在于顷刻之间？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1159016_comment'></div>乃知名将攻取，真自有体哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1159016_comment'></div>二月甲戌，改乘辕，其月丁亥，至桂州，诏徙护国军节度，复以枢密副使召。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1159016_comment'></div>仍曲赦岭南，民得休息矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1159016_comment'></div>遂磨桂林之崖石，以书其勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1159016_comment'></div>其词曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_37_1159016'>有宋之大，天覆地载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1159016_comment'></div>四海正朔，百蛮冠带。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1159016_comment'></div>蠢兹狂寇，起乎徼外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1159016_comment'></div>父戮于交，逃死獠界。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1159016_comment'></div>招纳亡命，浸淫边害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1159016_comment'></div>边臣罔上，习尚以懈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1159016_comment'></div>卒陷邕郛，乘流东迈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1159016_comment'></div>志图全越，肆其蜂虿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1159016_comment'></div>广城言言，梯冲附焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1159016_comment'></div>攻之五旬，掠民而旋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1159016_comment'></div>贼锋一至，千里无烟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1159016_comment'></div>还据于邕，五岭骚然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1159016_comment'></div>天生狄公，辅圣推忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1159016_comment'></div>情存义烈，志嫉顽凶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1159016_comment'></div>请缨即路，伏节临戎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1159016_comment'></div>英材遴集，猛将风从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1159016_comment'></div>贼之敢斗，实惟天诱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1159016_comment'></div>来迓于郊，奄丧群丑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1159016_comment'></div>当我摧锋，易如拉朽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1159016_comment'></div>僭补伪署，丛然授首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1159016_comment'></div>羽翼既剪，心腹既刳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1159016_comment'></div>虽欲自举，人谁与图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1159016_comment'></div>焚庐而去，回巢以逋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1159016_comment'></div>六亲不保，曰献其俘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1159016_comment'></div>厥惟邕边，南国之纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1159016_comment'></div>九洞襟带，列城唇齿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1159016_comment'></div>险固一失，兵粮无峙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1159016_comment'></div>庶民蚩蚩，鸟惊兽跂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1159016_comment'></div>我公之来，电扫云开。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1159016_comment'></div>叛涣斗破，纲领重恢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1159016_comment'></div>师成庙算，民得春台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1159016_comment'></div>天声远振，繄公之材。</div><div id='poem_sentence_68_1159016_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1053')">1053年</a>　夏，作大宋平蛮京观志并序，凿之郡壁。<div id='poem_1159017' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159017' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159017?labeling=true' target='_blank'>大宋平蛮京观志<span class='inlineComment2'>（并序　皇祐五年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1053年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1159017")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159017_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159017'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159017'>大宋皇祐四年夏五月，广源州蛮犯邕、管，陷之，乘江流暴涨，东陷九城，遂至广州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159017_comment'></div>广人怯战，登陴自固，贼得驻兵傅城，攻之五旬，云梯土山，极肆其巧，城坚不能下，乃还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159017_comment'></div>经途复残二郡，覆四将，再入于邕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159017_comment'></div>凡害将佐三十馀员，虏生口万计，牛畜资宝无算。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159017_comment'></div>所过焚荡无馀，楚越萧然矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159017_comment'></div>朝廷忧之，君臣为之旰食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159017_comment'></div>枢密副使狄公青抗章请行，愿授成算，上重其诚，从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159017_comment'></div>先是，命枢密直学士孙沔、入内押班石全彬同本路经略使余靖经制贼盗，命青以宣徽使、都大提举总其节制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159017_comment'></div>明年正月己未，青帅三将兵至邕州归仁铺，贼举众出城拒战，大败之，骑兵追奔十五里，所杀蛮众二千二百馀人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159017_comment'></div>伪署侍郎黄师宓等腹心将领五十七人死于阵，贼首侬智高其夜焚城自遁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159017_comment'></div>诘朝，引兵入城，俾供奉官贾荣就战场歛贼尸而殣之，为冢于归仁之南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159017_comment'></div>又遣郴县尉区有邻聚重伤还城而死、并活擒而戮，及奔而蹂践燔灼者，复三千二百二十八人，为一冢，瘗之于城之北。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159017_comment'></div>二月，有诏即其地筑为京观，乃命立石以志其伐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159017_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_1159017'>庸臣司边，率职不虔，盗起其间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159017_comment'></div>蠢尔异类，藏亡纳叛，以辅狡烦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159017_comment'></div>窥兹无备，乘虚袭怠，遂肆凶奸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159017_comment'></div>顺流而东，列城皆空，岭表骚然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159017_comment'></div>师徒桓桓，矢劲摧完，天下恻焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159017_comment'></div>帝命枢臣，握节属鞬，拯坠绥残。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159017_comment'></div>师行之律，赏罚贵必，其谋乃专。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159017_comment'></div>兵家之势，动静有制，所击无坚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159017_comment'></div>吁嗟群丑，狃于常胜，敢当其前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159017_comment'></div>驱彼犬羊，敌此熊罴，血膏于原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159017_comment'></div>弃甲如山，遗骸亘野，百里腥膻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159017_comment'></div>武功外扬，仁心内悯，念及幽泉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159017_comment'></div>肩䯗之葬，京观之封，铜柱齐年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159017_comment'></div>天声远振，皇泽重宣，永镇群蛮。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1159017_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1053')">1053年</a>　向朝呈进平蛮记表。<div id='poem_1158791' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158791' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158791?labeling=true' target='_blank'>进平蛮记表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1053年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158791")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158791_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158791'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158791'>臣某言：古者兴师命将，征讨四方，必有开府之宾，参闻策略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158791_comment'></div>所以庙堂成算，帷幄密谋，擒纵之奇，俘馘之实，以撰述备史氏之采摭焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158791_comment'></div>故窦宪燕然之勋，陈汤郅支之捷，震叠天声，与大汉传于无穷者，用此术也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158791_comment'></div>伏惟皇帝陛下龙德天飞，三十馀载，塞外无未羁之虏，域中无不顺之臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158791_comment'></div>以北胡之彊盛，而缔于欢盟；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158791_comment'></div>以西夏之陆梁，而终于屈伏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158791_comment'></div>夫何小丑，敢干天诛！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158791_comment'></div>彼侬智高者，蠢尔溪蛮，生自凶族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158791_comment'></div>稔知边鄙之无备，广招亡叛以协谋，直趋番禺，图据邕管。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158791_comment'></div>燔毁者十二郡，杀掠者数万人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158791_comment'></div>南方绎骚，殆且半岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158791_comment'></div>陛下出于睿算，特命枢臣，董统虎貔，奉辞讨逆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158791_comment'></div>金鼓一震，群凶席卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158791_comment'></div>此盖皇威奋扬，军政整肃，人思用命，使之然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158791_comment'></div>殿中丞冯炳奉诏掌管机宜，备见师行始末，自智高举事以致败亡，凡朝廷处置军前号令及贼之胜负，一能编之，词无虚美，事皆实录。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158791_comment'></div>以臣共在行阵，遂抄副本见寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158791_comment'></div>臣尝忝史官，见今之撰日历者，常执简于数年之后，至乃搜寻检访，罕能完备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158791_comment'></div>今冯炳于已事之际，编缉事实，一无遗坠，窃以方叔南征，列在《诗·雅》；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158791_comment'></div>充国西伐，叙于史赞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158791_comment'></div>非独显勋臣之绩用，于以播国家之休烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1158791_comment'></div>其冯炳撰《平蛮记》二卷，已依本缮写。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1158791_comment'></div>并臣去年准宣抚使劄子、准枢密院劄子，奉圣旨「杀到蛮贼尸首，筑为京观，仍立石其上，镌记年月及杀获人数」，臣寻撰成《京观记》，刻石立于邕州归仁铺蛮冢之侧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1158791_comment'></div>又于桂州北门之外，就崖石磨刻出师平贼、受算凯旋年月，以宣示皇朝威令，用肃远方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1158791_comment'></div>今并此碑文，别为一卷，同冯炳所撰《记》共成三卷，谨随表进呈，伏乞宣付史馆。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1158791_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1053')">1053年</a>　侬智高在特磨道筑宫室，由其母、弟智光、子继宗、继封居之，自将兵五百及六妻六子出奔大理国。靖张榜募能献策获侬智高者，得元卿招抚诸蛮六十族酋之计最善，靖尽皆准之，付诸实施。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1053')">1053年5月</a>　以狄青为枢密使、孙沔为枢密副使，命广西都监萧注等加紧搜捕侬智高。御使梁蒨、狄青、孙沔等言靖功多而赏薄。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1053')">1053年6月</a>　朝廷差韩殿侍特送敕诰，赐银二百两，迁工部侍郎，仍知桂州，靖有辞免状，赐银缴纳桂州军资库。作品：免转工部侍郎状。<div id='poem_1158766' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158766' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158766?labeling=true' target='_blank'>免转工部侍郎状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1053年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158766")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158766_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158766'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158766'>右，臣今月十三日，三班差使、殿侍韩某乘递马赍送到中书劄子并敕诰各一道，蒙恩授臣尚书工部侍郎，仍就赐银二百两者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158766_comment'></div>前恩未谢，后宠复加，内揆空疏，第深<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1158766", 1158766, "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>腼愧</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158766_comment'></div>伏念臣出于寒族，起自诸生，素乏轶群之材，久罹负俗之谤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158766_comment'></div>昨以蛮酋叛涣，岭服震惊，虽分守土之权，莫展擒凶之策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158766_comment'></div>属元戎之善胜，加迩臣之协谟，因此安边，幸于免戾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158766_comment'></div>岂谓皇明远照，宠数荐临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158766_comment'></div>且方上让章，盖惭非据，而未承报旨，更冒今荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158766_comment'></div>揣己力而实微，干物议而为甚，用倾愚恳，上渎天聪，愿回过恩，庶全薄祜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158766_comment'></div>俾雷雨之泽，无至妄施；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158766_comment'></div>则草茅之姿，免于深谴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158766_comment'></div>除就赐银已受领外，所有赍送到敕诰，不敢祗受，乞行回纳，已牒桂州军资库收管，听候朝廷指挥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158766_comment'></div>伏望圣慈，特赐俞允，但臣无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1158766_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1053')">1053年</a>　申朝廷乞补广南西路转运使空缺，仁宗亲择苏梦得从陇西以田曹副郎出充转运使。陇西及京师官员赠诗送行。苏到桂州，将赠诗汇编成集，靖为撰序。作品：诸公送苏屯田诗序。<div id='poem_1158943' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158943' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158943?labeling=true' target='_blank'>诸公送苏屯田诗序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1053年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158943")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158943_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158943'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158943'>今天子皇祐纪元之四年，广源州蛮入寇岭南，燔毁一十二郡，杀三郡守，驱掠吏民，还据邕州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158943_comment'></div>王师数万讨之，明年，大败蛮众，留屯万人于边，凡民之供役，运粮饷，完城垒，未得休息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158943_comment'></div>又明年，改元至和，诏以田曹副郎苏君梦得充广南西路转运使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158943_comment'></div>转运职，缓于期会，则军用或窘；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158943_comment'></div>急于聚歛，则民力益困。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158943_comment'></div>必须周才通人，乃称其任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158943_comment'></div>初，政府以资叙进拟数人，上惩其苛细，并却之，及见梦得姓名，遽可其奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158943_comment'></div>梦得正直自守，上知其名，故自陕右越录见徙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158943_comment'></div>乃知吾君之爱抚远民，不独专于利权也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158943_comment'></div>前相国太师杜公，弼谐元老，叙朝廷任贤恤远之意，著于篇咏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158943_comment'></div>宾客王公，当世宿儒，龙图包公，在朝清德；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158943_comment'></div>殿丞王君，后来文杰，并辔其作，以宠斯行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158943_comment'></div>其年十二月，君下车，出诸公新什为示，故直叙所闻，以刊于石。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1158943_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1053')">1053年</a>　用杨元卿、石鉴计，发诸峒兵勇袭特磨洞，萧注发官军殿后声援，以侬夏诚、黄守陵作内应，捕侬母侬阿侬及智高弟、子四人，侬夏卿逃脱，不知去向。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1053')">1053年10月24日</a>　收复特磨道。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年1月</a>　张贵妃薨，追册为皇妃，谥温成。下旬，有文。作品：慰温成皇后张氏薨表。<div id='poem_1158802' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158802' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158802?labeling=true' target='_blank'>慰温成皇后张氏薨表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1054年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158802")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158802_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158802'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158802'>臣某言：进奏院正月八日追册温成皇后张氏薨谢者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158802_comment'></div>函夏之广，闻问咸惊<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158802_comment'></div>伏以温成皇后德禀儒门，化恢嫔则，动守珩璜之节，退思图史之规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158802_comment'></div>《樛木》称贤，协隆阴教，藏舟茹叹，遽掩春华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158802_comment'></div>恭惟皇帝陛下特轸宸慈，俯追遗懿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158802_comment'></div>礼崇三翟，增象服以伸怀；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158802_comment'></div>惨动六宫，引鸾辂而加怆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158802_comment'></div>臣无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1158802_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年2月7日</a>　朝廷派内侍殿头张昭寿到昭州傅宣抚问，赐银二百两，绢二百匹、特赐翠毛细锦旋襕等冬服等，有谢表。作品：谢傅宣抚问表。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年2月</a>　有文乞请不赐冬服。作品：乞不请中冬翠锦衣袄状。<div id='poem_1158785' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158785' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158785?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞不请中冬翠锦衣袄状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1054年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158785")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158785_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158785'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158785'>右，臣准桂州牒，差人送到敕书一道，蒙恩赐臣翠毛细锦旋襕一领者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158785_comment'></div>伏念臣自遭荼蓼，甫及期祥，属蛮獠之猖狂，废几筵之号慕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158785_comment'></div>未成军伐，屡照天慈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158785_comment'></div>且枕块寝苫，礼虽可夺；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158785_comment'></div>而食稻衣锦，心所难安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158785_comment'></div>况栾棘之在容，顾曳裾而非称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158785_comment'></div>愿收涣汗，以遂素心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158785_comment'></div>已牒桂州，更不差人赴京请领。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158785_comment'></div>所有赐到敕书一道，谨具状封纳。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1158785_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年2月</a>　有状谢赐冬服。作品：回纳诏赐冬服状。<div id='poem_1158786' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158786' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158786?labeling=true' target='_blank'>回纳诏赐冬服状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1054年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158786")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158786_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158786'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158786'>臣今月十四日，进奏院递到敕书一道，蒙恩赐臣簇四雕儿细锦旋襕等冬服者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158786_comment'></div>祗荷宠光，不任感惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158786_comment'></div>伏念臣向遭荼毒，归守丘樊，遽属军兴，遂离丧次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158786_comment'></div>光阴过隙，祥禫未周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158786_comment'></div>墨缞绖以临戎，盖先国事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158786_comment'></div>褧衣裳而画饰，难处人情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158786_comment'></div>愿回渥恩，庶全素志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158786_comment'></div>所有前件细锦冬服，乞不请领。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1158786_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年2月</a>　有状谢赐绢。作品：谢赐绢状。<div id='poem_1158787' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158787' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158787?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢赐绢状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1054年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158787")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158787_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158787'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158787'>右，臣今月六日，伏蒙圣恩，差御药梁惟一赐臣绢二百匹，令臣迎亲归京者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158787_comment'></div>伏念臣本远人，素无通识，误膺擢用，莫补休明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158787_comment'></div>昨求外官，盖欲便于温凊，过蒙圣造，不令远去阙庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158787_comment'></div>未知所报之恩，更承非望之赐，上荷云天之施，下为乡里之光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158787_comment'></div>誓捐微躯，以答洪覆。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1158787_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年2月</a>　有状谢赐银。作品：谢赐银状。<div id='poem_1158788' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158788' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158788?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢赐银状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1054年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158788")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158788_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158788'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158788'>右，臣今月十三日，三班差使、殿侍韩喜乘递马赍送到中书劄子并敕诰各一道，蒙恩授臣尚书工部侍郎，仍就赐银二百两者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158788_comment'></div>伏缘杀荡蛮寇，收复邕州，并是宣抚使狄青专总节制，及孙沔、石全彬等经画。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158788_comment'></div>臣虽同在阵中，功非己出，并蒙恩宠，实不遑安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158788_comment'></div>除就赐银二百两，已受领外，所有赍送到敕诰，不敢祗受，乞行回纳，已牒送桂州军资库收管，听候朝廷指挥，及具状附递闻奏去讫。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1158788_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年2月</a>　所有赐物、赐银再次交桂州军资库返纳。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年</a>　陈执中为相，命靖改知潭州，靖禀奏，言边陲要事繁杂，乞留任桂州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年</a>　时田况为枢密副使，将此事直禀皇上，谓靖虽任满，而桂州事关重大，朝廷颁送赦书，赦免从叛兵民，靖呈表。作品：贺曲赦表。<div id='poem_1158794' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158794' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158794?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺曲赦表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1054年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158794")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158794_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158794'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158794'>臣某言：今月初一日，马递赦书一道至安抚司，以杀获蛮寇、收复邕州，曲赦广南东西路者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158794_comment'></div>登时同官吏集众宣示，军民依例施行讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158794_comment'></div>狂蛮窃发，递骚岭海之邦；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158794_comment'></div>庶汇重苏，远沾雷雨之泽<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158794_comment'></div>伏以国家接千岁之统，拥百神之休，一六合而同风，重九译而脩贽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158794_comment'></div>蠢然獠族，素附交城，父为戮而不悛，母同恶而增酷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158794_comment'></div>广招亡叛，庸济狡凶，窥边隙以渐深，极兵锋而为暴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158794_comment'></div>远趋南海，戈鋋肆掠于越郊；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158794_comment'></div>还据两江，文檄遍邀于黄洞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158794_comment'></div>妄祈枝附，潜觊土疆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158794_comment'></div>□王怒以遣师，辍枢臣而总律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158794_comment'></div>顾兹乌合，未测天亡，初居井以自深，俄当辙而来拒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158794_comment'></div>犬羊虽众，聿成膏斧之诛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158794_comment'></div>羽翼先摧，遂起焚巢之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158794_comment'></div>既已驱除丑类，恢斥边关，捷布继闻，德音遽霈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158794_comment'></div>念深黎庶，罹此悯凶，特推恢大之恩，仍协发生之候。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158794_comment'></div>此盖皇帝陛下，乾刚下济，天惠周施，泽兼被于存亡，民用忘于疲瘵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158794_comment'></div>拯其焚溺，匝南夏而永康；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158794_comment'></div>育以慈和，与万方而同泰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158794_comment'></div>臣无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1158794_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年</a>　又上贺表。作品：贺德音表。<div id='poem_1158795' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158795' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158795?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺德音表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1054年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158795")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158795_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158795'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158795'>臣某言：准尚书刑部牒，准皇祐六年三月十七日德音，改皇祐六年为至和元年，应四京及诸道州府军监县等，见禁罪人，限德音到日，死罪降从流，流罪已下并放。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158795_comment'></div>当时集军州官吏军民宣示施行讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158795_comment'></div>先天布令，以召四时之和；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158795_comment'></div>罪己兴言，特引万方之过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158795_comment'></div>邦刑是恤，圣德惟新<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158795_comment'></div>窃以日月之行，罔违常数；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158795_comment'></div>天人之应，必感至诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158795_comment'></div>永言合朔之期，或偶二交之次，遂成亏薄，著验经缠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158795_comment'></div>禜社责阴，春秋之故事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158795_comment'></div>避寝修政，帝王之旧规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158795_comment'></div>恭惟皇帝陛下道迪大中，志深寅畏，因三辰之示变，诏六职以修方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158795_comment'></div>特推汪濊之恩，躬行消复之要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158795_comment'></div>涣纪元之大号，期敷祐于群生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158795_comment'></div>更也之明，兆民共仰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158795_comment'></div>霈然之泽，函夏同欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158795_comment'></div>臣伏限守职边郡，不获抃蹈阙庭，臣无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1158795_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年4月</a>　改天章阁待制刘元瑜知潭州，余靖留桂州处理善后事宜。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年</a>　余靖往各地巡察，对曾从侬智高而后归附朝廷的黄守陵等三十六峒酋长，皆补团练副使官职，对已疏远智高的六十族酋长皆厚赐之。对清廉官吏给予勉励陞职，对旱情较重的地区，则发动士民引山溪灌田。<br /></div><div class='label1' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年8月</a>　建桂州新城。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='a8996cf452ef41049ec2f5bd7d360e7b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a8996cf452ef41049ec2f5bd7d360e7b");'><span id='a8996cf452ef41049ec2f5bd7d360e7b_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1056')">1054-1056年</a>，55-57岁</div><div id='a8996cf452ef41049ec2f5bd7d360e7b' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年</a>　余靖大力落实朝廷曲赦令，对兵毁严重地区减免赋税，组织府城铁作坊制作农具，复耕荒田，民心始定。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年</a>　春，遣返广南东路留剿兵马。赵节推率韶州兵甲回，靖作诗。作品：送曲江知县赵节推。<div id='poem_99563' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99563' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99563?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送曲江知县赵节推</a><span class='authorDate'>（1055年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99563")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_99563_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99563'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99563'>命将久征蛮，骚然数载间<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：郴韶共屯兵夫七千馀人。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99563_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99563'>一言巢穴破，千里鼓旗闲。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99563_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99563'>刀盾无私蓄，耕桑有复还<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99563_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99563'>居民此休息，遗惠重丘山。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99563_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_99563'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_99563_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_99563'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_2_99563_0'>⑴ 自注：徭人兵器尽输官库，避寇之民并即归业。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_99563_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年3月</a>　暮春，知杭州孙沔致函余靖，有文。作品：回贺孙学士启。<div id='poem_1158932' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158932' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158932?labeling=true' target='_blank'>回贺孙学士启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1055年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158932")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158932_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158932'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158932'>伏蒙尊慈，以荣升清贯，时惠华笺，欢慰之馀，但增祗悚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158932_comment'></div>窃以昔汉武用兵四夷，朝野多事，而严助、朱买臣之徒，以文学侍左右，内与大臣辨论得失，外使四方专达词令，然未有职事之称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158932_comment'></div>唐初开秦府以揽英杰，储将相之器，诚上选也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158932_comment'></div>今历兹显秩，实为殊荣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1158932_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年</a>　据苏安世《屯田手记》，是年三月初一日，幕僚属官欲为靖祝寿，为靖所止。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年</a>　靖通报越南李氏朝庭，侬智高已理授首，叛乱已平。李朝圣宗德政因侬智高本交阯所属，未能约束而致兵变，向宋请罪，靖予以安抚。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年</a>　知邕州陶弼于州城望仙坡建三公亭，纪念平定叛乱有功的狄青、孙沔、余靖三人。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年6月12日</a>　侬智高亲属四人在京伏诛，靖呈表。作品：贺诛侬智高母表。<div id='poem_1158793' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158793' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158793?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺诛侬智高母表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1055年6月12日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158793")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158793_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158793'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158793'>臣某言：据本州进奏官申，蛮贼侬智高等，大理国已斩除讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158793_comment'></div>奉圣旨，阿侬腰斩，侬智光、侬继宗、继封各处斩讫者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158793_comment'></div>卉服之蛮，敢干国纪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158793_comment'></div>藁街之戮，用正天诛<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158793_comment'></div>伏以国家道贯百王，德涵万县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158793_comment'></div>东渐西被，邈踰尧禹之封；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158793_comment'></div>北洽南翔，迥溢汉唐之域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158793_comment'></div>蠢兹凶族，素隶侯藩，尝窃地以逃来，因拒关而弗纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158793_comment'></div>而乃赘居边境，盗弄兵锋，驱掠吏民，燔劫郡县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158793_comment'></div>久安之俗，闻寇则惊，守长弃城而悉奔，士卒投戈而自溃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158793_comment'></div>乘此绎骚之势，肆行僭拟之名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158793_comment'></div>母号感星，年称启历，揉践者十二郡，屠害者数万人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158793_comment'></div>还据金汤，图为窟宅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158793_comment'></div>繇是睿谋独断，枢辅专征，庙堂之算有成，步骑之师齐进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158793_comment'></div>爪牙虽众，当一战以皆摧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158793_comment'></div>巢穴既倾，弃六亲而莫保。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158793_comment'></div>寓所生于假父之国，投孤族于远夷之君，过为巧诈之词，自作偷生之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158793_comment'></div>殊不知天下共恶，神理弗容，蛮貊虽遥，恩信可结。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158793_comment'></div>元凶支党，先从原野之诛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158793_comment'></div>顽媪孽童，卒伏市朝之法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1158793_comment'></div>国章明备，式昭雷电之威；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1158793_comment'></div>天网恢疏，难漏鲸鲵之戮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1158793_comment'></div>四方共快，万口同词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1158793_comment'></div>臣伏恨远守郡条，不获蹈舞阙庭，臣无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1158793_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年6月21日</a>　使者至桂州宣敕，依前守工部侍郎、充集贤殿学士，知桂州，赐银绢物不许上纳。靖呈表赐物仍缴纳于军资库。作品：免充集贤殿学士表。<div id='poem_1158770' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158770' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158770?labeling=true' target='_blank'>免充集贤学士表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1055年6月21日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158770")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158770_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158770'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158770'>臣某言：今月二十一日，进奏院递到诰敕各一道，蒙恩授臣依前守尚书工部侍郎，充集贤院学士，依旧知桂州；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158770_comment'></div>并准枢密劄子，中书、枢密院同奉圣旨，令臣分析儿孙或近亲骨肉一名闻奏者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158770_comment'></div>松楸之恋，诚本告归；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158770_comment'></div>雨露之恩，事出非望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158770_comment'></div>抚躬怀惕，闻命若惊<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158770_comment'></div>伏念臣素乏艺文，固无材武，幸逢圣旦，早列仕途。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158770_comment'></div>间者起自废居，奄遭荼苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158770_comment'></div>丧期未艾，蛮事遽兴，首预诏除，敢忘宣力？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158770_comment'></div>赖元戎之制胜，致阖境以再安，臣以非材，例增优秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158770_comment'></div>亦尝乞收印绶，还袭缞麻，狡寇尚存，私诚莫遂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158770_comment'></div>近以远擒贼媪，稍息边虞，愿返乡闾，修营垄墓，而遽蒙恩旨，加赐职名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158770_comment'></div>未伸上冢之诚，已掇要君之过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158770_comment'></div>再念臣前岁与起居舍人杨畋、阁门副使曹修同时受命，经制贼盗，畋等各怀忠荩，并练权谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158770_comment'></div>当单车制御之初，值剧贼猖狂之际，虽英、韶处置，偶失事机，而连、贺保全，皆由指授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158770_comment'></div>今畋等旧官未复，而臣屡承宠命，揆兹进退之理，弥深兢愧之怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158770_comment'></div>乞回过恩，庶伸微志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158770_comment'></div>臣今乞将所授集贤院学士及儿孙恩泽，并各回纳，只乞特与杨畋、曹修牵复旧官，所贵上有念劳之恩，臣无过分之责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158770_comment'></div>其有递到敕诰，已牒送桂州军资库收管，听候朝旨缴纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158770_comment'></div>伏乞圣慈，特赐俞允<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158770_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_1158770'>上冢：程刻本作「系首」。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1158770_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1158770'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_18_1158770_0'>⑴ 《武溪集》卷一五。又见《粤西文载》卷四。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1158770_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年6月21日</a>　有启谢再任桂州。作品：谢再任桂州启。<div id='poem_1158924' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158924' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158924?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢再任桂州启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1055年6月21日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158924")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158924_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158924'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158924'>伏奉恩命，特授尚书户部侍郎，依前充集贤院学士、知桂州，候今任成资日，仍令再任；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158924_comment'></div>并准枢密院劄子，奉圣旨，依前降指挥，不许辞让者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158924_comment'></div>伏念某本无远识，早玷通班，向缘蛮事之兴，遽委州麾之重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158924_comment'></div>墨缞从政，徒废居丧之仪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158924_comment'></div>尺籍理兵，素乏临戎之变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158924_comment'></div>赖睿谋之远照，命元帅以专征。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158924_comment'></div>一战成功，已滥分于赏典；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158924_comment'></div>三年奉计，当例被于更书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158924_comment'></div>忽捧诏音，就宣恩旨，以谓狂蛮干纪，既伏于逋诛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158924_comment'></div>服岭颁条，宜谙于故俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158924_comment'></div>俾留州任，庶晓物情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158924_comment'></div>再念某顷被中伤，尝居冗散，颇得田园之乐，靡思轩冕之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158924_comment'></div>当警急之期，闻命敢忘于濡足；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158924_comment'></div>及敉宁之际，私心诚愿于退身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158924_comment'></div>再露封章，上干旒扆，未从报罢，仍俾拜嘉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158924_comment'></div>此盖伏遇昭文相公道广包荒，诚深诱善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158924_comment'></div>洪钧造物，靡私动植之恩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158924_comment'></div>寒谷回春，曲借发生之气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158924_comment'></div>致兹樗散，荐被龙光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158924_comment'></div>谨当详练武经，励精政体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1158924_comment'></div>边亭警备，冀销桴鼓之音；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1158924_comment'></div>条教布宣，庶协蒲芦之化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1158924_comment'></div>上答乾坤之造，次酬陶铸之私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1158924_comment'></div>过此以还，罔知所措。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1158924_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年6月</a>　应衡山景德寺住持之请，撰文。作品：南岳云峰山景德寺记。<div id='poem_1158991' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158991' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158991?labeling=true' target='_blank'>南岳云峰山景德寺记</a><span class='authorDate'>（至和二年六月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158991")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158991_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158991'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158991'>云峰者，南岳五峰之一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158991_comment'></div>昔大禹登祭此山，得金简玉字治水之要，故有禹之行宫，科斗古碑，时有见者，遂名其溪曰禹溪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158991_comment'></div>梁天监二年，即其行宫创寺，仍锡近田以资僧食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158991_comment'></div>以岩栖谷隐之士，世所以推而重之者，谓其轻去轩冕，疏外声利，以全其高者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158991_comment'></div>矧以释氏之谛，离蕴去著，出生死海，以全其性，岂独脱嚣埃、易去就而已哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158991_comment'></div>自梁已降，代有奇人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158991_comment'></div>简文帝大宝中有法政禅师，身长八尺，布衣一食，独宿树下，虎兕围绕，每一入定，辄经累月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158991_comment'></div>忽一日，风雷震树，见神人具衣冠，端笏而前曰：「此宜立坛度人」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158991_comment'></div>师诺之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158991_comment'></div>遂奏置甘露戒坛，度僧五万，基址存焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158991_comment'></div>陈有高僧惠勇，修心于此六十馀年，群虎旦夕侍卫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158991_comment'></div>隋有高僧善伏，习禅智三昧，通宿命，亦能入定，一月乃起，常念幽途多苦饥渴，乃咒食冥饲焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158991_comment'></div>太宗朝有高僧义本，博通经律，子史百家，无不览者，内外学徒，顺风庭谒，至则开纳，深得人望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158991_comment'></div>无疾坐亡，葬于南岭，有双鹤悲鸣，绕塔三年而去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158991_comment'></div>至广顺中，寺主僧启仁，被诉陷法，籍没庄土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158991_comment'></div>皇朝建隆元年，楚文昭王马氏请而复之，尔后甲乙承袭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158991_comment'></div>殆景德中，改为禅刹，命僧智吉演法领众，其事上白，遂以年名赐今额焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158991_comment'></div>自智吉之后曰希顺、智宣、怀荀，三世相承矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158991_comment'></div>庆历末，佥议请今长老纯正绍隆法席。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158991_comment'></div>正师，成都人，俗姓李，天圣中遍参知识，深达心要，荐居岳麓之法润，宁乡之善果，及今居云峰，凡三迁法筵，皆当世名公，今相国刘公、资政孙公、致仕贰卿刘公而下十馀公署疏而请之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1158991_comment'></div>所至缁徒云集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1158991_comment'></div>且夫无生之说，用达于根本；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1158991_comment'></div>有为之果，盖勖于精进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1158991_comment'></div>故悲智异途，而同归济度；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1158991_comment'></div>福慧殊报，而俱出薰修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1158991_comment'></div>所以学心之徒闻言而得要，慕教之士睹相而生恭，随其机缘，示以开入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1158991_comment'></div>繇是提唱之馀，极力营葺，塔庙之制，华梵相参。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1158991_comment'></div>扶土而为像，度材而构厦，壹用常均，不侈不陋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1158991_comment'></div>七年中，为屋三百馀间，至于县廨庄舍，又五十馀间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1158991_comment'></div>皆率减岁储，不外干于檀施，此又人之难能也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1158991_comment'></div>以孙公与某尝同南征之役，又都官黄君禀岳之秀，而联郡之务，故致书求记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1158991_comment'></div>因不克让，而记其世次云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1158991_comment'></div>至和二年六月日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1158991_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年6月</a>　桂州新城建成。群牧判官王安石为作《余公桂州新城记》，年度刻于壁。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年</a>　是年大旱，靖视察旱伤州县，体恤吏治民情。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年</a>　到桂西，有诗。作品：留题龙潭。<div id='poem_99571' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99571' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99571?labeling=true' target='_blank'>游山五题<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其五 </span>留题龙潭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1055年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99571")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_99571_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99571'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99571'>峭岭盘远郊，幽泉生石罅。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99571_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99571'>沮洳成深潭，神龙隐其下。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99571_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99571'>气昏云雾朝，光寒风雨夜。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99571_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99571'>绝境邻梵宫，馀波沃农稼。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99571_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_99571'>秋态月色澄，晴蛟虹影射。<div id='poem_sentence_4_99571_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_99571'>势非蛟室卑，名将凤池亚。<div id='poem_sentence_5_99571_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_99571'>存身此蟠蛰，得时扶造化。<div id='poem_sentence_6_99571_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_99571'>何当岁大旱，移湫救函夏。<div id='poem_sentence_7_99571_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_99571'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_99571_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年1月</a>　朝庭派内侍省殿头高居简至桂州传宣抚问，靖呈表。作品：谢传宣抚表。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>　敕户部侍郎，有辞免状，不允，乃就。作品：免户部侍郎状。<div id='poem_1158772' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158772' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158772?labeling=true' target='_blank'>免户部侍郎状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1056年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158772")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158772_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158772'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158772'>臣今月十四日，进奏院递到敕诰各一道，蒙恩特授臣户部侍郎，依前充集贤院学士，候今任成资日，仍令再任者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158772_comment'></div>闻命惊惶，伏增陨越。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158772_comment'></div>伏念臣才非应务，智不逮人，徒以虚名，尝叨近著。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158772_comment'></div>顷遭谗搆，甘在弃捐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158772_comment'></div>属蛮事猝兴，起臣于丧次，而兵势未集，谋虑弗周，力小任重，日增忧惕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158772_comment'></div>及至归仁之胜，三军凯旋，破贼者乃臣青之勋劳，抚民者皆臣沔之经制，臣禀受节度，谋无己出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158772_comment'></div>逮乎远缚贼母，擒诛寇党，内则朝廷威令，外则夷獠协同，于臣愚拙，何功之有？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158772_comment'></div>昨闻转运提刑司举再任，臣寻以心力衰耗，不堪再任，已具状乞依旧分司，于韶州居住，庶得修营坟墓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158772_comment'></div>今来忽颁成命，就陟左曹，恩渥至优，实为过分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158772_comment'></div>清秩厚俸，谁不欲之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158772_comment'></div>事既逾涯，岂宜安处？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158772_comment'></div>伏缘本路外接西广六蕃，南连交趾九道，沿边溪峒，一百馀州，茍失抚绥，立生患难，非臣衰朽负谤之人，能堪久任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158772_comment'></div>所有降到敕诰，不敢祗受，已牒送桂州军资库收管，听候朝廷指挥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158772_comment'></div>伏乞检臣前奏，许令换一散秩，依旧分司，于韶州居住，所有边任，伏望别择材贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158772_comment'></div>干渎冕旒，臣无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1158772_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年3月</a>　接敕诰不许辞让集贤院学士 ，有表。作品：谢充集贤学士。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='ed5a325097094031a14296e729afc7af_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ed5a325097094031a14296e729afc7af");'><span id='ed5a325097094031a14296e729afc7af_link' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1057&endYear=1057')">1057年3月</a>　三月中旬，敕命知潭州。与桂州官员告别，赋诗。作品：酬和苏梦得运使。<div id='poem_99551' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99551' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99551?labeling=true' target='_blank'>酬和苏梦得运使</a><span class='authorDate'>（1057年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_99551")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_99551_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99551'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99551'>选任逢明主，休嗟尚散郎。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99551_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99551'>远均天雨露，全抚越封疆。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99551_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99551'>早振连城价，尝陪照乘光。<div id='poem_sentence_2_99551_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_99551'>宦途更险易，人事变炎凉。<div id='poem_sentence_3_99551_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_99551'>遽喜輶轩至，同期远俗康。<div id='poem_sentence_4_99551_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_99551'>交情重推致，民意乐舒长。<div id='poem_sentence_5_99551_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_99551'>况有江山助，无怀节物伤。<div id='poem_sentence_6_99551_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1060')">1060年</a>，61岁</div><div id='7c24c328738f48d19fcffc719f926216' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1060')">1060年</a>　仁宗闻交阯之乱不战而平定，大喜，派张焘为特使来祝捷。与余靖相会于桂州，靖有诗。张焘传仁宗口谕，拟令靖仍镇守广南，靖推辞年迈，仍知潭州为宜。作品：和运使张学士惠诗。<div id='poem_99480' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_99480_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99480'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99480'>澄清数路拥轻轩，列郡钦瞻已历年。<div -----title
南宁

showDetail'><a href='/Writing/99455?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢邕倅王寺丞惠韩柳碑文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1054年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a class='poemContent' id='poem_content_99455'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_99455'>南方异产足珠珍，薏苡兴谗不忍闻。<div id='poem_sentence_0_99455_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_99455'>一见知君清白节，箧中惟贮色丝文。<div id='poem_sentence_1_99455_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_99455'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_99455_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='3301416a8d0747d296282f5beb87281c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("3301416a8d0747d296282f5beb87281c");'><span id='3301416a8d0747d296282f5beb87281c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年</a>，55岁</div><div id='3301416a8d0747d296282f5beb87281c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年11月</a>　朝廷命靖主持邕州南郊享赦仪式。仪式时兵民云集，越南李氏朝廷亦派使参加。当众宣读朝廷赦书，中外边境臣民欢呼。有文。作品：贺南效赦表。<div id='poem_1158796' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158796' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158796?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺南郊赦表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1054年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158796")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158796_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158796'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158796'>臣某言：今月十六日，马递赦书一道至邕州，以十一月四日南郊礼毕，大赦天下者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158796_comment'></div>当时集本州官吏军民等，对众宣示，依例施行讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158796_comment'></div>昭事上帝，式遵大报之仪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158796_comment'></div>敷锡庶民，庸洽来同之福<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158796_comment'></div>恭惟皇帝陛下接千岁之统，逆三神之釐，震威九区，化覃万县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158796_comment'></div>偃闲师节，宣畅淳风，年谷屡丰，瑞典不绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158796_comment'></div>玉币涓洁，虔事天之诚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158796_comment'></div>坛庙肃祗，兼飨亲之孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158796_comment'></div>膺天地之贶，故二仪合祭而有严；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158796_comment'></div>承祖宗之休，故三圣偕侑而为始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158796_comment'></div>礼交乐具，物遂时康，均此纯禧，霈然诸夏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158796_comment'></div>神明来格，求福不回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158796_comment'></div>瑕秽荡清，与民更始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158796_comment'></div>至于斥去告讦，裁减赋租，诫诛求之官，释逋负之责，斯皆讲盛德之事，隆太平之基。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158796_comment'></div>九有欢呼，万邦同泰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158796_comment'></div>臣伏限守职边郡，不获抃蹈阙庭，臣无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1158796_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年11月</a>　又有贺表，由特使带回。作品：贺袷享赦表。<div id='poem_1158797' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158797' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158797?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺祫享赦表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1054年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22408, "北宋", "余靖", "poem_title_1158797")'>余靖</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158797_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158797'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158797'>臣某言：今月十六日，准枢密院递到祫享礼毕大赦一道，当时集官吏军民宣示施行讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158797_comment'></div>宗祊毖祀，讲堕典以亲行；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158797_comment'></div>雷雨湛恩，匝绵区而普及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158797_comment'></div>军民竦踊，中外欢呼<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158797_comment'></div>伏以国家祚禀赤精，运兴累圣，艺祖题期而立极，神宗弈叶以承休，迨文考之握枢，至太平而辑化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158797_comment'></div>并垂千古之馀烈，此皆百世而不祧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158797_comment'></div>恭惟皇帝陛下祗遹先猷，大宁诸夏，固尝备洁牲玉，奉见郊丘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158797_comment'></div>启八陛之坛，答二仪之贶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158797_comment'></div>侑三圣于上帝，祔群后于閟宫，亲籍田之耕，配明堂之享。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158797_comment'></div>惟兹合食之盛祭，久委有司之摄行，举是阔仪，允为大典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158797_comment'></div>辨昭穆之序，正乎东向之尊；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158797_comment'></div>均脤膰之禧，表乎祀事之重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158797_comment'></div>汉诏宽大，齐民乐康，减赋罢征，乃人心之至愿；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158797_comment'></div>恤灾宥过，实王政之所先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158797_comment'></div>垂髫尽识于升平，戴白同怀于悦豫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158797_comment'></div>臣无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1158797_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年</a>　是年，孙余惠应出世。仲荀曾患重病，隐而不告。长孙余尧臣中贡举。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='a80d806be0d948e998e2506e05004c3e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a80d806be0d948e998e2506e05004c3e");'><span id='a80d806be0d948e998e2506e05004c3e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>，57岁</div><div id='a80d806be0d948e998e2506e05004c3e' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>　到邕州金矿区察访，鼓励恢复矿山开采。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
信宜
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='abce61d53e5d4c8bbb9416ccc7073308_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("abce61d53e5d4c8bbb9416ccc7073308");'><span id='abce61d53e5d4c8bbb9416ccc7073308_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>，57岁</div><div id='abce61d53e5d4c8bbb9416ccc7073308' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>到高州怀德锡场察访，鼓励恢复矿山开采。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>是年，孙余嗣京出世。<br /></div>
